genealogical chart avncient historie onely trewe syncere cronicle warres betwixte grecian troyans subsequently fyrst euer cyon auncient famouse cytye troye vnder lamedon king laste fynall destruction vnder pryam wrytten daretus troyan dictus grecian souldiours present sayde warres digested latyn lerned guydo de columpnis sythes translated englyshe verse iohn lydgate moncke burye newly imprinted mdlv reader although battayles betwixte grecyans troyans laste fynall euersion ye cyty troy hisstorye worthye eterne memorye hath passed penne sundry famouse poetes great clerkes grekes latynes homer vergyle ouyde others whych theyr workes ther came handes men haue therfore hytherto ben holden chiefest reporter hystorye neuerthelesse part lye affection towardes theyr countreythemen homer fauourynge grecyans virgyle ouyde troyans partelye breakynge sayth theyr poetycall fiction historye peruerted verye trouthe therof theyr dygestes maye hope fynde trouthe theyr doynges haue onely laboured translator virgyle homer theyr peculyer vulgare language easelye consydered whome although confesse haue learnedlye ryghte well perfourmed theyr enterpryse therin yet hath ben beastly bolde vndertake wtout eyther wyt learning translate history namelye eanedes virgyle englyshe vnderstandynge searse word virgile met worke example man studyouse historye shoulde seke fynde doynges wyllyam caxton leawde recueil troye shoulde fynde thyncke assuredlye none thynge longe tedious brayneles bablyng tendyng end hauyng certayne begynnynge proceadynge therin ydyot follye make ende tyll bydden muche lyke foolyshe vnsauerye doynges orestes iuuinall remembreth wryt booke iuste volume filled mergentes outwarde sydes madnes whych wythout consydered tended purpose whych caxton recueil lyst wyth iudgement peruse shall rather thyncke doynges worthye nubred amongest trifelinge tale barrayne luerdries robyn hode beuys hampton remaine monumet worthy history yet hath wanted faythful trew reporter ye historye daretus phrigyan dytus grecyan curyouse worthy dedes theyr countreithes lykewyse preset al sayd warres haue dyligently regestred whose bokes although iniurye tyme long extant yet last beyng founde athene haue sin dewe conference ben founde hooly agre dyscourse ye sayd warres labores aswel darete dyte laste came syght handes lerned dylygent guydo columpna hath syncerelye pythely digested one latyne volume degree hath bene laste ye diligence iohn lydgate moncke burye brought englyshe tonge dygested maye appere verse estranayle well doynges hathe wythout doubte muche preuayled vulgare language hauynge prayse dewe deseruynges may worthyly numbred amongest haue chefelye deserued tunge verye perfect disciple imitator great chaucer ye onelye glorye beauty neuertheles lykewyse hapned ye chaucer lease ye prayse tyme wherin wrote beyng dede al good letter almost aslepe farre grosenesse barbarousnesse age vndersta dinge deuyne wryter bene time wherin kindes learnyng thancked god haue much floryshed euer anye former dayes within realme namelye dylygence one willyam thime gentilma laudably studyouse ye polyshing great iewell ryghte good iudgement trauail great paynes causing fected stamped nowe read ye sayde chaucer workes vtterly peryshed ye lest bin depraued corrupcion copy laste shoulde parte hys meaning haue ben founde euen iniurye almost hathe happened wryter pamphlite euercio troye printed xlii yeares agoe euen tayle hapned dercke vnlearned time suche ignoraunce bothe prynter correctour neyther shoulde seme eyther learned dnderstandynge englishe yt ye worke falsed verse either lacke folishe surplus displasinge ye wordes thereby ye sentence cosequetlye ye historye confused obscured place almost nothing gathered therof therfore muche meruaylinge hath happened whether lack copy dede otherwise yt boke thouly trew sincere english cronicle worthye historye whervpon many great clerkes language haue voutsafed theyr trauayles hath tyme whiche deede lacketh haue already doynges shewed selfes haue ryght good iudgement language bin purged falsyties redused nere mgiht conueniece auctours translation haue therfore taken vpon one studyous ye language countreyth although must confesse ye least able great nubre bring historian lyght somewhat truste perfecte polished inuertyng therin eyther matter sentence leauyng auctour commendacyon right apperteineth natheles would haue ben withdrawen myne attempte wt myght iustly haue recompted wt selfe consyder great enterprise vndertaketh goeth aboute brynge perfected handes men ye corrupted labour former wryters howe lyttle thanke gained therby shulde neuer haue dared haue bestowed hereof one penful yncke consideryng trauaylethe mennes doynges thought nothinge selfe therby men iudgmentes hath thancke deserueth shal discerne hereof may accompt iudgement like indifferent ma iudge whych hath purged ouergrowe felde thornes stone hath also sowed ye wyth corne shuld ye end partaker ye fruytes increase therof surelye euer shall take vpon hym thus trauayle others men labores whether ye lyst waye ye difficultie thing commoditye pleasure shall ensewe theym desirous vnderstande pryueties englishe tonge thincketh one worthy praise may say iudgemet trauayle ought thought muche lesse writeth owne inuecyo one commend ye quickenes ye witt thother declareth ripenes iudgement hauyng large fielde discourse thother copelled withi ye straight boudes ye writer one may vse ye frugalitye inuencion wytt thother must moderate yt hath greatest neade therof yet may passe lmittes one onely copye must perused many exaplars loked ouer therin maye chose lyketh fantasye yt shal seme come nere ye auctours meninge maye please pleasure reader therin shall compelled put theyr fantasye yet sparinglye yt maye neither adde take awaye shalbe thereto ledd certaine sure iudgmentes al thinges easie list practise maye sone discerne thus muche haue thought good set wrytynge worke thend reader maye admonyshed without trewe sincere englishe historyan lamentable battels destinye vtter euersion auncient famouse cytye troye also preuent malice suche shal happlye accompte trauayle herein rather rashe presumpcyon anye vertuouse imitacion wel doynge finis robert braham pthe prologue translatour myghty mar wt thy sterne lyght army hast power ye myght named arte easte tyl occident myghty lorde god armipotent shininge thy stremes rede influence dost brydell lede chiualrie soueraygne patron full hote drye complexion irous woode malencolyke nature brent collerike colour shininge like fiery glede whose ferse lokes ben ful drede leuene alighteth lowe downe sky iupiter bowe bene thy stremes passing dispyteous beholde inly furious thou causer art thy fyrie beames werre strife many sudrye realmes whose lordshyp cheifest capricorne crabbe thy power lorne causer art conteke strife loue vlcanus wife whilom yu mischiefe take helpe onely sake loue thy bellona dwelleth beyonde cirrha lybye londe vpon sandes rede helpe great nede succour stile dyrecte penne trace correcte whiche barrayne aureat lycoure thy grace finde succoure conuoy thine influence stumbleth aye fault eloquence reherse writen worde helpe mar yt art knighthode lorde hast manhode magnificence goddes yt arne highe prudence worke texplete ye refuse maketh clyo muse systren pernasus dwelle cirrha helycon welle renning full cleare stremes cristallyn called fountayne caballyn springeth touche pegase helpe also thou callyope mother vnto orpheus whose dytees melodius werbles resowninge harpe appeased wordes sherpe bothe parchas furyes infernall cerberus cruell founde coyed also bothe beast foule tree thy grace helpyng vnto thy golden dewe let lycoure wete dulled brest thy hony swete sugrest tunges rethoryciens maystresse art musciens mine helpe tenlumine wt thy worke beset cloudes dimme derke ignoraunce making procede theym lustye shall reade herte full drede whan prudent lysters hereto shall take hede makinge skill vouchesafe pray full beningly theyr goodnesse haue compassion erre translacion god take highly witnesse worke hertie lowe humblesse toke vpon good entencion deuoyde pride al presumpcion bokes olde antiquitye finde onely howe may vertue sewe theyr ample also eschewe cursed vyce slouthe idelnesse enioyneth verteous businesse yt longeth manhode dare sayne busyeth therto fayne haunte made prayer panim wise goddes humble sacrafise vpon wo great aduersytee onely mercy haue pytee turne ante fourme man thus gan praye coloure pale wan lande tenhabite standeth desolate alone awhaped mate comfortles creature releue endure ouide maketh mencion god iupiter herde orison hath routhe leste anone fulfilleth request might diuine grace made heuen shine beningly vnto earth adowne sodayne transmutaciowne ante brought fourme anon fete vpright gan gon thesaly salue kinge like liege toke theyr dwellinge within citye called tho egee ouide ye may beholde se people theyr worthinesse theyr strength great hardinesse mirundines longe haue bore name life ye reade may thee saincte mathewe called apostle much wisdome prudent aduertence besy labour wilfull diligence forseing great discrecion suppose mine opinion fable ante contriued wisdoe haue much acheued knighthod list loke manly dedes throughout troye boke al mischiefe wel haue theim borne full wisely prouided toforne fil werre peace gouernaile pelleus withouten fayle euery thinge seruiable diligent chambre table euer childe man vnto lorde al euer glad herte faithful obeyssaunce cheare yet countenaunce inwarde hearte outward shewing vncle grutching hooly hande worthy kingdome riche lande iason heritage onely tho yonge age pvnto pelleus payne herte falsly fayne shewe mente herte kept close yt nothing outsterte like addre vnder floures fayre herte tunge al contrayre benigne speche mening like serpent vnder coloure treason blente shewe goodly vnto allye inward brent hate enuy hoote fyre yet smeke couertly malyce yreke venim may pursute vpon iason fully execute museth euery houre time dradde se hasty prime folowe chaunge wonte done sodenly chaunge newe mone casteth wayes compasseth sore vnder coloure alway fell malice gan close hide like snake wonted glide venim vnder freshe floures sonne right hote shoures enuy hotter brent glede till time thought would procede execute meaninge euery dell port lambe herte lion fell double tygre slyghtly compace galle breste suger face man hath suspection purueyeth destruction neuewe within pretending loue fine gile malice yshet vnder keye entent man bewreye conceled hath full lytell rought vncle ne one thought whose meaninge conuenience malice linked innocence grounde deuise false enuye hatefull couetise whiche frette sore falsly winne croppe roote euery sorowe sinne cause hath bene sith go full yore many realme hath bought ful sore dreadful venim couetise ala let beware stande case pto thinke afore haue minde falshed draweth ende though bide last yeare two ende sothe shall sorowe woo bene false enuious hereof forth pelleus tell hath longe sought vpo thing till brought tydinges newe merueylous astoned house meruayle tho newly falle beside troy plage aobut eke eyen lokes moste horrible fourneys stremes visyble wolde tencrease glorye ram golde wynnen victorie fyrste must force myght vnto oultraunce bulles fyght theim vanquishe alder fyrst make theim humble oxe stall sithe theim yoke ere ye land manhode must take hand must also endure serpent huge great stature without fauour playnely haue oultraunce eke without wordes mo whiche serpent shortly tell lyke fende comyng hell pfull venym cruell hate skales harde plate armed stande defence brethe werse pestilence infecten wolde enuiron eyre eche place repeyre full foule corruption eke dredefull infection deth soth shortly deuyse fyne hygh empryse suche wolde quarell take hond ylyke one free bonde coulde bet selfe defende conquest eke ende myghty serpet slawe must anone custome lawe pout head tethe echeone arrace sowe theim selfe place ox eryd aforne seede sprange woder corne knyghtes armed passynge great myght eueryche redy fyght til eche brother ybrought groud mortall fate yeue dethes wound ende euerychone sowfastly non liue myght fatall lawe longer tyme lyued fellowe pand way dredfull peryllous desyreth ben victorious passe must manly endure fall take auenture estate excepcion chese wyll conclusyon may scape fauour ne mede begynneth vyse wel rede statute kyng may wyll entre assaye one hath begonne may chese tyll haue lost wonne yet ram expresse flese also bere wytnesse nothyng golde great treasour oetes kynge full hye laboure made kepe incantacions sorserye false illusyons pthat spoke realmes fer whiche many put theyr lyfe doubte hye desyre wyn great treasoure shyt within colchos londe ye haue harde deuyse whose pursuyte rose couetyse grounde roote wo myschaunce vayne reporte theim selfe auaunce whiche put theim selfe ieopardy without rescue lykely dye helpe ne sleyght armes vaile might againe ye cursed charmes stronge supersticious many worthy knighthode famous enhasted vnto deth ala ieoparde list liues case pthis lasteth forthe tyll afterwarde byfell pelleus platly hath hard tell great mischiefes destruction colchos wrought sundry nacions haue pursued thes auntres coquere tyll pelleus ferforth gan enquere knewe hooly trouth herte anone gan compasse myght slyght make neuewe iason vndertake hye empryse colchos wende way myght hym best shende pand gan pretende colour freshe hew ygylte outwarde lusty newe though treaso hyd within sawe also tyme begyn purpose tho fyrst made queint gan forthwith golde asure paint gaye wordes sownyng glorious knowynge iason yonge desyrous vnto suche thynge lyghtly wolde enclyne therfore thought honour flete lyue reste perfecte quiete thy supporte worthy gouernaile whose manhode may muche v auayle likelyhod eke moche amende soth saue v defende agayne al tho descryue mali wolde v stryue rebell ye world wherfore accorded within thy selfe plainly ne spare thyne entent sentence declare vvhan iason vncle vnderstade muche reioyseth take hand dredfull labour without auisement nought aduertith conueye make ye kyng wold seye condescende rather enclyne assente myght fyne comyng knightly hye empryse thus word worde shall deuyse right worthy prince preset place supporte hye grace goodnes excellet dign pacience fauour benygne displease may saye shewe efte declare wordes fewe fynal grounde cause coming ye lyste whiche ben noble kyng goodly wise without offence curtesye gyue aundience request ye disdayne goodly graunte may atteyne yle may auayle flese golde frely assayle goddes myne auenture lyste ordeyne fatall eure lyeth playnly fortune gouerne thynges comune werre peace conquest victorye armes renowne glory discomfyture bryngyng outraunce lyeth hyndre tauaunce ayen whose might mortal may chese wynne lese lyfe deth fyne labour ye lyste fauour gyue leue delaye accorded fully assaye lyke statute maketh mencion lyste make none acception vpon syde fauour fynde rytes playnly maken mynde euer fall shall vnder fonge lowly besechynge ye prolonge purpose make delaye grace sette daye myne enterpryse maye achyeue myne abode stant vpon leue saithe one word grauntyng ye lest haue fyne requeste pand whan kyng herde ceriously thentent iason sayd manfully stynt alyte kepte hym close whyle tyll last goodly gan smyle towardes iason said vnto hym thus iason quod albe thou desyrous vnderfonge passyng hye empryse counsayle lyke shall deuyse full prudently caste aforne mortall peryll thou lorne thynge lawe ysette chauntement may ylette remedyed fauour mede deth soth taketh hede guerdon platly twynne caste flese golde wyn helpe none manhode fortune streyght waye importune dredefull eke full rage saue deth lyeth passage victorye palme conquere sothly iason shall lere founded olde meruaylous workyng statute mortall thinge sore bounde vnder regalye rygour may modifye wherfore iason thou thinge attame leste afterwarde laide ye blame thy lesynge thy destruction faythfull herte true entencion warne selfe quyte man iustely shall wyte though thou youth thy wylfulnesse thy lyfe destroye without auysynesse sith iason peryllous case poynt point haue tolde al ye case auised put faulte surplus frely lyeth thinge syth thou mayst chese thou wynne lesse man iustly may arecte lawe mar hym selfe sette mortall man right may duelye passe hie lowe getteth none grace goddes lyste hym ordeyne euer caste hym darrayne diuers thyng furious drede wherfore iason euer thou spede haue openly declared hooly peryle fauour spared fer soth reason wyll ryght thou wotest wel lyeth might declare man lette manhode knightly caste sette vpon thing thou hast herde tell shulde longer mater dwell vaine thou knowest beware tourneth ball tyme thou gettest thou lyste put choyse word kyng rose vp anone vpon tyme whan shulde gone vnto meate iason syde ye shall ye lyste abyde time approcheth gan neigh fast offycers full busyly cast make redy busye cure halle bordes cure dyal hour gan marke pheb southward whirled vp arke hye lofte drewe none tyme kyng gone vnto meate entre halle oetes lordes knight aboute hym euerichon hercules also iason sette meate royall sea euery lorde lyke degree fyrste worthy man iason assygned kynge anone sytte owne borde hercules great lorde sette also faste syde marshall longer lyste abyde assygne estate shulde lyke hye lowe degree scaffolde hye alofte noise gan loude nothynge softe trumpeter eke clarioneres noble offycers full thryftely serued haue halle lyke season gan tyme fall deyntes may rekened sothfastly foyson plente kyngly fredom vnto hye lowe fulsomly gan reygne snowe ye hall ye manhod praised kyng renowne reysed gestes sothly sey whan hym lysteth chere festey lyke kyng thryfty wyse deynte man deuyse feast solempnitie grekes myght great nobely see kyng oetes worthynesse reporte therof beare wytnesse come lyue wante connynge ordre discryue euery course diuersitees straunge sewes sotyltees day serued place haue excused thoughe lyghtly passe though ordre sayne mine englyshe rude eke playne endite hye thyng forthe reherse kyng shewe gestes nobley ouer hath doughter sent speciall byd shulde forth anone broughte south though men sought world thrughout plain assure men might founde fayrer creature womanly porte manere demure sadder chere whose beaute lykely fade whan came grekes glade halle soth walketh vp downe womanhede pure affectiowne make chere vnto gestes newe thus medea rosen hewe freshnesse lyllye whyte entermedled kyndly delyte nature made face sprede egally white rede medlynge conclusyon ennewed proportion fynally excesse none one two one ioyned longe endure empresse called nature made lyke deuise beholde paradyse verye soth bothe one olde yonge sytten hall therto successyon borne heyre regyon father discent lyne abyde dure fyne syth ne ryght succede one heyre male reade also boke maketh mencion vnto yeres discretion able age maryed withstondynge also eke beaute womanhede one fayrest read yet none bothe haue youth let clergy desyre set passyngly speciall artes called lyberall expert knowynge beste vre konne lyste suche woman herde neuer telle helicon dranke welle tyme none semblable founde sothe ne none hable conceyue studye doctrine nature dispute termine coude also cause fynde sayde sondrye wyse rytes diuers sacrifyse encens ryches caste fyre shewe thynges lyke desire gootes horne milke blude whan mone equat stode fyfthe syxte house fortuned lokyng gracious houre conuenient fortunate enchauntement make worke sundry apparences well knewe heauenly influence aspectes bothe wrothe glade thynges made apperteyne suche experimentes whan lyst enchauntementes coude make wyndes blowe thondre lighten haile snowe frese also greue men payne sodeynely coude make rayne shewe wether list haue gasten men sodeyne erth quaue tourne daye vnwarely vnto nyght anone make sonne bryght shewe beames full persyng ful shene golden horne voyde nyghtes tene reise ye floodes wt many dredful wawe wha list coude eft wtdrawe eke yonge tree sere roote rynde afterward make againe kinde lusty braunches blome budde newe also wynter floures freshe hewe aray yerth tapyte hym grene beholde ioye sene many colour shewynge full diuers whyte rede grene ynde pers deysy ryche perled crowne floures winter made frowne vpon stalke freshly tappere sodeynely deadly chere coude somer winter tourne causynge daye mystes mone olde men coude make yonge efte agayne spronge coude shewe head berde ful hore graye crafte lerede tree wt fruite coude also make bare rinde leafe men stare eclipse mone bryght sonne naturally theyr course yronne apropred mai passe tytanes course kindly trase whan meueth vnder clyptik lyne clipse mott folow auctours list diffine discription bothe twayne full coniunction sonne beames red haue dwellyng dragones head mone set eke tayle nature maye fayle must fall eclyps veary nede sondry bokes like ye may read bycause certayne interfecacions diuers circle reuolucions maked ben heauen alofte whiche causen v fayle ofte freshe comfortable stremes v shad pheb bryght bemes mone hath made deuisyon sodeyne interposicion syght stremes visuall may beholde yet ysene luste fully comprehende phebus chaire cheuansende wonte aforehande see great ptholome kyng egypt telleth cause within boke compendiously bothe eclyps coniunction fall naturall mocion medee though clerke ouyde tencrease name vpon euery syde lyst suche thynges fable tell though poetes spryng well yet god forbede ye shulde gyue credence suche feynyng hyghe offence sith nature must denyed al suche affirmyng likewise diffyed euery christien stedfast beleue certainly wolde hyghly greue conscience wyse wene agaynst kynde whiche hye quene wight lyuynge creature shulde haue power plaine assure cursed thynges supersticious worke kynde contrarious pfor god almyghtye iudge iudges hath sette lawe whiche may falle amonge planettes eternally tendure afore ordeyned eternall cure whiche may clerkes lyst termine vpon syde bowen declyne discorde debate eternally yformed create fynger sapience alway meue intelligence lyke lordshyp bounde neuer yet eclyps yfounde mone beinge inconiunction haue tolde saue passyon eclyps tho kinde nature knot tyme lyst vnbynde whan goddes sonne starfe vpon roode sonne lyfe derked good whan heauen erth wt hye compunction haue sygnes shewed lamentacion earthquake light tourned derkenes dead body vpwarde gan dresse tombes againe deth liue stone rocke sonder gan ryue temple veyll kut two sygnes many yshewed tho ye wondre token meruailous great worthy dyonysyous vhiche athene clekes hym write called scholes ariopagyte whan sawe noble famous clerke bryght daye sodeynely derke although apaynym tho dayes infecte rytes layes moste chiefe principall phylosophers reken yet tyme astoned mynde sayde platly god kynde suffreth death doubte rounde worlde large shalbe dissolued ybrought nought sodayne chaunge hasty thought clergye knewe better skyll god may chaungen wyll hath power suche coaction vnder whose myght disposicion lawe kynde constreyned soth seye poynt poynt lowely obeye euery thynge hym lyst ordeyne elementes may course restreyne holy wryt doth witnesse ye may se request worthy iosue bryght sonne stode gabaon adayes space one degree shone shewynge token trewe knyght fynally gyue lyght myght hye prowesse cruell foon manfully oppresse whan fought knight iosue fyue kinges reignyng amoree longe laste pursuite chase tyll take hye trespasse dempt dead bible tell syth god thus hyghly lyst fulfyll knyghtes request orison wonder though passyon christe iesu incarnat sake sonne beames tho waren blak syth hath lordship planettes hym lyst must nedely fall medea though ouydyus fable writeth saith thus lyst name hyghe exalte yet truth somewhile doth halte albe passynge sorceresse chefest named chaunteresse pi wyll passe ouer agayne matere howe came meate ye shall en whan father thus sent se came anone commaundement came fynde tofore make beautie se men closet toke best araye tencrease euer shee maye nature worke royall apparayle woman gladly wyll fayle wha beautie haue pleteuous largesse embellyshe businesse ryche tire vpon euery syde ought mysse close hyde foule shall couertly wryed defaute outwarde espied pbut faire also well sayne porte womanly certayne comynge gladeth halle ioye vnto one se maner tho entree father bad take see besyde iason hym disporte womanhede recomforte pbut oh ala lacked hye prudence discrete auyse inwarde prouydence wysedome also perell caste aforne truste amayde tendre yeres yborne lyght vnhappy fonde wylfulnesse kynge gentylnesse commaunded hath confusyon dishonour destruction owne doughter borne heyre also womanly fayre sodaynly downe discende consydered myschyefe ende ala durst youth affye make sytte curtesye myght casuell mocion full lyghtly catche haue occasyon amysse ala dyd list take better hede therto auerte discretion wysely caste afore reason vnware chaunge womanhed whiche euery wyse man oughte drede euer yet mad wood ought reason coude aright good gyue fayth hastyly credence woman without experyence nother trust sykernesse ben double full brytylnesse harde assure vnto longeth nature theyr birth haue alliaunce doublenesse variaunce hertes fraile vnstable namely youthe meuynge mutable clerkes lyst tendyte albe sory wryte sayen chaunge mutabilite apropred ben vnto feminite affyrmed ful sage specially whyle grene age wexyng whan yt yonge whose herte full selde accordeth wt tonge trouth inwardely sought ye surplus remnaunt thought men may anone true patron fynde inconstaunce whose flaskysable kynde fro meuynge wynde hercules stronge binde nother sampson beleue woman herte make remeue blase whyrleth fyre fro flee desyre tyll accomplyshe fully delite nature kyndly appetyte kyndly seketh sewen fourme tyl course processe may performe euen woman refraine ne sewe luste fro man man cease till assayed wolde god nature apayed one fourme holdeth content whan boundes hath terme went desyre ferther procede styll abyte wyll excede example sortes woman wolde abide one duety shoulde holde paide stylle abyde faile foting doth ofte slyde content vnitee fast sewen finde pluralitee nature menynge shewed although among signes outward shewed ofte pretende maner stablenesse vnder hyd doublenesse well yreke outwarde eye full harde treason espye vnder curtyn veyle honeste closed chaunge mutabilitye desyre kepte full close mewe thyng leuest sewe outwarde haue laude declyne wt faynyng fraude pwherfore oetes thy wyt barayne thou afore prudence naddest sayne shulde folowe vnhappy case thou bolde thus suffer ala thine owne doughter inly freshe hewe straunge gestes entred newe folilye lete dele thrugh thin honor worship thin hele lost haste mischiefe brought strauge lande wt sorowe thought sclaunder thy name miserie sorowe shame ende made thou left sole myghtest well complayn make dole ala whyle prudent forsyght thou haddest grace record aright haue cast discrete purueaunce wysely weyed measure balauce fraude woman frayltye full selde sykertye latyn guydo doth expresse wherfore oetes verye rychelesnesse thou hast one augment thy wo without recure bothe two forgo fyrst thy treasure thy doughter deare passingly entere eke thyne heyre whe yt gone sayth mine auctour ther none thy daye occupye thy royall ceptre thy land gye pbut worth great prouidece waker kepyng busy diligence myghty mar god battayle might helpe defende ought auaile agayne wyt woman sleyght whose fraudes bene huge weyght theym lyst aye game goeth theyr purpose bydeth lief lothe slye prudent wyse storye playnly doth deuise medea engyne crafte father hath treasure raft working sleightie gyle ye shall heare within litell whyle sat meate tho tide father next iason side sodeynly freshe rosen hewe ful ofte tyme gan chaungen renew hundreth sithes litell space bloud goodly face vnto herte vnwarely gan avale therwithall waxeth dead pale eft anone therto take hede hewe returneth goodly reade still among temblyshe coloure rose meynt aye lyly floure though rose dele gan pace yet still lylye bydeth place till nature made theym eft ayene mete thus colde eke wt sodayne hete medea selfe assayled passyngly sore vexed trauayled nowe brent ga colde aye gan beholde iason yong gan desire loke hym set afyre beaute semelynesse euery thing inly gan inpresse sawe minde thought emprynteth forgetteth nought consydereth euery circumstaunce port gouernauce sonnyshe hayre crisped lyke golde wire knightly loke manly chere countenaunce many noble signe face also gracious beninge acceptable vnto plesaunce thought full suffysaunce without vnto alone well bethynke loke parsone time withouten drede meate drynke toke litell hede foode hath lost appetite loke hym hath great delite prynted remembraunce loue hath caught newely traunce ymarked fyery brond may escape honde yet eschewe stroke speciall yolde body hert vnto iason platly seye euer eft cast eye whan founde leyser opportune wysedome wolde contune loken longe lest men dempt amys maner woman kept close wonderly secre chere man could se ment none occasyon put theym suspection openly token sene cast rather men shulden wene encheson abstinence abode thus sylence onely womanhede honest shame chaste drede together herte met whych twayne haue mayde let meate drinke wold seme thus wit made theim deme cast theyr opynion thus blent discrescion cheare could euery thinge excuse gaue fooles matter muse pno chere vnbrideled tyme asterte one thyng closed hert alder chere declared maydens haue ofte syth spared shewe desyre dede falleth take hede flouren virgynitye theyr youth haue lyberty specyfy theyr hertes woulde kepe theym close bolde shewe summe theyr sentence thus medea kepyng aye sylence ne let worde lippes pace couertly sobre chere face ment sheweth eye sorte man could espye hoote fyre breste yreke selfe right thus gan speke sothe much good would god yong lusty man fayre semely sight assured owne knight plesaunt entyre berde ysprong shining lyke golde wyre wel ylimed compact measure well growe heyght good stature lyketh euery parte wele assent fortune whele ewred stande grace semeth vpon knightly face heauen beholde albe therwith herte fele colde yet sothe may none ala nill pyty leste knewe entent much trouth hym ment ala taketh maner hede albe brenne doth glede dead dare discure ala piteous woful auenture rewful helples mortall paine thus dead dare complayne frende foo chaunce ala find helpe succour case trewly nathles shall deuise nothing meane honest wyse lyke shall well openly founde desyre knyt bound wedlock neuer then twine meaning cleane devoyde syn grounded set vpon al clenlynesse without fraude doublenesse clean pure mine entencion lo aye maner condicion woman well fayne shewe one though thinke twayne couertly nothing sayne humble chere face playne enclose theyr lustes subtyltye vnder boundes al honestye theyr entent though trecherye withal surplus smothely couered though fayth afore pretend theyr fraude florishing defede speake full fayre word forth blede doublenesse enclosed end yet deceyte couertly yment vnder suger fayned cleane entent sothe existence truste well al apparence shewe one another meane whose blewe lightly dyed grene vnder floures depeynt stablenesse serpent dareth newfangelnesse playn seme wordes fair glosed vnderneth theyr couerte wile closed thing dearest theyr paye deny rathest swearen naye lyketh guydo wome endite ala cursedly would wryte agaynst theym haue debate right sory englyshe translate reprefe theym euyll seye leuer theyr loue deye wherfore pray theym take pacience purpose theym offence good perfyte euerychone reken trowe one hert trewe though amog chese loues newe wayeth wel nothing blame often tyme se men must puruay men refuse yf coulde wolde theim full excuse sytteth woman lyue alone store haue mo one praying theim grace hope theim trespace though makyng guido wryteth oryginall missayeth let hym beare ye wyfe syt well vengeaunce byte woman hath offended myght shuld well amended shulde receiue duely penaunce yf died withouten repentaunce dispeyred saluacion shulde euer haue remission yf content redresse may bene clerkes beare witnesse trouth alyue meane guido shulde shryue bytter clothe golde full stately wise whyle ye haue herde deuise medea chambre gone wherby selfe complaynynge euer one gaue issue paynes smarte sore hath wounded harte loue hath brought sodeine rage lykely soone aswage sothnesse furious god cupide hath fyre kyndled syde neuer lykly lete violent feruent heate encrease gan paine brest atwyxt twayne great debate stronge battayle feruently eche dyd assayle contek erne game departed betwixt loue shame metynge together vnset steuen albe fielde tho parted euen loue soth full hye renowne bolde hardy lyke fierse lyowne fereful spere swerd knife hote hasty auntre lyfe eke surquidous stoute full pryde chiefe champyon god cupyde causeth ofte free bonde full many peryll take honde caused hath full many man death many one yelden vp breth made ther woundes largly blede peryll loue taketh none hede get hym honour excellence fame pbut contrary enmye called shame lyke coward faynte hertles neuer dare sene pres lacke mahod draweth hi euer abacke ferd dreadfull wrake like chylde yonge tender age hath nother herte yet corage assayle feble myght yet full ofte hath stonde syghte many louer lete spede false cospiring brother dred drede shame allyed one assent haue piteously denyed vnto loue hert herdinesse ne durst worde expresse wha loue mahode willeth speake wood fyre brest reke vpon poynte shulde assaye shame cometh anone vtterly sayeth nay causeth loue horne shrynke tabashe chere pitiously wyncke cowardly cause tho appayre thus shame froward like contraire helpe drede loues folke feare doubtlesse shame nought ne kouthe aswell nigh ferre loue lawes shuld often tyme erre winde honestye cheyne bondes bridell breake reyne right horse trayse large lite nought louers wolde take charge vse wyll lust tensewe al shame kept mewe within brest wight knowe outward porte loue beareth ful lowe ne shame clekes haue compiled hertes daunger exiled al straungenesse feyned false disdeyne ne shame playnly wardeyne woman wrytyng olde without assaulte castell yyolde nede syege layne suche case longe treaty vayne nature louen processe pbut nowe ala dread shamfastnes haue daunted loue full lowe maner made humble port cheare haue eke vyolence manhode put sylence ben great cause morning paine thus amiddes either twaine loue shame euen vpon poynt medea stode tho great disioynt ne may paine endure hoote brent wofull creature betwixt meane loue shame whan loue wolde thing attaine desyres declare came shame anone put doubte redy dread lust deny thus stode doubtfull ieopardy loue shame maner traunce full euenly vphanged balaunce shame great loue yet yt well appeared syghes sore stormy cruell auenture dread shame durst discure fyre loue hath brest enclosed whiche full harde deposed thus hange amyddes betwene two ne wist best tyll fortune double face vnhappely hath wrought get grace whyrlyng whele causeth wretch full lowe adowne loute wha best wene sitte hye aloft plaine profe men may se full ofte gerinesse reuolution lady transmutacion full ofte time false full vnstable enhasteth thynges fooles full agreable ende confusyon vnder suger shroude poyson aye fortune maner wretch sheweth fayre semblant face flattery full beninge eye fully
