opportune shewe iason hooly herte made wt repentaunce sinerte daye meredien whan apollo beames shene southe plage gan wester fast oetes father hath ysent haste medea com hym anone bad shuld gone vnto iason hercules make chere amiddes al pres caught hath oportune space desyre sawe eke place father occupied thought bene espyed well apperceiuing great busynesse towardes iason anon gan dresse haste full knightly chere curteys wise gan drawen nere towardes ayen sawe let thus together met mede syghing first abrayde syth iason euen thus sayd phow iason helpe medea oetes daughter kynge colchos enamored achieued conquest golden flese cap vi iason quod thyne hye noblesse thy manhode thy gentilnesse thy person assembled yfeare thy knighthode first requere thy conceite thyne opinion arrecte presumption doublenesse yet inconstaunce womanhead neither variaunce bolde nothynge spare meaninge platly declare without deceyte wordes trewe playn beseching first shal sayne without goodly hede beningnely taken hede pacyently wordes ye lyste saye take best entent nothing greue thinges two myne hert sore ameue saye loue gentylnesse meane clerely expresse person nothing concele departe profe ye shall fele semeth first curtesye sothfastnes sith gentrye straungers euery maner wight bounde holde due right maken cheare trewely bycause iason se much manhode great worthinesse fayne businesse may lyke worde hert gan sike sake sayd thus ouermore fele full great anoy sore mened without auisenesse onely youth wilfull hardinesse flese golde getten ye may emprise euer assay perillous playnly achieue verye sothe ye coulde wene leue doubtles well assure finall mede great auenture deathe saue report shame ye wene getten name end playn shall tourne contrayre ginning shall fine varye wit man engine force might though neuer expert fight haue armes passing exercise ye sleyghtes olde newe emprise though best brethed endure deuise armure euer wepen bringe harded stele trenchaunt persing yet last whan hath sought without auayle may right nought pwherfore iason haue compassion youthe pure affection wilfully ye shulden thus lorne ben bloode line high yborne certaynly may none ye counsayle take none may helpe ease ala iason wyll ye appease manly corage case yblent counsayle bene obedient durst swere ye shuld haue victory ben remembred put memory perpetually knighthod win flese golde yonde within yle standes beside mar gouernour gide wherfore one selfe assente counsayle fully consent fewe wordes ye list spede leue lust worketh reade iason full humble chere answered sayd mine owne lady deare thanke best wise right thus ferre forthe may suffise power platly may attayne mine hertes quene lady soueraine ye may hooly well ensure life may dure trusteth right well liste fayne liue dye shall lust restrayne owne assured man obeye euer without chaunge doublenesse liue sothfastnes list trewe affection vpon life haue compassion gentillesse ye list haue suche chierte body saue good fayth verye due right ybounde owne knight vnto mine ende specially grace ye beningnely listeth selfe counsaile neuer erst degre ne seruice woman heade wordes ful goodliheade owne man listeth recomforte sothe reporte thousande folde plesaunt neuer erst merite gat graunt ne desert request prayer rather frely herte entere lyst vnrequired woo rewe vndisserued trewe ensure vpon fayth fast seruice shall vnto laste parseuer sothely shalbe slouth variaunce thereto trouthe finally saye withouten wene fewe wordes right meane list fayne flatter delude beheste deathe shall conclude parcas shall liues threde rend thus make ende vvell tha quod ful wisely hert ye must afore consydre aduerte aduenture ye shall take hande prudently perill vnderstande warely cast haue full well minde mortall harme tayle behinde well credible leue well impossible ginne honour also fine thilke flese hye power diuine preserued wyth marcys mighte therfore entreth fight full harde thence eskape fyery flawme bulles gape bene brasse trapped leuen ben dread lightening ye heaue tofore dint great thonder seuered hath full many toure sunder vnto ash man consume wherfore rede ye presume ram assayle lest ye laboure lese yet withdraw foote sith ye may chese good aduise discresiowne honour safe hye renowne ye list worthinesse onely folye hastinesse emprise head procede ye list like rede saue selfe woo al mischauce like ye shall mine ordinaunce ye commytte lowely lyste obeye without fraude seye iason ther tha sitting borde medea emprintynge euery worde waxed ire almost vnpacient sayd ala entent counceyle leue emprise certes foule cowardyse gyn thynge myght chyeue euery man wolde shame repreue eke reporte confusyon pride presumption toke whan large hye thynge great charge durst distrustyng myschyefe accomplyshe whan came prefe leuer myne owne lady dere ieoparde put selfe one wordes fewe smale pyeces hewe rather shulde cowardely forsake thylke empryse haue vndertake ye well knowe leue thus ala let counseyle plainly case euer happe falle trusteth ryght well shall none shulde cowarde harte fro purpose way diuerte without laude lyfe shulde lede shame eternall iustlye mede throughout worlde noted ouer euery lande spoke speciall iason hath hyghly vndertake wherof feare dare none ende make thynketh ryght well shall betide lyfe deth mischiefe abyde thervpon trouth ensure ferforth lyfe may endure shall parfourme haue nowe begon though honor may wonne muste deth beye wil leue bett deye liue ashamed cowardise slouth semeth hygh routhe man tappere dare shewe head whan hath one honour vyllanede time whan yt name slayne euery man shulde coueite rather faine dye honour liue wretche though thinge death stretche welcome beit shall well abyde betyde iason quod syth standeth ye algates desyre haue ought espye ye leuer shortly dye rather lyue haue ye saye shame yet ernest game suche monster vnwarely deale lyke dede hereafter ye shal feale therfore meued pytee greatly steered ye volunte without aduyse discresion counsayle elles deliberation lyst take meruailous voyage youth also courage gouerned ben chiefely matere luste two feare inparded ben ye purpose sewe impossyble ye eschewe sodeyne death nother free bonde crafte man hath power withstonde pwherfore thinke herte good entent cast yea yet ye shent tourne shape remedye suche routhe haue ye shulden dye father loue rather ye shulde wise loste shall offende vtterly displease friendes may ease shall fynde suche meane weye least se deye case thinke gyde shall sette asyde first discent stocke royall pand ouer myne heritage withall lykewise honour shal put abacke helpe shalbe lacke yfounde ye kinde ye lyste haue mynde deserue goodly quyte consyderyng first nat alite saue lyue stant ieopardye peryllous ye ought espye shall ordeyne crafte atwyxe v twayne parte hope shall well vpon poynt may fele faythfully ioye woo smarte full accorde body herte desire ye condescend vndertake make therof ende pthis sothly ladye sayde iason tho assented without wordes mo fulfyll euery circumstaunce euer thinge may plesaunce quod saine firste wt fayth herte plaine myght busy cure meanyng hole ye assure hereafter take wyfe holde kepe terme life dede accorde may wt hest fyne summe requeste except ye shall ordeyne repayre father reigne faithfully ye shall lede whan ye shall succede death heritage herte aye one lyke corage ye shall alwayes founden true cherishe chaunge newe like mine estate without varyaunce ye lyue haue remembraunce gentlenesse great nede none aliue may ought spede lyueth mortall assayle force marcyall dragon bulles yfeare first lere hooly manere howe shall gye like thinke specifye whan happeth mete againe none may helpe herin certayne case whiche platly ye shall fynde naught aske ye ayene kynde sothly quod iason al shalbe ye deuyse faith theron assure oh goodliest creature euer yet sawe vnto paye fayrest eke soth naye bountie ye ben incomparable death ye ben marciable whyle lyue saye fayth myne herte meneth tunge sayth wyll founde aldertrewest man life death euer grace pleasaunt perfourme hestes graunt fully worke saluation ye haue sayde full conclusyon truely ye bearen lyfe beaute haue prerogatife passyng echone list glose amonges floures doth rede rose somer amyd leues soote vere hath made roote humidyte kyndly ascende barrayne soyle clothe amend winter blastes haue shake bare sote blosmes freshly repayre medowes many sundry hewe tapited bene diuers floures newe sundry motlees lustly sene holsome bawne shad among ye grene pryght rose fayrest echone ryght hath nature set alone made first deuise aboue haue pryse ye bene bounte spring welle therto beaute sothly ye excelle beare life comparyson ne may made discrescion ye passen euery man may se finde vnto goodlyest euer yet borne without lorne helpe succoure fully destitute ne founde refute fro al fredom meward doth haboud passingly euer bounde ferre forth sely life may stretche sake death ne reche vnto might pleasure bene helpe goodly list sene neclygence shuld thing refusen ye would might reason full well merked noted eke wilfull nycetye folylye voyde away grace rage aman chase wilfull fortune whan beninge wherfore nowe hooly resigne herte body lyfe eke death hande ye lasteth breath othes affirme may parseuer mine endinge daye trewe spouse haue sayd sworne behested playnly toforne vpon euery thinge obeye may please till time deye shuld longer tarye behest shall neuer varye pthus whan medea sawe stedfastnes supprised hye gladnesse great ioye pleynly herte voyde euery wo smert lowly lust obeyd went thus seyde piason quod shall well ordayne meane waye wherby twayne may eft agayne leysure mete sone perfourme done matterlike entent shall made finall sacrament desire man shall vnbinde though nowe therto may leisure fide toward eue shall eskape trust right well time shape right secretly may mete yfeare shall sende priuy chambre mine shall conuye vnto chaumbre priue wey certayne houre withouten fable entent shalbe greable vpon point phebus wt light ywestred eke dercke night hath wt dimmesse shadowes black hemisperye fully ouertake oft giueth fauoure fortune vnto theise louers leysour opportune perfourme lustes achieue right anone shall drawe eue shall vnto closet send euery thinge make ende togither shall leysur speake euerich hertes breake eft declare summe haue spoken fill good leysur fully byhete shall ordeyne whan v lust mete set time euer say nay alway nyght whan passed day myghty ioue wysely succour hence forth wyll hooly whyle lyue wakyng slepe ye hestes kepe iason lowly gan enclyne sayd far man may ymagine wight may clearly comprehende wyll vnto liues ende seruaunt trewe faythfully quyte though saye lyte fayth shalbe nerthelesse though paynt compasse gay processe soueraigne hertes quene tyll dead shall trewly meane haue trouth whyle haue lyfe mind end ye shall hereafter finde theyr speche ende thus make medea shope take leue anone amonges prese first father syth hercules longer bode forthwith anone haste vnto chambre gone vp downe made many went none meine wetyng ment casting wayes purpose achieue wittes gan busyly meue thus rometh habytacle side let obstacle thinge would sore greue study till drewe eue leue complaining wo many thought walking fro pthe midday hour gone ouerslide tytan fast doth chayre ryde day arke east west compassed fyry stedes haue almost ouer passed orizonte drowen downe ful lowe golden waine man might know hidde fyery beames bright discence full farre syght hirenes cope myrke euening begon dirke twylight day gan faide hesperus beames glade ben freshe lusty merye gan recomforte hemisperye pwhan thus medea selfe alone hyghe desyre gan make mone longe abode knyght alwaye accountyng houres nyght full trouble busye thought hath full streitly serched sought ready waye wel setting purpose albe kept full close amyd herte quapping wawe dreade feare tyll hope gan adawe bad shuld ryght mery glad tyll dreade agayne made sobre sadde lest desyre troubled let thus abay yset amyd hope fearfull dreade also ne wyst best pfor desyre hygh affection hoote brent opynyon lust mete iason agaynst dreade come anone made fearfull lest espyed ill holpe remedyed onely fortune derke night whych made full glad lyght recomforted onely two good hope made glad also gan anone casten deuyse moone heaue would aryse whan horne pale wolde shed lyght vpon hylle vale gan acounte caste well tyme founde quarter passed pryme well knowyng arte sawe soth fourth part mone shadde newe lyght passed course aryght tyme coniunction three sygnes full computacion dayes seuen complete age pat time brennyng rage one darted cupides arowe gan loke beholde narowe euery dore listen busely wyght myght espye courte walke go man romyn fro sore dradde goynge vp downe whan herde noyse sowne wha heareth whisperyng venim sothly ere wished slept fast bed pytyous lyfe longe nyght led wtout respite though wyght coude knowe till hye mydnyght cockes crowe whych tyme whan al bushte styl taccomplyshe remnaut wyll euery made sylence cleped anone vnto presence aged vecke fer yeares yronne crafte mikle helpe kon thriftly bryng thing afore casten euery doubte pof yeares passed olde experyence hath gyue theim passyng hye prudence loue sleyghtes knowe made dogge bowe medea discureth al thoughte fro poit poit hath forgat righte nought charged release smerte recomforte troubled herte haste anone vpon waye vnto chambre iason conuaye anone rekles case gone hym forthe easy pase newe lere hath brought ye shal heare vvha cock comon astrologere midnight hour wt voyce clere began sowne busy payne beate breste wynges twayne time mynute wyll pace warne place tide season night medea awayte vpon knight full ready entre kepe lyst full lytell slepe ne parcell thought wha iaso chambre brought without espying maner wight anone conueyeth hym full ryght closet haste maye full well besene great ryche araye syde made take see first al ylke lease thre expert case sodeynly tourned brase olde vecke stare vpon mone walked hath theym left alone medea dores fast shet iason downe anone hath set first finde busy might chambre set vp light torch great cyerges ful royall aboute pyllers euery wall whych gaue lyghte like ye sonne shene cheste wrought crystall clene firste taketh passage whych toke ryche image pure golde full lusty beholde theyr custome rytes olde myghty ioue eterne increat yhalowed also consecrat whych image deuoutly ought humble hert iason first brought made lowly theron take othe vnto last lyef lothe shuld take vnto wyfe fro daye forthe duryng life herte vnfayned fayth inuyolate cheryshe lyke estate fro till tyme finde euer floured vyrgynitye myne auctour well reherse aye kept cleane touche man thought dede neuer amys herte hooly gyuen vnto iason euer mo anone hath put hande vnto swore fully ye haue heard saye requestes without delaye kepe aye life may laste oh ala soone ouercast hest fayth wt assured fraude flatterye ured couertly innocence trewe meanyng diligence euer deuyse deceyued falshed man though ye trouth apparent aboue yet doublenesse slyghly shoue though sothely allyed trewe meaning yt nothinge espyed vnder fayre chere faining fallaces might haue wrought case tha thy sake ceptre regallye lordes eke alie forsoke one toke hede pitye goodly hede loste friendes good fame iason saue fro shame yet moreouer forsoke heritage borne hye parage shulde haue succession heyre dissent region womanly wolde quite yfeare hath set mite one houre hath forsake vnto hath holy take trust thou shouldest haue kynde rich honour hath ylefte beynde exyle hath chose gone kynne sely mayde alone palas wepe thyne vnkyndenesse hath fro death fro distresse preserued yet thou takest none hede shuld haue died ne thy read thy conquest cause may shortly clause write bountie briefly comprehende effectually perfourmed ende wordes fewe ne may tolde thrugh yu hast riche flese golde manly conquered withouten doubte vnlikely haue brought whan thou helpe tho destitute thine comforte refute thou maiest denye erthly honour gan defye conserue heuinesse eke father hath richesse enpeyred pitie whose example woman may well lere shuld faith trusten man ala medea mykle sterres astronemye yet sawe afore destinye loue hath put gouernayle al crafte ne myght auayle slowe calculation caste afore constellation birthe eke wofull fate rekleshed sawe late suppose connyng fallyble doubtles semeth incredible wiste toforne piteously lorne ye shall se hereafter hastely story teacheth befell iason medee fyrst ye shall maner holly see gan wirche swore night ala hath forbore maydenhead great pitie yet mente naught elles honestye suppose went haue wyfe touchyng holde strife yet one thing dare afyrme sayne meaning twayne ne one wonder fer atwene truely gan meane honeste thynkyng outrage like maide innocent age perfourme fleshly false delight acheue fylthy appetite wrought euery thing entent contraire ala tho debonaire truste vpon curtesye acquite gentery hastely rewe vpon smarte woman ben pytefull herte wyll gladly shewen petie mishappe se man fall saue lyfe rather shoulde dye medea shortly seye castyng peryll shall fall desyres lustes holy obeyeth full might longe almoste night hath course rounde gone whiche tyme thus spake iason lowly sayde lady time aryse soone wyll pryme ye may see well day beginneth springe may howe byrdes synge prayinge beste wyse shall worke ye lyste deuyse ceriously euery thyng dispose beseche goodly freshe rose myne enterpryse bring vnto ende erst fro hense wynde saue thincke first treate maner ye shall countrey lete grece repaire agayne whiche lande great felicitie trusteth wel nothyng adrede reygne shall lede conquest wynne wherfore pray goodly begynne shall worke hast may good fayth anone wil daye pto spake saying ye shal myn owne iason vnto deare selfe conclusyon assented ful affection wittes hole herte enfourme ye shall asterte euery daunger lytell yle ye lyst bide whyle vp rose haste maye cofer treasour laye wet anone brought hode ryche ymage syluer fonde sothely meruaylous entayle whose power vertue auayle effectually entent agayne magik enchauntement syt force sorcerye made astronomye houre chosen equat none clerkes olde full long agone whilom wha flouring age vsed make ymages kyng called thelomee iason wylled hath medee beare ymage hym pryuely ye haue herd worke effectually euery thynge dyd assygne toke hym medycine made maner oyntment hym enoynt brent riche precious tha bawme agayne malyce eche fire flawme toke hym anone ryche rynge wherin set stone vertue venym destroye syde myght hym anoye stone furthermore might yf man coude beare aright within hand next skyn enclosed strength syght shuld deposed theim would gasen beholde euer hand holde vertue infallyble storye sayeth inuysible stone prudent clerkes call achates vertuous founde sothly cecile stone whylom wrote virgyll venus eneas sente first whan cartage went pand iason toke certayne byll wrytten lyke boke iourney myght much auayle bad wysely ne fayle bethought graciously spede first scripture rede ram touche wyse charging eke afore hye empryse humble hert great deuocion knelyng saye oryson vp downe wrytten bill praying goddes lowely fulfyll request mercy haue pitye mischiefe saue chiefe socoure toke hym vyoll lycoure bad manly without feare drede come vnto bulles reade hym cast knightly escape fast seeth theim gape theyr golles lycour caste hym nede lytel theim gaste theyr iawes togither shall glyewe syde shall eschewe bide lust hym lyst constreyne doubtles maugre al theyr busye peyne shall theim daunte therwt make tame hym list earnest game myght theym make louten encline theym bowen backe chyne lycour shall theyr iawes coharte lyghtly shall sundre parte offende noyen wight whe thus sayd vnto knight euery thynge gyue instruction playn doctrine informacyon shall scape daungers take hede worke auysely pand thus agreyd thought ye best parte men theyr rest awaked drewe towardes daye well sawe morowe graye lest men theym suspicio hye prudence discrecion atwene twelight rody morowe toke theyr leue wt saint iohn ye borow oft kyssyng louers whe twinne went left within beyng hope mete agayn daye iason fast euer maye gan ordayne iourney achieue thought would ano go take leue wyse wtin litel whyle maner rude style purpose sothly spare supporte playnly declare vvhan rowes rayes rede estward v full early gonnen sprede euen twelyght dawnynge larke custome gynneth sing salue heauenly laye lusty goddesse morowe graye meane aurora afore sonne wonte tench se blacke skyes donne derkenesse dymmy night freshe phebus coforte light brightnes beames shene ouergylt hye hylles grene floures eke agayn morowe tyde vpo stalkes ga playn theyr leues wide whan iason companye toward kynge full fast gan hym hye fonde lyke estate sceptre hadeful pompous elate hye see regally sittyng full kyngly amid cheualrye lordes enuiron pat tyme yonge champion vnder vowe standing ram sterne face tofore kyng cam besechyng hym magnificence day graunt lycence hys armes make mo delayes concluding playnly assayes daye felde found achieue lyke bound olde behest poynt declyne life death till parfourme fine holy auntres flese belonge kynge requyryng loger prologe goodly graut fine empryse kynge ful sobre wyse consydering summe demaunde iason spoke sayd shall commaud request perfourmed hast albe quod ful sore agast wylfulnesse thou shulde destroyed lest men thy death arected vnto therupon would blame set royall power ne let thy manly youth ieopardy sothe great vylany preiudice estate name afterward men put blame false reporte wrong opynyon withstode thy destruction pwherfore rede yu yet bet auysed counsayle let dispysed better honoure certayne thy country repayre againe wilfully take hande mortall thyng man may withstad rede fully myn aduise take hede therto syth ye wyse lest thou repent late yf thou wilt algate thy purpose holde rede almyghty mar praye thy spede gyde whatsoeuer shal befall eke praye goddes safe sound thy body restore thou gettest pand whan iason thus herd kyng dismayed stoned thyng knyghtly wise reuerence thankyng highly royall excellence grace beningnytye vpon death hym lyst haue pytye fully concluding touchyng battayle nother rede counsayle wyse purpose withdrawe lyke statute playnly lawe right far forth fortune wyll hym eure besyde auenture settyng asyde euery feare drede platly sayd wyll procede parfourme hath vndertake ydle mo skylles make allege againe iason full openly plaine touching ye surplus dredfull thing departyng thus sayd kyng audience tho lordes hereafter fall euer malys theron muse worlde fyrst excuse goddes platly acquyte though deye ye nothyng wyte ne man shall arecte skylle worke freely wyll agayne aduice hye prudence lyfe death presence hooly herte neuer flytte vnto goddes fortune commytte lyst ordayne againe whose wyll shall neuer plaine ne shall put blame betide honour ioye shame thyng thus ende make tyme leue take tho stande one one toke hande wyse forth gan hym dresse anone thyncke expresse vvhan titan wt feruet hete drawen vp dewe fro leues wete towarde myd morowe diffine vpon houre whan clocke nine iason full manly full like knight armed stele cherefull glad lyght gan dresse hym forth hap euer fal sayd dieu vnto feres boote vpon stronde lone whan came londe water vessell lafte fyrst remembryng crafte medea circumstaunces shulde kepe obseruaunces euery thing well mynde anone full manly fynde shope forth went knyghtly pase toward bulles forged wer brase point whan iourney gan medea wexed full pale wan sore agast nothing might glade ruthe see wo made teares chekes twayne full pyteously gan destylle rayne fordewed wedes blake aye sorowe made sake lyke woman fearefull doubte armes ful maly brought sobbe syghe peace lest hast ought rekles fro point point bad life hath hym lad pand se shulde defende gan anone greces assende touret hye pynacle myght haue tho none obstacle lettyng nother haue syghte hym owne chosen knight euer amonge wordes brake stoundemell thus selfe spake po thou iason souerayne hertes heale thou ought knew wo fele sothly trowe shulde asterte trewe thy hole herte god praye iourney leste may tyme tournen best kepe ye saulfe sounde euery membre yefe might fully remembre taught fourme euery thynge fully perfourme day thine honour anaunce se hole pleasaunce certes iason fylle ought amisse fare well helth worldly blisse fare well mirthe solace welfare fortune grace one harte suffisaunce plo gouernaunce first fro ye time lande hath nome first whan thether come bulles fell dispiteous caste fyre flawme furious fro mouthes wonder large huge againe whiche chiefe refuge hym saue brent enoynted oyntement body kept damage thilke fyre full rage smoke darke full horrible whiche escape almoste impossyble man estate without comforte counsayle medee whose doctryne iason worke scaped mistes darke syre blases blake eyre cloudy hath make hym made discrete sage vertue onely thilke ymage whych necke bare wherby prudent ware ye bulles haue feersly gaped hath theyr malyce auysedly scaped enfection theyr troubled eyre hath vanquished dispeire effect agayne foule fume would man vnto death consume ymage ful preseruatyfe diffend saue lyfe surely kepe drede ful ofte sythe wrytte rede vertue thilke oryson vnto hym full protection fell therby distresse rather sykernesse preserue mortall case toke lycoure vyall therwithall full lyke manly man one toke bulles nought forgat warely cast therwtal theyr iawes closed fast vertue mightely englued ther hath vtterly eschewed hole enfection smoky leuen whe eyre gan clere al ye heauen ye mystes wasted toforne maly hert raught hath horne sterne bulles vyolence drew forth defece yo keth maner plough made go pase vp eare londe lyst buxom fonde soyle smothe bare playn redy made bearen grayne renges tourned vp downe tho theym rebellyowne humble meke redy desyres playnly fulfyll pand iason lyke champyon gan enhaste towardes dragon beast ryght great mostruous foule horrible deadly venimous armed scale large thicke breath perillous wicke eayre pestylence venim vyolence full deadly eke mortall throte issued al flawme fyre fournes mouthe lyke leuen downe south east wont tempest smite right dragon sothely wite mouth flawme blased wherof iason lytell first amased hert dreadfull thynge wha remembred ringe feare dread layd asyde gone ringe set stone ful ryche noble right vertuous whych teacheth great ysydorus mine auctour also finde comenly cometh ynde must kept chaste wonder cleane colour surmounteth euery grene whose vertue venym destroye withstand may anoye dragon serpent adder snake specyally betake yholden opposyte worme euen agayn syte without abode sothe may chese venym force must lese stronge vyolent rage stone doth ful great damage whan hath vertue blyue peces smale gynneth ryue selfe abydeth whole whyle land called cecyle worme yt bufo beareth ye name men malice make tame venym vtterly expresse take quil mine auctour beareth witnesse wha wyll worke large ende stone set line right agayne wormes heade holden tyll deade sothly vertue nature venim last may endure presence ryche stone finde bufo ryght anone myght therof brusteth eue twain onely kynde may restrayne goddesse called nature whych next lorde al thyng cure hath vertue gyue herbe gras stone whych man knoweth selfe alone cause hyd closed hande wyt man vnderstande openly myght workyng iason vertue rynge ston yt might hi auauce hath dragon brought vttraunce fonde maner resystence hym wythstand force diffence neyther venym none stryfe wherfore hath beraft lyfe manly wise fielde outrayed iason full glad well apayed hath wt sword spet many stroke layde hym men newe oke bryght skales hard dure well vnneth ne might endure hym dysmembre smite head anone stede sede gan tethe head arace right forth selfe place gan sowe right men corne vpon land eared aforne whych fede sprage wonder grayn bright armed knyghtes standing ye playn anone wt sharpe swerdes groude eueriche gan hurt wounde tyll eche felowe hath cruelly yslawe theyr fate fynal lawe none theim shuld vyctorye death reioyce memorye yfeare thus haue made ende iason gan wende vnto ram dylygence fonde power defence maner stryfe rebellyowne mightely ram draweth downe set hand vpon eueryche horne slewe first hath shorne flese golde passyng ryche world ther treasour lich maketh delay take boote hast may roweth forthe yle hercules meane whyle vpon bryncke many mo abode iason till ydo euerychone finde blyue onely ioye aryue gan thanke theyr goddes gracyously hath yfall flese hath knyghtlye wone shone cleare somer sonne brought hym vnto lode feares abydyng stronde whan apollo dayes arke ye west almost yronne marke fast gan downward drawen declyne wawes full watry gan shine yet passed occian iason come many manly man coferes presence kinge acheued euery thynge longeth conquest ram oetes soone euer cam make hym chere outward hath hi pained albe herte sothely fayned full sory withouten dread exployte happye spede iason flese hathe wonne lyke sothe feyners koune theim lyst craftely compace shewe outward faythful meanyng face albe venym closed hole within meaning maner syn ryght kyng wyth loke forhead clere made vnto iason outward right good chere gan hym speake wordes fewe frendly head many sygnes shewe though conquest hole euery dele poit point like wonder well full glad fortuned vnto ende hath contuned ioyeth speche countenaunce fortune lyst far forthe auaunce paleys gan fayre conueye daye daye ful rychely festeye albe nothing done herte le felt full great smerte treasour despoyled hath ryche flese forgo domage confusyon thus great dyuysyon atwirt chere meanyng thoughte oft fareth yt dewlye sought many man meanyng false double calme couer trouble hyghe malyce hyd desyre rake falsly wycked couert fire ful hote brennynge inwarde enuye wel hym cowd theim espye knewe theyr meanynge false fraudelet ala ful many innocent deceiued wote meane namely suche trouthe wene euery cheare men theim make innocence best take wyse thynke well ryght certayne iason euery dell hath take gre ye kyng hath wrought aduertyng ye grutchyng thoughte doubtles tho sat king full sore ram hath lost euermore hath vtterly ysayne thoughe still grutche therin gayne fynally necessety tyme might none playnly sawe may chese algate flese must lese whether lyef lothe fayneth chere though wer wroth onely gentilnesse signe outward grutching doth expresse daye daye verye curtesye cheareth iason companye whych tyme aboute enuirowne euery partye regyowne people came staren gase vpon ram mase loke wonder deme lyst whose dome lytell tryst oft varie tourne fro wysely taketh hede therto comon people chaungeth phane day wexe morow wane doth mone flaskesable trusteth shall finde full vnstable glad iason sped wel sory lyke neuer adell sayd woder myght agayne dragon bulles fyght agaynst force marte yle alyue might astert sayde perauenture craft wrought dyscomfeture charme sorcerye thus eche theyr fantesye gan deme hym longe daye last bout makyng delay ful glad lyght medea downe descedeth chambre outwardly pretendethe sadnes chere nothig ne knewe nought could men coceiue hew secret meaning hath womanly demened eke prudently auoyded discrescion fantesye suspection man coude working deme nothyng well shuld seme porte cheare cause whi processe drewe pryuely towarde iason lere secretly bad ere wyse ne leue chambre come eue matter hadden treat shal knowe leisur whe mete anone entred night sole hym selfe without torche lyght medea hath waye take abode sleples sake wonder deuoutly desyryng gesse treate holynesse touching matter contemplacion smitte deuocion freshe venus holde memorye alone oratorye openly ypocrytes praye dyuers angel ioyning waye people commended haue night dispended vayne glorye none laude selfe thynkyng fraude secretly ilke twayn alone without light eyther sonne mone long nyght haue led wythout rest thought beste speake slepe till pryme cast lese tho time thus nyght together dispende dull comprehende obseruaunces relygyous prolyx workyng compedyous demeth selfe ye get well ye wote euery faculte hath knowyng experyence men wyll hym rather gyue credence wherfore saye ye wyse whych rude man deme thyng namely passeth knowing also wyt fordulled myne imagynatyfe deme practike speculatyfe wherfore passe let ouer slide forthe thynke ye list abide playnly tell iason medee whych accorded assented grece wede goeth shortly ende vnwyst father euery wyght saue alone hath trouth plyght trewe well wo vnto last mo phow iason conquest medea felowshyppe retourned agayne thesalye cap vii whan iason iournee full rychely lyke vnto degree refreshed colchos kynge withall might lykynge moneth passed gone grekes assented one purposed hath shortly yf might medea stele away nyght takyng wt hym great treasour ye rych flese ful assent also hercules pbut medea thou hastest fast thou slawe wysely cast shuld befall yu thy iourney toke mischiefe forsoke false eke vnkinde othes wherof fynde thou eue morowe thy fatall chaunce thy pyteous sorowe weptest gan thy selfe rende tyll death made wofull ende vaine maken rehersayle wote nothynge howe might auaile howe iason vnkynde none receyued hath penam tallionis goddes disnaturelnesse mischiefe wretchednesse made eke ende though cruell hate felle mar loo mortall fate twayne made ende suppose lyke writeth guydo gynnynge vertuous ende foloweth full contagious ala yf hadde taken hede aforne mischiefe forlorne wyll afore mischiefe se may eschewe haue aduersitie ende platly deuyne euen lyke right medicyne auayleth whan sycke dead may helpe stomake head lectuarye emplaystre pocyon receite confection herbe stone lech knowe whan corp layde earth alowe por whan beast tourned careine myne auctour sayth veyne recure seken halowe ere leyne salowe veryly fantasye helpeth doth remedy thynge perfourmed due date vertue hath tha wha cometh late right case veryly semblable worldly trust false full mutable caste peryll tyll falle stede sugre ofte tasteth galle blended luste tho present future slouthe necligent theim ne lyste afore mischiefe caste tyll snare englued faste prouyde graceles full indiscrete wilfully richeles caste peryll tyde sewe lust reason goeth aside befell whylom two medea iason also pbut euer iason fynde playnly harme alone great damage fynall smerte lacke wysedome ne wolde aduerte shuld fall wha iourney toke father folyly forsoke syth wrought wylfulnesse without counsayle auysenesse lyst harmes bewayle lyte nought myght auayle let alone complainyng damage well wote touchynge passage take good plyte mone hastynesse began soone chesynge houre fortunat alone frendes desolate colchos forsoke shyp gon haste byddynge iason hercules companye comyn thesalye without tarying forthwith worde yentred ben within shyppes borde cause wynde good euery thyng tho luste stode thus assented stale awaye nyght treasure catche myght ladde plente vitayle forthe anone began sayle many coast many sondry yle towardes grece meane medea glad good chere iason syttynge yfeare hercules gentylnesse comforte busynesse al faynyngly maner sake louers full queynte make tyll haue hooly pleasaunce lust fulfylled vttreth varyance iason preued vtterly hath forsaken full vnkyndly medea paine sorowe wo guydo ne wryte wordes mo maketh none mencion bycause trowe myne opynyon sorowes ende euery deale rehersed full openly weale methamorphoseos write full plaine naso recordeth certayne death heuynesse percell eke vnkyndnesse iason telleth playnly howe medea hath sonnes slowe lyke father visage telleth eke put rage falsly hym excuse loued called ceruse eke pistelles taketh hede deadly sorowe may beholde rede howe trouth aboughte sore medea ye gete boke auenture wyll nowe busy cure hooly tourne stile iason werre made lamedon like guydo openly described grece aryued first whan iason hercules also ylonded many mo within land reygne thesalye kyng pelleus chiualrye caste hym playnly wyll fayle mete neuewe ariuayle whan mette countenance chere made outwarde hoole entere soueraygne gladnesse knighthode highe prowesse renowne manlyhede expleyte good spede fortune encrease name hath caused noble fame colchos honour repayre albe chere vtterly contraire entent euer came agayne face hole playne welcomed hym al herte full sore astoned euer asterte auentures colchos peryllous retourned victorious couertly treason hyde delaye gan sette asyde iason chere full benyng heritage fyrste gan resygne septre crowne kingdome ye leste perfourme summe beheste like assured bonde iason toke honde gan vncle full lowe manere first thanke herte entere pand ful knightly gan pray goodly wolde saye mattere fret herte sore daye daye encreasyng euer besechyng hym graunt hym audience touchyng wronge vyolence done vnto hym whan harme ne ment troye lande colchos wente saye kynge troye towne within bondes region whan myne great aduersitye winde wether fordryuen sea v refreshe lande dyd aryue purpose hym stryue rest v wo lytell whyle forth anone go sothe maner harme ne thought vnkyngly malyce sought agaynst v fynde occasyon byddyng haste voyde region notwithstanding come peace lyke brother knoweth hercules vnto wyght doyng distresse wherfore praye hygh noblesse purpose condiscende whiche platly fynall ende sette full conclusyon hooly worke destruction lyke auowe whan thense went ye goodly lyste assent one strongly spare maugre myght troye fare may fynde fauoure v refreshe golde treasure eke curtesye v strength also cheualrye pand pelleus without abode anone matter vnderstode assented herte wyll also voyage theim go worthy regyowne kynges duke lordes renowne accorded one saieth naye go theim helpe may iourney chiefe solicitour hercules worthy conquerour pand haste retenewe make towarde spartos hath way take whiche yle grekes pertinent fully obeying commaundement whiche pollux castor eke also worthy king mighty brothern two fynde tyme gouernours bare crowne like noble werreours brothern also vnto eleyne poetes lyketh fayne iupiter deyte vpon leda begat three beautie dyd excelle eleyne lyke bokes telle conceyued tyndarys yle vnto londe ioynyng cecyle therfore fynde yle called tyndaris byrth lyst endite forthe thyncke hercules wryte hath besought noble king twain mighty hande busy payne graunte wende troye warde shortly ende assente saye one nay power catche may againe tyme lyst assygne hercules chere full beninge thanked behyght forth wente haste might toward messene stronge mighty londe within whiche noble king fonde knightly man worthy thelamon lorde prynce region armes one manlyest lyue egall beste whan knew hercules com ioye hath hym armes nome receyued maner thynge lyke sat worthy kyng whan wiste sothly mente without anone dyd assente hym gone troyens greue hercules goodly toke leue hym enhasteth thesalye agayne pelleus telleth hym certayne howe hath spedde besechynge hym also haste may letter sende lordes call assemble worthy knyghtes thrughout lad yt nigh ferre suche knewe yt experte werre also counsayle sage wyt yronne age force without experience whan manhode mente sapience loketh well may double auayle longe haue vsed trauayle lyke playnly suppose may helpe moste iourney dispose vnto age experience wytte youth force hardinesse sytte whan one entent fully accorded worken assent quarell grounded vpon ryght thrugh helpe grace yt hath treble myght nede drede spere wt shelde knyghtly wyse holde feilde knighthode fame glory armes conquest victory assured vpon multitude manhode grace lyste conclude ptherfore let v auenge wrong first right make selfe stronge efte force manly shewe knyghtes chose taken fewe auoyde encombraunce numbre shall foe beste encombre hercules hath sayde kyng pelleus tho right well apayde thought counsaile righte good hercules without abode great haste meine gon prouince called pilon whiche duke noble fame fynde nestor name full renowmed stronge chiualrye eke kinred allye hercules bloud whan plainly vnderstode purpose hole cause coming graunted hym without taryinge go hym selfe hym voiage worthy baronage ready agayne certayne daye hercules faste euer maye repaired ayen thesalye gathered holy nauye lordes full redy apparayled well enarmed rychely vitayled pand pelleus hath taken fyrste sea euery lorde lyke degree yshypped ready gon hercules also iason behestes manly fulfyll towardes troye citie spylle sothly fynde abyde vpon wynde pnowe iason hercules prynces grece assembled aduenge ye vncurtesy done theim lamedon expedicion towardes colchos cap viii vvhan sote stormes apryll vnto roote full lowe gan destille lustye licour many holsome shoure reyse vertue hyghe vpon floure phebus ascendyng sphere brest smote beames cleare ram full colerike halowynge veer equinoctiall whan mayes kalendes entren sothe zephirus swete breath smothe tendre brauches enspireth doth spryng euery bushe freshe blosomynge hylle water reuolued snowes whyte yt phebus hath dissolued bawme vapoureth vp lofte eyre herbes softe rote vertue colde wynter hydde hath full myght force ykydde erth herbe euery tree shade braunches humiditee araysed sonnes heate moyster raynes swete whan siluer welles sheden stremes ryuers gylte sonne beames newe greene againe largesse shad vpon euery playne nightingale wodde ronge full amorously welcome songe lusty season freshe desyrous namely hertes whiche ben amorous whan sea calme blaundishinge fro trouble wynde wawy boylynge tempest sure escape season grekes forth shape towardes troye erles duke kynges shyppes stuffed wt maner thynges werre myght auayle ryght anone began sayle whan redy without abode eche shyppe water rode whan winde lust gan blowe ioye se go rowe whiche made hast speden waie short tyme comen ben troy hauen called symeonte whan phebus fer vnder orisente westred men myght hym se grekes byn past peryll sea cast ancrees thynking best shippes night reste ye morowe whan larke songe worthi grekes maly stroge began lande haste myghte troye grounde tentes pighte afore towne great dylygence ne founde maner resystence whyle sette good awayte euery syde leste deceyte tyll houre sonne bryght morowe shade rody lyghte amyd fielde vpon euery tente whiche tyme one assente grekes assembled euerychone byddyng kynge anone iason fyrst hercules many worthy beyng prese ben tente pelleus ycome wha lordes grece al assembled place met eche degree set pelleus whan al whist styll right thus began ye sentence wyll po noble worthy hye estate lowe whose knightly fame throughout ye worlde yknow reported fer shineth sonne grekes yet neuer thynge begonne ne victorye ende ye lawrer fer men may wende crowned ben thei toke suche thier happe se lande pwherforeye lord worthi renowne ye remembre kyng lamedowne wronge yt vpon wrought whan harme none ne thought must quit shortly ende come stroie shende wherfore anone haste may lette v set without delaye fyrst rede taken hede thre thynges helpyng nede pfirst aduyse good discretion defence good saluacion prudently wardes make none oures mischiefe take ylke daye lacke prouidence seconde diligence might hole entention labour full distruction come foe selues glory pand thirde may victorye inioye platly laste ouer ye maye afore well caste knighthode hardinesse may vanquishe shal hye richesse conquere possessyowne knowen troye towne plentie shalbe founde golde tresour doth passingly habounde shyppes sothly wene receiue ne shall mow susteine habundaunce yonder within citie wyn god v graunte wyll pand also faste kynge styll noble knight stronge hercules presence worthy prese said counsaile highely comende wyse begynnynge preysed ende effecte purpose brynge counsayle mornynge tofore discured byn daye v arme haste maye fielde payne deuyde mayne twayne tone shall kyng thelamowne gouernour hye renowne kyng pelleus shall haue gouernaunce wisely theim saue selfe iason brother shall secretely go vnder citie sonne shynes bushaile thicke vynes shall v hyde kepe v full koye lamedon kyng troye anone may may espye grekes cheualrye citie yssue anone v fyght venge hym fone whan cometh shippes warde nestor duke shall first warde mete hym castor shall also whan seeth time knightly haue ado helpe nestor nede thirde warde pelleus shall lede whyles ye thus occupye iason shall v faste hye vnto citie vnwist echone doubte shall wyn anone doth counsayle auayle trouth ye may fayle conquere citie yonde tofore ye gete pand accord wt al stregth might enarme theim stele yt shone full bryght againe sonne morowe whan riseth wrought hercules deuiseth pof battaile betwixt grecian troians wherin troyans discomfeted kinge slayne citie taken rased destroyed ca ix kyng lamedon whan herde tell coming list longer dwel went many noble knighte flouryng youth desyrous fyght tho mighten armes beare coude shote handell durste spere pand whan assebled fielde eueryche armes depeint vpon shilde brouded bete vpon coote armure lamedon busy cure set ordre wardes maketh fielde forth waye taketh towarde grekes lyne right fully purposynge abide fight ware behynde aduerteth casteth mynde great sleyght treachery shape coude espye forthe wente wardes set grekes anone hath met herte bolde astoned duke nestor first sturdy wall whose manhod neuer founde lacke full knightly vpon horse backe herte men knightes eke gan prese many worthy greke lamedon sturdely mete whiche tyme felte full vnswete frounter many manly man sharpe speres first together ran eft swordes sharpe kene ygroude thilke daye geuen many wounde met thus euery syde thrugh plate maile woundes bledde wide basenettes riue ye crowne noyse stroke eyre gan sowne blode tho shad new grene soyle chaunged hath hewe dyed playnly red vpon whiche full many man lay dead many worthy lost lyfe certainly mortall stryfe grekes discomfyted echone ne castor socoured anone folke troy manly haue bore many knight grekes ylore castor entreth bataile knightes sore assayle worthy troyans yt spere shielde grekes agayne recouered haue fielde many one lieth slayne vpon grene thrugh girt body wt sharpe speres kene troye mortall stoure driue backe tyll came socour hast worthy lamedowne whiche entred like wodde lyowne made waye vpon euery syde made swerde glyde deth manly hym bare well vnneth none dare abyde stroke rydynge vp downe made waye enuirowne renges hath foen soughte dai armes meruailes hath wroute manhod worthines grekes hath brought suche distresse swerde flyen death marciles many sleeth slaughter grekes wer confuse tyll pelleus came rescuse irous wood fall rage thought wold ye great pompe aswage troye dyd anone vnhorseth many one felly slough stode aforne many harueys hath yt daye torne made sheldes ryue sonder beholde wondre til lamedon people sawe go backe pelleus brought wracke wherof herte felte full great payne beseching efte repaire againe kyth might like men endure fielde made recure tyll duke nestor knewe lamedowne amid fielde kynge troye towne right anone without abode agaynst hym full great pace rode whan kyng first espye hye dispite rancour enuye knightly wyse gan tourne againe nothynge agast hye disdayne yrons herte enbolned pride horse fyersly smytyng syde ye pricke ran red bloud forth nestor like wood rode anone spere brake full knightly kept horse backe full delyuerly againe quite speare full sharpe whette byte thrugh sheld brest gaue woude fro hors felde hi groud whiche fall kyng nothyng ferde vprise ayene knightly drewe swerd angre fret hym herte rote vnhorsed fyghte muste fote wherof partyfull confuse tyll one cedar came rescuse made knight ye selfe yere yonge freshe lusty noble chere syttyng tyme noble stede whan gan take hede saw kyng foote mischiefe fight gan forth pryke hast might toward nestor spere hytte sadell made flytte downe ground afore kyng lamedon anone full lyke champion recured vp hymselfe defendeth many stroke eche spendeth sharpe swerdrs kene byte eueriche gan foyne smyte tyll lamedon dispyteous chere face rased viser strype one sinet ryche cercle basenet large perle goynge enuyrowne creste fyersly beate downe whyles nestor thus afore hym stode face depeint bloud certainely soth conclude grekes great multitude rescued lamedowne slayne faste bore downe vnto earth amonge horse feete castor thought ne wolde lete helpe behelde yfeare yrously toke mighty spere cedar spake late gan ryde pricke deadly hate came toke doubtles troyan knight called segnerides cosyn cedar whan hath sene courser rode anone bytwene spere smote castor stroke broken two castor withouten areste hath spere amyddes brest segnerides gyue mortall wounde lykely neuer sounde wherfore cedar caught hath suche enuye anone fell melancolye dispyte boylynge herte segnerides beholde smerte maugre grutcheth amiddes ye fielde myght castor toke shelde vyser rancour rage wounded hym amyddes vysage eke horse fro hym also caughte squier manfully raught certainely stode suche disioynt worthy castor poynt haue taken troye tho foote must haue go ne pollux many manly knyght mo vii hundred stele armed bryght rather come castor rescue whiche sore gan sewe maugre castor fond force reste enemy hod horse restored hym agayne pollux certayne anger feruent ire agayne troians rancoure set fyre al one vpon theim set mode fortune met troian knight called eliatus armes yonge freshe desyrous wonder semely yet tendre age kinges sonne also great cartage neuewe eke vnto king lamedon pollux hath like fierse lyon without compassion pytye mercye within renges slayne ful cruelly lamedon whan gan take hede inwarde dole felt herte blede whan hym sawe point vpon deathe full pyteously yelden vp breathe vpon playne lay beforne whiche anone made sowne horne time came riche araye seuen knigh tin haste may vpon deathe auenged merciles theyr great crueltye grekes haue confouded lyeth one dead another wouded might hold tacke mortally made theim go abacke gan tourne theyr confusion fynally daye wyth lamedon triumphe fielde ygone saue ala towne anone vnto king came messengere hath tolde wt ful piteous cheare grekes haue citye take pthen se wo tho make would haue made piteus herte bliue dole sundre riue sore gan within selfe mourne wist partye may tourne weuer abiding longe afore sawe mighty grekes stronge citie another hoost behinde almoste wo went minde sodeynly backward behelde toward citye sawe come felde first hercules iason theyr sleyght wonnen ye towne hast cruell hercules mighty giaunt force pereles lyke lyon wood dispiteous tygre ramage furyous gan newe theim troye assayle sworde perce plate mayle laboure full mate feynt longe fight werinesse atteynt came lusty freshe grene force might sustene rode among theim yonder cruell wise seuered theim sonder put theim hooly high mischaunce rule gouernaunce kinge oppressed al dole wardes destytute sole mischiefe left infortunate comforte fully disconsolate hercules full dispiteous loke sharpe spore stede felly toke cruelly rode forthe lamedowne earth fiersly bare downe vpon hast might downe horse sodeinly alighte mightely rent basenet swerd sharpe grounde whet smote head grace cast forth selfe place amonge horse cruel violence without pytye reuerence arage raught horse agayne like lion renning playne bare slough ca weye many troyan yt time made deye like shepe forskatered wide destitute gouernour guide ne reade shortly conclude grekes double multitude gan theim enchase death ful blyue wel vnneth left one alyue felde haue ben day victours triumphe like conquerours citye toke waye rende adowne wall sparre rafter treasour rich towne toke anone theyr possessyowne euer grutche lefe lothe found plainly wt gothe temple great violece goddes doyng reuerence spoyle without dread feare vnto shippe euery thing beare mercyles croked olde lame theyr swerdes made cruelly tame childre soukyng theyr mother breste kill sley withouten arest yong maydens wepyng distresse full gentyl borne great semelynesse theym led may excuse theyr freshe beaute falsly misuse waste bren consumen roude aboute brake adowne ye wall exyone kinges doughter dere passingly entere life meane lamedon meke bening condicion hercules hath anone take dreadful pyteously gan quake delyuered vnto thelamowne entred first towne gift receyued hath gree bycause surmounting beautee treated would like kinges doughter shuld syth hath wonne victorye worship owne glorye hauing regarde highe degree shuld rather knightly honestee knighthode wedded therfore sith blode gentill bore false lust agayne goodlihead vsed beautye womanhaede dishonestly sinfull wise royall blode lyke high empryse doctrine nature right like nurture gentil knight consydered fyrst birth kinrede grene youth eke maydenheade good fayre womanly therto kinges doughter byrth also haue wed coulde haue shame thelamo sothe thou blame errour thy gouernaunce kindled ful highe vengeaunce hote sparke enuye ye world ye fire gan multeplye like quenche hete hatred olde bren lete newe flawme taketh hede smoke dread storye hereafter shall knowe wha towne bret brought low bothe toure wall wt ye soyle made playn nothing stode might sein vtterly grekes theym oppresse makyng waste like wyldernes pfor good treasour ryches infynyte many iewell full pleasing delyte theyr shippes towne lede shorte tyme homeward spede treasour stuffed habudauce good sawe wether stode wynd also theyr lust ga saile home lad yong exione many mayde mo troye grece go sayling forth within litell space escaped fro sea grace vnto land aryued merely whose commyng grekes vtterly ioyfull theyr good spede specially guido reade theyr shyppes wt golde treasour lade wherof herte wexe wonder glade outward well borne ouerthrowe haue fewe ylorne theyr meyne thanke theyr goddes al grace theym fall wt ye treasour yt haue home brought full many pore made vp nought throughout yt lad habudauce much good great suffisaunce wight among theim nede many day blessedfull lyfe lede yeare yeare reuoluciowne theyr manhod theyr high renowne theyr honour ran round world theim toffende many lade hath doubte theyr knighthod wyse vntill storye last agayne deuise matter ferther procede fauour goodlyhead wil rest lytel space tha vpborne wt supporte grace taccomplishe vndertoke ende first boke make quakyng hand dreade onely feare shall reade lest ye ala hasty mocion ne haue compassyon pytye routhe vpon rudenesse lowly besechyng gentilcesse mercye onely nigh ferre ye finde fayle erre correcte ye flyt grace hooly commit pthe translatour complaineth misfortune troians losse theyr city liuely describyng tykle estate fortune gouernaunce beginning chapyter secound boke persewing matter sayd historye ca x enuious ordre fortunat meninge worldly thynge false flikerynge nil suffer v present life lyue reste without werre stryfe blinde fikel vnstable course false ful mutable sitteth highest ca downe encline whe least weneth bring hym ruine awaytes gladly ben sodayne face parted twayne shewe hole wha lest tryst well deceytes wist engine trappes knewe courte euery daye newe sothe well affirme dare mortall man may life beware vneuen peysing balaunce counterfete fayned countenaunce lo ing playn cheare flatterye vnwarely blere mannes eye begile sothe face blandishing smothe hath fro high degre made low full falsly smile make mowe yet somewhyle varyaunt hewe vnto pretendeth trewe whylom fauorable false like deceiuable reise one bring another downe false lady transmutacyowne giueth renowne victorye doth theym floure honoure glorie appayre false fame giltles perde put man blame goodly beninge disdeyne also malygne agayne make hym lowte lowe fro see great kinges throwe theim auayle high toures plonge worthy emperours hyll hye prosperetye vaile like aduersytye ryche emprishe rancoure dysdayne eft pore enhauce agayne false goddesse eyen blinde set one afore another goeth behinde doth one renne maketh another halte one high rich exalte plonge pouertye man may haue securytye suger hony distilleth bottel fylleth bytter gall mirre aloe thus lady wilfull rechles froward peruers hath seller drinkes ful diuers fraude falla ministreth piment bawme ypocras sodeynly soote past custome giue cast conclude falsly fine bytter eysell egre wine corrosynes fret perce depe narcotikes cause men slepe thus theim aproche swete bitter broche thus reygne quene varyaunce whose ioye alwayes fineth mischaunce trusteth ouercast deceyue playnly last estate soeuer double lady mutabilitye se example king lamedon hath brought confusion litel cause thing nought crueltye hath deare abought wherfore reade euery man take hede gin quarell nede litell fyre vnder ash reke may kindled breake flawme men may apease best suffer moste shall haue ease therfore ye kynges lordes euerychone make myrroure lamedone well ware violence vnto straungers none offence whan come fer region ne suffer theim none oppression within bondes haue wrong owne though ye strong mightye eke among liege another daye perauntre may befall ye ful lytell thynke sodeyne case thus may ye aquyt ythanked another place auenture ye may fayle grace therfore ye may espye theym good cheyre curtesye prudently consyder witt lorde gentilnesse syt euery straunger goodly haue nothing may honour saue refreshe frely disporte may good reporte whose cotrary hath much wo wrought afore time well sought first troye thus vtterly destroyed people sorowe wo acloyed lad exyle farre theyr cytye lyuing thraldome captiuitye exyone ye haue herde tell led grece thelamon dwell guido ca teache take great vengeaunce wreche eyther parte trouthe heare great routhe boke ye may hereafter rede ceryously ye list take hede gladly aye reuolusyon fatall thing disposicion enuyous alway meynt wo world go truely may aduert thought value thyng nought mortall cause werres first begonne strife debate vnderneth sonne meued first small occasyon caused great confusyon man harmes halfe endite cause deare inough mite eche one redy destroye man litel stryue brother blode vnkynde greatly drede ala ne take better hede olde troye newe smal encheso trouth knew fynally brought destruction olde bokes make mencion many worthy many noble knight slayne felde duresse fight kynges prynces siege ben deade wha attropos lyst breake theyr liues threde tel mischiefe wo want connyng fele also pen quake tremble hand lyst lorde dradde sea lande whose worthines thrugh ye world doth sprede rude makyng shal beholde reade whych colour full naked bare mercye spare disdayne list haue pytye feare tremble shuld se pbut onely mercye yt doth hert embrase byd presume fully grace seyng hym vertuous good mercye annexed vnto royall blode prince longeth nigh ferre aye fore ryght pytye preferre support high noblesse ayene style dresse wryte forth storye newe troye ordre seryously mine auctour latyn guydo wryt praying ye reader wher wordes missit causyng metre halte lame correct saue blame let hym wayte haue curyosytye sith rime englyshe hath skersytye dull certayne ne guido ensewe clerke curyous man whych latyn hath rethoryke set wordes ca lyke sewe style translation worde worde like construction maner gramariens like stile rethoriciens toke storye translate clio came late craft hath great experience leue wordes folowe setence trouthe metre set also asyde arte tho guide reduce whan went wrong taking small hede eyther short long trouth lette curiosite making metre purposyng much varye dyuers contrarye vnto guydo discordaunce conforme fully substaunce onely meanyng conclude one albe ne waye gone sewe floures eloquence peyntyng haue none excellence sundry hewes noble freshe gay ryche coloures byggen ne may must procede sable blacke ennuyng ye fynde lacke axe mercy fro twyn fauour nowe begyn haste stile forth right directe erre pray correct tyme whe troye towne destroyed yt king lomedowne also slayne crueltye hercules tofore cytye sonne storye telleth v heyre ycalled priamus wonder manly discrete eke prudent time troye absente father lost hath lyfe tyme hecuba wyfe sonnes aboute castell laye knightes get may hath theym mightely werreyed father falsly disobeied vnto hym rebell wonder longe albe priam saute huge stronge theim assayled oft many syth strength like knight kyth get armes worship honour theim daunt like conquerour cast fully departe day day life gan ieoparte tofore walles preue mighte many baron many worthy knight flowing yet lusty bloude age flouryng knighthode assautes maner strife first auenture life herte men lyst behind dread death sothly find afore castell hygh thyck ywalled wife hecuba called pryam ful worthy degre fiue sonnes yonge doughters thre pof whych eldest hector called also fer phebus compase naturall daye cercle goeth fer hym withouten doubte reported renowne name worthynesse noble fame like bokes specifye roote stocke chiualrye knighthod soueraygne floure sour well worship honoure manhode dare well expresse patron myrrour high prowesse ginning grounde yfeare wonder benynge lowely cheare discrete also prudent vertuous dedes actes merueilous remembred ben long gone alone excelled euerychone olde auctours reade ye may finde knighthod yet make mynde pthe next brother called parys nature gaue deuys shape fourme beautye semelynesse recorde excellent fayrnesse time withouten dread ferre passed reade eke full manly knight vsed shuld fight hand beare mighty bowe archer man coud knowe none might foud seke fer nere shoting might hardely pere founde whan alexsandre called also pthe third sonne hight deiphobus worthy knight chiualrous armes ful great renowne man high discresciowne wife cousail min auctour within werre ful oft vpon toke knighthode many high empryse storye lyke shall deuyse pand boke like wryte vergile poete olde wt soueraintye style king pryam also hecuba sonnes two recorde vergelius one named pollidorus priamus grene youthe ye cominge grekes kouth troyewarde haste anone golde treasour many ryche stone hath sent forthe besyde vnto kinge ful great trust haue kepyng till tyme sawe conclusyowne shuld befall towne eke fine werres shoulden take vpon theym grekes tho make thilke kyng false couetyse treasour ye haue herde deuyse whan sawe fortune varyaunce toward pryam vnhappy chaunce lyke tyraunt murderer also childes throte made cutte two full crueltye made men burye priuelye man might treason vnderstond besyde sea depe vnder strond pthe sonne also reade vergile called fayre ganimede iupiter hath forest hente vpon daye huntinge wente bare vp aboue sterres clere heauens made butlere eternally hym wonnen stede hebe owne daughter dere pthe fyrst doughter kyng pryamus hoote creusa sayeth vergilius eneydos sothely wedded vnto eneas eke storye sayeth enee wonderfull natyuytye father fynde doubtles tyme called anchyses hym begat venus goddesse fayrnesse wyght could neuer yet se man passyng beautye storye touchyng workyng shall declare many wonder thyng great loo vergyle hath giue eneydos booke worshyp enee compyled hath like ye may se knyghthood many strong batayl hym acheued wan itayle full long time royall towne troy brought confusiowne conquest yf ye lyst take hede poete ye may ordre reade armes wrought al age comyng also cartage fro troywarde within litell al ye may behold great vergile panother doughter also founde kyng pryam birth secound called cassandra ful great sadnesse maner diuineresse eche arte experience thynges future fully prescience tell afore shall betide fame sprang costes wide kept chaste aye virginitye eke prayer honestye led life deuocion rite religyon pagynisme vsed tho dayes obseruaunces keping layes pthe third doughter boke saith mo hardy armes noble founde called sonnes naturall exceptinge neuer one worthy knyghtes manly men echone name lyste knowe shall fynde wryte vpon arowe story eueryche begynnyng fyrst eldest brother pand while pryam syege laye tofore castell gette may therabout hath many way sought wofull tydynges vnto broughte grekes haue taken troye towne slayne father worthy lamedowne citie olde foundaciowne full piteously tourned vp downe worthy lordes gentle men echone taken slayne ylefte one lyue grekes crueltie ruyne ala citie exion owne syster dere lad exyle eyen cleare pwherfore kyng herte astoned sorowe nist sodayne wo gan hym constrayne sobbeth wepeth mortall payne thought herte wolde sondre breste hye distresse myghte haue reste teares gan selfe destylle deye fynally wyll pand fortune falsly varye drery herte gan bytterly warye hym deceyuable inly cruell vnmercyable dispyteous sterne face vengeable deuoyde grace enuy raged thought hath hir worst mali hi wrought felly shewed myght worlde neuer wight wo suppose maner age reaken harmes damage whiche anone euer maye hast chaungeth ryche araye tryste heuy deadly face pale astoned mortall tale desyre haue dead countenance enclined head lyfe lad clad blacke sodaynly syege brake wolde tho lenger abyde folke anone gan ryde pyteously gan likwise wt morne toward troy attones efte returne pand whan hath cyty founde plaine soyle euen wt grounde hye walles whylom thicke longe ybeate downe made stronge toures paleys pryncypall buildyng excellent royall famous ryche great noblesse founde tourned wyldernesse people slayne syster ladde awaye wo ne wyste saye constraynt aduersytie harmes wyll cured time right fully sure vpon syde foude might recure wherfore nought sobbe wepe fro brest wt syghes sought full dede broken pale dead visage thus ala furious rage full pyteously hooste without respite continued dayes three tyll laste darke skyes blacke gan wo partye slacke tempest deale gan withdrawe wepynge bladyshe gan ye wawe whan floode wo ouer paste ebbe ioye folowe must haste sorowe euer wolde hertes shende terme euery wo must ende though fredes may wepe wayle deth teares may avayle wherfore kyng care hath sought waye citie repaire caste hym fully wolde make vertue necessytie manfully tene whan eyre gan wexen clene mystes cloudy sorowe deale adawe gan morowe heuynesse derke nyght chaced awaye sonne bryght newe ioye aye fyne wo muste gladnesse whan sorowe ygo pryam certayne space whan sorowe gan lyte lyte passe wysedome pytious smerte gan prudently plucken vp herte eyen wawes gan clere anone wroughte ye shall phowe pryam sonne lamedon succedynge father buylded cytye agayne cap xi sorowe aswaged syghes olde longe processe lyke tolde worthy kyng called pryamus herte nowe desyrous vpon playne waste wilde stronge towne newe buylde deuyse cytie edifye shall assautes vtterly defye enmyes mortall foone riche toures walles harde stone aboute countreyes enuiron made seke euery regyon suche workemen curyous wyt inuentife castyng meruaylous suche coulde crafte geometrye sotyll fantasye euery good deuysour mason hewer crafty quarreour euery wryghte passyng carpenter may founde eyther lyeges lad lefe ioye hym leue royall sete soueraygnly reygning quyete procedyng forth ye list heare vnto effect anone matere phow king prya send anthenor grece haue restored ayen sister exion ca xii hateful harme dred kindled longe sparke olde hatred roote debate grounde enuy yre newe flawme hertes fyre grayne malyce causer offence rancour rusted impacyence hast newe made festred sore smert whan thou art one raked herte disdayne mercye mayst lete man whyle lyue quyete deluest vp malyce manyfolde debate newe buryed olde falsly quyckest strife restore enuious serpet slayne yore felly hath addre enuyous rest awaked pryamus venim persyng ille made wery lyue lyfe tranquille meued hym iniquitee vpon grekes auenged peace held reygne lyeges ioye souereygne without anoye perturbaunce serpent hath wyth newe remembrauce without aduyse discrete areste hote flawme kindled breste olde enuye freshe rancour meynte lykly neuer queynte pryam nowe entenciowne cast compasseth reuoluing vp downe howe strong ryches meyne noble mighty newe citye habundaunt shortly conclude plentye multitude men armes chyualrye stered haue fantesye ala whyle vnhappy chaunce dead take vengeaunce vpon foon fyre hote enuye brent inward melancolye standing purpose yt man chauge may domages auenged day iniuryes yt thei haue wrought pand tyme sought purpose conuenient anone hath lordes sent knightes called euerychone come haste excused one namely theim hygh degre obeying humylitye bydding hooly made delay come echeone agayne certayne day sonnes also tho present hector except tyme absent stronge mighty regyon panomye subiection kinge pryam held worthynesse amende thinges redresse hector gone panomye certayne cause iustifye reason thought best settle theim quiet rest aye iust prudent well aduysed pacient demeaned gouernaunce lothe vengeaunce might easy wise treate reforme thinges small great lothe noble worthy knighte haste execute vnright causeles rygour condempne full worthy solempne kinge priamus lordes great small within troye held court royall lyst cost spare ceryously meaning declare see lordes enuyron gan shewe hertes entention po worthy lordes assembled present faythfull trewe herte entete well knowen discrecion great domages foule oppression ye grekes haue vpon v wrought without cause thinge nought daye sayeth yet late trowe newe yet date freshe remembred mynde vnto blode ye kinde suppose foryetfulnesse may put away mortal heuynesse harmes olde whych aye renewe agayne mynde saye certayne trowe playnly thought yet grene ne dyeth nought haue slaine olde progenitours whylom noble werreours cytye brent brought vnto ruyne robbed falsly rauyne tourned wildernesse grece caryed rychesse father slayne hyght lamedon without cause iuste occasyon raught fro golde treasour semeth foule errour might ryght amendes well chalenge eke desyre fully aduenge afore goddes full high offence onely reason conscience passyng theyr mortall crueltee one thinge greueth vngoodly agaynst gentyllesse without regarde worthinesse byrth ne royall blode fayre eke good meane syster called exyon ala theyr confusyon disuse kepe like degre day day dishonestee thrugh honour name lorn cosiderig nought stock born blinde take hede aduert roote kindred surquidrye indurate syth borne highe estate ytreated like ye may se may coniecte lowe degre gouerned passing dishonestly ye may thinke demen truely wyues maydens companie eke allye yhaunted vsed theyr luste grekes haue better truste ne spare nother blode age thus liue torment seruage without routhe mercy pitee toucheth well semeth equite ryght ye ought echone ful might wronges ye offended seke waye might amended worke one assent sin procede like entent theyr malyce cursed crueltee one auenged herte wil thought one accord ne varye nought force doubled pouste right reason good equite requyre vengeaunce yt doth ye wroge though differre longe truste also goddes rightwisenesse shall helpe harmes redresse fauour v innocence chastice wrought offence palso ye knowe citye stronge mighty great suertye toures high walled werre also fer shineth sonne sterre none like reken may force therto peregall ye knowe also shall eft founde cheualrye habounde except armes olde assayed yet dreade neuer dismayed haue plenty also vytayle frendshyp eke ne v fayle theyr might v succour wherfore reade without soiour set vpon theim sith well able time nowe semeth couenable manhode byd make delaye venge wronge hap euer maye differring oft drawen domage worke time double auauntage purpose lacketh neuer dele manhod assured wel holde hasty rakell worken wilfully werre also stant auenture aye mart doubtous eure reade first grekes sende wyt harmes amende without stryfe werre debate may sayne fortunate yf contrarye reason condiscende conclusyon graunte askyng equite righte haue cause preue might proceden rygour shall assaye fyrst measure fer ryght reason eke requere disdeyne yf lyst quarell deuoyde wylfulnesse yrooted vppon good sykernesse great offence demaunde amendes fyrst pacience god fortune hope wyll assent ende shulde repent better peace haue redresse gyn werre without auisenesse therfore let v wofull auenture paciently aye suffre endure porte humble playne tyll v answere send ayene though myne entencion meaued iuste occasyon irous sort proceadyng vengeaunce wyll put remembraunce letten slyde foryetfulnesse wronges voyde heauinesse toward grekes axe wyll exiona restore v againe whiche dere stynte hatred debate werre surplus mortall eure shall dessymule prudently endure harmes olde forth pacience ye accorde vnto sentence saye vpon ye full auysed yf sonde despised lyste reason obeye may iustly seke nother waye haue redresse saue purpose senden anthenore whiche man discrete well auysee specially mater treatee wyse eloquent ye well knowe passyngly prudent whan kyng tolde tale anone counseyle consent echone anthenor iourney vndertake hast gan ready make without abode wyll one denye take hym embassadrye full well auised discrecion toke went informacion poynt poynt great charge hym caste stande large without errour coulde good theffecte full playnly vnderstode euery thyng prynted thought went hath forgat ryght nought worde caste fayle shyppe goth began sayle short tyme companye aryued vp thesalye citie called monosyus fortune kynge pelleus tyme anthenor anone vnto kynge right way gone guydo hath conceiued pryme face right beningly receyued whan knewe cause comyng bad hast without tarying anthenor fell visage shortly saye theffecte message troian knight astoned neuer adel full demure auysed well hasty rakle sayne abydyng loke face playne pelleus manly chere sayde effecte right thus ye shall pthe worthy kyng called pryamus wyse noble manly famous knighthod passyng excellent hath fyrst goodly wyse seyt troye royall chiefe eitie full entent message shall saye wordes playne ye disdayne paciently gyue audience remembryng fyrst aduertence harmes full longe ago wronges ye wrought also full cruelly eke troye lande progenitours iniuryes destruction causeles without occasyon ye shewed haue cruelty mercyles destroyed citie slayne father named lamedowne cytie brent beat adowne nother lefte paleys house toure lad awaye rychesse treasour nother spared reherse slaughter woman childe man might none swerde astert yet one thynge yt hathe herte syster called exyon hold kept kinge thelamon dishonestly agayne gentrye great dishonour great vyllanye kindred lyke ye may se treated cherished like degre wherfore syth ye wyse knight ye ought aduert haue syght thinges iust affection consydre discrecion gentilnesse equite wronges might amended wherfore pryam great auisenesse fully busynesse herte desyreth peace reste sendeth beseching beste ye wil busy diligence make hym litell recompence may haue restytucion knightly mediacion syster withouten longer space remenaunt wyll let pace strife werre onely eschewe desireth fully sewe peace quyete hole affection pursue measure reason finallye lyke ye may se occasyon werre fle consyder holde sage fine fully message pwhan pelleus hym playnly vnderstode sodayne yre hert waxed woode cheare loke fell furyous rancoure right melancolyus ne might attempre appease hasty fyre gan herte sease anone full dispytous wise gan pryamus threten despise malyce set sond nought al meanes yt anthenor hath sought gan also troian knight manace bad haste auoyde place vpon peryll fall might anone went syght haste meynee without abode taken haue see gan saylen thesalye theyr waye fast gan theim hye shorte tyme aryued vp salerne mighty strong citye fortune royall towne anthenor fonde king thelamowne paleys hath waye nome first finde come accepted vnto presence beningly without offence exyone present tyde auenture standing syde reuerence womanheade anthenor toke better hede albe custome kyng thelamon hye despyte indignacion euerye troyan could espye specially enuye rancour onely bytter rage hert might neuer yet aswage al pacience anthenor hath giuen audience anone ful sobre wise tayle gan shall deuise psyr quod supporte grace ye graunt oportune space declare cause cominge reherse without tarying matter hole brefely sentence make kouthe magnificence signifying without displesaunce priamus hath gouernauce troye towne hath vnto sent faythfull meaning clene entent besechyng first goodlyheade wronges forgotten eke deade ye onely hygh noblesse equite gentilnesse ye restore exyona agayne ye hold speake word playn sothe like estate wherfore prayeth stinten debate euery harme put memorye knightly honour owne glorye sende home make delyueraunce goodly withouten varyaunce ye haue holde many longe dayes ne tarieth setteth delayes ne let founden slouthe sothfastly great routhe recorde ye haue abused may trouthe goodly excused shall lett lightly ouerslyde ye beningly list prouyde sende home like haue sayde lo charge layde without abiding certayne goodly answere ye sende agayne pwhan thelamon herkened tayle hasty yre gan wexen pale fyery collor hath made woode face aualed blode within herte gan frete bite wyth loke askoye tourned vp whyte hye disdayne face dispytous pale smilyng laughter furyous gan rake fearful mortall fyre fretinge hate brent desyre shortly made conclusyon anthenor put ilke obiection sayde frende euer thou wonder greatly meruayle auenture sodaine newe thinge vnprudently meueth nowe thy kinge vnto make sonde thou foole wha thou toke hod eyther vnhappy elles infortunate bring proude embassete wyl nothing haue loke thou say ne aqueynted lyte nothing platly delyte short wordes thou list heare hym ought prayer ne haue delyght ioye ne feste thinge wherof maketh requeste wote well whyle go troye selfe mo reforme thinge amys offence shortly thus certaine thing wrought lamedowne manhod wonne ye towne slewe kyng helde knightly wise meting felde euerye man might se ieoparde first enter cytye graunted memorye onely signe mine hygh victorye withouten contradiction grekes haue possession entere exiona nowe thou claymest well syker thyne asking vayne truste right well certayne thou gettest one worde yf may shal first made full greate affray leue liue euer grutche agaynst striue sittyng leue whilom great gat spending blode wrothe therwith wood kepe shall founde many mortall wounde troye towne thense wan good fayth fer forthe shall lightly fro handes pace alone standeth grace beaute semelyheade bounte godlyheade shal reason shortly fine sothe feminine euer sawe without dreade porte conning womanheade hath alone existence souereynte perfect excellence priamus ought thou ca sayne lyue getteth agayne bye many deadly wounde sharpe swerdes square speres groude shal first reysed strife shall cost many mannes lyfe agayne restored take forsothe yu gettest list may wel beginne supose shall litell winne none otherwise haue tolde wotest yu great foole holde put thy selfe ferre ieopartye execute embassadrye manly grekes boldly offende beware therfore sende vpon thy selfe rancoure pride go thy waye yf thou abide longer sothly syght thou wotest ye pryse yt haue hyght thou scapest liefe lothe anthenor anone shyp goth forth sayleth hym list delaye towarde yle called achaye whan taken hath lande ryuayle auenture fonde worthy kynges pollux castor ryght anone troyan anthenor without abode courte fare vnto message declare together present right thus sayd sentement pthe noble kynge troye citee hath vnto sent wyll besechyng full lowe maner vouchesafe vnto prayer equitie condescende goodly helpe certeine wrong mende touchyng syster called exion may haue restitucion agayne discrete aduyse syth ye manly wyse lykely oppynion ye good medyacion may easely agayne restored cheryshe peace vnitee wherfore prayeth wt herte entere goodly wyse done deuere holde byn knyghtly sage wyll playnly surplusage wronges olde put suspence desyreth knyghtly hygh prudence stynte warre nouryshe peace nother rakle rekles euell auysed workes caste afore shall fall thynges future aduertynge ferre seeth peryll werre wyll hym conforme vnto peace reste conceyueth beste euery man vnite sewe prudently also eschewe debate hole full occasion lo fyne entencion commyt vnto iugement pthis castor yre inpacient hastinesse ne might abyde cruell herte swolen pride brake anone right despiteous face sayde frende knowe trespace euer grekes vnto thy kynge axe amendes wonder thynge v neuer dyd none offence saue made maner recompence wronge wrought lamedon whiche fyste sought occasyon agaynst grekes vngoodly wyse caused v vpon hym tho ryse one manly hym sette due ryght quyte dette lyke deserte haue playnly serued nothig wrought hath deserued axe amendes gynneth late coueyte mortall hate vtter malys enmyte outher peace accorde vnite effecte hereafter shall fele dare
