hereafter v deale bargayne shall full dere ben abought frendeshyp sothly set nouhgt ouermore speake lykely semeth vnto pryamus loued lyte thincke value myte whan sent forth message thou folye dyddest great outrage take hyghe peryllous thynge vnto grekes bryngen suche tydynge throughe thy lyfe put inpartye counsayle faste thou hye syght lest thou repente pand anthenor forth shyp went wynde gan sayle anone towarde yle called pylon hast whan dyd aryue shope hym forth court blyue duke nestor maner thynge housholde helde royall kinge anthenor full sad auysee tofore nestor syttyng see whan admytted sayne tale tolde full openly playne poynt poynt ye herde afore vayne reherse alway concluded hath one ye haue herde touchyng exion pbut duke nestor face nothyng red hewe asshes dead fret collor inwardly blode eche extremitee withdrawen downe alowe vnto herte yre sore made hym smerte gan quake euery ioynt vayne hande vnneth may restreyne melancolye venged lyke lyon wood wroth fer hym selfe alyenate inwardly rancour passyonate loke reserued furious syghte tho rule hym selfe vnneth myghte felte anger great aduersytie syth amyddes crueltie sodeyne haste one brake euen thus anthenor spake po thou quod al thy wordes whyte suppose thou wottest full lyte tofore thou haste thy tale tolde meruayle howe thou arte bolde thus presume myne eares offende pryam proudely pretende maner tytle thy kynges name worthy grekes put blame vniustly foule hardynesse requere haue redresse iniuryes wrought lamedon boldely affyrmyng false presumpcion vpon grekes wronkes outragious whiche myne eres odyous fretyng eke bytyng kene lyste may susteyne hearyng hatefull sowne ner honour hye renowne refrayned shulde cruell wyse execute full hastely iustyce rygour mortall law bestes wylde fyrste drawe thervpon thy fayned tale dismembre peces smale despyte pryamus thy kynge teache bryng tydyng presumptuously tale newe lorde hym better knewe thus shuldest thou haue thy presupcion thy last mede fynall guerdon without mercy lyke haue behyght hast bego syght vtterly doth great offence vnto myne eye haue presence disdeine causeth myne vnreste pthan anthenor thought best holsom longer abyde caste wysely rancour pryde beste beare fayre shyppe gan anone repayire haste possybilitee without abode taken hath sea gan sayle homeward faste drawe sodeynly boylen gan wawe sea ryse cloudes blacke appere wynde wake wonder gastfull also heauen dredfull fyre bryght leuen thonder smote gan tepest driue toppe mast asunder gynneth ryue alofte poynt drowne fell wether gan theim frowne naught awayte death euen poynt yeldyng vp brethe ne sawe none remedy styll amonge gan clepe crye vnto goddes auowes make deuoutly vndertake eche growen age escape go pylgremage lyke rytes paynym wyse goddes sacrifyse substaunce myght sodeinly wether derke nyght newe lyght grace gan adawe sea ware calme smothe gan ye wawe happe amonge euerychone tempest perished one tofore troye within lyttell space aryued euerychone grace eschaped safe euery ioypardye bothe anthenor companye temple toke ryght way prayer full longe laye many another also sake thankyng goddes yt lysten slake euery peryll tempest sea vnto kynge goeth lordes full royall paleys dongyon pryncipall sat abode full solempnelye heare reporte embassadrye knyght hath hym fall hath tolde kynge tofore lordes anthenor hath fyrst made mencion tofore kynge iuste relacion exployt ordre wyse howe vncurteously receyued kynge pelleus thretes wordes despyteous suffred kyng thelamon ferse cruell wood lyon afterwarde gan also complayne despyte bretherne tawyne rebuke great dread nestor howe happed spede lyfe myght vnneth escape tolde gan ende make iourney eke repayre wherby pryam fully dispayre outher force yet aduenture syster neuer might recure conceyueth aduertence cleare reporte experte euydence aye theim beninge vngoodly ayen malinge sheweth selfe debonayre ayeneward fond cotrayre frowardly euer theim quite shewing sygnes set lyte frendshyp ought could aduerte wherof ful sorowfull herte constrayned ryght nede tho compelled iustly procede haue redresse onely rygoure profered peace myght haue fauour admitted tytle rightwysenesse hygh despite hasty wylfulnesse euery meane measoure vayne saue onely werre engendred disdayne began caused olde hatrede gan anone broyle brede newe enuy within kynge breste priamus without areste inly irous rancour fret disdayne sore ground whet must lese wyn vpon grekes wyll werre begyn therin ieoparde manly knight lyfe deathe bycause ryght cast hym first nauye sende hast grece fomen offende like knight force haunte knightly wise cast daunt pompe grekes sturdinesse fynally theyr pride oppresse pbut saye priam infelycitye newe trouble hap destiny aboue hateful influence descended vnware violence meue ye thus thou canst liue peace sodayne sorte fortune gracelese chaunce vnhappy without auisenesse wilfull lust fonde hardinesse haue put thy soule tranquilitye make werye thy prosperitye sauourest yu bitter swete canst lyue peace quiete thou art trauayled wilfull mocions ouer maystred thy passion lacke reason hyghe prudence derked blinde prouydence full barayne cast afore se harmes folowyng thine aduersitye thou slowe wisely consydre want syght made thus slydre myst errour falsly forueye pathes wronge right weye voyde reason wylful hastynesse thy guyde thy maystresse discrecion prudet sadde auysely haue lad trace sensualitee though ful selde mannes power sufferaunce selfe refrayne whan sodayne yre doth herte strayne thou shuldest afore better haue cast thi chauce wrought counsayle put balaunce thy sykernesse ala diddest thou haue symuled dele wo cast thy chaunge wel afore prime haue forgotten wronges olde time thought afore thine aduertence oft falleth experyence while men theyr busynesse vengeably olde wronges redresse double harme beware fall agayne newe snare domages forgotten cleane false reporte rumour freshe grene renewed swyfte fame fleeth fer hurt lordes name namely whan purpose wende head forsee ende pryde sodayne heate voyde selfe quyete aduertyng worke auysely prouerbe teacheth comonly stande sure enhaste hym meue yf shall greue walketh surely playne stumble vayne onlesse lyste folye neclygent put hym wylfully auenture hym selfe reche eschewe peryll holde wreche sothly pryam thou rechelese commytte thy quyete peace dredfully durynge date cruell fortune fykell fate whose maner custome comonly whan man trusteth suredly goddesse blynde full vnstable hym moste deceyuable hym abate royall stalle sodeynly doth make hym downe falle tryp throwe backe gayne striueth shal haue lytle tacke slyely gylefull snare make man welfare pantre fraude englewed wha least weneth remewed therfore man may hope affyaunce fortune rule full varyance ne lete wyght ease iuparte ne recke game departe tourne chaunce outher well wo selde one doth game go ye may see example pryamus foly desyrous worke head folow wylle troubled calme tranquille boke hereafter shalbe founde hym citie platly confounde vtterly confusyon afterwarde longe successyon shalbe red story fable remembred dytees delytable pleasaunce shall sample beware lere hasty lust rashe voluntee gyn thyng wherin suretee dependeth aye stryfe werre debate play vnwarely cometh check mate harme ydone late amende whose fyne ofte wende story ye shall see lette pryam alwaye myrrour hasty errour tymes correcte anone poyntill wyll directe maner trace rude story remnaunt conclude worthy kyng euer one sentence aye fyred feruence hath breuettes letter sente lordes holde parlement comaunded al hast may come anone assygned daye euery warde party towne assemble noble ilyowne chiefe reigne echone hym present noble kyng anone tofore theim shortly wyll declareth thus began psyres quod bycause ye wyse nedeth longe processe deuyse reherse comynge cause tell shortly clause meane maketh delaye ye wotte day sent grece counsayle knyght myne anthenor call haue recured exiona agayne whose message tho vayne grekes full vncurteysly receyued dispyteously threte rebuked poynt haue dead vnneth myght escape head put hym hygh offence blame muche redoundeth alder shame day day must encrease ordeyne remedy therfore measure haue offred haue v werre stryfe yprofred hyghe despyte rancour heate malys cruelly v threate wold peace purchace wronges done felly v manace ye harmes yt haue v wrought purpose playnly thought redresse amendes make vtterly werre v awake whose ioye fully encrease greuaunce wolde god repentaunce contryte herte stynten myschiefe lykely fall eke grefe outher parte myght ouer slyde ala rancour pryde swole new threaten god defende halfe deale sore infortune euer shulde fall purpose euery v syth haue deuysed thus v must resyste wyll malicious myght god necessitie deffence wyll none beste holde vnto entent worke one assent purpose sonest shall achieue discorde may quarell preue parte hertes one victorye may way gone chiefe conquest peace vnitie ryght discorde aduersytie wherfore read wyll harte lette v set grekes smerte sothfastly ye lyste se dare affyrme farre stronger grekes vpon euery parte haue armes parfytly arte accouted knighthod crop roote plenty haue horseman foote arrayed well eueryche degree therwith also stronge citie withstonde fomon euerichone counsayling syth ordayne anone fyrst tassemble holy nauye stuffe strongly wt chiualrye grece hastely sende proude grekes manly offende iuste cause tytle ryght theim werre force might townes bren fyeldes waste herte vnfayned also v enhaste quite deserued haue read shall none saue cruellyf theim vengeaunee ne hath eare ne let greuaunce though tofore fortune victours slewe father progenitours vnhap fyrste put downe remounteth ofte hyghe renowne charge duble varyance werre stryfe aye balaunce day assured wele see morowe cast downe whele victor ofte lykewyse aduenture vanquished discomfyture hym afore victorie vp syth downe armes stant glory martes chaunce man may assure cometh must take eure gery mar sudden influence gyue man whylom excellence wynne pryse lyke conquerour sodaynly falleth somer floure honour make fade whan aspectes glade man lysteth wrythe olde renowne goth away blythe floode ebbe foloweth aye men deserue prayse daye though day phebus mery shyne morow may bemes downe decline thicknesse mistes trouble ryght mar chaunces double vp downe low alofte fortune whiche chaungeth ofte lyst whele make man assende vnwarely downe agayne descende stounde mele honour auaunce asweigh throwe mischaunce fauour set vp full hye erst auale twyngling eye playe vnstable tourneth ball whyle one goeth vp hath fall reyseth one doth another loute euery man whan cometh aboute must take tourne playe requireth experte fraudes lereth shall hir sugre fynde gall ymeynt hony aye bitter spreynt peace werre honour fame dignity renowne shame lykyng lyst graunt therfore man hap muche auaunte pfor though grekes whylom lofte may happe hereafter full vnsofte wherfore echone shewe worthynesse named strength hardinesse fortune playnly commytte lette feare manly hertes flytte stonde hole meanyng playne therupon let se ye wyll sayne one voyce gan reyse sentence hyghely preyse one herte manly gan expresse wil one despende goodes rychesse bodyes put ieopardye one wolde tho denye graunt thanketh echone gaue leue lyst gone dissolued hath parlement euery man waye went repayred mansiowne kynge alone lefte ilyowne sole hym selfe inwardly musynge purpose myght brynge soth nothyng elles thought therupon fyne thus wrought kyng pryamus makyng thus mone tolde chambre alone many wayes castyng vp downe perfourme conclusyowne fulfyll fyne entent fyrste prudently hath sent sonnes come hym haste well borne baste tassemble yfeare purpose lyke ye shall haue counsaile nedeful purueaunce grekes maken ordenaunce fyrst selfe alone pryuely ordre eueryche set dewe see lyke age degree hector fyrst floure chyualrye repayred home panonye acceptable euery wyghtes grace nexte father taken hath place pand whan pryam leyser espye syghes sore castyng vp eye echone syttyng enuyron gan declare hertes mocyon first might ought wil expowne salt teares gan hym selfe drowne inly wo outragyous wepyng sobbyng furyous vnneth myght word breake vnto distresse speake openly inwarde meanyng shewe tyll last wordes fewe gan abrade pyteous fare euen thus sentence gynnyng declare pmy dere sonnes louyng kynde suppose ye haue mynde remembre discretly aduerte eke imprente full freshly herte grekes agayne ryght lawe cruell swerde mundred haue slawe auncetours whylom hyghe renowne destroyed brent beate downe fyrst troye walles olde vngoodly also withholde myne owne syster called exion full great shame confusyon hyghe repryfe worthynesse semeth kyndenesse nature ye ought agreued inwardly herte sore amened suffer hyndring name treated alder shame ala nyl ye besynesse highe despyte knyghtly redresse tauenge vpon crueltie recure fynde iniquitie sith ye myghty stronge certes semeth ye byden longe day day ye differre knyghtly wyse gyn werre force myght manly assaye pure sory ye lyste delaye confyrmen vnto desyre hate bren hoote fyre vpon lyke ye may see frettynge yre auenged lyke desert quyten mede ye ala lysten take hede whyle renowne doth freshly shyne vnto luste hertes declyne consyderyng lyke well kouthe selfe tender youth fostred brought forth echone fro thilke daye first ye coud gone tenderly could might thynge inward syght ye shuld aduert alway newe newe nature sorowes rewe remedye mine aduersytee whych toucheth also wel sith ye wote sore doth greue ye shulden shape myne harmes releue sodeinly thus gan mourne towardes hector gan face tourne sayd hector truste ioye mine heyre also like reygne troy daye successoure named art souerayne floure worthynesse manhod well al thy brother knighthod dost excelle armes lyke conquerour called stock worshyp honour hertely praye though thou syttest styll wyllinge nowe purpose fulfyll execute desyre fynally mo full fayth bryng thinge take nothinge doubte chefetayne also gouernour purpose vtterly socour thine hande iourney committe hooly herte thou ne flytte confourme good auysement vp perfourme fine mine entent reason best syt whych art prudent ful wyt strong deliuer flouryng eke youthe ye fame ye world kouthe yonge yeares olde discreciowne eurous loue passyng renowne vnto whose thy brother shall obeye stande lyue deye codescede accomplyshe request thou felest answere leste pand whe kinge hath shewed setece demure cheare humble reuerence worthy hector example gentrie soft speche teacheth curtesye answere gaue sobre countenaunce effecte substaunce pmine owne lorde father dere beningly ye list heare force great might eke summe nature ryght euerye thinge kinde doth constrain bondes large chayne sytting doth enspyre ende euery man desyre wronges done haue amendement lawe ryght conuenient namely nobylytye kinde hath endewed set high degre great reprefe shame wronge vnto theyr name eche trespasse must consydered iustly measured qualyty hym offended also parson wrong werre conteck debate greater grefe high estate suffer harme case auenture wronge vniustly endure iniuryes compassed malyce offence discrete aduyse theim famous manhod well renoumed borne gentyl blode one holde wretch wherfore must greatly charge retch onely knighthod worshyp eke wronges done mendes seke state consydered high noblesse plyte stand worthynesse whan beastes reason rude blinde desyre iust instinct kinde pand parte trusteth certayne ye haue sonne woulde half fayne vpon grekes auenged trouthe say faythfully yre theim bren doth glede thurst blode mede ryght eldest age amonge sonnes wt rage fret within iustly knighthode right hand shed grekes blode shalle fele peraunter wene whan time cometh sothe shalbe sene pbut firste rede wisely minde cast afore leue behinde ye begyn discretly aduert prudently consydre herte onely gynnynge ende yt middes way wil wed fine fortune theim lede ye thus amisse ye may spede counsayle mine opinion worthy lytell discrecion haue pryse cast course thinges ordre ceryously waye trace wo delyte though ginninge haue appetite yet ende playnly fable may thig fall comedable worthe ginninge fortunate causeth strife great debate wherfore sothe begynninges dread well knowe fine shall succede ginninge grace well fortuned whan ende middes lyke contuned wele ne may conteme well better rather absteine put doubt standeth suerte doth hath aduersitee humble estate royall herte pray let offende bolde say mocion good fayth none entencion nothing meue offence onely magnificence procede heade wilfully ne hast meue foly gyn thing wil shende lacke ye se tofore ende take hede aduertence consydre good prouidence grekes haue theyr subiection europe affryke many region ful large wide knighthod famous rychesse wonder plenteous right renoumed also worthinesse supporte dare wel expresse ful peryllous theim displease disturbe yf quyet nowe parturbe standeth fully peace drede though assye helpe v nede loked euery parte aryght egal vnto grekes might pand though also mine aunte exion agayne right holde thelamon good redempcion put v vnto destruction rede bye halfe deare many v perhappes sytte mo might sake death vnderfonge ende make wisedome lyke semeth may happe also shorte time fatall course shall fine whe attropos thredde two shal twine wonne go enmite thought sorowe wo slaughter men death confusyo wherfore reade without discencion without wo endure put selfe auenture holde best worke wyse doubtles cowardise saye high presence forcause holde prudence fortune knowen ful doubilnesse syth sure put sykernesse thus effect worde hector helde hym styll whan yt hector ful high prudece cocluded hath fine setence ful demurely kept lippes close therwithall paris vp arose gan tale thus afore kinge lorde quod lykinge highnesse taken hede semeth shuld litell dread knightly wise vndertake vpon grekes werre make one theyr pride confounde sith passingly habounde chiualry within towne haue plenty possessyowne eche thinge may werre auayle stuffe selfe royall apparayle longeth assautes marciall speciall helpe succour many region v worke theyr destruction pompe pryde manly abate grekes malyce amate al herte stoute semeth shortlye nede doubte parte dismayed wherfore reade let delayed shyppes fyrst ready make selfe wyl fully vndertake liking plesaunce empryse hooly gouernaunce assure put certayne exyona recure agayne fourme shall wrought haue waye deuised thought likely hereafter done vnto declare anone first haue cast strog myghty hand rauyshe lady land high estate make taryinge mightely troye brynge maugre might conclusyon ye may haue restitucion chaunge ye desyre therupon shall longe ado behete grekes stronge shall tale prolonge wil sayne excluding euerye doubte aduise shal well brought first shal purpose fine goddes haue thrugh power diuine shewed reuelacion therupon auisyon late agone laye slepe vnto ye take kepe ye may fayle despayre haue recure fayre ye haue much care pand maner hoole wyl declare dreame magnificence ye lysteth giue credence tale shal dwelle ceryously ordre tell trouthe fable fayne lorde souerayne pfirst ye remembre minde daye last inde aduyse commaundement matter entent specially cheirte knowen betwene whych toke vpo tho charge within bondes land large pthe time desyre spede titan beames rede geminy droue chayre golde toward crabbe take holde named paleys diane bent moone wex wane halowed sonnes stacion nigh middes moneth iuyn season early morowe whan phebus auoiding nightes sorow doth pirrous wayne vp drawe aurora estward doth adawe water teares rounde siluer dewe causeth habounde vpon herbes floures soote ful kindly noryshyng crop roote pvp rose bed anone ful desyrous huntinge gone pricked herte lusty freshe plesaunce loue dewe obseruaunce diana daye magnifie called lady venerye reuerendly rite obserue citherea tho serue feres hertes releue cast v fully til drewe eue within forest playe v disporte plesauntly v recomforte longeth loue lustynesse thilke day venus goddesse ysacred full great excellence great honour dewe reuerence done vnto one fryday aduenture fall whan ga haste v woodes grene hope day game sene great labour riding fro til full many bucke doo strengthe slayne might fynde herte ychased houdes hinde downes dale lowe till phebus high vpon dayes bowe amid arke meredien beames ful hote shene busy vpon chase befell wonder diuerse case fortune happed sodeynly seuered companye sole selfe amonge holtes hore finde game desyrous euermore ware thicke thyn ful great harte sawe afore ryn downe launde vale grene sothe ne might sustene swift nigh hym nere though hym sewe pricked coursere nigh ye death many sundry shawe syght fer withdrawe al euer sewe myght anone lost hym syght wood dabare name faynt gan wexen game mine horse whych tho ryde fomyng full whyte vpon euery syde flankes blode distayned pursute sore constrayned sporres sharpe dyed redd harte prycked stede vp downe ful busy thought laboure auayled right nought tyll last amonge bowes glade aduenture caught plesaunt shade ful smothe playn lusty sene soft veluet yonge grene fro horse alight fast bowe aloft reyne cast faynte mate werynesse layde downe vpon gras vpon bryncke shortly telle besyde ryuer cristall welle water reherse like quicke siluer streames ran whych grauell bryght stone golde agayne sonne shone pwhere ryght anone werynesse sodayne slepe gan oppresse syth tyme first borne neuer asleped toforne lay heard wonder sweuen thought high downe heaue wynged god wonderful cheare mercuryus appeare dele first aferde gyrde croked swerde brought also hande slepy yerde plyaunt wande serpent goyng enuyrowne fete also lowe adowne semed also stode cocke singing houres trewe clocke mouth god mercurye pypes set songe wonder merye whych swete sugred hermonye made mine eares melodye semed tho mine aduyse rauyshed paradise thus god dyuerse liknesse wonderfull expresse shewed selfe apparence like descryued fulgence boke methologies rehersed many poesyes many likenesse like ye may se take moralitee longe yerde right lyne whiche syde wrongly may decline signifyeth prudent gouernaunce discrete folke yt theyr purueyauce cast peryll befall pypes loude shall musyke entuned trewe betokeneth eke many lusty hewe sugred dytees great excellence rethoryke eloquence god soueraigne patrowne cocke swete lusty sowne iustly kepeth houres night vtterly aduise inward sight voyde waker diligence theyr court stouthe necligence sworde croketh againe forged ymade vayne reuoke right weye wrongly trouthe forueye serpent whiche tolde wrincled ye may beholde vpon yerde goeth signefyeth falshode wood wrothe lieth wayte many sleyghty weye ginnes trouthe werrey god eloquence kinge brought eke comminge citherea louers serue iuno pallas called minerue venus liege delite head flikered douues white loke beninge eyen debonayre aye circuling snowy winges fayre declare sothly sentence douues innocence theim loue yt trouth meane yt theyr groude shuld honeste cleane ytokned clerely witnesse without soyling vnclennesse freshnesse rose redde somer lustyly doth sprede wynter theyr coloure fade signifieth hertye thoughtes glade yonge folkes ben amerous feruent hope inly desyrous whan loue gynneth theyr hertes floure till longe processe maketh theim loure wynter vnweldy age lust palled dulled rage feblenesse somer gone folkes knowe wott well mo one therfore venus fleteth see shewe trouble aduersytee loue stormye lawe whych byset many sturdye wawe nowe calme rough taketh hede hope assayled aye sodeyne dreade next venus pallas behelde spere bryghte shelde raynbowe rounde head colour grene blewe rede tofore discryue growyng grene freshe olyue therupon browes fowle braunches sawe syt like owle first shilde pallas goddesse signifyed expresse vertue force manly high diffece agayne vyces maken resistence spere sharpe kene ygrounde iust rygour forged confound theim false put abacke mercy shall medle wt ye wrack shafte sothe shauen full playne lest mercyles right ne wrought vain werre make false release oliue betokeneth peace owle also odious songes syngeth feastes funerall declaring playnly fine euery glorye onely death hath memorye raynbowe grene read perse signifyeth chaunges ful diuerse oft falleth werre battayle winne sodeynly fayle stable blew chauging grene pallas playe alwaye meynt wt tene alder last nowe haue minde nimphes iuno came behinde whyche custome fulgencius telles abydeth floudes depe welles iuno theise poetes fayne mayden fruyte barayne pecock freshe quene ysacred fethers shene splayed abrode large sayle argus eyen emprinted tayle pthe water ronninge ryuer floud labour men haue good great trouble besynesse day nyght suffer rychesse euer floudes rowe let beware aye flowe nature ryght course dewe folowing ye moone must ebbe esewe dread aye vpon full lest fortune freshe fethers pull ryche folkes shine golde shene sith chauche lady quene pand argus eyen set aye behinde nygardes hertes yt oft sythes blinde aduert goodes ende like ebbe sodeynly wil wende whyche nothinge consydre sight fayre lusty fethers bright pecock vnwarely fall awaye right ryches shortly daye theyr mayster sodeynly forsake saying adewe then theyr leue take iuno barayne fruyte right naked bare destitute gredy hertes couetous gather desyrous nothing haue suffysaunce fret dred putteth mischauce imagening world wil fayle theyr feare agayne ye wynd sayle till one must departe fro thus good aye fine wo namely theim pinche spare dread clerkes declare fruite good spende large euer set lytell charge frely parteth treasour commune discretely seeth time opportune hath ioye put good mewe herte fredome list sewe gentylnesse taketh hede therto pand wyse pallas iuno freshe venus adowne descended like haue shortly comprehended vnder guyding mercurius whych vnto began tale thus pparys quod lyft vp thine eyen see lo goddess nombre thre whych heauen wyth theyr eyen clere dyuersly vnto appere feast wherof tell shall goddes aboue celestyall iupyter helde owne borde none absent saue onely discorde despyte present auenged set entent wyttes many wayes sought tyll last euen thus wrought olde poet lyke yt tolde toke appel rounde pure golde greke letter grauen vp downe whych sayd thus conclusyowne without strife let gyue anon vnto fayrest theim euerychone discorde lady goddesse conteke maystresse hath appel passyng delyte brought feast malyce despyte cast downe among theim borde deynous chere speaking worde waye fast gan hye sodeynly inly great enuye courte appel hath broughte great werre conteck wrought hertes ilke thre longe may staunched amonge theim selfe gan disdayne whiche beaute seueraygne whych theym hath tytle right coquere burned apple bryght first gan thus beaute stryue rancour almost theyr hertes ryue wite ryght shuld first possede plo yet enuye reygneth womanhede one fayrer holde eche woman kinde would haue parte prise aboue eche estate sothe eche theim owne aduise hath ioye beaute haue prise none foule doth myrrour prye shene fayre owne eye like foole selfe doth quite aumber yelowe cheseth white goundy eye deceyued soone colour cheseth moone colour fyre made fine encreased spice wyth wine oyntementes confection night false illusyons appeare wonder freshe fayre loke full derke day light ayre prefe early morowe nede beaute borowe nature hath selfe disposed therfore fasting box vnclosed make thy chose byddeth ouide whan euery drugge pot set syde lest haply thou sentence deceyued lightly false apparence dayes craft ful ryfe wise first began stryfe betwixt iuno venus pallas decended sodayn case one assent touchyng theyr beaute dome therof committed vnto speake called art parys holde arte ful prudent right wyse wel auysed thy dome shal fyne ne may fro decline must obeyen one assent without strife thy iudgement hercke first thou procede eche theim shall thy mede consydre ryght take good hede therto thou appel graunt vnto iuno shall gyue plenty richesse hyghe renowne fame eke worthynesse habundaunce golde treasour reyse hyghe honour thou alone shalte excelle thy guerdon lyke telle pand yf pallas goddesse prudence lyst fyne conclude thy sentence may lady appell thy mede shall assure wyt eke sapyence thou shalte hooly haue excellence wysedome discrecion discerne clerenesse reason also fer phebus cast may lyght shall prudent knyght worlde syth fyrst began iust reporte manly man thy name none equipollent pand venus true clene entent lyste graunt conclusyon appell haue possessyon freshe goddesse syt hyghe aboue shall ensue haue vnto thy loue fayrest lady tofore worlde hereafter shalbe bore grece thou shall knightly wynne aduised thou begynne iustly deme thynge spare pand anone gan loke vp stare greatly astoned best tyll laste spake mercurye sayde certayne ne wolde gyue dome naked myght haue fully lybertee eueriche aduisedly see well consider euery circumstaunce fayrest vnto pleasaunce goodlyest speake womanhede wolde dome procede pand anone ye haue herde seye desyre mekely gan obeye haste busy cure dispoyle clothing vesture lyche statute dome bonde point wolde withstonde myght haue full inspection fourme shape eche proporsyon discerne remembre vysedly ordre euery membre erst iudge ryght pbut whan yt thus syght gaue venus appell right anone bycause fayrest eche one excellyng sothly beatie moste womanly goodly see tho demed playnly syght stremes eyen bryght yleche glade egall lyght like yt sterre yt sheweth towardes ye night whiche called hesperus shene venus selfe freshe lusty queene whiche anone heauenly emperesse dome harty hyghe gladnesse appell hooly hath glorye wonne thus iustly victory reioysed tell feares beautie dyd excell hast trewe affection concluded hath fully guerdon full demurely lowe lofte mercury sobre wordes softe deuoyde doublenesse slouthe lyke behest holde wyll trouth sodaynly without iniurye disapered god mercurye streyght heauen ryght waye toke anone slepe woke pwherof lord loue drede ye aduerte wisely taketh hede behest affyrmed certayne vnto assured vayne goodly venus lyke haue tolde wherfore rede ye herte bolde sende stronge mighty hande without abode grekes lande fourme haue sayde thus hope ye shall well apayde whan haue spede wenus hath hight home retourne lady bryght shall ye best lyste speake vayne exchaunge syster wyn agayne thelomon withholden hath yore lo say touchyng theffect hooly myne aduyse tho satte hym downe parys hym selfe full well aquytt saye pryam ala thy wytt neclygence taken kepe thy truste sette dremes slepe full thynne forsothe thy discrecion take grounde false illusyon procede lyke fantasye vpon sweuen meint flattery ala reason tho nothynge thy guyde pallas wrongly sette syde receyued dewe reuerence iuno eke sapience good lokynge debonayre treasour hestes fayre refused ala wylfulnesse loue goddesse eke also vulcanus wyfe whose seruyce euer werre strife preferred appell possede againe ryght paris toke none hede saue vnto luste sette asyde trouth ala yt ful great routh myghty ryche noble towne troye brought full confusyowne knyghthode hath forsake prudence golde choyse ytake woman holde hym therto roote wo story ceriously shall tell dreames longer dwell write forth deiphobus thirde sonne priamus tale began open audience kynge shortly sentence lyste trouthe spare euen thus gan fantasye declare pmy lorde quod euery wyght aduerte shulde caste syght future thynge peryll doubte serche wel within eke without poynt poynt alwaye reaso caste doubtes tournen vp downe shulde wyght purpose wende matter make ende eyther presume manhode thought casteth doutes achieueth lite nought plowman alway cast aforne many graynes fielde corne shalbe deuoured foules rauynous doth sowe fieldes plenteous shulde neuer vale playne cowardshyp throwe abrode grayne let suche drede layde asyde holde folye longer abyde yt parys brother make hym stronge shyppes venge wronge vpon grekes payne might preue shortly knight reason ye consyder may man iustly may saye nay parys hath counsayled wele trouth fer fele errour purpose contrary wherfore let hym longer tarye holde waye stronge nauye auenge shamefull velanye grekes haue done ye lyst take hede alder dayes v kynred eke fynall execucion recure touchyng exion demeyne dishonest wyse agaynst ryght title iustyce wherof thinke giueth hert wounde shame newly doth rebounde vpon v ally wherfore best espye parys take maye voyage suche freshe lusty age manly wende grekes lande force myghtye hande maunger grekes proude elate rauishe lady estate tha ye may knighthod brother ye lyste chaunge redy short conclusyon se restytution exyon parys wende counsayle shortly thus end pand faste full discrete sage helenus fourth sonne age rose seate humble reuerence praying father graunte hym aundience may say presence openly shalbe fall secrete thynges soberlye thus tale began cleane entent trewe affection pmy lorde quod supportacion grace wherin trust let none offence vnto luste displease yf conceyte declare syth meane decetie neuer yet fayled sentence fyll efte experyence lyke tolde partie pryuye treate eke generall without meanynge doublenesse folowed dyd expresse remembryng ye shall fynde trewe yf god wyll shall new spare say lyke conceyue dede fraude deceyue declaryng fyrst trewe entention shall folowe conclusion pthat yf parys grece wende trusteth well wyll v shende goddes reuelacion haue made playne demonstration eke knowe astronomye neuer yet prophecye deceyued shulde fall none lyste counsayle call taught thyng shall betyde wherfore praye rancour pryde enuye wrought olde hatred take vengeaunce ye procede aduyse lyke ye purpose saye playnly ylyst glose ye shall repente ye parys sende grece whiche god defende wytte full well conclusyon shall fully tourne destruction fynally vnto ruyne lyke gan afore deuyne fyne folowe shall subuercyon towne wall house paleys citie al goth nought ye get forme semeth ought ynough suffyse haue sayd syth ye wyse yf ye aduerten sawe doubte ye wyll withdrawe hande tyme domage assayleth constraynte rage better betymes absteyne purpose whiche yet grene hede thus hastely assente thynge shal echone repente plenerly shall nothynge socoure shal folowe despyteful death without excepciowne one abydynge towne fyrst selfe playnly endite shall vengeaunce grekes byte fury mortall tene wyfe fayre hecuba queene shall lede lyfe grekes crueltie sorowe wo captiuitie lyeges sworde shall pace cruell death withouten grace innocentes merciles shall blede aduyse ye procede wylfulnesse werre make folyly thus vndertake parturbe quyete rest shal retourne nothyng best ruyne v mischyefe fall counsayle afore ye prouyde letteth wylfulnesse sette asyde specially whan death tolde must fyne ye purpose holde lo without wordes mo grece parys go pand wyse whan helenus playnly sayde guydo telleth v tryste heuy pale deadly face agayne resorteth syttynge place whose sentence astoned euerychone sat sylence stylle stone powerles hertes efte resume speake worde man dare presume prese kept lyppes close laste troylous vp arose yonge freshe couragyous also aye desyrous haue armes manly longeth knight whan chere ful glad light sawe father brethern euerychone inly troubled thus spake anone poh noble worthy syttyng enuiron hyghe prudence great discrecion manfull also hyghe courage sodein fere hath brought rage new trouble cropen brest sentence coward priest syth echone ye shall euer fynde desyre veryly kynde lyue lust voyde awaye trauayle deadly hate battayle wyt fynally applye sewe lust lyue glottony fyll stomake restore mawe reste ease euermore drawe sewe inwarde appetite ioye delyte eatyng drynkyng couetyse studye fully deuyse may folow lust without ryght nought elles setten store ala shame ye dismayde sytte mate astoned afrayde wordes hym helenus fearefull drede lyttle mouse quaketh speake fyght moreouer agayne skylle ryght preiudice goddes taketh hym say shall fall thynge future specyfye yf spirite prophecye graunted hym alone speciall though connyng perygall goddes hauynge prescience shewe afore sapyence shall betyde outher euyll good let let wyght woodd hath wyt gyue therto credence man crafte scyence mortall hath connyng deuyne fortune course fate termyne suche cause hyd conceled secree reserued goddes priuitee men may dyuyne folye take hede lye wherfore rede mattere one al lorde dere exclude drede may disturbe herte let nothyng perturbe highe courage helenus hath tolde yf herte bolde manhod wold helpe venge wronge let hym go hyde temple stronge kepe close contemplation wake praye deuocion without socour dayes nyghtes suffer suche lusty knyghtes haunte youth grene lustynesse manly armes preue hardinesse may haue better acqueintauce tyme comyng vengeaunce enmyes cruell foen sith comaunde yt parys may forth gone execute fyne entent afore purposed parlement vpon grekes offention perfourme payne talyon wronges olde whiche yet fame rehersed vnto aldershame world ye wote lece therwithall troylous helde peace sodeynly present began one holly one assent troylus counsayle greatly preyse manhode heauen reyse freshe courage hygh prowesse feruent zeale hardinesse one herte greatly commende ryght anone made ende pryamus whan done vpon tyme houre none mete goeth within great ilyon sonnes syttyng enuyron mete called hath parys deiphobus also full wyse secretely bad shulden go day lordes mo panonye haste maye make ready agayne certayne day wyth araye worthy cheualrye maye get companye towardes grece saylen hastely kynge sodeynly next day made counsayle call euen thus sayde afore poh noble lyeges beynge nowe present purpose saye myne entent without abode ye lyste thyncke vnwyste grekes pryde tyrrannye malys olde compassed enuye many wyse haue agayne v wrought whiche grene foryet nought day day encreasynge euer mo remembraunce renewed wo whan recorde casten vp downe greues exiowne seruytude amonge doth soiourne whiche ofte day causeth mourne hath herte almost asonder ryue consyder se lyue whose crueltee haue dere bought albeit haue meanes sought haue reste without whan grece sent anthenore peasably syster recure paciently surplus endure nought toke hede offred goodlyhede herde lacke gentilnesse recorde whiche doubleth distresse pwherfore must teacheth surgerye sharpe irous seken remedye cutte away roote rounde dead fleshe festred wounde whiche wyll voyde wt oynetmentes softe albe applyed full ofte right must attempte duresse get recure whan fayrenesse may none haue wherfore aduyse purpose hast sende paryse forth grece lady wyn bringe home shal within strongly kepe mauger sayth nay tyll see agreable day fayne lyke myne opinion haue exchaunge exion syster namely loue may fayle shal thus goddes v fauourable counsayle also acceptable echone whan thynge toucheeh comonte wyttye men affyrmed comon ought confyrmed thyng touchyng shuld fyrst appreued euerychone achieued wherfore caste aduise plainly worke forthwith withall noble pryam sodeynly pea amonges prease whan whyshte alder syghte knyght vp rose percheus highte sonne great euforbyus de transformatis sayth ouidius fayneth whylom soule pithagoras hooly transsumed wryte ouyde touchyng wyll longer byde tell forth percheus afore kynge whiche gan tale thus pmy lyege lorde vnto hygh noblesse displease worthynesse though presence maiestye shall saye acquyte towardes fayth trouthe sothfastly may slouthe touchyng honour without dread zeale fayth bren doth glede harmes byd ye beware doubtlesse affyrme well dare ye stande firste aduyse ye purpose senden forth paryse doubte shall rewe god well wote olde newe father called enforbius discrete wyse ryght vertuous knowyng afore euery thynge prescyence wyttynge tell playnly philosophye heauenly sawe eye na thyng might secretely hyd hym ne yet pryuytee ne knewe wyt sage laste whan age hundred yere locke grey hore well bethincke complayned sore wepte also pitie tenderly fully affyrmyng parys vtterly wente grece rauyshe hym wyfe shulde insue suche mortall stryfe vpon v sothly citie shulde scindred asshes tourned shulde nothyng v socour grekes sworde shulde cruelly deuoure hye lowe playnly spare none wherfore praye amonge euerychone tell haue ye despyte wronge venge putteth respyte rancour olde reade ye lete tranquyll quyete hastynesse ye submytte fortune lyste falsely flytte trouble auncient enmyte newe sterynge felycitie ye iourney thus assente ye euerychone full sore shall repente yf ye wyll algates thether sende parys stede let wende lest voyage spede loe counsayle fully rede sayde vnder supporte grace pand sodaynly gan echone chace penthens loude agayne hym crye repreuynge hym prophecye father confusyon pbut oh ala reuolucion ioye wo felicitee thing tofore ordeyned must nedely state thynges wt fate englewed shall fall may eschewed whiche caused tassent one al hast parys shulde gone vnhappely wt hap enuolued pand thus concluding counsaile dissolued casuelly loe befell ryght aduyse vnto eres ran cassandra great afraye sodayne wo gan cryen welaway palas quod ala wyll ye shall parys grece go worde braste wepe full piteously inwarde syghes depe gan wayle sowne payne furyously noyse complayne wofull rage many pyteus sowne made mortall lamentatiowne deade might withholde heare torne fystes folde sayde ala hundred syth ah stormy fortune lyst thou kythe thy cruell force oure aduersytie vpon v eke citie mortall yre gery violence sword vengeaunce worse tha pestilece poh troye troye gylte ala hast thou done thy trespas euersed tourned nought wylde fyre thy synne dere abought ah pryam kynge vncely thy chaunce hast thou gylte outher greuaunce thy goddes wyrched vnryght prouoke shewe cruell might vpon thy bloud ala hast thou oh mother myne oh hecuba also maner cryme importable offence hast thou comyt haue recompence daye abyde oh noble worthy quene thy sonnes suche vengeaunce sene oh wofull deth cruell horryble ala ye credible counsayle suche harmes eschewe mortall purpose fully remewe go ordeyned thought hart hath costrained vnneth may wo endure father wofull creature helde streight way falleth plat groud wepyng water drownde chekes gan teares rayne myght constraint paine vpon hym gan clyppen crye besechynge hym shape remedye pyteous voyce yt knewe ful wele matter playnly euerydele shall befall full mynde sodeyne harmes shal insue behynde clamour vayne shall fall clerkes sayne ne may well men eschewed eke fortune great aduersytie hasty ire furyous wood aye vnkynde vnto troyan bloud causelesse agaynst sore agreued rancour sodaynly amened blind awaite catche trauce vyolence vnhappy chaunce hath wt sweyght tourned whele vnstable enuyous mutable hasten troyens theyr confusyon wylfulnesse vndiscretion agaynst grekes quarell make therupon haue counsayle take haue achieued ye herde deuyse without assent wyse yf diffynycyon hector herde concluded reason matter helenus counsayle take percheus aduerted wysely sentence without faynyng gyuen full credence cassandra neuer lyst lye aduyse harde prophecye poynt poynt caste aforne mischief tho lorne floured yet theyr felycitie without domage aduersytie fortune fortholde course alway whose wyll abydeth sayth ye nay caused voyage forhead playne blandishing vysage sugre shad venim roote bytter taste shewing soote wrynckled double like horned snayle fayth face fraud ay tayle haste troyans accorde one parys shuld grece gone ye haue herde sayne herupon cast theim ordayne phow priam king sent paris deiphobus others worthy troy grece aduenge rauishinge syster exion returne rauyshed faire heleine wife menelaus brought troye ca xiii time approched whe ye son shene golden wayne whyrleth vp atwene cleare sterres hyades read haue theyr scyte bulles head pleyades seuenth sterre bryght whych syxe appearen syght seuenth draweth asyde couertly doth beames hide whylom hath done great offence vnto v causeth absence dare shewe stremes cleare systren openly appeare whelom god mortall syn committed cryminall noysed kouth thrughout ye heue alone amonge sistre seuen shroudeth v shamefestly chere pand titan zodiak sphere atwene sterres taken see bul sixtenth degre vpon time ioly grene maye flora hewes gaye hath euery playne medowe hil vale floures quicke nothing pale ouer spred clad lyuery newe brauches blosme diuerse lusty hewe byd v fully glad lyght assuraunce fruit haue hight agayne autumpne list shake vine ripeth euery grape thus season lusty disporte embraseth hertes newe recomforte onely hope kinde dewe holsom fruite shall blosmes sewe whan time cometh reuolucion thus may ye lusty freshe season whan byrdes synge theyr hermonye time pannonye repeyred deiphobus parys theim brought chosen deuyse thre thousande knightes redy gone theim grece shippes many one ful vitayled may theim nede shippes nomber rede two twenty like wryte guydo without ado kinge commaundeth vnto eneas anthenor polydamas al haste theim redy make parys knyghtly vndertake ye haue herde iourney acheue time whan toke theyr leue pryamus shorte conclusyon sheweth effect entencion specially theyr deuer done recure syster exione ye haue herde tofore tell shuld matter dwell whan ready without soioure parys first lord gouernour voyage made pryamus brother called deiphobus theyr leue haue take longed deutye ship right manfully without abode gan theym selues dresse name venus goddesse mighty ioue taken theyr iourney anker hoist forth large sea gan saile haue winde wil water calme blandishing still without trouble boystous wawe costes ginnen fast drawe grekes lande nothing ne theim let fortune theyr course met grekishe shyp mine auctour telleth thus whych king menelaus towarde pyram famous stronge citie visite duke high degre nestor hight menelaus brother eke vnto king famous wise worthy great agamenon greatest name reputacion amonges grekes worthinesse menelay storye beareth wytnesse husbande quene heleyne syster brother tweyne castor pollux whych tolde hand worthy knightes hold time like degre strynester theyr cheif citye helde housholde solempne royall loue tho speciall wyll herte accordinge dede atwixe theim two brotherhede none could lyue alone eke mayde hermyone yonge doughter quene heleyne fayrenesse inly souereyne passyngly excellyng beaute pand thus troians sayling sea towarde grece amonge wawes wete auenture theim happed mete kinge menelaus sayling theyr syde none theim list pryde enquere passen forthe swyft lusty pase none theym could knowe aye wynde peasebly gan blowe troian flete causyng whyle approche noble yle called cithera daye hauen haste may anker cast boud theyr shippes stroge theim list tarye longe take lande ful many lusty man araying theim freshly pnow yle passyng excellence temple great reuerence buylded olde foundacion honoured region throughout land fer nere feast day aye yere yere like fil reuolucion repeyringe thither great deuocion honour onely venus goddesse grekes al theyr businesse honoured euery maner age giftes brynging pilgremage great offryng sacrafise vsed theyr paynem wise pfor phane knele wake herte contryte theyr prayer make statue gaue euery questyon perfect answere ful solucion ceremony venus loute euery thinge wherof doubt hadden ful declaracion thus grekes vpon citheron halowe feast riche great araye rytes dewe fer forthe may hope fully better thryue pand fortune aryue vp land aduenture case tyme feast halowed many greke coming fro euery coste temple go pilgramage theyr vowes acquite place reliques visyte parys espye chosen hath companye worthiest chese may temple toke right way ful wel besene knightly wise honour sacrafise ful humble grekes liche many ouche many iewel riche golde syluer stone riche perre spendeth like degre quit manly oblacions ful deuoutly orysons demeneth ioye se pnow parys passing great beaute amonges euer alyue none might wt striue troian greke speake semeliheade wonder freshe lusty reade porte full lyke gentil knighte whose person haue sight gan prease nigh fere royally bare gere prease high estate loowe knight desyren knowe men asken busyly whense came cause coming enquyring one one prudently kept theym euerychone nothing openly espyed theyr answer selues guyde euery thing kept secree eueriche theim auisee albe openly declare ne list spare tolde playnly cause cominge howe pryam stronge mighty kinge father royall renowne came also exiowne thus eche theim gan rowne pryme face whan came towne therupon ymagynatyfe sore musyng much inquisitife eche suspection deminge therof lyke theyr opynyon rathest nothinge ne knewe folkes done thinges newe whyles matter treate sondry wise among theyr wordes greate saying theim gan anone atteyne eares quene heleyne nigh beside regyon herde relacion reporte come bytwene fayre heleyne freshe lusty quene anone sothe vnderstode without delay abode casteth solempnytye freshe folke phrigia se wel god wote entention se parys deuocion vnder colour holy pylgramage temple taketh voyage great meyne royal apparayle parys se wyll fayle pbut oh ala lusty newe fyre herte hath nowe enflawmed desyre go vigiles spectacle none holynesse heare myracles hath meued shal befall maner woman drawe thether platly conclude sure multytude ygathered lybertye see may finde oportunitye theyr desyre ful narowe awayte couertly theyr eyen baite place set theyr plesaunce pryuely haue dalyaunce sygne casting eye token shewing hert drye touche hades stole amonge prese arme fote catche vp theyr lese lyst free bonde nature holde honde ayen whose sleyght auaileth wyt myght theim list yt wronge ryght aye achieue sayth yea nay agayne whose lust defend man may pthus guydo aye cursed false delyte speak harme hath caught appetite throughout boke woman say yll translate agayne wll hath aye ioye theyr honour ramuerse ryght sorye must reherse fel wordes booke yfounde woman mikle bounde echone goodly kynde dare theim say finde guydoes write throughout troy booke redde feare herte quoke veryly wyttes gan fayle whan therof must maken rehersaile like decrete guydo wyte ye shall heare anone chit quene heleyne cause went herte deuoute offryng presente temple venus goddesse thus word word sayth expresse po mortal harme dread fraude ycast sleyght womanhead euery wo ginning crop roote agaynst whych helpe may bote whan lust hath dryue theyr herte nayle aye deadly venim seweth tayle man hath power restreyne recorde take quene heleyne inly brent ala desyres newe lust dele straungers knewe nat ne neuer sawe beforne wher ala ful many lorne cruel death embrased cheyne without pyty saye thou quene heleyne ghost spyryte ala hath meued sole fro thy lorde royaltye thy house go among prease yu wery liue home peace wentest straungers se taking hede vnto thine honestye thou shuldest haue kept thy closet secretly haue passed folyly absence thy lorde ala thou wilful rakel case se afore shuld sewe al sone thou drawe mewe coulde kepe home tho thy boud thou wetest hare among ye houndes caught wilfulnesse thy desyre coudest compesse though thy lust lyst refrayne many woman hath caught trayne goyng halowes seke syt theim better home kepe close theyr chaumber fle occasyowne neuer shyp shuld peryl drowne ryue rocke tempest rente caribdis dreached yshent go wrake wether yll kept hauen styll wil occasyons eschewe dread peryll sewe must nedely necessytie beware endure aduersytie fote fro trappes spare let take hede fall snare harme ydone late compleyne whylom noble quene heleyne selfe kept home secrete close ne wicke lose reported yet grene freshe newe whose chauce vnhappi eche ought rew cause destruction many worthy confusyon husband many mo grekes syde troye also storye ye shall reade pand quene fast may spede temple hath way ynome full royally whan come ful deuoutly within citheron made vnto venus oblacion presence syght many one many iewell many ryche stone pand whe paris thing espied temple anone hath hyed ful thriftely hast myght wher forthwith syght goodly fayre freshe quene cupides darte whet kene ware hath marked astoned nist much meruayleth semelinesse womanhead porte fayrnesse neuer erst ne wende nature coud ought haue made fayre creature aungellyke beaute feminine goodly se sothly dempte liklynesse beaute goddesse herte aye assure ne mortall creature heauenly fayre celestyall thought partye eft consydereth auysely feature ordre curyously aye reason euery thinge good inspection golden heare like sonne streames freshe phebus bright beames goodly heade fleshly face full replete beaute grace ylike enewed quickenes coloure rose lyly floure egally nother wite none excesse much lite within cerclynge eyen bryght paradise compassed syght eche hert ye beaute ga perce certaynly shall reherce shape fourme feature guydo doth ordre ceryously head foote clearly deuyse want englyshe therto may suffyse wil tunge nothing like want also floures rethorike sewe flouryshyng peynture discryue fayre creature coloures feble feynte nother ennewe wel depaynte eke acqueynted muse nine therfore excuse echone neclygence defaute onely eloquence remit guydo se descriueth ordre beaute take presumpciowne pbut wil tell parys vp downe gothe temple eye cast towardes heleyne gan presen fast brent hoote loues fyre enflawmed greatly desyre oft chaungeth coutenaunce cheare euer neygheth nere nere ydarted eyen tweyne likewyse freshe quene heleyne hote brent herte priuely albe man outward could espye thought neuer erst fore men euer yet bore se none fayre like pleasaunce loke harte suffysaunce temple taketh hede nought compasseth casteth thought may catche oportunitye speake lybertye hooly busynesse felt inly great distresse oft chaugeth coutenauce hewe venus hath theim marked newe brondes fyred feruence enflawmed sodayne influence egally brought rage saue eye atwene message eche fyxe haue cast theyr sight conceyue wyst anone right within theim selfe theyr herte ment nere euer parys wente seke fully get occasyon might ful relacion theyr hertes conceyte declare secretly befell parys nigheth nye place quene heleyne stode see atwene tweyne broke al sum theyr whole hert gaue yssue theyr inward smerte done lest espyed whan people occupyed temple stare gase mase kept theim close worde asterte man treaso myght aduert theim twayne ne would mene last parys quene concluded haue wyth shorte auysement fully fine theyr entent set time betwyx theim certayne whan appoynten mete agayne lest men theim suspection made ende without sermo syth departe albe lothe soberly anone parys gothe temple brest euery parte fully gyrt loues fiery darte shippes helde right way anone al hast may whan assembled chiualrye one al companye fewe wordes shortly tofore theim tale thus began lordinges quod shortly expresse cause kouthe youre worthinesse father grece v sent ye knowe chief entent recure sister exion handes mighty thelamon thinge ought espye impossible shortly mine eye waie fer se great strong countre allyes aboute euery side herte inly full pride yelde vp hath disdayne therof treate vayne therfore best deuise sith power may suffise werrey regiowne egall might renowne lacke men holde felde may win spere wt shelde tencountre multitude wherfore best conclude sith fortune hath v hither brought goddes haue eke v wrought graciously make v londe venus temple fast stronde whiche aboundeth ful great richesse grekes offringe vnto goddesse londe sea fro many sundry porte men woman hyther haue resort place worshyp venus wife kinge menelaus present ful riche wel beseyne manhod might atteyne rauishe temple spoyle theyr treasour chesen coyle chefe iewels chargen somers wyth golde syluer wyth prysoners maugre theim shyppes brynge night without tarying may fayle euer saythe nay ye assenten worthye pray wherfore haste ye redy make euery man anone harnes take arme hym well best aray assente without delaye theyr shyppes byde till night whe phebus chaire wtdrawe light vnder wawes sterres appeare heauen theyr streames cleare moone time aryse shope theim forth ful thrifty wise manly troians armed stele bryghte temple holding theyr waye aryght casten longer tarye proudly enter sanctuarye chappel called citheron without reuerence deuocion done venus oratorye cleane theyr memorye honour dread obseruaunce fynally theyr attendaunce myn auctour sothly diffine ryght nought onely rauyne token came theyr hande rychesse treasour lande golde syluer stone riche iewelles releques sacred holy eke vessel without abode sacrary yfeare theyr shippes carye wonder thynke good kil sley theim withstode likewyse pytie se theim blede grekes ship lede lyued captyuytie ful many yeare troye citye pand while goth parys heleyne embraseth armes tweyne full humble great reuerence found maner resystence sat womanly ther parys yolde vtterly herte hap yolde came therfore yelde lesse feare stryue woman sholde anone gentilnesse wolde comforteth best may led forthe without delaye vnto shyppes full busyly set wardes kepe honestly temple retourneth agayne spoyle robbe make playne temple withe walles wyde pnowe stode castell fast besyde ystuffed well grekishe souldeours whych awoke wyth noyse pylours nyght gan make shoute therwithall anone yssue oute armed stele temple reskewe manfully theim sewe befell whan togyther mette wyth speres sharpe swerdes kene whet pthey ran togither tygres wilde like wood lion bore vnmilde fayninge foud theyr fyght albe felde departed ryght troians doubled nomber vtterly grekes encoumbre mischefe made theim fast flee pursute ful cruelly theym flee without mercy castell gate rescuse came late skermyshe fine deathe nowe thei yelde vp ye breath mightely troians theim assayle withstade might theim auaile manhod felde haue wonne ryght cruelly begonne hasty wyse ransacke castell shyppe broughten euerydell treasour golde may win morowe salen begyn stuffed good grekyshe sea towarde costes troye citye sea calme fully theyr tempest stormes ill cleare also bryght heauen space almost dayes seuen castel called tenedowne aryued sixe mile towne glad light land wente finde parys sente messager streyght vnto kinge enfourmeth home cominge theyr exployt tolde theim euery dele pryamus lyketh wonder wele manly haue borne made publyshe towne tydynges new great solempnitie hygh lowe cytie ioye moste eke leste remembraunce halowe holde feste thanke goddes full humble wyse obseruaunces sacrafyce aulters great deuocion whyle tenedon holdeth soiourne quene heleyne whiche hap gan rewfully complain vnkouth life dwellen straungers disconsolate amonge prysoners ferre sequestred away countrey solytarye captiuitie wepeth cryeth pyteous chere wawes vpboyled eyen clere wherof stremes chekes rayne constraynt inwarde peyne full often sythes songe wel away sobbing voice fer awaye departed menelaus whose absence rage furyous hateth lyfe curseth eke fortune wo euer doth contune without soiourne alway brethern pollux castor loue doughter dere pale grene wexeth chere whylom fresher sene lyilye stalke grene ala chaunged rosen hewe aye elyche wo encreaseth newe lyke woman beholde aye wepte water wolde ptill laste heauynesse parys came gentylnesse recomforte appese rage besyeth hym sorowes aswage sayeng ala may mene ye one oh goodly freshe quene lyst thus selfe sorowynge diffygure wonder greatly ye may endure moche water causeles thus shede weping haue dewed wede like conduite streames ran downe penitaunt contriciowne ye disraye ala ye let fare let ouer go wepynge thought heauinesse lady distresse make ende greuaunce ease comforte pleasaunce men may truste well ye shall haue foly sorowe thus raue lette passen ouer sharpe shoures trouth ye youres lyste shal haue suffysaunce ferforth haboundaunce haue ye amonge grekes ensure nothyng feare shall holde haue hyght trouthe true knyght worde dede herte entire anone dolefull chere myght forsobbyng tho suffyce answered agayne full lowly wyse pi wote quod lothe lefe syth caught take mischiefe vnto wyll may seye bounde must obeye vnder daunger may flee holde distrayned captiuitee pye wot also nature dreade ne longeth vnto womanhead straunge soyle stryue rebell namely quarell shall haue fauour susteyned yf ye lyste haue pitee myne goodlyhead ye may god deserue thanke mede wyll rewarde iustly geue tho comforte care wo pnow lady myne quod parys maye lyke deuyse shall trusteth ryght wele trouthe ferre feele thyng may pleasaunce ye shall haue habundaunce ensure heste fallyble agaste fully credible wordes hestes euerychone therwithall ladde ryght anone place royall apparayle comforte wolde auayle secretely betwene two parys fyrste without spake vnto sayde lady dere fayne speake herte entyer hope ye shall hereafter fynde wherfore praye enprenteth mynde saye remembraunce saye syth ye purueyaunce ben goddes brought therto fortune eke dare affyrme playnly fyrste disposed haue worste good ye must take wherfore reade suffer ouer shake heauynesse loketh ye glad lyght countrey though ye owne lande faythfully tunderstande ye shall haue moche habundaunce euery parte full suffysaunce semeth pleasaunt one thyng dare well auaunt countrey shalbe founde euery thyng plenteously habounde ful grekes yonder though ye ben farre sonder lande called achaye cause whye ye shoulde dismay syth ye worshyp reuerence honour greater excellence shalbe cherished ye afore ye playne ye haue forbore owne lord left sole ye maken al wo dole ye shall haste sette better ease certaynly displease offende vnto womanhead stede hym purpose dread wedde trewe man loue serue euer without faynyng lyues ende lowly kynde dylygent eke laborous whylom menelaus euery thynge lustes obeye haue trouthe tyll tyme deye pand though wordes plain loue god haue disdeyne request grutche least stocke royall descended come hygh bloud menelay byrth good loue farre trewe erst chaunge newe pwherfore leue thus playne wepe let comforte bosome crepe wo appease worth haw lette myrth herte adawe beseche womanhead wordes ye lyst take hede palas quod myght befall haue ylefte frendes one straunge lande al alone shuld tha stil complaine one haue cause god wote pley yet chekes kepe drey salte teares ala wyll none ende myne aduersyte good fayth agaynst kynde sodaynly tabandon mynde thilke thyng eyther ioye smerte worlde sytteth nexte herte ala sore destrayned syth goddes haue ordeyned better chaunce hope vnto must take gre humbly accepte also sonde weake power withstonde wherfore shal agayne wyll striue al wo herte fele ryue consent lowly admytte thylke thynge fro whiche may flytte maugre wyll necessytie fully obey ye lyst wil helpe although sayed nay thus playneth al euer may little little sorowe aswage shulde aye lyue wo rage lese selfe tender creature herte stele ne myght endure aye woman maner kynde sorowe make ende tyll leysure wepte haue full laste whan gynnen dull make sorowe happeth faste grace soone ouer caste lyghtly catche comforte smerte tender yt men may conuerte fro wo ioye thought disseuer storme may laste euer clerkes wyse bookes lyste discerne thynge vyolente may nothyng eterne stormes phebus bryghter comforte counsayle parys adawed olde sorowe euen lyke glade morowe veray kynde seweth dercke nyght processe herte wexeth lyght wepyng dryed well lyke storye shall anone v tell howe parys receyued troye retourne maryage heleyne capitulo xiiii vvhan ye quene called heleine adawed drery peyne wawes heauy cheare chekes gonnen clere parys herte freshe amerous haste hath sente kyng pryamus horse men apparayle clothes golde full noble entayle made heleyne wrought none ryche perle many sondry stone agayne commyng troye towne parys tenedowne shappeth lede troye pryamus mette waye full royally faste myght hye many lorde companye full many lady freshe well beseyne many mayde ryde agayne fyrst estate communers nowe parys prysoners set order tweyne tweyne rode next quene heleyne deiphobus vpon syde knyghtes enuyron dyd ryde nexte hym rode worthy eneas troyan called pollydamus meane suynge eche degree gentylmanly ioye see eche kepyng certayne space forth ryden softe pace tyll kyng mette sodaynly receyued hath full solempnely beste coulde goodly toke rayne hande quene heleyne conueyed forth citie great preyse abode see sondry folke shoued faste croude shyrle trumpettes yreysed loude vp skye goth blysfull sowne whan people entreth towne many nother dyuers instrumente tofore gate went sondry wyse made melodye heauenly armonye musycke touched vpon strynge corde euen one iustly accorde wolde herte rauyshe ioye whan entred troye amydde palayse pryamus alight anone faste euer myghte chambre ryche well besey quene heleyne haste dothe conuey comaundyng eft herte wyll thought offycers fayle nought thynge bethyncke spyces parted anone ye wyne drinke kyng toke leue tyll supper whyles chaungeth attyre pbut ioye towne euery place men went vp downe rude sothly wryte muche herte troyans delyte safe sounde retourned parys wende haue ben ioye paradyse well sped iourne hath one loste meyne wherof herte glad lyghte haste nexte nyght wryte guydo without tarying longe erely morowe larke songe pallas temple myne auctor sayth assured othe eke fayth bond wedlocke heleine euermore laste atwixte tweyne knotte knitte sacrament thus done fully thassent first kyng also thaduyse citie fauour paryse feast great solempnitee continued muche royaltee weddyng myrthe solace towne eyght dayes space shulde wryte reuell ye daunces freshe aray countenaunces scole touch lokes amerous priue grutche yt ialous great iustes bourdes tornaye amydde palestre many sundry playe dyuers course eke euery feste large plente done leste straunge meates maner seruyce haue none englyshe deuyce passe ouer pbut whan weddyng came vnto ye ere cassandra fyrste dyd espye thousande sythe ala gan crye pyteous wo vntressed heeres sayde thus albe spreynte teeres wretched troye errynge case within thy selfe suffer trespase consente vnto suche folye susteynyng foule auouterye parys shulde taken vnto wyfe quene heleyne whose husband alyue oh wofull troye cruell thy fate beware almost late tyme come thou shalte destroyed many father shall sonne see hole morne shalbe slayne eue amyddes fyelde wyll sore greue many wyfe shall carefully bewepe se husband large woundes depe gryde body pale colde grene ala shall ye sorowe mowe susteyne pah wretched mother shall ye endure se child cruell aduenture afore slayne withouten remedye wyll helpe though ye clepe crye pah mother myne heccuba quene shalt thou byde ye sharpe stoundes kene thy worthy sonnes se afore slawe fyelde cruelte ydrawe pah blynde people death yu takest hede nylte thou worke rede case prudent wyse take awaye heleyne fro paris right requireth withouten lorde iustely restore pwhat trowen ye thefte cruel dede shall passe thus nay nay withouten drede sword vengeauce shal ful sharply byte offence shall beare wyte paleys house se within throwe toures hye layde erthe alowe ala ala saye heleyne vnhappy woman causer payne harde vnsely also gracelese vnwealfull woman disturbler peace thou hast v brought mischefe kyndled bronde burne v yfeare ala thou arte grounde roote many drery feast funerall shall beholde amonge v towne wise cassandra vp downe aboute ran subarde strete crieth one euer mete full ofte syth ala welaway tyll pryamus bycause affray noyse tho make without abode anone doth take bounde fast fetred pryson without mercy remyssyon toke hede sadde trouthe wordes routhe shet vp bondes great stronge without pitie abyde longe thus pryson whyle let morne grekes wyll agayne retourne thunhappy tyme whyle false fortune frendly gan smyle vpon troyans bad mery highly gan goddes hery wenyng ioye haue assured weale nothyng aduerting tournyng ye whele lasteth stable throwe whe men trust make mowe tourne forhead face wrythe suche ioye hath doublenesse kythe wrappe clerenesse vnder cloude agaist whose might ther mai hi shroud whe flattereth lest triste ioye troyans lyttell wyste hath mente confuciowne whyle aboute towne wende grekes haue gotten full recure domages haue sure thilke pray ye paris wonne wycked fame rumour yronne swift wing al yt haue wroughte menelay fydynges ybrought whyles abode nestor pirrha firste temple cithera spoyled robberye golde treasoure tyrrannye vpon men troyans execute assaylyng suite grekes made cruelly ne spared vtterly man woman came waye ne toke ladde praye theyr shyppes also fyght afore castell nyght pand alder laste heareth wyfe loued derely lyfe tenderly god wote thousande folde herte waxed colde stone therto pale hewe hertye wo inly gan renewe fyrst whan harde name sowne without anone fell sowne ne myght endure stande til duke nestor toke hym hande hym adawed deadely swowe ala quod haue lost howe lyues luste hertes suffysaunce ah death come make greuauce fully ende thy cruell darte wounded euery parte herte also korne euery veyne wyfe myne owne heleine deforced fro welaway farewell ioye farewell olde playe haue straungers possessyon whiche wyll full confusyon ala cheryshe trete fayre heleyne swete ye gone pensyfnesse sleath may wayte death amyd wo menelay shope hym go reygne lyttell besyde axeth horse said wolde ryde sole complaine yt felte greue whyle nestor wyll leue go hym consolacion frendly ryght hauynge compassion hym comforte full myght leading many worthy knyght reygne menelaus pthan fyrst story telleth v sent kyng agamenon castor come anone pollux myght comen three saw brother mischief brought almost murdred owne thought without abode wyse agamenon gyue hoope consolacion dyd labour diligence entere sayinge hym ye shall poh brother mine wo heuinesse deadly sorowe thus inly may oppresse knightly hert trouble manhead furiously ywys nede though ryght required vtterly sorowe hadden cause yet semeth iuste prouidence ye slyly shulde dyssymule offence sith eche wyse man aduersytie shulde fame chere kepen secree inwarde wo bynt hym distresse manly force rathest compesse spyryte ire melancolye people myght espye doctryne prudent whan man furye rent fayne chere tyll tyme se leysure vengeaunce kyndell may fyre sorowe shewed shall fayne taketh hede doth thynges twayne causeth frendes syghe sore enemyes reioyse thy frende herte sorye nature thyne enemye glad thy mysaduenture wherfore herte wha wo doth haboude faineth gladnesse thyne enemye confound shew chere thou roughtest nought greuous thy thought yu hast moste matter complayne make good face glad porte ye faine teares though thou distylle rende thy selfe thou woldest spylle helpeth ledge thy greuaunce honour nother pursuite vengeaunce sorowe makynge mowe execute though last ay ther cometh therof frute men say dissimule wronge slyghe herte stronge peasyble smerte token hath manly herte wepe woman rage whiche contrary hygh courage word weping auenge paine meanes worshyp attayne let v sworde wordes fyght tunge appese mahod preue might worde winde water wepe though tempest fluddes depe two encrease euer mo may augment wo foon therof dole heauy chere encrease ioye wherfore brother whyle acoye cruel tourment byndeth sore prouerbe hath sayd full yore prowesse manly knyght proued mischyefe myght assured aduersitee strongly susteyne wo cowardly courage submytte euery peryll honour flytte dispeyre hope alway wele haue truste trewe stele tacheue aye take hande fynally vnderstande hym selfe hath good fantasye set vpon put inpartye befall happe happe may takyng chaunce tourneth play fyne suche gladly victorye fayle selde palme glorye tyme speke wordes fewe oh brother myne manhode shewe plucke vp herte make stronge venge damage wronge shall echyone helpe lay hande kynges duke lordes lande atones busynesse behyght harmes redresse despyte euer v lette shall v lodge tentes sette euen fyelde afore troye towne beseage destructiowne albe therof set daye brother first haste may let maken letter without sermon lordes region matter touchynge vyllanye come gyther shape remedye theffect sayne pand thus released somwhat payne menelays cofort brother whan sawe myght none tale kynge made ende thrugh ye lande letter sende fyrst kynne allye come helpe hym curtesye pand fyrst menelaus came achylles patroclus alder nexte stronge dyomede many another helpe nede echone open parlement accorded full assente gouerned agamenon lyst ordayne discrecion voyage made hym gouernour hooste chieftaine emperour amonge full vnitee vpon troyans auenged bee purpose neuer remewe fyrst fynde parys sewe voyage toke ye worthy brethern tweine pollux castor recure heleyne yet neuertheles bokes lysten tell kynges longer wolde dwell alder faste parys agone toke shyppe folowed hym anone many worthy company doubtlesse yf olde bokes lye sayled dayes three troyewarde large see tempest rose wyndes dyd awake heauen derke cloudes blake haue day tourned nyght bryght phebus mirked light fyry lenen stroke thonder smote maste shyuerde sonder derke lyghte myght adawe sea gan swell many sturdy wawe rose hyghte large mounte fell downe swapped frounte euen shyppe plunged full lowe vp downe forcast ouerthrow shyppes tempest fro fomy water grene whyte blo feruent boylyng pytche blacke storme wynd al goeth wracke hydously blastes theim dryue euery borde gan ryue peryshed scaped man atones reherse dead drowned tempest sodaynly scaped none say certaynly except brethern bookes tel one heauen lowe hel lordes made tabyde eternally pand fayne theyr poesy goddes haue theim defyed like heauen ystellifyed theyr shyppes ware ygo wrake made sterres zodyake sygne transfourmed vtterly whych clerkes called gemyny whych sygne constellation mercury house mansyon kinde femell masculyne whych egle also dolphyne haue theyr arysyng reuolucion tayle also aboue dragon exaltate thyrd degree gemyny whych sygne hathe pouste hande armes man oute doubte like lucina halt course aboute wyse brether twayne heauen rapt poetes fayne tempest ye get wise grekes sea ende made ful wylfully ernest first came vnhappely theim echone ginning theyr wo finall chaunce brether two phow ye grekes assembled adueged yt troians rauishing helein ca xv bvt asmuche dare frigius boke whilom curyous fourme troiens grekes descriue lyke sawe auctour lyue shape fourme complexiowne partye theym troy towne grekes good auisement time trewse amonge theim wet seyng maner theyr gouernaunce porte theyr chere wt euery circustauce namely tho high degre forgate one loose qualyte condicions also theyr stature descryue dare cure grekishe tunge beginning heleyne like tofore ye haue herd seyne beaute peace pand furthermore speake achilles ryght fayre great semelynesse aborne heyr crispyng thicknesse eyen glawke large stepe great shuldred brode wt brest ful square mete endure armes fel coragious grounded vpon ryght wolde quyte hym like knyght pcilcus ayax right corpulent well cladde set al entent ryche aray ful curyous although body corsyous armes great wt shoulder square brode almost horse folde compas wise rounde sphere musyke none pere hauing voyce full melodye right well entuned hermonye inuentife counterfete instrumentes aswell smal grete sundry wise longing musyke yet good practike armes eke noble knyght man orped hardyer fight desyrous haue vyctorye deuoyde pompe hatyng vaynglorye ydle laude spent blowe vayne pof vlyxes shall also sayne noble worthy dayes ful wyles sleyghty curyosytye though crafty speche enbroude sleue yet al wil leue ay bolde bayarde blynde cast peryl way finde right wil stumble forth haed vnconning take better hede beaute discryue sothe al tho alyue renowmed reken hath fifty shippes brought iourney salerne royall chefe citye earles duke many worthy knight eueryche theim stele armed bryght pand duke tenter amphiacus earle daryon noble theseus ylke foure full worthy renowne voyage came thelamowne pand olde nestor cruel hert thought pylon hath fyfty shippes brought pthe kinge dyames yt full worthy eke kinge hight also thoas brought theim theyr companye hundred shippes knightlye guye pand thelamou ycalled pyleus armes fell spytous brought lande ferre sixe thyrty shippes werre pamphymacus kinge polibete thyrty shippes brought flete calcedoyne mereo kinge ydameus theyr ledinge foure score shippes theym crete pand vlixes grekes dyd mete fyfty shyppes stuffed trace towardes troye proudly pace pduke mellens full manly men brought eke hym great shyppes ten moreouer duke prothecatus pand duke named prothesylaus hauen called athene brought fyfty shypp enarmed bright shene phylyarcha stronge myghtye yle pand machaon guydo doth compyle brother polydris also countrey trycionyco brought two twenty shippes finde pand phyces mynde achilles came fyfty full numbre pand rhodon troyans encombre came twenty shyppes wt kyng thelapolus pand duke hyght antipus lande hesyda men call whiche folke nyghe cherles sayle crossed agayne bryght heauen numbre came shyppes eke elleuen name full famous worthy duke called amphymacus pand polibethes stronge
