knyghtes arme yt place gan full streyte lace doublettes made lynnen clothe certayne folde aboute hym goth also dempte moste sureste arme batayle areste dyd fyrst desyres sabaton greues cussues voyders payre brech alder fyrst mayle eke ne wolde fayle haue mayle payre brase therwithall custome payre gussettes pety coote garnished golde vp vnto throte paunce plate whiche selfe behynde shot close theron fynde enuyron abordure smalle mayle chose newe entayle surmyd foe hole breste plate arere dors behynde shet elles syde armes rynged wyde voyders fretted mayle cordes rounde freshe entayle vambras wynges rerebras therto theron sette besaguys also vpon head basenet stele within locked wonder wele craftye syght wrought viser wolde haue plate bauer brest fastned aforne canell pece easy borne gloues plate stele forged bryght wold armed light thicke iackes couered satyne wolde haue mayle wrought ful fine hawberion late wrought cassade weight ouer lade hym selfe welde lyke lyfly man wyll haue chose geseran boublet hawberyon sure gepon ouer polrynges rechinge knee sleues eke longe vambras may cured ner pryckynge palet plate couer wyll haue also vyser saue face onely aser wyll haue payre plate lyghte welde hym well whan shall fyght wyll haue target spere pauade body targe made stronge laste wyll haue dartes caste poilax headed fyne stele pycked square laste wele swerde enemye mete wyll haue bowe shete arblast standen syde pand foote ryde array selfe fomen sayle many one busye nayle felowes harneys make stronge dresse sette wronge poyntes tasshyes maner thinge suche case longeth armynge haue connynge euery thynge telle vnto longe dwelle fayle ye mot haue excused suche crafte lyttle vsed ignoraunce doth pennelette order dewe termes sette ofte chaugeth suche harneys deuyse ye therin expert wyse disdeyne speake place armynge grace right lyst correcte euerydell pand hector sawe al well euery man armed arrayed worthy knight longer hath delayed aduysedly wardes make prudently badde shulden take grounde haste put certayne stande order endlonge playne man founde recheles pand gate called dardanydes without abode hector made vnshette bad men shulde fette presence done haste pcyncynabor brother borne baste vnto hym fyrst euerychon pand lord named glaucon kynges sonne lycye heire many baner auaunsed eyre two hector gaue guarde gouernaunce fyrst warde hath thousande knyghtes sette speres rounde swordes kene whette brest full many ryche shyelde chosen fielde amonge beste endure myght agayne grekes manly fyght vnto hector bad anone goddes name shulden gone gate sothly rede pand lest fyll mischiefe nede assygned selfe place manly chere kynge trace wysely hym awaytyng thousande knyghtes haue ledyng wynge knyghtly abyde wayte hym vpon euery syde hym sonne archylogus age man ryght vertuous fulfyll longeth knyght herte also myght pand next hector gan deuyse next warde kyng fryse time called zantipus vnto hym stronge desyrous assygned wayte banere thre thousand knight armed bryght clere whiche warde kyng alcanus also hector commaunded go byddyng mekely dyd obeye full knyghtly taken haue waye gate passyngly arrayed towarde grekes baners displayed penons vnrolled euerychone pand hector assygned hath anone noble yonge lusty freshe free brother troylus goodly se whiche knyghthode suffysaunce thirde warde haue gouernaunce thre thousand knightes yonge age flourynge force hardy courage suche custome wont lede hector brotherhead full goodly spake sayd partynge brother quod herte louynge towardes kyndnesse though haue party gret gladnesse thy manhode ferre kouthe knyghthode thy grene youthe yet doubtlesse fantasye ful ofte daye stande iupardye pensyfehead busye drede whan remembre vpon thy manhead lest thy courage vyolent thy lyfe neglygent thy selfe put ferre aduenture surquidrye moche assure thy force knightly sterte euery peryll thy manfull herte hauynge regarde suche mortall stryfe wylfulnesse nouther death life aduertence thy sauacyowne fortune turneth vp downe whele meuable hye lowe martes ire wynde doth blowe whiche causeth ful ofte syghe thincke wake whan shulde wynke reuoluynge aye thy hasty wylfulnesse gentyll brother hardynesse thus ylke daye vpon euery syde praye wysely prouyde hate yre thy foe pursuynge excede settynge let prudence kepe mene wysdome eke holde agayne reyne thy herte thy fyerse courage fyred haue thy grene tendre age deuoyde drede eche peryll endure ennemyes thy mysauenture reioyce myne owne brother dere myghty mar praye herte entere thus euery day troyans grounde handes kepe sounde lyke wolde dyd pto anone humilite manly wise yonge lusty knight worthy troylus herte freshe light answered agayn sayd glad cheare mine owne lorde brother deare god tofore fully shall obeye fullfyll lyst seye vnto gentilnesse decline none recklesnesse poynt commaundemente hole herte best entente shall take hede playnly none ye haue sayd mine owne lord bother lothe offende greue wise lowly toke leue forth rode lyke manly knyght beholde noble syght amonge men haueth hym wele thre thousande knightes armed stele enuyron rode troylus fyelde day beareth shielde passant golde thre lyon rychely champe asure wrought full craftly gate yssued anone ladde knyghtes euerychon grekes holdyng next waye pand hector hasteth euer may prudently wardes ordeyne noble worthy bretherne twayne kyng hupon andelius assygned story telleth thus fourth warde guye wysse lande called larysse brethern two reigned longe hupon passyngly stronge stature lyke chaumpyowne saue hector troye towne none hym egall myght delyuer better knight foen passyng despytous whiche brother andelyus foure thousande knyghtes hadde lede seuen thousande sothly rede lyke wryte guydo worthy hector assygned hath also one brothern called dimarchus noble knight armes ryght famous manhode passyng excellence hector taken haue lycence rode waye amonge prese gate dardanides pthe fyfte warde haue ledyng hector commytted kyng cesoyne lorde prynce brother called pollidamas cysones hye stature might armes passyngly endure vpon full many man behelde kyng bare nothynge shyelde fyelde gules fynde sygne guydo maketh minde forth rode full sterne pase noble kynge pollydamas whan hector lene take whiche euer one full busye make syxth warde diligence kyng called pretemense full worthy werre peace pand duke hyght sterepes whyche also full worthy honde toke folke poenye lande gouerne fyelde day whiche people hath custome aye without plate hawberion mayle swyfte horse fomen assayle mighty bowes arrowes sharpe groud harneys mortally wounde folke hector eke also deyphobus assygned go fyelde guyde lede waye faste gan theim spede passe dardanydes full discretely hector chese panysers cladde mayle plate commaundyng yssuyng gate archer fyelde gone many worthy well armed euerychone awayte lore folke spake tofore poenye hadden none armure prudent hector make sure agrest myghty regyowne hath chosen full worthy renowne best knightes euerychon pand kynges esdras phylon assygned taken hede fotemen haue nede whiche phylon ordeyned full rychely rode chere yuery whyche wheles wrought full curious tree ycalled hebanus whiche tree groweth ferre inde blacke hewe also fynde korne tree wyll anone nature harde stone whan graue eyther rounde square pure golde roued chare fret perle many ryche stone suche trowe none worlde shall fayne ladde mighty knightes twaine men armes within eke without armed stele rydyng rounde aboute worthy kynges esdras phylon hector hath called hym anone one brethern falle guyde leder name pytagoras pand great troyon eneas tofore made mencion hector good deliberation seuenth warde assygned hath kepe vpon stedes lusty lepe suche vsed moche ryde full manly knightes haue syde whiche ewpheny vnto troye towne come ferre regyowne succour hector sake hym leue take rode full proudely forth eneas gate wonder knightly pase brode fyelde tyll haue atteyned pand whyle hector hath ordeyned lyke myne auctour reherse eyght warde folke perce worthy knightes manly ryght wyse whiche committed paryse day tawayte busyly hector tho full beningly spake saide thus departyng oh brother myne maner thynge whan thou arte passed dardanides daye ferre put prese amonge grekes iupardye lest thy toen mischyefe espye haue olde newe date hertes full freshe mortall hate fyre brest hath enbrased harde araced wherfore brother loke thou euer wise ferre fro kepe nye misauenture fall vpon may succoure daye mine owne brother deare parys full humble cheare answered sayd euery thinge would obeye vnto bidding rode waye anone meyne felde cite ninth warde ordre dresse whych thought hym selfe lede whych put sothly rede fiue thousand knight borne troy towne worthyest greatest renowne passyngly famous knighthode borne discent troians bloud pand brethern taketh wt hym ten suche knewe manly men forayne stocke regallye lyne borne bastardye hector great chyerte knyghthod could theim se whan knightly purueaunce wardes set gouernaunce lyke mar selfe fast gan spede without abode take stede whych bokes called gallathe horse hauyng soueraynte ferre men ryde coste dare maketh great boste shape heyght also fayrnesse strengthe loke great swyftnesse lyke horse perfourmed oute wt wyer men might tourne lyke dare maketh menciowne hector rydeth troye towne armed came wonder well foote head full rychly euerydele shone bright son somers daye pryam helde ryght waye whan come kinge reherseth ordre euery thynge hath done ordynaunce lowly sayd plesaunce noble royall excellence haue chosen busy dylygence thousand knightes full suffysaunce fyue hundred haue attendaunce persone alway ye footman cyte shall awayte euer one wherfore lorde fast gone lowly praye worthinesse sewe v good aduysenesse towne alway eke ye togyther kepe knightes meyne beseche full myght within boundes shall fight ye suffer none theim passe kepe ye hole selfe place atwyxe v stronge cyte haue nede ye maye aye se v releue kepyng asyde specially abyde lyckly partye sustene euer amonge shal men go betwene exployt trouthe reporte parte mar lyst fielde sorte power ilke daye fatall ye shal castell wall refuge saue v smerte specially one thynge ye aduerte deceyt fraude treasowne compassed behynde towne foen recklesnesse whyles hooly busynesse agaynst theim fielde fight wise therto haue syght nothynge tourne vnto domage engine worke ye sage victorye maye conclude grekes fraude v delude engyne vnware vyolence hopyng alway none offence highnes haue sayde worde pryamus abrayde beningely cheare countenaunce sayde hector sothfast suffysaunce fynall truste supportacion thy discreat disposycion hooly put thou list ordaine next god shall fayne fayth hope sikernesse welfare sothfastnesse committed hole thy hande gouernaunce playnly lande thou ordaynest must nedes prayer make nowe goddes aboue celestyall preserue partye eche myschiefe aduersyte thou mayst home ayene cite repaire honour laude victorye praise renowne memorye thy name put remembraunce perpetually thine honour auaunce fare well mine owne sonne deare hector tho full humble cheare leue toke forth rode anone amonge lordes knyghtes euerychone roote noblesse knyghthode groud strengthe hardynesse stocke therto inuincyble muche possyble nature myght graunt kynde touchyng manhode bokes fynde hadde soueraygne excellence gouernaunce medled prudence nought asterte wyse ware shelde fynde bare vpon brest troian champyon chyefe golde gowlys lyon depeynt therin baner bete selfe amydde strete toke waye dardanydes beholde huge prese noyse trumpettes claryons baners vnrolled longe freshe penons red whyte grene blewe blacke wyse hector hath ytake felde wythout wt herte hole entente mar selfe tho presente guydo maketh mynde rode warde lefte behinde manhode would abyde smote stede sharply syde fell courage hath horse payned fyrste warde hath atayned vale hylle tofore frounteres astoned fell cheares grekes platly aferde lyke knyght euen afore theyr berde gan prease theyr foo mortall pand whyle vpon troye wall sondry place hygh toures freshe besene may floures ladyes ascended towne fayre yonge standinge enuyrowne quene heleyne passyng fayre sene kinges doughters goodly pollycene many whych womanheade herte full busy dreade inly agaste feare afrayde whan behelde fyelde displayde brode baners tendernesse loue kyndnesse pale dreadfull theyr lordes theyr face hyden eke feare bolde lyfte vp theyr syghte heholde armure cleare bryght glytterynge aye agayne sonne shene theyr hertes tender myght sustene theyr dreade thus lette theim dwel grekes forth shall tell yf ye list abyde whyle must fordulled style agayne dyrect agamenon well maye make exclamacion ignoraunce staunt lyght causeth full cloudy syght makynge speken werre lacke tearmes must nedely erre conningly wardes sette cruell alecto busy lette nyghtes doughter blynded derknesse crafte armes trouthe expresse ordre dewe felde descryue chauncer nowe ala alyue refourme rede lacke slower spede noble rethor excelle making dranke welle vnder pernaso mus kepe hylle neuer yet might slepe vnneth slombre whych ala playne sayne though wede pollymyte coloures forth wyll endyte cometh euen thought playnly write ye kinge hath wrought manly knight great agamenon lyke latyn maketh mencion pwhat trowen ye entente founde slowe neclygente grekes halfe wardes make nay nay lyst wake tyme sothly slepe lyke kinge daye felde kepe neclygence myght herte fade daye fynde made syxe twenty wardes well deuysed prudently man might amende ordynauce fyrst gaue gouernaunce manfull noble patroclus wt ladde myn auctour telleth thus myrmydones myghty stronge folke achilles longe besyde thylke meyne whych brought countre cominge siege troye rode forth theim waye syelde made delaye fell daye achilles kept tente sycknesse daye ne wente lechesse made abstene woundes freshe grene caught daye tofore whych heale theyr akyng sore counsayle kept selfe close bedde daye ne rose hope onely better endure whan restored vnto cure men toke patroclus armes passyngly famous discent come great kynrede also hym reade hoboundaunt golde rychesse ferre commeded gentilnesse name hygh dyscrecion pnow aye suche affection entyre loue trouthe faythfulnesse great desyre inwarde kyndenesse busy thynkyng great feruence much frendship wt thoughtful aduertece huge brennyng passyng amerous betwyxt achilles patroclus theyr hertes locked cheyne soeuer shall fayne tone hath wrought brother vnto brother herte confermed wyll goodes commune death euer contune without chaunge theyr loue abode pand patroclus forth anone rode fyelde myrmydones tente abydeth achilles pthe secounde warde kinge menon assygned agamenon pand worthy kinge ydumenee duke called menestee thre thousand knightes stele armed clene wyth folke comen athene assygned wyth theim go pthe thyrde warde king ascalapho sone hyght phylomene knightes came cumane pthe fourth warde without lettynge archelaus noble worthy kynge prothenor securydan whych dayes stronge man assygned holly three knyghtes theim boece myghty lande famous pthe fyfth warde kinge menelaus folke regyowne called spertence full high renowne yles adiacent baner wente pof menelay freshe couragyous vi warde kynge epystrophus assygned kinge gelyde many worthy rydyng syde prouynce famous yle called guydo fordesyle pthe seuenth warde thelamonius called ayax great kynge famous assygned shortly termyne folkes salomyne brought many another mo foure earles hym went also ptheseus eke amphymacus thyrde called doxus fourth named polyxarye viii warde shall tarye good aduyse daye assygned vnto kinge called thoas payax cileus ix warde tho ladde tenth king philoctetes hadde pand kinge xi assigne sothly byrth lyne renowmed great encrease mighty kynge called pallamides kinge naulus son highest borne blode duke nestor full famous knighthod xii warde ladde grekes syde melancolyke surquedous pryde kinge honux son one maberte fyelde hym selfe aparte ordre hadde wardes thyrtene proudly musterynge endlonge grene agayne troians redy fyght pand eke kinge vlyxes hight ladde fourtene rede pand eke humelius kinge lede fiftenth mine auctour writeth thus pand duke called curibulus sixtenth gouernaunce daye knightes king prothesylay assygned great ordinaunce enforce theim vengeaunce vpon death worthy kinge hector slayne grekes ariuinge pand kinge rodus ladde seuentene kinge occymene pthe eyghtenth warde ledinge zantipus lyde kinge kepe committed garde grekes syde xix warde pand twenty mine auctour lerneth v kinge called amphimacus like kinge guyde theim wysse philoctetes kinge larysse one twenty ladde eke reade two twenty hadde king diomede pand eneus kinge cyparye whylom noble worthy thre twenty gouernayle troians proudly tassayle xxiiii swerde spere shelde pking prothecatus lad felde pand carpenor carpedye kinge werre expert right wise workynge fiue twenty riche well besayne grekes syde brought playne pthe syxe twenty sothly laste could se afore caste euerye thinge good inspection wise kinge great agamenon prudent werriour ordayned emperour grekes hoost wysest echone pand wise forth grekes gone felde pompe full royall thensignes token marcyall haue take grounde passingly araied theyr standerdes richly tho displayed brode baners many freshe penowne againe winde ye made hidous sowne right dredfull playnly heare men sawe many cristes cleare many tufte golde syluer shene meynt fethers red whyte grene deuises wonder meruaylous folkes amerous token borne shewe openly loue brent inwardly high empryse daye fulfylle herde loude noyses shryle ferre felde dreadfull sownes trumpettes claryownes kalendes bin sheding blode noise almoste rage wood fomy bridelles mouthes blede furious neyhing many bastarde stede ppraunsyng horse vpon eyther syde ensygnes might pryde grekes partye troye also knightly wise haue ado euery warde standing place pthe first asunder lytell space began approche ful entent hector tho ful vnpacient formest syde troye yre man might accoye lyke lion hungry rage yssued furyous vysage towarde grekes mighty stede sporres made side blede knightly herte inly toforne mortall yre rode forne brenning full hote melancolye whych thinge whan grekes gan espye ppatroclus withouten abode surquedrye afore wardes rode toforne hoostes syght encountre playnly might worthy hector whan sawe fer lyne right dyameterre rode vnto hatefull tene spere sharpe grounde kene throughout shelde tho enuyous rage smote hector without domage except onely head stele afore whet forged wele plate mayle mightly gan glace skinne nothing might race albe came wt passing violence yet hector done hath none offence saddell one flytte though sturdely hitte might backward bed bow chine partye make encline pbut fatally confusyon mighty man troian champion ire aye brenning vpon hate aye fret sore left spere mine auctour wryteth thus sworde rode patroclus auysed fully shall dead furiously gan aymen head roue downe maner let brest bassenet sayth guydo great payne stroke parted twayne mortall swerde whetted kene patroclus myght sustene vpon horse fell downe grounde caught last fatall wounde pbeyng present knyghtes euerychon delyuerly vpon anone worthy hector stede adowne descended like wood lyowne hatefull yre brenning fyre hauing hert inly great desyre spoyle armure anone full many riche stone ruby saphyres ynde dayes playnly finde kinges lordes knightes naye battayle went best araye sothly hector whan first gan se multitude stone perre patroclus oryent sheyne vpon arme hinge horse reyne meane hole entente catche praye diligent couetise theyr alder syghtes ptyll king meno wt thre thousad knigh armed stele rounde sodaynly vpon hector fall dead corp patroclus saue purpose hector may haue lybertye riche kinge spoyle caused hym angre boyle king called menon irous wood sayde amonge echon oh gredy liowne oh wolfe rauinous oh hatefull tygre passing enuyous aueryce oh beast insaturable desyre sothly vnstaunchable pvpon praye thou shalt ye fede go elles sewen thy mede trusteth well conclusyon fyfty thousande thy destruction one entent playnly fayle thine hatefull pryde attones assayle sodeynly speres sharpe whet euery halfe gan besette maugre force might manhode enforsyng theim reue stede sothfastly great violence constrayned strong defece sayth guydo fall vpon kne might magnanimite manhode hath horse recured maugre grekes ferre assured strengthe great might recured like worthy knight stede agayne amiddes foen right lyne rode kinge menon full desyrous auenged furye hasty cruelte therupon set hole delyte mortall cruell appetite sothe slayne anone saue kinge called glaco came rescue kinge theseus sone hight archilogus haue tolde menon reskewe thre thousande knightes gan sewe full assented attones battayle life death hector assayle awayte vnware set al whyle euer met sworde killed bare downe fynally gayneth raunsowne greke durste mete went felt full vnswete phe made waye aboute euery fledde death feare rode made patth ful plaine reade patroclus agayne repeyred spoyle might amid felde grekes syght would praye lightly lete till idume mighty king crete two thousande cladde plate mayle worthy knightes hector assayle while inly desyrous haue tolde spoyle patroclus newe agayne confusion like finde came king merion hector might theim take hede force reft hys stede sothly none boote compelled fight foote knighthod herte resumeth wt swerde consumeth withstande horse man furyously troian knight began armes legges shoulder bone hewe amid mortall fone grekes might afore sustene reade slewe fiftene theim busy take slaught gan among make ne durst abyde afore face pand merion selfe place meane toke vp patroclus heuy cheare face full piteous stede layd beforne tente anone hath borne alway grekes cruell mode hector furyous wode felly abode fyghting vpon fote felt full vnsote presumed vpon presse manhode ne woulden cesse beset rounde euery side hauing trust great pride fynally mischiefe take dempt might escape handes shortly none aduenture stede lyklyhede recure force casten let attones gan set specially amonge theim euerichone finde sothe one grekishe knight right worthy fame pand carion playnly name enforced hector oppresse whan mischiefe distresse beset grekes enuyroning tyll fortune aye awaytinge longe daye fell fight rescuse came troian knighte midde grekes whan beset hent two dartes sharpe kene whet furiously fyrst shoke toen ye herte smote carion darte felde gan glide playte mayle throughout outher side fatally deadly wounde caryon glode anone togrounde amonge hundred knightes ferys afore conspyred fell chearis haue slayne hector maner waye eft agayne yonge knight troye full delyuer raughte another spere cast one sawe yfere auaunce selfe hector felde plate playnly shelde line right ne asterte might roue herte pand hast coude vpon troians gan crye aloude enhaste theim knightly succoure worthy hector stode aduenture amonge grekes hauing refute sole selfe helpe destitute whych crye grekes vnware pfyrst came worthy cincibare brother hector borne baste ridinge selfe tofore haste ye knightes tho guyde wonder proudly pricking syde sodaynly together one froshe grekes fall hector rounde beset aboute manhode great route enbushed theim backe thre hondred knightes yt spacke astoned gan theim withdrawe thurty first cruelly slawe maugre theim hector manhede amid felde taken hath stede entred amonge prees daye knighthode pereles helde blody sworde hande tho felde agayne stande helpe playnly rede brake karfe two threde knotte cruell attropos onely let purpose leyser spoylen patroclus therfore ire wood furious full cruelly grekes quytte mede whiche face faste gan spede whose sharpe sworde bathed theyr bloud dyed red dyd hym good vpon tho auenged daye lyon played vpon grekes manhode haunte pryde mortally gan daunte hym fledde rode makyng hote streintes bloud endlonge renne shede vpon ye grene ptyll tyme duke great athene called whylom menesteus thre thousande knyghtes full famous lorde guyde fyelde hath take vpon lefte syde deceyte full secrete wyse pwhere troylus ye folke frise whiche hath daye lyste seke knighthode kylled many greke lyke tygre gredy praye troylus bare hym longe daye sleynge grekes many worthy knyght whyle busyest fyght pagayne foen kyng antipus kynge hyght alchanus vpon grekes ylyche freshe newe making side blody hewe one assent thre mahed specially vpon bay stede euer troylus rode euery greke sworde abode sodaynly made sterue plate gan depe kerue pand continued tyll duke meneste troylus sawe great cruelte slaughter grekes made hasty yre face pale fade phent spere threwe rest troylus smytte euen amydde brest sternely maugre renowne earth anone bare downe myddes mortall foen cruelly hym besette anone hym treyne layde hoke lase rounde maner compase spere darte swordes forged bright hym selfe deffendeth lyke knight great manhode honour auaunce albe lyfe hanged balaunce stode felte full vnswete poynt deth amonge horse fete great awayte duke meneste howe troylus myght haue take mortall hate castynge thought myschyefe take escape nought euery halfe besette sworde spere kene grounde whette alone ala mortally bestadde seased hym forth haue ladde tyll mesers worthy knight troye gan crye stode waye sore abashed ryght furyous wyse oh ye noble worthy men fryse manly knightes aye preued fyelde moste renowmed spere shielde consyder vnto hyghe fame aduert glorye name daye throughe neclygence power myghty vyolence grekes troylus ytake sool fyelde ye haue hym forsake shall rebounde alder shame ye soth greatly blame worthynesse floure betake grekes lacke succoure yf ye taken hasty wreche shameful reporte honour shall apeche perpetually saye therof amys defaute troylus taken whiche named worthy famous worde kyng alcamus melancolye felte herte ryue yre hente spere blyue pryckyng enchasteth might tyll playnly syght busy troylus lede full knyghtly syttyng stede ran one fell downe dead efte agayne pale nothyng redde rancour longer wolde lette greke fyrste mette body smet spere men myght se therof poynt fere brest plate shulder bone ground fel downe dead anone tho forthwith worthy fry came flokmele downe grekes fal myghtely maugre diffence sette vpon great vyolence troylus daunger free knightly magnanimyte maden hym recure stede specially helpyng nede zantipus stronge manly kyng whiche disdaine commyng meneste gan spere grate shielde mayle thicke plate sore smote meneste dead ne armour whiche ire gan tremble tho shake troylus handes take escaped prysoner dispyte berde maugre power wherfore gan hasty hote enuye knyghtes furyously crye mighty renowmed stronge payne venge wronge vpon troyans mete face pand hast gan mightely enbrace sharpe speres grounde byte felly foyne together smytte pfor tho began great mortall werre fyre brast shene sterre basenettes plate bryght ye fielde flaumeth ye fereful light lyfe death toke tho hede downe plaine length bredth wardes gan proudly auale lokes ryght enuyously pale aproche assemble yfere hate brennyng man may stere gan hurte spere sworde darte mortally vpon euery parte slaughter gan greatly rewe ylyche alwaye newe newe hector grekes worthynesse rode manly dyd oppresse mercylesse slowe bare downe without excepciowne furyously routhe see pand new duke meneste repayred full enuyous herte hondes troylus sterte slaughter eke meyne rode busy slee troian people whan myght mete tauenge nothyng wolde lete tyll casually amonges prese pa knight mette hyght myseres whyche dispyte meneste rescuse worthy troylus maugre put hym praye befell selfe daye mete agayne aduenture meneste cote armure marked hym armes bare sodeynly ware might taken hede furiously mightye stede spere amyd renges bare hym ouer made hym fall mauger might earth adowne pand fynde howe kynge hupon descended storye lyste lye two thousande knyghtes companye whiche grekes felly gan sette ye berde kynge prothenor mette archelaus noble werryour boece lorde gouernour helpe onely prothenor lyke tygre wood bore gan troyans assaylen deth many one selfe daye sleeth kyng hupon chyualrye full fell tyme melancolye full many greke gaue dethes wounde thus gan eche confounde mortall hate amonges tyll fortune knyght pollydamas pon troye syde sonne anthenor knightes hym selfe tofore grekes right enuious pryde amyd wardes fallen syde gan breke knightly disseuer againe whose sword might perseuer inly furyous pand helpe came kyng remus wynge parte breakyng many spere darte agayne grekes thre thousand knightes beholde felly fyghtes sothe vnto troye luste heauenly aioye see grekes brake asondre noyse loude thonder fyelde stroke gan aryse pand remus ye haue herde deuise vpon grekes enuyous fyelde came menelaus worthy knightes spartense agayne remus maken resystence full proudely makyng delaye worthy remus kynge menelaye horse backe sharpe speres whette amydde fielde byn together mette manly prowesse renown horsebacke eche bare downe none stroke tho might shone whyle anthenor sonne pollydamas lusty freshe lyght delyuer myght desyrous honour attayne mette fielde neuewe heleyne mighty duke called mereus flouringe youthe ryght vertuous freshe armed newe lusty courage sothe twenty yere age whyche yonge noble knight right renoumed bothe herte might fortune befell ala troian knight dan pollidamas spere throughe shelde maile plate hytte hym cruell fate amonge grekes fallen downe dead whiche thyng menelaye toke hede sawe hym lye slayne grene herte remembrynge quene quene heleine neuewe dole full delyuer pa remus rode cruelte also ferre might se full knightly mette berde smytte sharpe swerde vpon head hatefull tene stede might sustene wounde passingly mortall stroke perillous fall knightes wende dead pand hent vp began fle troye warde great pase pbut befell pollidamas maner theim behelde made theim repayre knightly felde except bidding hadde worthy remus home troye ladde pale dead woundes wide tho came grekes syde pcelydys lusty freshe kinge dare sayeth wrytinge sothe boke lyst tell celydys excell beaute semelyheade shape porte goodlyheade surmounting dare list descriue fayrnesse tho time alyue limmes compact clene rede yonge freshe quene feminye beaute floure kinge celidys loued paramoure vpon hooly plesaunce printed remembraunce chiefe resorte sothly herte vpon eche houre aduerte fynally departed nought day night houre thoughte fully owne knight pbut fortune lusty freshe light smote stede sharply syde surquedrye proudly gan ryde mortall hate full furyous pase right lyne pollidamas spere made flytte sadell tho sytte marked great might eft ayene noble troian knight pollydamas despitous face celidys departed fro place swerde smyt heade stede fell downe deade grekes great confusion tune fierser lyon hector grekes knightly gan enchase oft made theim lese place euer rode necessyte afore swerde made theim fle suche vengeaunce hath theim take felde fayne forsake pursewe would neuer fyne till amonge people salomine hector met worthy kinge famous lorde hight thesalus many troian daye yslawe hector towardes gan drawe kynge tenter eke grece also manly knight prudent two raught spere haste vnwares hector ran shelde plate mayle stele speare head forged wele sharpe square kene ygrounde hector gaue perillous wounde hector tournen gan stede proude center aquite mede full wysely haste myght ryght ferre seuered syght wherof hector melancoleous herte wood furyous akynge wounde grene haste tauenge constraynte tene greke shortly mette bolde waye sette without mercy death anone read encountred one whiche pryde purpose wolde diuerte sworde roue herte herneys melancolye whiche stroke whan grekes gan espye astoned one entencyon peryllously sette hym enuyron suche assaute gan aboute hym make though manhod might take accorde great multitude cruelly gan include lykelyhode mortall stryfe myght escapen lyfe hym fell enuyous tyll kynge whiche hyght theseus grekes syde onely gentylnesse suche routhe caught vpon dystresse se hym stande nye vpon wrake thus vnto hym manly pety spake oh flour knyghthode rote hardynes welle manhode stoke worthynes whylyst ye haue none aduertence thy lyfe saue knyghtly prouydence wylfully drede thy lyfe iupardest take lyste hede mortall peryll howe thou art besette amonge many closed yshette alone ala deuoyde socoure thy selfe wylte fauoure fortune lyketh ordayne euery wyght ought complayne beholde suche worthy knyght whiche world cast clere lyght worthinesse wyll withdrawe reklesly day thus slawe pyteously thy persone lese withdrawe thy hande yet syth yu mayst chese thy hygh prowesse compelleth preye suche myschefe thou ne deye pand whan hector hym gan take hede thanked hym goodly hede maugre sothly power myght grekes lyke worthy knight eft scaped mydde foen went way euerichone blody sworde alway honde waye pollydamas fonde full lyke man busy payne defende selfe agayne kinges twaine menelay thelamonius vpon full furyous wt spere greke thelamowne pollydamas smote earthe adowne compellyng none bote agayne theim two fyght eu fote assented fully wroke fyrst haue hewen broke mighty charnelle bassenet whan vyser smet face naked bare fell hym mortall snare haue take storye deuyse sent forth full cruell wyse towarde grekes many worthy knyght whan hector therof syght sawe myschefe pollydamas caste fully socoure case prycked wooder lyon rode aboute hym enuyron swerde made large space tyll came selfe place amonges grekes furyous wood pollydamas selfe tyme stode socourles deuoyde remedye tyll hector caste eye grekes made hastely withdrawe thirty fyrst hath slawe seuered maugre pryde tofore sworde durste abyde agaynst hym make none obstacle knighthode hyghe myracle pollydamas myschyefe fyrste awhaped grekeshe hande frely escaped pbut freshly tho kynge epystrophus menelay thelamonyus knyghtes togyther hole close agayne troyans getten alose new entred battayle great strength passynge apparayle mightely troyans compell waye dare dwelle notwithstandyng great worthynesse hector knightly hygh prowesse fought manly tyme read cowardly haue slayne stede constrayned fyght fote many greke felte full vnsote none aboute hym stode swerde ne shadde bloud though thycke layne voyded made space playne compasse rounde behynde eke afore fete well hath hym bore day greke none certayne hardy hande hym layne stronge sturdy wall whan brothern called naturall sawe hym fote amyd foen frushe fell euerychon founden hym story maketh mynde deffende selfe tygre doth inde helpe high renown fallen fyrst kyng thelamowne hector cruell founde gaue hym many blouddy wounde tyll one named dyndaron hath ferre amonge renges gone bore hym manhead hath wonne passyng myghty stede pand brought hector sothly stode amonge grekes bathed bloud whiche haste ful knightly strode amonge lyke mar himselfe rode full many greke makyng sterue sworde whetted karue daunted hath enuious pryde tyll deyphobus entred syde fyelde knightly chere hym brought many good archer boeme whiche arrowes kene fethers pecock freshe shene vpon grekes haue fyelde recured shotte muche assured mayle thicke plate stele perced haue harneys euery dele pand deiphobus full lyke manly man kynge tentran horse backe tho ran furyously gan swerde enbrace wounded hym euen amyd face vyser felle tene horse backe myght sustene thus grekes troyans yron agayne hath fielde ywonne yrons wood theseus full knightly withstode knightes ladde pand read hector brother hadde story sayth hyght quintilene yonge freshe lusty armed bryght shene whiche kinge called modernus proudely falle vpon theseus twayne togither assent falle hym great aduisement fynally vnhappy chaunce knyghthode broughte hym outtraunce cast shortly shalbe dead whose purpose hector gan take hede vnto gentery myght loude gan crye besechyng nothyng deye lowely byddyng dyd obeye withdrewe vengeaunce hector fully remembraunce theseus daye tofore towarde hym goodly hym bore whan hym sawe mischyefe dystresse knightly thought quyte gentilnesse lyke longeth euery gentylman pand theseus full lowly tho began thanke hector escaped pbut kyng thoas tho hath faste yraped fyelde knightes many specyally calydony pcame phyloctetes myghty kinge also agayne troyans haue ado fyrst thoas spere ran pfuryously cassybellan one sonnes kynge pryamus gaue hym tho wounde greuous without recure fell downe dead whiche stroke hector gan take hede herte gan death complayne haste dyd busy payne brother auenge myght many one made lyght knighthod horse backe sothfastly went wrake grekes syde came waye worthely bare hym daye ptyll duke nestor entred fyght fyue thousande stele armed bryght agayne troyans grekes socoure hym mette auenture pthe kynge esdras mighty bolde kyng phylon chare golde worthy noble chyualrye agresta came iaconye kynges sonne lande full renowmed worthy hande semble together ran tyme many worthy man hath loste lyfe vpon eyther syde slaught large woundes wyde soyle bodyes laye dead lyke ryuer ran streames red cheres grysely pale fade bloud men might go wade ancle slaughter huge pand kyng phylon socour refuge vnto troyans bare hym stryfe many greke made lese lyfe day well sworde whette vnwarely sore besette multytude grekes rounde aboute lyfe playnly stode doubte lykely myght escape grekes shulde anone take ne helpe worthy iaconye esdras loude gan crye ala quod routhe pyte pworthy phylon kyng shall taken amonge grekes necligence haste ye diligence rescue noble worthy kynge attones without taryinge maugre tho maden resystence grekes swerde myghty vyolence haue rescued noble kyng phylon large gone escape wonder gladde lyght pand hector many lusty knight retourned deiphobus also pollydamas many mo troyan knightes desyre newe causen grekes sore rewe assent fully purpose suche mischiefe grekes enclose might fewe shulde escape therupon knightly shape began freshely assayle fielde grekes gan faile power lese lande fynally mighty hande force troyan knightes grekes maugre mightes brought day confusyowne pbut menelay kyng thelamowne sawe febly apeyre knyghthode made repeyre lyke men haue selfe deffended tyll eneas troye descended ewfremus duke manly man knightes newe began efte agayne grekes oppresse hector aye worthynesse lyke lyon sterne face euer one gan enchace compelled great necessytye echone afore sworde fle constrayned ryght nede whiche thynge ayax gan take hede herte great compassyon se slaughter confusyon grekes syde guydo maketh mynde gan loke backe behynde sawe many warde stode abrode many baner penowne abode amyd fielde hole broke redy attones wroke nede troye towne whiche wardes without excepciowne hole floure grekes chyualrye pto anone ayax gan hye herte sore agreued crye hath commened haste theim comen reskuse amonges reffuse fast gan assemble noyse horse earthe gan tremble furyously together flynge might men stroke heren ringe speres sharpe harneys borne sheldes wrought stele horn brest sturdy square brode pand fynde ayax rode pto eneas also great enuye atwyxe theim two death might ire apease herte nother might haue ease tyll speres sharpe ground whette horse backe togyther mette copyng sore haue hytte eueryche earth smytte beholde knightly syght bothe foote fyght lyklyhead tho theyr wood rage fall full great domage amonge horse bycause stode vpon soyle ouer spredde blode pbut phyloctetes ayax come hath vp amonge horse ynome knightly fought made memorye sothly elles troians victorye fyelde playnly sayne tyll philoctetes wardes twayne euen face manly theim withstode spere fyrst hector rode vpon shafte fynde brake sothly vpon horse bake kept well fell stroke remeuinge sturdy oke sat sadell vpryght chine wyth spere ryght lyne body depe shyelde philoctetes smote fielde lyfe hys knightes doubt pbut tho came great route pkynge humerus vlixes eke brought many worthy greke ten thousad knightes manly men echone gan troians assayle anone cruelly euery halfe certayne multytude haue theim belayne dispayred disconsolate longe fyght waped mate gan withdrawe faynted battayle eke theyr horse sothly gan fayle theyr syde went vp downe pbut parys tho troy towne entred ful manly wyse fyrst mette kynge fryse vlyxes nye allye parys smote great enuye hym slewe wherof grekes sore abashed wyth spere pvlyxes rode auenge might fyrst parys syght brest gan spere throwe fynally bare lowe fayling parys sothely reade vnder slewe mighty stede maugre grounde gone would haue fall anone pbut troilus tho mette berde furyously sharpe swerde smote vlyxes throughout viser lyke condyte small ryuer downe face bloud streames ran vlyxes tho lyke manly man stroke astoned stede stiffe wall swerde mightely gan race vmber troylus face gaue large mortall wounde stroke passingly ioycounde grekes supposing theyr thought troians fynally brought vnto outtraunce sothly hadde saue hector wt knightes lad parys deiphobus al brethern knighthod famous troylus also laste wounde alway noble knight yfounde one ioyned one vpon grekes sodaynly gone pand worthy hector alder fyrst began grekes enchase afore ran like beastes fledde fro death euer one thus killeth sleyeth mette durst stroke abyde foen freshe woundes wyde slaught made alway renewe thylke daye blody rosen hewe hath theyr plate harneys steined thought bloud heaue rained soyle redder might tho ben aye ylyche swarme grekes flockmele fledde way guydo sayth ylke daye hector formest playne frounter grekes layne behynde knyghtes garde lacke hym warde wherfore sought full longe grekes sawe new wexen stronge knyghtes agayne repeyred whych theim selfe greatly dispayred absence tho se full inwardly recomforted glad hert haue theyr lorde receiued theyr gladnesse hath perceyued pspake vnto theim full affectiously lykewyse prayed theim full beningly remembre knyghtly herte consyder wysely aduerte first wronges grekes haue yore ago ouermore also grekes daye victorye farewell aye honour glorye troyan bloud conclusyowne fynally eke towne shall mortally tournen ruyne honour wont shyne throughout world worthinesse eclipse shall tournen dercknesse ye daye lyke men quyte wherfore praye man ne atwyte hygh renowne cowardise sette vpon full manly wise spare dread death praye pand echone full lowly gan obeye desyre withouten longer tale entryng certayne vale vpon grekes worthy knyghtes folowing hector sodaynly fall full mortally ware hector tho greke would spare euery theyr confusyon killed slewe aboute enuyron knyghtes riding side made theyr foen maugre pryde lese lande flewe sighte ptyll kinge ye thoas hight grekes syde inwarde gan dresse newe fulll knyghtly gan oppresse troye knight manly pthat afore slayn cassybellan one sonnes king pryamus rode fortune fell thus brother frushe mette assent enuyron besette sadell many greke beheld amonge horse smyt felde rente first basenet cruelly head smet vnarmed myschief stode psaue duke furyous wood athene riding tho great pase reskued mortall case knightes rode helpe without abode spere sharpe whet kene pfyrst fell quintiline busy thoas haue slawe bretherene made also withdrawe whan quintiline horse throwe pbut parys drewe vp mighty bow duke let arowe glyde plate hit side vpon rybbe made sore blede whych stroke ne toke hede bycause onely feruent amid foen helpe thus kinge thoas amonge horse bore grounde poynt death many mortall woud onely naked head duke fully deuoyde dread knighthod perillous case amid foen hath holpe king thoas lyfe made scapen fre hector aye cruell enmitee iliche freshe nothing would leue vpon grekes manhode preue enforsing destructiowne pand rode amonge theim vp pkinge humerus hath bowe take shote gan redy make hatefully therin set arowe hector marked hath narowe smote euen amid face might ferther pace hector smyt great payne wt swerd roue head atwayn pthe death grekes know mine auctour saith haue horn yblow vnwarely dreadfull sowne seue thousad knight came one adowne hector without abode force theim rode maugre theyr might tho withsette slowe tho way lette would stynt playnly tyll came father worthy kinge pryam many worthy full famous renowne wyth knyghtes fast towne laye daye men horse foote knighthod crop roote kept close full high prudence tyll hector came vnto presence besought great nede thre thousand would spede vpon grekes theyr full rage fall theim auauntage haste worthy priamus knightes freshe desyrous towarde grekes hath waye ytake mordre gan vpon theim make many grekes laye dead playne pryamus hath theim sore belayne euery halfe great might full fast fledde syght sore newe vpon theim sette pand fynde tohether mette phector ayax cruell auenture stedes stronge wonder sure storye sayth haste konne lyke wood lyon together ronne great might yt lefe lothe vpon playne vnhorsed bothe pand whyle menelay kinge sodaynly camen ridinge slewe troye worthy admyrall thus slaughter passingly mortall renewed aye celidonas neuewe slewe kinge thoas mada met mine auctour writeth thus grekyshe kinge called cedeus wt swerde stroke sette ye vmber eye smette pand sardellus troye eke whyle slewe worthy greke lorde name high prowesse although guido name doth expresse pand also came margaryton troye side agayne thelamon two inly set fyre high disdayne hatefull yre met horse backe yfere kinge thelamon sothly lere gaue vnto deadly wounde cruell pbut tho came troian phanuell prothenor smote downe stede thus sone playnly reade pryamus nothing nat dismayde grekes haue euery parte outrayed knightly daye theim borne many greke fatally hath lorne life sothe hate enmyte kinge anglas fall meneste athene duke gouernoure spere yre olde rancoure ran smet tho amyd shyelde al sadell yet helde pand duke spere none swerde anglas rode anone yt owmber roue nigh nase astoned stode mase sawe condyte blode streame rode asyde fully deuoyde feare vnto time staunched pbut deamor owne brother deare behelde mortall blody cheare pof high disdayne rode meneste vnhorseth vp anone sterte might fully vp aryse another brother full creuell wyse fall thre attones weten vpon meneste fully purpose shall lese lyfe knightly bare stryfe agaynst theim wonder se vpon cruell theim thre one thoas eldest echone sleye busy euer one broke haue basenet pbut tenter sawe beset grekishe kinge made mencion herte great compassyon thought playnly manhode releue might fomen greue nought busy payne hector tho fallen twayne pvpon tenter meneste pand theim slayne ne ayax vnto hector faste gan hye thousande knightes companye withstande meneste saue handes might haue pbut parys tho king perce fiue thousande reherse worthy knightes many troian mo vnto hector one ygo thryfty wise cydyng rowe parys made trumpet blowe whych came knightly enbattayled many troian full well apparayled whych fielde hector conueyed one herte fully haue obeyed vnto bydding troian knight freshe newe begyn fyght vpon grekes ferre forth slayne many manly man aye slaughter pyteously reneweth many greke sore herte reweth theyr great losse destructiowne wrought vpon theim troye towne specially hector finde whych day dare maketh minde hande thousande knightes slowe neuer adawed sowe greke none dare waye dwell wt swerde coud theim compell lese theyr grounde necessyte lyke shepe afore wolfe fle pand reade amiddes victorye hector hath met vnder tentoree pamonges grekes mereon kinge spake without tarying oh thou tratoure thy houre aprocheth faste thou art come sothly thy laste thy fatall daye hath course yronne truste well westrynge sonne caste platly quyten thy mede swerd haste thy bloud shed thou bolde daye disturben ryche praye spoylyng kinge patroclus cause thou presumptious disturbe thou shalt anone deade downe sterte smote first head pand spoyle also gan haste pbut meneste came faste whan behelde trauerse backe wt spere lacke smote great violence without syght aduertence worthy hector takyng hede wound sore gan blede went made faste bynde pand meneste stale away behinde purpose sothly maye mete hector ylke daye pbut ybounde sore wound staunche blede furyous erst tofore repeyred angre al tore aye yre herte fret bare downe euer met slayth kylleth mercyles tho put theim selfe prease hardy wyth hym mete boke lyke wryte darete sothe storye sayth men may gyuen fayth full credence possybylyte guydo clearly ye may se caught latter wounde fynally grekes confounde affermed certayne thousand knight wt hande slayn without theim tho spake rathe newe alway gan swerde bathe grekes bloud sodaynly ouerlayne cruelte greke none high low estate ne awhaped amate knighthod manly excellence none maken resystence vtterly durste take hande daye hector wythstande pand made also mencion thylke daye kyng agamenon sayth guydo came felde cause great presence withhelde grekes syde al goeth vp downe hector playeth wood liowne theyr tentes fledde socours troye proudly victours sewed theim trace theyr bloud wan treasour great good spoyled theim full great dystresse armure theyr richesse fell theim ware home troye good bare fynally daye wyth myschaunce grekes brought vnto outraunce without recure sothe euermore euery parte belayde sore manhode hector ye mighte helpe many worthy knyght felly agayne grekes wrought mischief playnly brought ne theyr owne pyteous slouthe pryde onely folye routhe theim theyr volunte daye euer soneraynte recured theyr hygh renowne lordshyppe theim dominacyowne whych shoulde haue laste continuall victoryously perpetuall haue endured saue cruell fate redy aye fortune debate agayne thynges gynne wilfulnesse make theim fine aye wretchednesse theyr enuyous disposytion sodayne chaunce reuolucion vnware tourning false whele wyll byde thinge wele ala freyle deuoyde sykernesse cause dimmed dercknesse hath troians false opynyon yblinded theyr discrescion specially fordercked syght worthy hector prudet manly knyght se afore shulde sewe good aduyse mischyefe eschewe folowed theim backe behinde ala wilfully made blynde daye sytten softe victorye hill alofte ne could neclygence se fall theyr felycite put abacke theyr aduertence lacke reason high prudence hap haue voided theyr grace presently set afore theyr face man commendable fortune fauorable blandeshing forhead cleare smyle plesaunt cheare onely fauoure helpe oute myschyefe beset aboute refuse hap wylfulnesse fortune auoyding vnkindnesse whan ministreth grace another tyme shall embrace whan hath nede helpe succour catche fall rather ingratitude frowardly mowes delude whan best weneth stande sikernesse fortune aye full brotilnesse remouable ready flytte pher welfull houre yt lyst admytte fauour allyed another time shall denied leuest finde fauorable houre sothly fable vnto man graunteth desyres thousande yeares peraunter one condescende vnto lust sende pa hath fall daye vnhappely worthy hector wilfully wrought head grekes spare fatally snare theim lyke conquerour victorye tryumphe honour might haue brought thrugh hye renown palme conquest troye towne daye refused folylye pfor rode hector cruelly amonges grekes slowe bare downe casually mette thelamowne meane ayax nygh allye hate cruel hote enuye hector rode lyke wood albe full nygh bloud yet yonge lusty knight dyd power full myght without fayning haue borne hym downe whose father hyght also thelamowne hym begat storye telleth v eryon syster pryamus ayax flourynge yonge age freshe delyuer great courage sette hector knyghtly hygh prowesse met theyr woodnesse theyr stedes manly champyons eueryche lyke tygres lion began fall proudly assayle furyously seuere plate mayle first speres longe large rounde afterwarde swerdes kene ygroude fyghtyng thus longe contune tyll befell case fortune token sygne apparence nature kyndly influence whych hertes doth full depe myne namely theym borne one lyne whych cause peraunter twane naturally theyr rancour restrayne theyr yre modefye onely nygh allye vnwyst therof vnsure tyll taught onely nature naturally bloud wyll aye kynde drawe vnto bloud may fynde whych made hector kyndely aduerte meued stered herte knyghthod gentilnesse whan ayax sawe worthynesse pspake vnto full beningnely sayd cosyn saye trewly thou lyst grekes forsake come troye dare vndertake thyne allyes thy kynrede thou shalt withouten dreade full well receyued partye theim blode royall sothly decended hyghest degre ryght shall suffyse vnto kyndely great plesaunce repayre vnto thyne allyaunce gentyll herte sythe nothyng good confedered owne bloud conceyue thy worthynesse whych nature doth kyndly impresse troian bloud thou art descended whych grekes longe hath offended wherfore reade leue theim vtterly aunswered agayne full humbly sythen byrthe greke youthe among fostred eke tyme natiuitye taken ordre degre knighthod eke amonges theim aforne ouer bounde sworne trewe theyr nacion making bloud none excepcion swore would conserue beheste hector made requeste manfull gentilnesse would knyghthod worthinesse shewe vnto hym great affectiowne make theim troye towne onely withdrawe grekes pursewe theyr tentes make theim remewe resorte agayne vnto towne knighthode routhe compassyowne without assaylynge anye affraye made grekes ilke day sythe vnto theim ought ynoughe suffyse fielde knightly wyse manhead fully possessours theyr fomen fynally victours like tofore fully defyned whose request hector enclyned ala hasty wilfulnesse made anone without auysenesse amydde fielde trumpet blowe wherby troians fully mighten knowe wil shulde withdrawe custome playnely lawe vsaunce nyghe ferre amonges experte werre whan moste feruent fyght vpon grekes preue might chaced lowe stronde weake power withstade troye one desyre gan sette shotte wylde fyre brenne shyppes high mischauce fynally put outtraunce pand trouth ne hector vpon routh makyng troyans repayre ayene towne vngraciously confusyowne story shall specifye tho put ala iupardye lyfe death whiche elles might haue sure whiche againe shall neuer recure phow grekes suite opteyned kyng pryam trewce eyght wekes battayles trewce ended capitulo xxiii haue matter complaynen sore fro daye farewell euermore laude victory fro towne denyed disposyowne mortall fate whiche contrarye matter lyste lenger tarye troye entred citie shet gate suretie daye lyke made mynde thus ende guydo fynde wende haue done peraunter best pand sonne ygo rest toke ease ylke night tyll morowe tytan clere bryght shadde beames hemispherye makyng daye shewe merye whiche tyme troyans anone right hole lusty fyght gan arme theim purpose full daye foen mete platly maye hole wyll playne entent eke commaundement tofore hector redy make slepe morowe whan wake whiche thynge neclygent pryam grekes haue ysent messangers day pryme take trewce onely tyme eyght wekes whiche pryamus hector wyll story telleth thus hath graunted auctoritye wyse citie whiche tyme whyle leyser haue grekes gan burye graue bodyes afore slawe lyke rytes paynem lawe might busy cure brent sepulture enclosed lyke estate thus helde feast funerall fro day day duryng aye peace pin whiche space fynde achelles patroclus death hath sore playned teares rayned inwardly loued hym herte anguyshe cruell smerte longe abode lamentacion dyd make great affection large toumbe remembraunce myd fielde tho vsaunce amonge grekes great reuerence lyke honour excellence pof royall burying patroclus ygraue protheselaus toumbes korue marbyll graye nye together playne laye werke rychly ywrought earth together brought solempnely lyke obseruaunces rytes circumstaunces grekes vsed sothly tho dayes fro poynt poynt longeth layes suche estate royall holden feast funerall two whyles trewse doth laste pand troye busyed full faste might bufy eure grene hurtes woundes cure aduyse surgerye full well experte shapen remedye swolle sore soften payne space monthes twayne restored helth euery thynge whiche time priamus kinge psuche sorowe made cassybellan herte wyght ne hym recomforte heuinesse day day inwarde tendernesse full pyteously gan sobbe wepe pand body made kepe aboue earth certayne space tyll chosen worthy place burying sepulture guydo v fully doth assure pin venus temple ryche shryne made men toumbe myne marbell greye metall rychely whiche put full solempnely dead corp cassybellan beinge present full many manly man phane cytherea whiche thynge cassandra within selfe consydered behelde sawe vp offred helme eke shelde sworde also vnto mar stede inwarde wo felte herte blede heryng noyse pyteous crye tender wepynge sorowyng vtterly troye lamentaciowne frend throughout al ye towne gan make slawe afore sodeyne rage herte tore inwardely might restrayne furyously crye complayne sayde ala full ofte welawaye poh wofull wretch ye daye vnhappy eke graceles also infortunate inly wo bego ye may suffre great harmes kene whiche ye lykely hereafter sustene duryng syege towne belocke seynge foen redy wroke aboute beset euery syde venged great pryde wote ryght well ye may eschewe ne shall vnto death pursewe euerychone besyeged place without mercy rewth grace ala ala wyll ye besy ye wofull wretch shet cite grekes seken peace sworde vengeaunce mercyles hygh lowe execuciowne noble worthy royall towne euersed ybrought nought lyst ye consyder thought modres child smale stretes shall face dead pale lye murdred grekes cruelte yonge maydens captiuite wepe shall myserye wo seruitute towne also famous ryche ala pyte grekes fyre shall destroyed shorte tyme sothly heleyne v ala bought dere syth sake shall euerychone poore ryche exceptyng neuer one ende make wofull pyteous yre shalbe furious vpon v none meane saue onely death v go betwene pthis noise pyteons crye cassandra dredefully gan make aboute euery strete ye towne euer might mete lyke mynde tyll pryamus faste made bynde shytte vp routhe harde albe sayd trouth pfor neyther wysedome discrecion counsayle wyt prudence reason trouth rede withouten lye spirite trewe prophecye auayleth suche sapyence place audyence man inly neuer wyse counsaylyng hyghe deuyse workyng outher eloquence eche thynge se aduertence falle afore reason amyd eye discrecion yet dole without fauour holden fole vnfauoured wisedome vayleth nought neyther trouth dere bought cassandra wyse rede dispysed taken hede troye confusyon cruelly ythrowen pryson whyle wyll lette dwelle grekes forth wyll telle fyrst pallamydes gan grutche agaynst yt chese beyng absent kyng agamenon haue lordshyp domynacyon namely syth worthy suche dignite gouerne great myghty hoste throughout world come euery cost kynges prynces worthy renowne therof indignaciowne pand sayd himselfe poustee amonge grekes greater degree concludyng maner weye power ne wolde obeye peace werre subiection syth ne election platly affyrmyng thre whan chose kynges degre thurty tyme absent whiche swore entent accordyng opynyon pin wyse agamenon grekes shulde haue suche gouernaunce plo myschyefe lyeth varyaunce amonge lordes whan accorde drawe fully one corde enuye cause suche dyuysyon couetyse domynacyon eueryche wolde surmounten felowe cursed vyse often hath withdrawe hap grace many regyon whan discorde false discencion allyed ben hertes stryue among lordes kingdom may thriue tyll reformed agayne peace amonge selfe playnely lease whyche thinge grekes token hede thought good ferther procede matter pallamydes ymeued amonges prese wyt set quyete made rancour lete accorde fully herte nowe must style agayne dyuerte vnto werre telle maner trewes mette yfeare lyke storye maketh mencion worthy kyng great agamenon trewes passed ygone haste gan ordeyne anone myght waker dylygence deuoyde slouthe neclygence sette wardes full auysely pand achylle full prudently fyrste warde comytteth lede seconde vnto diomede thyrde also kyng menelay fourth daye phe meneste duke athene lodyng stele armed clene wardes folowyng agamenon kyng full manfully ordeyned hath shall procede worke dede full circumspect werre peace pand worthy hector reckles sette wardes towne knightly wyse discreciowne troylus yonge freshe lyght fyrst warde many lusty knyght hath assygned wardes set prudently ne myght bet forth hast hym lyste longer byde many worthy rydyng syde gate went towne towarde grekes troyan champiowne fyrst whan sawe fyerse achylle ne coulde lenger kepe hym styll smote horse felly syde towarde hym cruelly gan ryde whiche thynge dispyteous eye whan achylles sothly gan espye agayne hector manfull hardynesse herte enuyous gan stede dresse fyelde together mette rounde speres poyntes kene whette encountryng knightly excellence eueryche great vyolence force bare vnto grounde full ofte happeth founde whan stronge doth mete peregall eueryche fall hector fyrst strength assured stede agayne hath anone recured lefte achylle tho gentilnesse great hast forth gan hym dresse amonge grekes rode kylled slewe hym stode wt sworde made woudes wide brest side perced hath waged euer sheltrous brake made disseuer herte thought good hath sworde grekes bloud continued tyll achylles caught stede agayne amonge prese entred amonges troye swerde made large weye sleeth bare downe yt euer met none hardy hym lette tyll befell melancolye phector mette rydyng sodainly sawe eche come ferre without abode eueryche caught spere ran together reste pbut hector fyrst smette brest spere playnely tale shyuered peces smale achilles necessyte grounde goth wolde none vnhorsed earth laye hector haste may enforced hym catche stede many greke great nede came rescue achylles loue put selfe prese thrugh help horse doth attaine enhastyng al might payne auenged great iniurye sodeynly wood furye sworde ful sharpe ground whette phe smote hector vpon basenet sadell made hym remewe whiche stroke might eschewe noble worthy knight force great myght maugre foen sadell hath recured manhode assured sodeynly herte wexed wroth arage achylles goth sworde smyt head basenet bloud red face gan ronnen downe lyke ryuer chekes enuyrowne hym selfe deffendeth knyght tho newe began cruell fyght atwene two se wonder euery stroke great dent thonder range eyre none wolde spare soth fyght fare lyke wood tygres bore rage sterne bulles whan sauage semyd sothfastnesse two full worthynesse contune longe fyghtynge endure tone cruell aduenture must haue dead necessyte whiche thyng great petye bycause worthy knyghtes bothe whyle fyghtyng fell wroth busy grekes tho begyn wardes entre troye storye maketh mynde partye lefte behynde fyelde enhaste euerychone knightly wyse mete fone prease also yonder knyghtes two seuered sonder pand tho came sterne dyomede knyghtes whiche dyd lede full lustly selue place hath mette proudly face worthy troylus horsebacke neuer yet manhode lacke countre storye doth v lere eueryche vnhorsed knightly hath feare pbut fyrst horse recureth dyomede haste gan spede tassayle troylus stondyng vpon foote sawe none bote knightly yet dyd erst man agaynst hym deffende tho began dyomede hote fyre wonder enuyous hatefull desyre sworde rancour none ryche cercle full inde stone tyme troylus basenet full cruelly hath raced smet troilus nolde wtdrawe hym deffendynge hath stede slawe whiche sat tyme dyomede mauger must alyght nede whan fote twayne dyd myght cruell payne eueryche assayle swordes sharpe plate mayle gan seuere sonder race wood lyon mortall chere face tyll grekes stronge stoute felle myne auctour boke telle haue might caused dyomede sodeynly recure stede troyan knightes tother syde haue troylus brought stede ryde pand horsed two without efte togyther go stronge foynes yfeare ran eche felly tyll laste cruell dyomede lyke ye may myne auctour rede case hap aduenture whiche man fully may assure fortune false vysage tyme troylous avauntage hym fallen myschyefe whiche thynge hym reprefe though toke amonge great aroute euery halfe grekes set aboute syth doubtous euer fyne fyght vp derk bright wyght may aye vyctoryous peace werre ylyche eurous let euery man syth hap sette doute take tourne commeth aboute though troylus take diomede tyme shall quite mede storye telleth place dyomede lyttell space troylus ladde forth prysoner reskewes stele armed clere many troyan came pryckynge nede maugre myght dyomede troylus haue handes take tho began slaughter sake euery halfe wonder telle troyans grekes felle pthan fyelde entred menelay whiche troyans ylke daye full busy auenged cruell enmyte pand whan parys sawe hym fyelde towardes hym ryght waye helde purpose wardes sette eche tyll together mette tho skyrmyshe slaughter gan outher parte many manly man pand whyle hector ne wolde cease amonge grekes cruelly prease new new hym read alyke freshe bloud shede sworde trace ysene grekes ne myghten sustene resyste stande afore face rode aye gaue place ptyll knyght whiche boetes hyghte yonge age whan syght hector slewe grekes mortally euery syde hauynge mercy preased encrease name perpetually purchase fame furiously herte aferde caste platly mete berde whiche thynge hector gan aduert hyghe rancour enbraced hath herte sworde indignaciowne rofe hym euen nauell downe fro crowne great payne fyelde parted laye twayne hector tho assygned hath stede squyer bad shulde lede troye towne without abode furyously rode amonge grekes euer mercilese slewe tho put selfe prese shedde bloud herte despiteous whiche thynge kyng archylogus rydyng besyde sawe gan espye boetes cosyn allye cruelly hector slawe towardes hast gan drawe vpon death auenged rode great cruelte fully purpose hector quyte sodeynly gan hym smyte hector vnwarely hyt head myghtly fell downe dead parted two cruell aduenture notwithstanding mighty stronge armure agayne stroke deffence geuen suche violence holpe hym maner thynge pand anone prothenor kynge hatefull yre fole hardynesse surquedye hastinesse melancolye indignacion caught herte presumpcion assayle hector warde folyshe pryde goth attrauerse syde furyously dispiteous herte commonge might aduerte onely came backe behynde vnwarely guydo fynde hector smote horse grounde muche manhod foude anone knightly herte without abode sadell sterte ryght fyersely prothenor purseweth fynally hande escheweth sworde marked hym wele basenet breste stele twayne without fayle roue downe paunce mayle fell downe full pyteous wise whych stroke grekes sore agryse pand specially hardy fierse achille behelde lyked full yll pfor prothenor nygh cosyne descended lyne death hath heuynesse inwarde thought great distresse worlde ne wyst much payne wo death archilogus auenge full desyrous herte many waye caste wardes gan seke faste many greke hector haue fall conspyred fully sothe amonge theim one entente hector assayle nought would auayle daye cruell rage might haue none auauntage troian knightes fauour fortune vpon grekes mightely contune thrugh conueyeng hector might anone haue put theim flyght theyr tentes maugre stryue pursuite forwouded driue laye swowe many greke merciles slowe longe daye till drewe nyght sothly lacke lyght troians knight ful worthy renowne aboute hector repayren towne entre honour glorye daye grekes hauing victorye thus leue theim towne within forth grekes tel begyn vvhan hesperus faire bright sterre agaynst eue hath caste streames fer west rathest gan appeare whan twylight pale cheare maner morneth thabsence sonne night aprocheth coopes dunne time titan toke leue clerkes call crepusculum eue whych elles meane lyght phebus absence dercke night twylight hatte meane daye night departing theim betwene fully nother ymeynt heauen clustered depeynt bryght sterres eueninge whyche tyme agamenon kinge lordes sodaynly hath sente come echone anone tente assembled yfeare tryst heuy ruthfull cheare gan ye slaught hector complayne affirming playnly ne maye attayne vnto victorye alyue wherfore gan conspyre blyue death many sondry weye echone concludynge whyle troy lykely grekes wynne alone within chiefe deffence protectiowne soueraynly vpholder towne mighty castell stronge wall vnto grekes deadly foe mortall ne myght great force endure neuer aryght agayne foe sure standyng hole sayde degre whyle floureth felycitye wherfore echone one entencion condiscende conclusyon slyght awayte lyinge whan moste busy fyghtynge amonge myschyfe distresse achylles busynesse might vnwarely hym assayle hym slea nothynge fayle pand grekes gan prayer make achilles vndertake empresse fynally suite manhode execute hasty deth mortall foe achylles without wordes mo request assenteth perfourme luste gan hooly hym confourme tyme lett hym beware reade hasty iourney spede vpon hector power kythe lest fortune awronge face wrythe loke wyth frowarde cheare brynge vnto handes nere sorte hap hector folylye put lyfe death ieopartye lest vnto happe euen lyche fall selfe dyche hector compassed hath shape wonder escape sith hector without dreade brennyng yre great hatrede achilles death puruey hym founde place saye conuenyent execucion trowe gayne raunson mede herte quyete onely death mete ende fyne mattere boke ye shall heare thus grekes made haue ende theyr counsayle anone wende eueryche theim home theyr lodgynge toke theyr resten till morninge phowe troians toke kinge thoas prysoner led captiue troie ca xxiiii vvhan aurora syluer droppes shene teares shad vpon freshe grene complayning aye weping sorow chyldrens death euery somer morowe saye dewe soote enbawmed hath floure eke roote lusty lycoure aprill maye larke messenger daye custome aye aurora doth salue sundrye notys sorow transmewe phebus ryse ioye gladnesse hermonye leue heuynesse taking leue sainct iohn borow time grekes morowe lusty herte early aryse armed theim theyr best wise theim caste daye gone felde mete fone pand hector hath morowe also cast fully grekes haue ado yssued knightly troye herte hath great desyre ioye daye grekes fyght wyth ladde many lusty knyght cyte borne forthe rode selfe aforne pand eneas many worthy folowed wonder fast pand paris next deiphobus pand syth troylus coragious wardes made troye towne dare maketh menciowne within boke troye syde fighting men yt went ryde hundred thousande armed go felde fyfty thousande mo haue theim cast daye eue one entent grekes greue pand mette strongly syde gan assemble together ryde full cruelly great hatrede theim tho paris lede entred full mighty stronge archeres perce lande many arbalasters theyr arowes filed sharp roude wt quarelles square whette ground full many greke hath reued lyfe amiddes mortall stryfe pagamenon felde come towardes hector hath ynome right way threwe stede amonge knightes lede spared nought great prese pand therwithall anone came achilles awayte hector tho layne sodaynly might payne phector smote head sore wt ye stroke mine auctour sayth basenet bowed ycrased pof stroke hector amased achilles shuld anone yfall ne eneas knightes worthy troylus come go betwene twayne swerdes kene gan achilles felly assale hewe playtes perse mayle tho began slaught euery syde men foote theim ryde plike condyte woundes ga blede whyle cruell dyomede hap aduenture case rode mette wyth eneas ryght anone founde smet hym gaue wound lykly recure therto better cure pand therupon full despyteously thys diomede melancolye repreued hath troian knight enee sayd hayle thou art whylom gaue pryamus kinge fell counsayle hasty bytynge haue slayne sodayne violence last troye presence trust wel haue well minde amyd fyelde eft fynde thou shalt thy counsayle mortally repente fortune hereafter assent brynge aryght vnto hande good leyser thine owne londe pi full sette thy laboure quyte trouth swerde shal kerue bite kenely thy troian bloud shede fynally death shall thy mede beare atwene twayne wt word might restrayn diomede rode sodaynly vpon enee tho furyously smote hardy cruell knight payne great myght horse made fall maugre myght knightes stroke lyked full yll pand hector hath achylle assayled basenet perced hath swerde smet hath narowe brought ye poynt hye mychefe suche disioynt constrayned hym necessite hym take ne sodayne rescue thys chyualrous pthat called sonne tydyus meane fell fyrse dyomede achilles hath holpen nede force armes twayne smote hector tho great payne gaue wounde full greuous nothyng mine auctour wryteth thus astoned knight manly man swerde haste smote diomede furyous wrothe horse earth gothe pryde surquidrye pthe anone troylus espye without abode downe stede alyght dyomede foote fyght eche theim sothfastnesse aquyte selfe lyke manly man nother muche lyte degre manhode wyte pand fought hector achilles togyther mette agayne amonge prees ran yfeare fyersly theyr rage wood lyon ramage right sothe faired fighting tyme menelay kinge full proudly shope troians mete pvlyxes eke also pollymete came neptolonyus ppallamides eke scelemus pduke meneste nestor thoas pcurrynulus phyloctheas pand theseus made mynde knyghtes proudly came behinde pand partye theim towne came kinges without excepciowne assembled ffence agayne grekes maken resystence except knightes yt hector ladde wardes made hadde daye sayeth latin boke knightly wyse fyelde yt toke tho began fell mortall fyght daye ful many worthy knight fate handes fynally fall fortune amonge wardes pagamenon noble mighty kynge sodaynly came rydynge ppantysylaus waye mette agaynst anone horse sette full knyghtly rode agayne mette sayne horse backe while wrothe violence vnhorsed bothe pand menelay parys mette newe whych two well togyther knewe full desyrous eche dere pbut menelay caught fyrst spere hytte parys wyth busy cure surenesse stronge armure mighty plate woude small effect greued stroke vnto grounde gothe whych fall parys wexed wrothe wonder confuse also red shame lest reporte hinderyng name came eares quene heleyne daye might atteyne menelay holde chaumpartye lykly sowne vnto vilanye whych herte greued full sore adrastus kinge withouten rode kinge vlyxes fonde knightly fought hode hode fought downe earth lowe horse vlyxes hath throwe ful proudly sygne victorye sente horse home tentorye pand tyme amonges prese pfull sodaynly kynge pallamydes fall hupon locke hore yre wounden sore fell dead grouelyng ye groud mortall swerde kene ygrounde besyde neptolonius assayled hath kinge archylogus whych selfe manly gan defende faught many stroke spede diffence would none eueryche theim hath vnhorsed pand tho came riding stede ppollidamas gan taken hede amonge renges lytell besyde kinge pollamides doth ryde fiersely tho full lyke manly man smote stede ran maugre might worthinesse storye playnly beareth wytnesse onely venge death kinge hupowne stede proudly bare downe rancoure cruell hete despyte gan rehete pand tho besyde kynge scelenus deadly hate herte full yrous kinge carras aduenture hath met furyously stede hym smet pand also kinge philomene duke fall athene maugre manhode might hath horse berafte fyght lad proudly syde lyst shoulde abyde pand philoctetes worthy kinge also selfe tyme remus ado euery sothly reade felowe made voiden stede pand theseus king strong amid fyelde rode amonge great prese hathe met curyalus worthy king knighthod famous two armes wonder stronge theim selfe fought leyser longe til eche woundes freshe grene felowe threwe horsback ye grene afterwarde fynde two vpon foote knightly ado armes inly desyrous manhode passyngly famous pand whyle sonnes naturell pryamus bare theim wonder well amonge grekes vp downe ryding prudently together abydynge made slaught grekes full pyteous kinges duke lordes right famous reade worthy thelamowne tyme mette kynge sarpedowne theyr speres squared full sharply eueryche hath wounded mortally shelde plate haberion mayle storye maketh rehersayle harneys wexed bloud red fell almost bothe dead great myschyefe amonge horse fete whose bleding soyle gan wexe wete theyr harneys gan destylle while kinge thoas fyerse achille kynne allyed pamyd fyelde hector haue espyed faught beset amyd foen vpon one accorde gone mortally would auayle euery halfe gan newe assayle hate herte borne yore haue beset troian knight sore ala head hath smet violence ryche basenet wounded felly head ne toke none hede worthy man floure chyualrye defending tho myghtely pkynge thoas smet face wyth stroke rafte nose two shorted halfe dele whych stroke brother naturele manly hector fast gan theym hye succoure first espye great myschyefe theyr coming manly bare theim fightyng pagayne grekes ye thoas haue take thelamon made wake newe assaute sharpe woundes kene take lefte vpon grene men borne home tente pand kinge thoas home troye wet maugre grekes may hi helpe deiphobus also anthenore haue sent forth troye cyte pand menelay tho began se pso rode parys stande asyde shope shorty hate cruell pryde would fallon chaunce sodainly giuen mischaunce pbut ware kept self narow pthat menelay marked arowe head wt venym enoint intoxycate square poynt king dreadfull wounde dispayred men founde whych great haste bare tent anone surgyens hath sente fyrst head toke wounde albe yperced full profounde harneys depe bone cunningly theyr craft echone drawe instrumentes subtylly certayne oyntmentes serched haue wounde enuyron make cleane corrupcion prudently first token hede venum nat procede rounde compasse clensed aboute bounde sure without defensyues made euery syde menelay longer would abyde bad haste bryngen forth stede pin purpose full parys quite mede finde selfe daye lyst longer put delaye euer fall grene wounde forth rode tyll hath founde aduenture vnarmed fyelde without swerde pollax spere shelde bowe hande recklysnesse refreshe werynesse pand menelay spere anone hath take yre felly gan shake towarde parys great auysenesse shoulde haue slayne lyklinesse ne eneas whych thinge beheld bore stocke stronge shelde defende auenture destytute naked armure pparys tyme suche peryll wherfore haste hath eneas ordayned knightes armed bryght stele paboute parys kepe wele myschyefe confusyowne hym conueye vnto troye towne right despyte kinge menelay awayte parys laye pwhom hector ytaken sodaynly vnto troye ladde hym vtterly ne grekes come defence agaynst maken resystence pof hector came weye full many greke made deye remnaunt put vnto flyght mahode yt day might troians made grekes fle vnto tentes necessytee theim sewe ne would neuer leue slee kill tyll drewe eue phebus gan faste weste drawe home thought best tytan goyng downe whan gan entre troye towne gat shet lodging wende daye thus made ende tyll morowe rowes red phebus carte gan ouer sprede afore vpryste oryent tyme king pryamus hath sent wyth pryue counsayle inwardly secre pand specially sent name pfor worthy hector ye greatest fame pfor parys eke deiphobus pand troylus freshe desyrous pfor anthenor pollidamas pand troian called eneas daye cast gone felde mete foen paleys come lordes haue right waye ynome vnto kinge within closet vssher dores shet eueryche lyke degre place take dewe see worthy kinge made mencion gan declare hertes mocion meninge afore theim specifye sayd syres affye pto knowe ye king thoas cite taken prisonere yet belocked prisowne whych euer hath vnto troye towne enemye great vnto power v offended aye ferre nere many wise albe lytell retche ferre force might stretche wt grek came besiege town willeth destructiowne therupon hath busynesse wherfore dome rightwysnesse reason equite saye playnly semeth vnto acceptable ye thynke counsayle comedable like hath cast death shape holde rightfull escape death receyue guerdon ryght requireth also good reason death death skilful guerdonning vnto witte right well syttyng psay aduise playnly case pand fyrst tho spake eneas sayd lorde none offence highnesse gyue audyence thrugh support full wyse shall reherse playnly deuise worke mattere semeth fyrst lyege lorde deare noble royall excellence consydre shoulde full high prudence euery worke operacion caste afore conclusyon fynall ende may sewe wyse man onely dewe se gynning ende nought attones peysen thought weye theim iustly balaunce fine ensewe repentaunce saye platly meane ye ought sene kinge thoas one pryncipall amonge grekes yt bloud royall ye consydre descended lyne wherfore haue thus foule fyne slayne whyle pryson happen might conclusyon ye therto assente afterwarde shoulde sore repent pi preue thus aduenture fortune rule man may assure lordes another daye grekes take happe maye sonnes full worthy renowne kinges towne trusteth well suche lyke gentylnesse ye theim shewen distresse quyte case semblable fortune theim fynde fauorable man constrayne may binde wherfore lord haueth thing mind pfor yf thoas shorte auysemente shall dead hasty iudgemet another daye grekes wyll v acquyte rygour make malyce byte euer nother spare high lowe degre though peraunter bloud thinge worldes good might fall ye ne would se wherfore reade let kinge thoas honestly kept presowne like estate still towne lest sayd another daye lorde happe maye casuelly take auenture eschaunge ye might best recure without
