stryfe owne man agayne matter sayne fynally full rede pto counsayl hector toke good hede according reason commendeth opynion pbut pryam euer one entencion stode alway fixe conclusion playnly affirminge greks may espye kinge spare gentrye arrecte cowardyse anone dare venge v foen dread hauynge none hardynesse herte nother rightwisenesse yet neuerthelesse assente shall lyue wyll myne entente desyre fully condescende pand counsayle made end without saue eneas ygo pand troylus eke anthenor also hall excelling beaute quene heleyne purpose se eke hecuba quene ladyes goodly sene many mayde yonge lusty worthy troylus eneas labour busy payne comforte fayre quene heleyne stode werre dreade womanheade thilke time herte entere well could made theim good chere hauinge conninge iuly suffysannce cheare dalyaunce hecuba beyng hall example vnto woman bounte hauinge soueraygne excellence wisedome eke eloquence besought theim tho wonder womanly counsayled eke full prudently haste nigh ferre auysely kepe theim werre ieoparte theyr body folyly aduerte caste prudently diffence knightlyy towne theim gouerne discresciowne spake fayth could nothing feyne heleyne toke leue longer dwell went waye forth tell phow grekes morowe amonge selfe complayne make sorowe harmes great murmur rage losse costes great domage haue endured folylye lastynge werre wisten neuer whye death slaught many worthy man dead sith yt werre began hunger thurst watche colde also full great vnreste sorowe thought wo together thinge nought sothfastnesse grounde sought noyse rumour eke ran throughout ye hoost yt day man amonge pore souldiours bare bronte euer shoures mischiefe werre comonly though plain haue remedy sondry thinges sit theim full vnsoft thus grekes complayned haue full ofte many mischief hath theim fall might haue eschewed ne foly gonne werre grece nat come halfe ferre mischief confusyon daye lamentacion pwhich encrease nexte night derked without sterre light cloudy blacke thicke ayre dimmed skyes foule nothing fair windy eke tempest belayne almost drenched smoky rayne felde astoned yonder sodayne stroke dreadfull thonder opening hidous leuene semed high heauen cataractes hadden vndo cloudes skyes two sodainly wexen blake like goddes would haue take wrake newe assented one lande drenche deucalyon world without refuge ouerflowe freshe deluge winde also sternly gan blowe tentes standing rowe forpossid ybeten downe furyously confusyowne flod raught stading place bare theim forth fro then large space wherof myschyefe great distresse great laboure hertye heauynesse grekes bydde nyght tempest lacke lyghte tyll floude gan agayne withdrawe wynde appease day gan dawe heauen gan agayne clere without cloudes freshly appere phebus eke feruent hete soyle dryed vp wete moysture enuyrowne playne grekes tentes sette agayne adawed nyghtes sorowe apering glade morowe arayed nothynge peace fyelde fyrst went achylles ye shall entencyowne daye fyght wt troye towne vvhan dryed lusty large playne wt pheb bemes ye haue hard sain troian knightes full worthy renowne descended ycomen downe fyelde toke fyghtyng place achylles mete face tofore went lyke tolde lordes knightes bolde fyrst fynde without abode vnto hupon furyously rode meane hupon stature lyke gyaunt bokes v assure achylles sharpe spere body perced fere fylle dead wounde kene kynge octamene fyersly hector wolde haue gone without abode hector hath slaine anone cruelly quytte fatall mede sodaynely agaynst diomede pa zantipus worthy kyng gan drawe full pyteously hym slawe ryght anone kyng epystrophus eke kyng hyght cedius one assent proudly battayle begonne hector mortally tassayle spere fyrst epystrophus ran hym herte despyteous guydo also doth deuyse rebuked vngoodly wyse hym sore herte meued wherof hector furyously agreued hath mortally wounde made large hym ne geyneth plate shelde targe fell dead amonge men echone hector bad shulde gone furyes depe downe helle suche proude wordes amonges tell quod men take hede thus whan waged mede panone brother called cedyus suche sorowe made epystrophus hertye dole wofull chere pytie se inwardely death thought thousande knight yt brought auenged manhode despyteously hector fall hym founde fyghtyng wt foen force th euerycone sore enuyrowne haue beset fro stede downe haue smit pwhom cedyus aye cruell rage whan sawe ouauntage hector vnhorsed stede sworde lefte inwardly hatred markynge hym great payne force armes twayne fully purpose withouten delaye slea hector playnly maye stroke descende myght downe hector hate indignaciowne sworde full sharpe whet shoulder hath arme smet reuyd hym lyfe eneas amyddes stryfe came rydyng ryght wood furious mette kyng amphymacus fell slewe hym rage grekes holdyng passage pthere discended fyrst menelaus pand kynge thelamonius pthe great duke also athene moche manhode sene vlixes eke cruell diomede eke also helpe nede came kyng machaon alderlast great agamenon wardes fell sodeynly vpon troyans full manfully diffende selfe agayne grekes proude put full knightly coude eche sothly mette spere sworde enuyously sette mortall hate betwene whan sonne merydyen mydday angell passyng hote shene grekes gan felly tene myghtely falle troye made geuen weye force necessytye pand achylles full cruelte amonge renges gan hym drawe kyng phylem enuyously hath slawe pand amyd grekes time hector maugre slewe kyng alphenor pand eke kynge called dorius cruell irous vertue knyghtly honde troyans wonne haue agayne londe vpon grekes made flee pand thylke houre troye cite epystrophus full manlynesse felde haue take worthinesse grekes proudely none knightes fauleth attones seuered made twinne gan fyelde fast vpon wynne phauyng tyme companye amonges tho dyd guye pa certayne archer whiche fynde monstruous wonderfull kynde myddell vp vnto crowne man remnaunt downe bare horse lykenesse fygure horse heire monstre nature skynne growyng enuyrowne full rough thycke voice ye sowne lyke neyhynge horse reade though face length brede shape mannyshe yet sothfastnesse colour semblable lykenesse vnto fyry hoote brennyng glede whose cyen eke flawmyng also reade blase ouen mouthe syghte vnkouth soeuer met berde man horse sore ferde face hatefull odyble loke hydous horrible aye custome vsaunce bokes made remembraunce go vnarmed fyelde without sworde spere axe shielde nothyng coulde myster fynde good archer bare bowe styffe wonder stronge also tyller longe arrowes lyke tyller bushment trussed wonder ner syde aye ready hande outher sea lande fynde none armure agayne shot playnly myght endure horse stede couser durst abyde nouther fer ner fledde anone full myght fast hym syght passynge odyous lyke deuyll monstruous founde none hardy knight horsebacke force might holde horse whan myght hym se anone backe wolde flee archer fynde wryten eke day slewe full many greke wounded arrowes kene throughout ye plate forged bryght shene none afore hym abode tentes faste away rode myght hydous loke endure tyll befell wonder aduerture whyle troye helpe archer sewe chase lodgyng ner slewe mischiefe dreade pbesyde tent mette hym dyomede archer necessyte stode ne myght hym flee maner way backe remewe lyfe deth myght hym eschewe many troyan tho backe flyinge go wracke pwherfore anone worthy dyomede cruell herte faste gan hym spede towarde proudely dreffe archer great aduysenesse fyrst arrowe smytte dyomede thrugh harneys made blede whiche stroke wexed wood wroth monstre hydous loth went pase hym vnarmed fonde yt sworde helde honde gaue hym laste fattall wounde fell dead grouelynge vnto ye ground death grekes reioysynge haste hertes resumynge began selfe recomforte fyelde proudely resorte pby conueyinge policenare worthy duke well hym bare vpon troyans day fyelde whan hector slaught behelde vpon duke anone gan sette stedes fyersly mette phector hym slewe full great hatrede gallathe stede rode forth amonge prese ware mette achylles speres longe large round purpose fully eche confounde ran yfeare yrous right wrothe stroke vnhorsed pbut achylles dispyteous herte fyrst reade sadell sterte busy inwarde peyne gallathe taken reyne therof euer hector depryue bad men lede home blyue hector none bote full lyke man faught standyng fote amonges grekes fomen knightes loude gan call stede shulden sewe haste horse rescue ben attones fallen vpon achylle pand maugre force agayne haue hym berafte plaine vnto hector restored agayne knighthod moche self assureth dispyte sadell recureth whiche afterwarde full dere aboughte lyke lyon day wrought amonges rydyng death fled sword fere whose manhod troians efte begyn vpon grekes fielde agayne wyn pbut befell amyd great fyght anthenor certayne troyan knight amonge prese fer ygone grekes take anone tentes sent haste albe sonne called pollydamas rescue hym dyd dylygence manfully neclygence founde hym lyste seke full dere bought many greke day worthynesse cause onely derckenesse gan drawe towarde nyght made ende onely lacke lyghte grekes went home lodgyng eke troyans tyll mornyng pthat pheb gan bryght beames shew aurora newe gan dewe herbes sote grene leues hayes freshe greues syluer bryght rounde perles fyne clerely agayne sonne shyne shewe selfe oryent shene hylle vale euery grene rody morowe tyll hote beames bryght phebus fyry stemes vapoureth vp moysture ayre wether cleare agreable fayre attempre also hete whan troians caste mete fomen platly maye went beste arraye wardes fyelde rowe pagaynst grekes slowe shope forth without longer lette tyll togyther manfully haue mette speres swordes clere ran together dispyteous chere tyll shyuered sonder many spere sheldes stronge selfe ryuen peces many targe ax rounde brode large basenettes tho smyte shrede full many knyght mortally gan blede sothfastnesse tell day slayne many man outher parte troye towne albe guydo maketh mencyowne person specyall nouther syde generall saue concludeth playnely fyght lasted fro morowe tyl nyght troyans haue ful dere abought day fortune holpe nought tourned hole confusyowne repeyred towne tentes grekes fast spede ptill morowe senten dyomede vlixes troye cytie trewes onely monthes thre kyng pryam therto wolde assente two message wente certayne knyght borne troye towne hyght dolon great discreciowne also ryght famous rychesse curtesy gentylnesse deuer dyd diligence conueye vnto presence pof pryamus paleys royall sea chyefe pryncipall satte lordes enuirowne many knyght full worthy renowne gan hym fyrst specyfye hooly substaunce embassadrye trewes theyr entent tolde assent wolde kyng benyngnely herde aduyse prudently answerde thervpon honour saue good leyser wolde counsayle haue lordes fully hym gouerne matter lyke discerne pand conclude shortly euerychone assented except hector alone vnto trewes wolde denye hector sayde trecherye onely slaughter false treason axynge vnder occasyon fyrste burye grekes dead vnder coloure therof dread afterwarde selfe vyttayle well knewe stuffe gan fayle enfamyned leste shulden dye sought space selfe purueye outwarde sygnes dyd espye wherfore quod lyketh lye apparaunce dare presume whyles waste thus consume oure stuffe within dreade wyll prouyde yt haue nede auauntage myght v hyndryng damage whyles encreasen amende shall store discrease dispende yet neuerthelesse euer touchyng trewes monthes thre sythen ye assent accorde sentence discorde wyse varyaunt thus trewes confirmed graut outher syde thought beste bycause shulde quyet reste meane whyle ease releue felte woundes sore greue myght leyser haue sore recure yt meane trewes thus endure fell treatee communyng pof anthenor thoas kyng anthenor delyuered shulde kyng thoas troye cyte pand thoas shuld grekes home againe enchaunge ye haue herd saine one accorded pand ye troian byshop calchas remembred hym vpon doughter dere called cryseyde eyen clere troye lefte behynde whe went thense bokes maken mynde felte passyngly great smerte tenderly sette herte enprented eue morowe chiefe cause grounde al sorowe lefte behynde towne without comforte consolaciowne caste sothly absence specially great offence hath wrought agaynst troye hym thought shuld neuer haue ioye tyll doughter recured hath agayne pwherfore calchas story sayth certaine wyttes many wayes caste best might trewes doth last recure doughter maner waye fynde vpon certayne daye porte wonder humbly wepyng eye wente full pyteously complaynyng teares albe reyned whose inwarde wo sothly feyned knee anone falleth downe tofore great kyng agamenowne besechynge hym humilite mercy hyghe pyte kynges syttyng place haue routhe hym grace wo haue compassyon maye haue restitucion doughter loued praying deuer prudent mediacyon anthenor pryson kyng thoas myght eschaunged lyste benignite requeste goodly assent graunt forth anone sent kyng pryam haue creseyde calchas sake therwith al leyde charge wonder specially went embassadrye pto troye towne kynge pryamus calchas odyus hatefull eke throughout towne reporte vp downe treatour also false worthy enhonged halse treason doublenesse euermore sayd eke expresse deserued hath ryght lawe shamefully fyrste drawe afterwarde moste horryble death may haue yelden vp breth lyke treatour dyspyteous wyse herte thyncke deuyse eueryche affyrmyng iudgement death none fully equypollent deserte falsenesse yonge olde playnely bare wytnesse concludyng eke iniquyte wolde assent degree vnto nothyng myght herte please creseyde hym ease caste make delyueraunce leuer gyuen hym mischaunce hym myght haue good large pbut fynally effect charge ferforth dryuen ende priamus hath grauted shal wende kyng thoas shortly vnto father dan anthenore euer grutche kyng parlement hath thervpon geuen iudgement vtterly may repealed worde sentence assealed must parte eyen glade sorowe playnely made departynge hereafter ye shall whan agayne cometh matere phow duryng trewes iii monthes hoctor walked grekes hooste talke hadde betwyxte achylles hym capitulo xxv truse affyrmed ye haue herd deuise outher syde yt full wise full assented euerychone tyll three monthes comen gone lyke reade certayne daye whan agreable morowe graye blandyshyng pleasaunt delyte hector harte caught appetyte lyke guydo lyketh wryte daye wolde grekes vysyte full well besene wonder rychely many worthy companye suche none chese tent fyrst achylles fynde soth troyan knyght vpon stede hath take weye ryght full lyke man made mencion pnowe achylles great affection herte daye nyght worthy hector haue syght neuer yet none occasyon myght hym haue full inspection hym beholde good lyberte vnarmed myght hym neuer se wonder knightly aswell porte chere mette yfere ryght manly countenaunce laste fell dalyaunce pbut achylles fyrst began abreyde vnto hym euen thus sayde hector quod full pleasynge leyser naked may se syth neuer myght haue syght whan thou armed knyght shalbe full greuous whiche inly enuyous thou sayne slayne anone handes twayne soth hooly pleasaunce cruell death take vengeaunce full ofte werre eke fyght haue felte vertue great myght thy force many woundes kene vpon full freshe byn grene many place shedyng bloud thou furyous wood aye compassynge destructiowne many mayle myne haberiowne thy sharpe swerde racyd hath sonder cruelly seuered yonder mortally sygnes shewe plate stronge persed yhewe harneys forged bryght stele myght neuer yet assured wele thyne yre whan thou lyste smyte thy sworde ne wolde kerne byte fleshe full depe full profounde sheweth yet many mortall wounde body large longe wyde yet appere vpon euery syde day day full sore ake smerte whiche thynge semeth herte enbolleneth newe nowe whan see hyghe despyte auenged fret olde enuious rage may neuer brest aswage tyll vengeaunce fatall sute cruell death execute pand one thyng greuaunce whan haue fully remembraunce mynde consyder vp downe howe thou hast made fynall deuysyowne pof ala hym patroclus yonge manly vertuous loued skylle ryght euen selfe full myght hoole herte inly kyndnesse tongue may telle expresse hast thou made departisyon v hole affection yknyt one hertie allyaunce without partyng disseueraunce entyerly faythfull hertes twayne ylaced locked chayne whiche myght none aduersyte lyfe death sonder twynned tyll cruelly thou madest v departe thrugh hert inwardly doth darte wyll neuer soth thought trusteth well ful dere shalbe bought death hym nothyng perauenture ended yere vpon onely sake cruell deth vengeaunce shalbe take ensure without bonde may lyue myne owne hande shall death execucyon without abode longe delacyon ryght requireth without dreade death death fynall mede selfe theron shall wroke ye world hereafter shalbe spoke achylles venged soe pfor patroclus loued though enuyous thy death inly desyrous ne wete put blame well wotte thou arte hast death many day desyred thervpon inwardly conspyred thus shortely atwene v two death without wordes mo whan fortune lyst tyme thereto shape hope fully thou shalte escape truste none saye vtterly pto hector hastely answerde againe sober countenaunce auysed well dalyaunce nothyng rekles pand euen thus spake achylles syr achylles without fayle thou ne oughtest greatly meruayle though power full myghte herte dewe ryght day day thy death conspyre euer one compasse desyre laboure early eke late pursue full cruell hate thou oughtest wonder wyse fully knowe sentence wyse maner taketh hede ryghtwysenesse may procede wyght loue al myght death purseweth destruction ouer confusyon hath layde syege aboute cyte kinrede also vpon thervpon felly doth presume mortall hate werre consume v euerychone ywysse fynde herte lawe kynde suche one loue ryght equyte haue chere sothly degre werre may frendlyhead debate loue aryght procede pfor sothly loue speciall faythfulnesse hath orygenall hertes ioyned conuenyence one accorde difference doubylnesse may degre nother ioye aduersyte lyfe death asunder disseuer loue contuneth euer pbut hate contrarye whych sothly hert varye procedeth rancoure eye men maye se debate enuye stryfe enmyte mortall slaughter nygh ferre mother whyche sothfastnes werre fyne wherof longe seuereth hertes frendship cutte atwo causeth loue leyde full lowe pbut wil thou knowe thy proude wordes herte thoughte sothe agasten ryght nought shall furthermore breake without auaunt trouthe speake saye playnly hense two yeare maye lyue werres swerde knighthod forthe acheue hope sothe mortally greue grekes maye mete thou shall fele full vnswete ye contynue werres haunte shal pryde surquedrye adaunte suche wise handes two werre fully ado well many greke full sore shall rewe well wote olde newe grekes gathered one surquedrye founde euerychone onely lacke discrescion vndertake presumpcion highe thinge syege layne selfe ouer charge vayne empryses withouten fable byn weyght importable peys great heuynesse fynally oppresse pride auale lowe enclyne burthe shall enbowe backe chyne vnwarely causen fall ye haue done saye one pand ouer full suerte pthou achilles speake vnto fatall deathe first shall assayle tofore thy swerde thynge auayle agaynst thy worthynesse pand great hardynesse courage wyll vygour force myght meue thy herte manhode knyght take derryng darreyne betwene v two thilke quarell befall whych stryue wyll assent playnly ieoparde tyll death one v departe lordes kinges prynces wyll accorde yfere fully one assent holde stable herte entente felde onely v tweyne haue sayde quarell may darreyne ended condiciowne happe thy highe renowue venquishe dryue outtraunce make fully assuraunce fyrst lorde priamus kinge shall vnto grekes maner thinge crowne sceptre holy submitte poynt varye nother flytte fully yelde subiectiowne lordship within troye towne pand lyeges captyuytye shall go theyr waye cyte leue quyte gouernaunce without stryfe varyaunce thervpon make securyte deuoyde ambyguyte tofore goddes othe sacrament shall swore full good entente ouermore fayth also saue assure pledge ye shall haue meane whyle kepe side choyse hostage abyde troye towne worthiest ye lyst chese also beste ye shall nothyng euer saye pand achilles without wordes mo lyste accorde therunto haue sayd thy honour encrease make werre sodaynly cease lykly laste longe betwene troians grekes stronge thou shalt onely wt honour fame throughout worlde winnen name therwithall lyte thrugh thy knighthod many man profite fro death shall escape alyue countre hole sounde aryue lykly cruell aduenture dead werre endure come therfore let prolonged let daye atwene v two ioyned haue sayd condiciowne diffence onely towne haue victorye fortune ouer axe elles anone ye breake vp siege werre lete suffer v lyuen quyete grece home ye gone thinge achilles anone hote yre furyous also brenning full hote anger wo assented despytous cheare pand gan anone hector dresse nere sayd would delyuer vtterly fro poynt poynt axynge therin made none excepciowne hole herte entencion requeste accepted euery dell semed leked right well parte caste gloue adowne sygne token confirmaciowne lyfe death holde daye agayne hector happe happe maye vnto hector lyfely sterte toke vp glad herte euer yet man knyght quarell toke foe fight man sothe ryght deuyse glad high empryse pof whych noyse great sowne ran eares kinge agamenowne anone selfe came tente lordes parliament pwhere achilles hector yfere wytte mattere would assenten fynally put quarell full ieopardy parte atwene knightes tweyn ye haue herde fully dareyne pand one voyce grekes denye sayde nolde suche companye kinges duke lordes eke also bothe life death ieoparte atwene two course fortune theim submitte daye face chaunge flytte troye conclusyowne ieoparde ne wold liues towne handes onely knight put auenture fyght ppryam except whyche sothly case within selfe fully assented playnly put sette ieopardye hooly honour regallye supposynge aye made memorye hector shoulde haue victorye empryse toke hande pbut priam might tho withstande agayne many one entencion contrarye opynion bothe grekes troye syde helde peace let ouer slyde grekes parted echone pand hector achilles gone home troye leue whyle while dyrecten shall stile tell troylus lamentable wo made parte lady fro ala fortune gery vnstable redy aye chaungeable whe folke trust thy stormye face like desyre fully embrace thy ioye away tourne writhe wpon wretch thy power kythe record troylus yt whele lowe false enuye thou hast ouerthrowe ioye whych lady make hym twynne best wende haue sured woe hath endured muste nedely helpe hym complayne whych herte felte great payne inwarde wo great distresse haue cunning expresse knewe partynge creseyd almost wo payne deyed fully wiste departe shal sentence iudgement fynall father gyuen parlyamente wo tourment al rente poynt haue fallen rage man might appease aswage hidde paynes brest ga dare lyke man furye gan fare sorowe daye nyght make complayninge onely sake sawe aweye leuer playnly deye lyue behinde absence thought without presence dead sayne teares gan berayne eyen gan bollen brest sighes tho vppe swollen sobbynge sorowes depe ne rore wepe sore loue herte gan constrayne ne felte litle payne wepte also piteously gan crye desyringe aye might dye rather parte fro troye owne knyght lust lyues ioye chekes teares downe destyll fro eyen teares round drop tryl fordewed haue blacke wede eke vntrussed heyre abrode ga sprede lyke golde wyre forrent torne yplucked sheres shorne ouer freshe rosen hewe whilom ymeynt whyte lylyes newe wofull wepynge pyteously disteyned like herbes april bereyned floures freshe dewes swete right chekes moyste wete cristall water vp ascendinge hye brest heauenly eye aye amonge lamentaciowne full ofte sythe fell swowne adowne deadly pale fordimmed syghte ofte sayde ala myne owne knight mine owne troilus ala shal parte rather let death spere darte herte vaynes kerue rage sterue rather ala fro knight twinne pand wo oh death nilt thou come helpe make ende shulde troye wende abyde grekes gone dwell amonge cruell fone ala ala wofull creature shoulde werre endure wretched woman selfe alone amonge men armes euerychone thus gan crye longe daye playnte full great affray pyteous noyse till drewe night vnto owne trewe knight full tryst heauy came agaynes eue might ought comforte releue pbut sothe hath creseyde founde swowne liyng grounde pyteously vnto wente wofull cheare armes hente toke vp atwene theim two began newe suche deadly wo routhe pyte sene cheare pale grene coloure like ash deade fro face gone red chekes deuoyded bloude wofully atwene theim two stode ne might worde yspeake redy deathe wreke vpon selfe naked swerde besyde full ofte gan grounde glyde armes fell swowne selfe gan teares drowne stille dombe stone mouthe wordes none wery spyryte flykered brest death stode tho vnder reste without maynpryse sothly lyfe thus semed stryfe whiche theim two shulde fyrste ypasse death portrayed herte face coloure men go theyr graue thus wo gan togyther raue disconsolate longe nyght good fayth yf aryght processe hole theyr bothe sorowe made till next morowe poynt poynt specifye longe would occupye euery thynge make mencion tarye translacion shoulde wo procede semeth nede psyth maister chaucer afore matter hath well bore boke troylus creseyde whych mayde longe deyed rehersyng first troilus cotrayre ascende vp loues stayre surquedrye became one compaynye loues folke olde game whan cupide subdued full tame brought lowe subiectiowne temple walked vp downe gynne hooke leyde amid eyen cercled creseyde whych daye might asterte brest perced hath herte went home pale dead wan wise troylus first began seruaunt mayster telleth thus till holpe pandarus whose comforte mediacion boke made relacion great laboure fyrst came grace continueth many yeares space till gery fortune gan vpon frowne fro must go towne sodaynly sythe se lo ende false felycite lo ende worldly brotilnesse fleshly lust lo thunstablenesse lo double variacion wordly blisse transmutacion daye myrthe wo morowe aye fine ala ioye sorowe creseyde kinge thoas anthenor shall forth gon ala vnto grekes euer theim dwell pthe hole storye chaucer tell ye lyst man better alyue processe halfe well discriue englyshe gilt sayes rude boystous firste olde dayes full fer parfection lytell reputacion till came poetrye gan tunge first magnifye adourne eloquence honour laude reuerence throughout lande giuen songe laurer englishe tonge giuen excellence right whilom ful high sentence perpetually memoriall pof columpna cardinall petrack frauceis giuen italye reporte neuer fayle honour dirked name registred house fame amonge highest sete mayster galfride chiefe poete euer yet language name shall pallen none age euer yliche without eclipsing shine parte neuer fine magnifye writinge plianly till dye god praye soule bringe ioye pand lefte wil agayne troye storye tell first guydo within boke thus speaketh troylus rebuking full vncurteysly sette herte folyly vpon creseyde full doubilnesse boke guydo list expresse teares complayninge wordes white softe blandishinge meynt fayning flatterye outward farsed many false lye vnderhid varyaunce cured aboue fayned countenaunce woman falsly teres borowe theyr herte though sorowe lyke would trouthe deye thynke one say serpent vnder floures fayre venym hydeth doth repayre sugre afore galle hydde behinde propered aye vnto theyr kynde dyuerse double nature rathest deceyuing men assure vnder coloure euery thynge werke fayre aboue foule dercke hydde man may espye though wyth wofull eye outwarde wepe pyteously tother eye laugh couertly whose sorowes tempred alley theyr coloure euer meynt rayes vpon chaunge mutabylyte stande hole theyr truste theyr suerte sure doubylnesse alway double theyr sikernesse seminge one best varye lykest corde contrarye thus varyaunt accorde hoolest seme discorde guido sayth fewe none herte apayed one yet one twayne thre foure theyr speche fayne lyke one mo hoole theyr loue well eke wo eneryche shall hym selfe deme next lyke doth seme thus hope stadeth eche theim trewest aye redyest forto fall serueth best next appayred thus chaunge theyr loue fayred let man truste catche maye farewell morow though sure daye fayre chaunge lasteth yeare folye bye deare thilke treasour whyche harde possede flieth away men therof nede yf happe chapman sayth guydo yet daye men maye se sheweth large fenestralles chaumbers high lowe downe halle windowes eke euery strete also eke men maye wyth theim mete pylgramage oblacions spectacle cityes townes sayth guydo selle telle eke sayth sentement fraude fully equypolent fraude sleyghty compassinge woman lyke workyng set faithfulnesse wening theim finde stablenesse shall theim fynde stedfast mone poynt chaunge soone yonge caste rage olde falleth dotage wherfore counsayle bothe two caste brydell lightly let theim go pthis teacheth guido god wote hath delite speake cursedly alway woman throughout boke men maye se lyst loke theim hadde enuye specyall good fayth right wrothe wt al theim lyst debate yre latin translate inwardly hert felte blede high dispite clause rede resowned conclusiowne onely malyce accusasiowne woman full euyll mote thriue generally secte descryue whiche made discrecion good badde none excepcion blame foule mote falle cause one hynder dare well affyrmen rode agayne one bad ben hundred good though one double newe hyndreth trewe example also though shewe one whylom shrewe good take shall hede hinderinge womanheade though twaine thre double faine agayne sothly colayne vyrgyns inly full grace leuen thousande holy place man may fynde kalender full many mayde parfyt enter death stable trewe theim rosen hewe marterdome blysse heauen wonne also bokes telle konne lylye vyrgynyte vyolettes parfyte chastyte ascenden aboue sterres cleare sercle nynthe sphere ioye aye gladnesse eterne wherfore sothe discerne though clerk shrewes haue missaid let good woman therof mispayde lacke one blame eke men maye sayde trewe reprefe though another thefe worse degre though hanged tree vnto woman hinderyng none amonge hundred though yt one gouernaunce vicious agayne byn ful vertuous yf ye lyst thousande ye may fynde though guido write haue kinde double men shoulde goodly take agayn maner grutching make nature workynge hath full great powere harde course holde restreyne guyded reyne coarted dewe righte therfore eche man full might shoulde thanke god taketh paciently yf woman double naturelly shulde men laye theim blame though min auctour hider name writynge onely cryseyde vpon blame leyde counsayle lyghtly ouerpasse myssayth place hyndre woman eue morowe taketh hede let theim wyth sorow passe ouer ye list rede tyll ye come diomede sente troye towne ceryously made menciowne fyrst delyuered pfor anthenor kinge thoas troylus gan conueye many brynge weye pand dyomede waye gan brydell lede tyll brought father tent calchas full good entent receyued lodged laye speche duryng daye maner hole euerydele rehersed ceryously wele troylus boke ye haue herde saine wryte ofte holde vayne pbut guydo sayth longe nyght cryseyde hath forsake owne knight gaue herte vnto diomede tendernesse womanhede troylus herte colde without fyre byn asshes olde none accusacion onely kyndes transmutacyon appropryed vnto nature selde neuer stable endure experyence men maye ofte lere nowe tourne agayne matere must resorte though ferre began wryten werre pof battayles trewse descripcion pallase ilion great pestylence grekes hoste whereby enforced seke trewse whiche vpon suyte obteyned thyrtye dayes capitulo xxvi tyme passed trewse ytake next morow wha tita hath forsake vnder partye hemysperye al night full merye aurora liynge syde bed hym lyst longer byde shope vp caste streames shene pon troy wall whan hector armed clene fyelde faste gan hym hye fyftene thousande companye worthy knyghtes manly men fynde troylus tenne knyghtes eke baner sewe hast parys gan remewe towne perce londe eche mighty bowe honde arrowes sharpe trussed syde knyghtes aboute ryde also thre thousande fynde pand deiphobus next came behynde thre thousande knightes armed clene whose plate sonne shone full shene pand nexte hym came troyan eneas reade sothiy day troye towne hundred thousande knyghtes renown lyke recordeth dare frygyus boke guydo writeth thus pand grekes toforre day seuen thousande goeth menelay knyghtes echone whiche tho dyd lede many went dyomede next seweth hardy achylles mayne called myrmydones pand zantipus worthy kyng eke thre thousand knight wt hym lad fyelde agayn towne alderlaste great agamenowne suche nombre grekes felle wonder heren telle whan wardes felde abrode take place without abode pa grekyshe kyng phillis hight anone hector syght towardes hym syttynge stede spere gan faste spede hector hath commynge sayne hente spere rode hym agayne shyelde plate rounde gaue hym hys laste fatall wounde vpon whose deth auenged full many greke gan hector flee fyrst worthy kyng famous pthat grekes called zantypus hye disdayne onely phyllys sake towarde hector hath course ytake spere ran full ryght hector fyrst hyt suche might harneys speres head zantyhus fell grounde deade death grekes sore coplaine dyd myght busy payne euery halfe furyous wood auenge troyans bloud passyng cruell hardynesse gan troyans tho sore oppresse many one day ne myght asterte brest yperced herte dead slayne amonge prese amonge whiche cruell achylles slewe lychaon eutorbyus noble knyghtes ryght worthy famous ycome countre agayne grekes helpen citie troians costrained narow spere quarell darte arowe hector wounded throughout vyser face lyke ryuer red bloud downe began rayle harneys auentayle wherof astoned whan syght full many troyan toke hym flyght cyte faste gan drawe chase full many one slawe myght efte felde remewe euer one grekes sewe vnto walles almost towne tyll hector troyan champyowne knyghthode gan taken hede albe wounde sore gan blede yet manhode gan recomforte maugre fyelde resorte namely whan inspectiowne walles toures towne heleyne heccuba quene syster fayre polycene many lady gan beholde hym thought anone herte gan colde shame knygytes shulden flee lyke lyon crueltee made theim tourne manly euerychone waye meteth meryon grekyshe kinge nygh allye achilles bookes specifye sworde hector smote bodye clouen hath two achilles sawe deade parted atwo euen fro head het spere thought ne would fayl hyt hector shelde plate mayle rode tho full enuyously myd shelde smet cruelly stroke hector neuer adell remeueth sat faste well swerde anone taryeth nought achylles enuyous thought knyghtly ran vpon coursere creste shone bright clere myght hector hath hym smyt perced throughe basenet raced eke auentayle stroke many pece mayle achylles constrayned nede maugre myght stagre stede enclyne bowe backe whiche tyme hector hym spake sayde achylles well aduerte great enuye thy cruell herte specyally thou haste well ware therfore counsayle thy selfe put farre aduenture one thynge playnely ensure desyre luste daye fyelde yf mete may trust ryght wel gayneth socour ne shal acquyten thy labour mortally vnderstande sworde holde hande thy life thou shalt thes escape cruelly vengeaunce shalbe take efte whan mette euen vpon thy head pof thyng whan achylles toke hede aduertynge herde sayne ryght wolde haue answered agayne pvorthy troylus knyghtly entred made sonder twynne manhode companye worthy knyghtes tho dyd guye hyghe prowesse owne might hath grekes put agayne flyght slayne day dread syxe hundred knyghtes sothly reade losse whyche grekes faste gan flee tentes necessytee tyll menelay dyd busy cure make fyelde agayne recure whose manhode yt day doute worthy knightes fyelde grekes recured anone pbut tho fro troye came kyng odemon hast possyble may came enbushed vpon menelay hym vnhorseth selfe place suche wounde gaue hym face death wende escape doubtles anone hym take helpe troylus lad vnto ye towne grekes suche prese came downe rescue hym great nede pthat odemon myght tho lede kyng menelay towarde cyte whan dyomede came meyne many worthy rydynge hym aboute troylus mette amonges al route sodeynly hap aduenture hath vnhorseth eure anone hent stede bad squyer shulde lede vnto cryseyde onely sake besechynge wolde take gyfte owne man syth day loue wan amyd fyelde great myght hym whylom owne knight haste waye went therof made vnto present pprayinge full humble wyse lyttell gyfte despyse receyue remembraunce pleasaunce pitye womanhede seruaunt called dyomede remembre become knyght anone harte glad lyght full womanly bad hym repayre agayne vnto lord playnly hym sayne ne myght kyndnesse womanhead gentylnesse refusen hym platly grace straunge place kynde founde comfortable euery thynge seruysable may lykely mynde thynke hym true kinde pwith answere messager gone vnto lorde tolde hym anone worde worde lyke hath sayde therof full well apayde hym thought playnely herte recured paynes smerte forth hym armes knyght pbut day duryng stronge fyght troye manly haue borne grekes myght stande aforne tentes haue chased ne kyng agamenowne grekes driuen clene fyelde whiche thyng anon behelde came vpon many worthy man tho new slaught agayne began euery halfe vpon large playne grekes haue troyans laine efte agayne haue fyelde ywon troyans canstrayned tho begon lese lande tyll pollydamas whiche knyghtes besyde gan fall vpon endlonge grene troye full manly sustene grekes gan enchace whan came loste place stronde euen vpon see thrugh knyghthod made fle lyfe dread whiche mischiefe whan diomede behelde sawe pollydamas mortally pursued chase horsebacke fyelde yfere cruell herte hent anone spere spryngyng rode hym full ryght agayne tacquyte lyke knyght lyste partye fayne stede helde agayne reyne pand raught spere threwe rest dyomede smote breste mortally lyke founde hym vnhorseth greuous wounde ryght anone knightly herte pollydamas attones sterte vnto horse dyomede reyne proudely gan lede pvnto troylus foote stode forbathed grekes bloude euery halfe whiche shadde amonges knightly ne myght endure sustene sharpe sworde grounde kene pand delyuer maugre foen sadell vp sterte anone force armed vnwarely aduenture case sharpe swerdes none whette achylles together mette worthy troylus rancour pryde achylles smote fell syde downe horse lowe grounde notwtstanding grene mortal woude rose agayne fast gan hym spede myght recure agayne stede nought wolde auayle sodaynly freshe battayle troye made mencyon compasewyse beset hym enuyron eueryche armed bright clene hector tho furious tene pa dare telleth maner howe daye thousande knyghtes slowe whiche withstode onely diffence achylles maken resystence tyme death standyng ieopardye certaynly yf bokes lye lyklyhode myght tho escape mischyefe dead take hector hym furyous pbut read kyng thelamonyus rescued hym great nede caused hym recure stede notwithstandyng disdayne duke lorde athene case herte hole entent helpe achylles wonder dylygent hym ladde many noble knyght pbut bycause drewe nyght storye maketh rehersayle made ende battayle troye entred towne made menciowne hauyng delayes mortally foughten thirtye dayes without lette interrupcyon outher parte great destruction aldermost nathles great pryde lost grekes syde psaue pryamus lost specyall syxe sonnes called naturall made great dole heuinesse storye lyketh expresse mene whyle hector certayne face wounded agayne thus haue cruell rage euery parte receyued great domage tyll pryam hath troye sent downe trewes vnto agamenowne six monthes assente wolde therupon hath counsayle holde lordes beste echone accorded therto graunte axynge conclusyon pand whyle within ylyon durynge pea outher parte assured woundes fully cured play worthi hector protector towne ryche royall chefe doungeowne ilyon troye bare name whiche buildyng suche fame shuld commende vp downe dare doth discrypciowne wante cunnynge termes aplye boke doth specifye worlde newe ryche hyghe deuyse buildyng lyche whiche stode delyte sayth twelue stone whyte alabastre shortly conclude twenty pase latytude grounde ypaued thrughout wt crystall vp hyght performed euery wall stone man fynde dyamountes saphyres inde royall rubye oryent lyght derkenesse dymme nyght enchaced beames shene euer amonge emeraudes grene stone maner man worlde deuyse recken pryse value richesse ther wrought large gret roudnes sayth dare iuory pyllers thervpon set corner pured golde aboue hyght ymages wonder huge weight many perle many ryche stone euery piller halle one massyfe golde burned clere bryght wonderfull man syght worke merueylous fasshyon lyke estymacyon thynge ymade founded fayrye worke wrought fantasye wytte man lykelynesse bokes dare doth wytnesse lyke recken syght apparaunce thynge celestyall seeth boke ye get wrytynge myght neuer se albe dyd excelle therof thinke nowe telle retourne agayne pryamus whiche whyle inly curyous myght busy cure ordeyne sepulture sonnes afore dead pand tyme sycke laye dyomede loues stripe wounded herte felte inwardly smerte woful syghes whiche brest abreide full ofte adaye loue creseyde shake feuer newe caused hym full pale hewe wexen megre poore lene pyteously gan hym abstene meate drynke solace sene deadly face ofte daye wolde complayne dissease mortall payne prayinge grace wolde se vpon woo haue pytye mercy taken hede seruaunt onely womenhead playnely elles seye sake sayde wolde deye pbut cunnyngly full sleyghty wyse kepe hym lowe vnder seruyce delayes helde hym forth hande caused hym stande full vnsure betwene hope dispayre whan grace shuld haue repaire put hym heuynesse daunger newe brought hym distresse disdayne encrease payne double brought trayne woman holde man full narowe whan hurte cupydes arowe sette many fell assayes day day put hym delayes stande vnsure betwyxe hope dread ryght creseyde lefte dyomede entent sette hym fyre woman kyndly aye desyre whan man haue brought trauce vneuenly hange hym balaunce hope dread lynke hym chayne fyne vnsure bothe twayne dryue hym forth yeres serue force lyue sterue fyne loues fyry rage wolde haue hym seruage locked hym vnder suche keye wote lyue deye wherof doubte thus lette hym dwell forth wyll story tell matter eke resorte agayne myne auctour recordeth certayne trewse wered gone twelue dayes suyng one grekes haue faught wt towne great damage confusyowne outher partye aduersyte whyle great mortalyte sworde pestylence amonge grekes fatall influence noyous hete corrupte eyre engendred tho great dispayre theyr lyfe fyelde leye day day sodaynly deye wherby theyr nombre fast gan dyscrece whan sawe ne wolde sece theyr aduyse kyng agamenowne trewse sent vnto towne thirty dayes priamus kinge without abode graunted axynge phow andromecha dreame forwarned death husbande hector day folowing entred fielde wher admonyshed therto hauing respect next day slain achilles capitulo xxvii vvhan moreyne wofull rage pestylence began aswage trewse wered gone grekes caste meten foen vpon day plate armed clene whan phebus rose beames shene full pleasauntly gan shede lyghte pbut fynde tofore selfe nyght andromecha faythfull trewe wyfe worthy hector hym louyng lyfe gette chyldren two wonder semely inly fayre also pand lamedowne called tone yonge tother ne myght gone pand astyonax read hyght fetured well passynge fayre syghte guydo lysteth endyte moder pappes whyte yonge tyme suckynge arme brestes embrasyng nyght made mencyon slepe wonder vysyon note sothe may neuene outher dreame veryly sweuene fro aboue reuelacyon whylom kyng scypyon shewyng outher oracle goddes warnyng myracle sothnesse slepynge laye thought playnly nexte daye phector went fomen assayle wonte armed battayle ne shulde escape vtterly fate hondes falle fynally ouermore attropos shall fyne euermore lyues threde twyne shewe force fell myght parodye worthy knyght proche shall without wordes mo fyelde playnly go astoned strete short breth laye abrayde vpon death syghe stynte slepe pyteously brast wepe constraynte herty sorowe specyally wofull morowe sawe stocke worthinesse wonte manfully hym dresse arme hym stele borned bryght troian wall hector worthy knight fete fell downe lowly declaryng vysyowne quakyng herte womanhead wherof god wote toke full lyttle hede therof hygh indignacion platly affyrmynge discrecion trusten suche fantasyes dreames shewed gladly meinte lye full iapes illusyons whiche playnely conclusyons elles folkes delude albe people rude therin whyle haue affection iudge deame oppynion dyuersly may pretende ofte falle happen wende foloweth lyke conclusyon dread whiche lamentacion encrease gan andromecha swone fyrst cryed ha sayinge ala myne owne lorde dere trewe wyfe ala nyll ye whyche faythfull hoole affection desyreth aye saluacyon vp rose deadly vysage lyke woman caught sodayne rage kynge pryam hecuba quene haste went selfe mene wyfely herte trewe stele ceryously declared euery deale pyteous dreame myracle onely deuyne oracle yshewed goddes purueyaunce tolde eke fynall ordynaunce fortune false dispocisyon fully purueyed destruction lorde without delaye fyelde yf go daye pwherfore prayeth deadly hewe vnto kynge mercy rewe vpon wo haue compassyon ordeyne hyghe discrecion lordshyp soueraynte lorde may destroyed reckeleshead wylfulnesse worde kyndnesse aye moche loue founde tofore quene sowne fell grounde sayde ala deadly chere helpe case myne owne mother dere womanhead routh grace lorde fyelde ne pace deuer motherly pytee benyngnely goodly se knyghthode hygh prowesse restrayne renowmed noblesse ylke day handle spere shelde go armed fylde pand twayne assent beste condescende vnto requeste fynally accordynge one whe wardes redy euerychone pon yssuynge troylus fyrst parys next grekes fall pand hym troyan eneas kinge sarpedan pollydamas kyng eroys kyng epystrophus eke kyng ycalled forcyus plate mayle eueryche armed clene alderlast came kyng phylomene withall kynges lordes renowne deffence come towne grekes knyghtly debate pand pryamus sothly gate conueyed theyr goynge set wardes noble worthy king full prudently sapyence gaue congee lycence vpon grekes proue myght agaynst full redy fyght fomen royall apparayle amyd fyelde abydyng battayle pbut pryamus meane whyle lyke guydo remembreth style thylke fyne ye haue herde sayne whothy hector repayred agayne hym contermaundyng ne shuld gone thilke day fyght agayne foen whyche thynge hygh despyte brent whan sawe lordes went gate alone abode whiche wexed furyous wood hooly cause arettynge wyfe cheietie tender lyfe puttyng fully occasyowne abydynge day towne preiudyce worthynesse disencrease hygh prowesse leest tongue hygh estate false reporte derogate caste anone full knightly herte lyfe death shulde hym asterte within fyelde daye founde though wt many mortall wounde shulde peces hewen sonder vpon playne dismembred yonder hole manhod herte sette anone without longer lette agayne arme hym full dyligent agayne precept commaundemente father rode waye feare whyche anone would deye wife newe crye gan shoute papes also hangynge oute lytell chylde armes twayne tofore lorde gan wepe playne besechynge routhe pyte would vnto sorowe se least wyfely trouthe manhode haue herte routhe vpon childe vpon also whych bare armes two might criynge kepe whan sawe wofull mother wepe knelynge downe vnto sayde sobbynge might abrayde mine owne lorde haue mercy lytell chylde whych ye se pyteously afore wepe crye haue mercy lorde v dye haue mercy eke vpon cite myne owne lorde haue mercy cruell death passe shall echone lacke helpe ala ye gone pthis crye andromecha eke syster cassandra phecuba fayre pollycene heleyne eke lusty freshe quene atones fell beforne heyr vntrussed weping torne loude gan crye place besechynge mercy grace thilke daye abyde towne hert haue compassyowne complaynte wofull mone sith truste towne alone abode resystence agaynst death chiefe defece onely affiaunce suerte suffysaunce eche thinge theim might greue pand yet ne might herte meue abyde yet goodlyheade besought womanheade would encline herded herte stele might lytell droppe fele onely pyte woo rewe lykly renewe fynally destructiowne cite lykewyse towne death soth shulde fully ruyne yet might enclyne ne would conclusyon indurate harted lyon alwaye continuinge rage whose herte might often aswage nother prayer lamantacion restrayne opinion euery peryll layde hath asyde waye gan anone ryde wife none bote rage kinge ran amased mortall wo vnneth might speake diffaced rewefull sight hewe knoweth wight loste bothe might strengthe plat fell grounde length tofore kynge routhe sene pbesechinge entente full clene grace consider wolde wo helpe hector ago seynge faythfull womanhead request raughte anone stede pricked onely sake great haste hath ouertake worthy hector within cite hent reyne great difficulte maugre made tourne agayne suche wise durst sayne albe full lothe therto prayer force also stede made alyghte areste eschewe ne myght ne would agayne father striue albe felte herte ryue melancolye hertye yre disdayne newe set fyre inwardly stered blode lyke tygre lyon wood depriued newly praye right fared ylke daye lyke bore tuskes whette whyle grekes troye mette furyously walkynge vp downe diffence sothly towne troylus fyrste baye stede aduenture mette diomede eche surquedous pryde sharpe speres gan togyther ryde guydo sayth without dreade one bothe anone deade ne menelay knightly go betwene furyous tene smette horse full knyghtly wyse pand mereon mighty kinge fryse menelaus marked hath full well wyth swerde ful sharp groud stele vnhorsed threwe hym grene stroke might tho sustene menelay wood lykly euen stode lyfe shoulde thense eskape grekes ful hastely theim shape meryon ye haue herde sayne sette rounde vpon playne cesse auentayle euery parte cruelly assayle destytute wofull case pbut helpe came pollydamas knightes gan nighe nere sawe taken prysonere maugre vpon sette theyr handes pollydamas fette whose reskues great strife many one therfore loste lyfe grekes rather shoulde escape handes hasty rape caste theym playnly shoulde dead fully purpose haue hadde head stode mischyefe great disioynt selpe euen vpon poynt pcame troylus knightly arraye manhod made suche affraye amoges reskuse kinge maugre theim cominge deliuered mighty kinge fryse cruell death ye haue herde deuyse thervpon came thelamonyus proude armes euer surquidous thre thousande full worthy euerychone vnhorseth pollydamas anone among knight proudly bare hi downe pbut troilus hath thrugh hie renowne myd foen get horse agayne troye sore belayne euery halfe throughe grekes pryde ne might afore theim tho abyde newe newe hardy achilles assayled theim myrmydones compelled necessyte mischyefe made flee home walles gate towne great domage confusyowne theyr partye abacke gone pthe whych thynge margaryton behelde sawe howe game gothe herte gan wexen wrothe passyngly haue disdayne storye recordeth certayne bothe hardy famous sonne also kinge priamus noble knight great worthinesse sawe mischyef distresse theim troye add gan fle caste anone auenged vpon achilles great might ran full lyke manly knight horse backe townes sake enforseth achilles take amyd felde amonge knightes pbut achilles ala befall daye slewe cruell aduenture troians mighte endure felde holde homeward gan hie mortally maken noyse crye first death margaryton pand pursuyte king thelamo made chase hys crueltye home gate troye cite slewe killed alwaye rode albe parys manly withstode brethrene baste borne al ground haue lorne lefte forsake vtterly felde home wet brought shelde dead corp margaryton theyr gate shette anone whych mischiefe hector gan beholde yre herte gan wexe colde sayd platly without delaye would auenge death daye made haste stede fet vp sterte basenet vnwyste kinge lefe lothe gayne forthe anone gothe tyll passed gate towne furyous tygre lyowne whose coming thick swarme tofore sworde grekes gan fleen thought tyme withdrawe fyrst finde hath slawe two worthy duke wyth theim met busy waye let one ycalled eurypalus pand hyght halcydius troians felde agayne haue newe manfully begon grekes sewe folowe trase yet myschiefe dan pollydamas tyme grekes take hector hath borne sake forest belayne thrugh knighthod reskued hi agayne put grekes great distresse manhode worthinesse euer thylke daye rode sharpe swerde bathed bloud cruell merciles pbut knight called leothydes shope anone hector mete yrous hete set full presumptuously hector tho deuoyde mercy anone slewe threwe felde whych thinge achilles behelde great slaughter woundes wide hector made vpon euery syde gan anone compasse herte vp downe caste aduerte grekes neuer maye sure agayne foen fyght endure kepe felde theim stryue whyle hector alyue wherfore caste shope many weye engyne hector might deye auauntage might finde pand therto eke pollicenes inde worthy duke also assent onely herte hole entente hope stode syster wyue loue felte herte ryue grace better stande caste fully take hande high emprise haue tolde bolde hector slew none gayne whych anone achilles hath seyne yre wexed herte wood bore tygre theyr cruell moode vpon hector auenged furyously gan fle pbut hector caught quarel sharp ygroud threwe gaue wound throughout thighe vpon syde felde might abyde withdrewe anone wente men home vnto tente made anone surgeyn binde mortall wounde fynde whan staunche ceaseth blede haste agayne toke stede leest wounde deade afterwarde great dreade thought fyrst auenged vpon hector might se happe sorte yf would fall thought paynes hym beste remedye hande might dye lyfe routhe mite hector might acquyte deathe deathe conclusyon holy entencion desyre fully suffysaunce death vnwarely gyue mischaunce pbut time hector vp downe wonte playeth lyon amonges grekes many sondry place swerde gan theim enchase death might hi seen fledde afore like swarme none hardy wythsette grekishe kinge mette hap aduenture whiche sothe cote armure embrouded full many ryche stone gaue lyght sonne shone full bryght cleare ioye sene perles white emerawdes grene full many one therin sette cercle basenette rounde enuyron auentayle veluet fret aboue mayle saphyres ynde stone red whose arraye hector taketh hede towardes fast gan drawe fyrst fynde hath hym slawe force manheade hente vp afore stede fast gan wyth ryde wardes lytell syde good leyser playnly maye spoyle ryche arraye full glad lyght newe empryse ala false couetise whose gredy fret great pytee hertes may lightly staunshed etike draweth great distresse defaceth high worthynesse full ofte sythe conqueroures theyr fame rente away floures desyre hauynge gredy thuoght hygh noblesse sothly longeth nought suche pylfre spoylynge robberye appartayne worthy chyualrye couetyse knighthod lere one chayne maye knet yfere kouthe ofte suche rauyne hath cause roote ruyne many worthy lyst take hede lyke ye maye nowe hector reade sodaynly brought endynge onely spoylynge ryche kinge desyre hadde horse backe whan ladde reklesly storye maketh mynde caste shelde backe behynde welde selfe lyberte haue oportunyte spoyle wyght spare hys brest disarmed bare except plate diffence agayne stroke maken resistence ala tho reckles floure knighthod mahode pereles foo ylke daye alone awayte laye mischiefe hate enuye fielde might ought espye achilles cruell venymous hertye moste melancolius whych couertly houing beside sawe hector disarmed ryde hente spere sharpe grounde kene yre hatefull tene vnwarely hector might aduerte palas smote herte throughout ye brest dead fel adowne vnto earthe troian champyowne neclygence onely shelde death odemon behelde worthy kinge might hym refrayne pbut achilles rode payne hit amyd prese maugre might myrmydones dead guydo sayth certayne wounde fel grofeling ye playne knightes shelde alofte ylayde caryed full softe vnto tente haste leue deadly wounded man full sore sycke tyll maye releue drewe eue troye great reuerence laboure theyr diligence complaynte lydgate death hector ca xxviii bvt nowe ala shal forth procede storye wo dreade fele hande bothe tremble eke quake oh worthy hector onely thy sake thy deathe lothe wryte oh shall helpe quod howe wo begone sorowe knowe ende none suppose sith worlde began ne neuer wofull man whylom great myght renowmed euery maner wyght throughout worlde high lowe none sothe could know man armes famous yet yholde victorious tofore time remembred stile vnto daye ala harde nother hector playnly none pollicene worthy brother power mette theyr might ouersette felde force daunte pryuely dare auaunte pbut nowe ala mayde tender age hath sodaynly brought suche rage streames eyen twayne perced hath clouen euery vayne herte maye asterte dead thrugh constreynt smert pfor shall nowe wishe teache ala shall nowe leche ala shall helpe saue death graue hope playnly none saue mercy ala gone nother prayer treasour rychesse force might nother high prowesse highnes bloud byrthe kinrede maye auayle helpen nede meue sadde trouthe vpon wo euer haue routhe pwhat newe furye inportune rage hath brought hertin suche outrage agaynst whych nowe debate pto loue beste deadly doth hate pand good fayth wysely lyste aduert lytell wonder though hate herte syth come hither fro ferre kinrede make werre whyche confusyowne knightly brother worthy renown haue fatally mine handes slawe whych worlde felowe worthynesse manlyheade ala ala nowe maye quake dreade lyfe fallen dispeyre howe shoulde bolde haue repeyre dare ala come theyr syghte woful wretche vnhappy wighte howe shall hardy appeare presence eyen cleare certys se none mene weye fynally must nedes deye dispeyred stande euery syde helpe con prouyde ryght anone scaldinge sighes depe achilles braste wepe deadly cheare pale funerall face tourned wall routhe pyte sene hertye furye paynes kene oppressed thoughte lyfe death rought nought continued till drewe nyght titan hath withdrawe clear light euer one like wofull man ilyche like coloure pale wan without slepe fretinge sorowe ptyll lucifer next morowe tofore sonne beemes cleare full lustely gan appeare oryent whan achilles vnpacient wythout reste peace quakinge aye feuer newe sene playnly hewe tyll abrayde anguishe sodaynly called one pryue counsayle trusteth well vnto telleth euerydell fro poynt poynt howe stode sent forth bycause could good message streyght troye towne full aduise informaciowne mattere hecuba quene wisedome mene might discrecion finde waye saluacion vnto lorde loued quene anone go matter wisely gan conueye tofore grace would preye enioyeth gyue audience tale none offence phe foole newe lere wherfore quene goodly gan euer liketh sayne word ylost spoke vaine tale man could amende craftely gan discende substaunce tolde clerely oute premiss full well brought aboute fynally conclusyon chiefe sayde entencion effectuelly would make peace vnyte atwene grekes folke troye whych thinge knewe better weye werre alder ease witte prudently appease mortall stryfe bytter rage allyaunce onely maryage lyst wise worthy quene pthat doughter fayre pollicene maye wedded vnto achilles theyr might fynall pea hecuba discrescion wytte medyacion prudence might brynge pryamus fully assentinge pthat achilles might doughter wyue might parfourmed blyue lyke tofore made mencin couenaunt onely condicion grekes shall theyr werre lete suffer lyuen quyete maryage ylke twayne parfourmed knyt vp chayne pand ye quene hath knowen entet full soberly good aduysement tofore worde asterte full pyteously sighed herte laste sobre cheare euen thus sayd messagere frende quod touchynge thy requeste make beheste leste condescende lyeth bringe ende thy lordes wyll herte entiere herevpon must fyrst requere kinges wyll lyst assente purpose whych thou arte sente ouermore must wytte also parys willynge eke therto whych thynge euery circumstaunce wyll selfe maken enqueraunce pfull faythfully priam parys meane whyle theyr aduyse without within dayes thre whiche time come againe achilles sende fynally thou shalt knowe ende matter aunswere playne home goeth achilles agayne pwith full glad cheare lorde please set hert better ease auysedly high discrescion hath made relacion tolde tale thrifty wyse could wordes deuyse brynge hope lordes herte full relese paynes smerte wherby made sorowe withdrawe thus whyle hope gan adawe pamid breke hecuba quene pto priam spake pollycene touchinge sonde achilles profre make peace tolde forgate nothinge wherof astoned priamus kynge spake worde halfe houres space selfe gan inly compace full prudently might meane achilles would haue pollycene vnto wife aye wonderynge laste syghinge wonder sore hath disclosed conceyt herte sayd ala howe sore doth smerte remembre may haue peace great offence achilles towardes playnly slewe worthy hector crueltye hooly vpon euery side hoole assuraunce gouernour guyd mine platly sayne therwithall myne eyen twayne alone sothfast lyght shelde protectour thrugh great might manhode agayne mortall rage grekes werre croked age pbut nowe ala confusyowne slayne worthy renowne achilles maye minde herte neuer fynde allyed mortall foo roote grounde sorowe woo full harde herte appease loue causeth mine vnease euery halfe cruel foen proude grekes harted echone agaynst nowe fortune contrayre tourned newe quarell apayre causeth grekes wood furyous ala presumptuous ponely hector berafte awaye sythen choyse maye agaynst herte though anger ryue matter assaye shall stryue though lothe sytteth full sore yet eschewe harmes lykly hereafter fall saue myne sonnes consente achilles moke trewe fynall peace atwene grekes also cite without playnly howe haue vnto wyfe doughter pollycene pbut leste treason meane firste wende behest make ende wythout fraude mine aduise pto whych counsayle assenteth eke parys rather conclusyon made none excepcioon pin trete quene heleyne menelaye neuer shoulde atteyne recure agayne vnto hys wyfe whyche parys without noyse stryfe grutchynge vnto entente within selfe fully assente therby hopynge without feare dreade perpetually heleyne possede right luste man shall saye nay vpon thirde daye pachilles hath wytte mattere hecuba sente messingere tolde aunswere kynge ceryously gynninge endinge assenteth well therto pand parys eke selfe also playnly tolde touchinge peace purpose holde fyrste heste brynge aboute sure therof nede doubte shall haue purpose euerydele worke prudently wele herevpon informaciowne messenger troye towne without abode haste maye achilles helde ryghte waye tolde hole effect mattere alwaye feruente entiere herte brent hole glede sawe none way spede onely peace ye haue herde telle pand aye brest sighes gan swel loue pollycene caste alwaye amonge throe kene purpose waye fynde whyles busy mynde shoulde purpose brynge aboute selfe casteth many doubte panone dispayre rage vp sterte cruelty caught hym herte whych hath throwe suche thoughe power beheste fulfyll dede except hadde well lesse dreade euery thinge put certayne wening greke would luste fayne desyre varyable selfe thus fauorable parfourme nothynge denye lusty fantasye maner louers euerychone suppose acheue anone thinge lyst take hand disioynt matter stande though impossyble theyr foly aye credible achilles trusteth fynally fulfyll hestes vtterly supposinge aye worthynesse manhode hygh prowesse whych selfe gloryfye pryde surquedrye grekes shoulden despayred theyr truste theyr might appeyred vpon troians wynnen lande withdrewe hande helpe theim therwithall also home grece wolden go syege onely sake quarell vterly forsake pbut daye fyerse achille theym abode cite spylle whyche thinge lordes assente assembled heren entente amonge theim thys achilles byddinge pallamydes gathered yfere tofore theim lyke ye shall heare achilles hath tale begonne sayd syres muche konne wysedome high prudence renowmed eke sapyence throughout worlde discreciowne worthy also renowne kynges duke whose royall name east west floureth yet fame knyghthode manlyhead saye pray taken hede saye yf ye consyder playne entent commyng hyther good auyse entencyon grounde founded reason cause roted maner ryght ye lyft vp syght aduerte clerely mynde full ferre backe wytte set behynde prudent lokyng aduysenesse fyrst whan foly hastynesse toke vpon v come ferre agayne troyans gynne werre ieoparte lyues euerychone loue one man alone ye wote trowe meane pkyng menelay defrauded quene telle trouth lyste feyne ye well wote onely heleyne groude gynnyng debate many worthy estate recurlesse remedye lyfe good haue put ieopardye landes lefte eke regyownes cyties also ryche townes whiche absence stonden desolate wyues chyldren eke disconsolate woe abyde mournynge distresse whyles soth expresse day day beset euery ryde lye felde death abyde sorowe care labour wo ye wotte well also sith fyrst tyme werre began grekes many worthy man hath loste lyfe thrugh deathes fatal woud hytherto haue myght lyued sounde home grece assured well ioye ne comen vnto troye remembre full great pyte pand ouer saye also amonge troyans cruell mode haue moche loste bloude hath full ofte made pale hewe pthis day also grene newe hector suche mortall wounde quarell sharpe grounde aboue thygh kene head daye afore dede happe yshape death vnneth might escape whiche yet freshe vpon sene large wyde yet grene smerte whiche yet ful sore coplayne pand good fayth semeth heleyne ye aduerte wysely thought suche pryse shulde nat haue bought lyfe good yfeare honour yput dreadfully hangen ballaunce yf ye remembraunce conceyue aryght casten vp downe sodayne chaunge reuoluciowne fallen hath syth werre began slaught death many worthy man sake hath loste lyfe yet worste mortall stryfe doth moste rebounde damage disencrease eke disauauntage lykely dayly ordenaunce made therfore remedy shape outher syde fyne onely heleyne abyde troye styll towne let v caste good inspectiowne ease maner waye pso kynge called menelay chese hym wyfe londe lyke estate suraunce bonde vnder wedlocke confyrmed vp newe vnto hym wyll founde trewe syth without gylte synne may law heleine twyn dyuerse cause ynowe thrughout ye world euery wight yknowe auoutry foule vyce lawe preiudice pthough menelay iustly forsake whan lyste take shall hym better queme please v shall full great ease whan werre brought ende whiche lykely many man shende forth contune great labour importune ne shall whyle mowe sustene soth withouten wene troyans yet flourynge myght wt haue full many worthy knighte helpe hye lowe degre therwithall stronge cite euery parte without eke within lykely wynne purpose though euer abyde wherfore wysedome let v voyden pryde wylfulnesse onely prudence haue eye aduertence profyt vaine glorye honour shineth victory wysedome withdrawe honde sith may constrayne bonde fortune whele abyde stable wherfore rede become mutable gery goddesse double chere let v gyue vp suche thynge lyeth whyles may alder worshyp saue werre laude yet haue consyder well manhead pour foe hector dead whyle honour floure counsayle fortune loure sayd ere chaunge bryght face whyle beste stonde grace one assent one oppynyon without contradiction herte wyll one honour partye pall grece home returne longer soiourne quarell haue longe sewed doutles may eschewed full great damage without fayle haue done shall folowe tayle wherfore beste folye vp resygne whyle hap welfull benynge blandyshynge face fayre tyme beste make repayre whyle stande party enmyes honour perygall fer aboue playnly coulde haue eye felicite whyle ascencion pbut lest man wyll make obiection may honour saue repayre playnely haue helayne agayne cause whiche thynge anone answere shall pif man fantasye dishonour vyllanye arrecte wolde maner kynde go home leue behynde shortely saye holde shame syth haue one great name pa heleyne byrthe good amonges v ycome kynges bloud psyster pryam lorde troye towne pexiona thelamowne kepynge hath shall feyne troye towne parys hath heleyne syth nowe may none let tone set agayne tother surplus olde enmyte betwyxe v troye cite counsayle ease one assent wysely appease hence wende tale ende pto anone kyng menelaus yre wood furyous pand kyng thoas duke eke athene myght longer hym sustene suffre hym reckles spake attones vnto achylles onely inpacyence courte perturbed without prouydence tumulte gonnen repreue pthis achilles proudely comeue agaynst hym opynyon sayde shortely conclusyon vnto read ne wolde assent condescende nothyng mente gouerned case pfor whiche thynge anone achylles full yre rancour herte sodaynely see sterte went waye rage tryste pale wood vysage shortly sayde lyke fayne ne wolde longer payne helpe spede agayne troyans maner nede pand bad anone hardy achilles knyghtes called myrmydones spere shelde helpe grekes entre fyelde kepe close home within thetr tente thus yre gaue commaundement men ye haue herde deuyse withdrawe euery hygh empryse whan euer go battayle whyle scarsenesse vyttayle fell hoost fleshe bred wyne many greke brought vnto fyne ne myght endure distresse constreynt hunger dyd oppresse ptyll laste kyng pallamydes nothynge reckeles hath therupon made purueyaunce remedye redye ordynaunce assent counsayle echone phe hath sent wyse agamenon worthy styng messa besyde lyttell ile onely prouyde grekes myght spede releue great nede pand thelephus kynge lande gentylnesse hath put hande large wonder free renowmed muche humanite succour commaundyng aye anone purueyours hast gone euery party aboute enuyron landes regyon faythfully serche euery coste take vp vytayle grekes hooste pand full hastely made stuffe shyppes playnly lade euery thynge necessarye grekes water carye requeste kynge agamenon without taryinge delacyon pand kyng plente vytayle fraughte ylade gan anone sayle towarde syege meynee aye costynge grekyshe see pthe wynde good kyng blyue nauye troye dyd aryue fewe dayes grekes anone ryght repeyre full glad light exployt good spede well hath borne nede pand pallamydes anone sayth guydo shyppes gone consyder loke aboute nede within eke without amende repare lyste coste spare euery thynge without neclygence touchynge charge dylygence tyll trewse fully ronne werres newe agayne begonne whiche many man sothly dere abought ceryously wryte howe wrought purpose playnly sentence vnder supporte pacyence dvrynge one deadly cruell hate stynte may cesse date atwyxe grekes towne great damage destructiowne outher parte felynge full vnswete tyll daye caste mete wont proudely wt spere shelde wardes entrynge fyelde armed full bryght vpon outher syde pand enbatayled stoute full pryde full knyghtly haue chose ground take large baners wynde yshake tyll togyther sodaynly haue mette pand alderfyrst deiphobus hath sette freshe lusty herte yrous pvpon kyng called creseus enuye storye telleth horsebacke together ran pdeiphobus fyrste spere blyue throughout breste euen dyd hym ryue vnto herte spake deth grekes playne sore loue suche woe make astoned haue fyelde forsake gan anone vnto theyr tentes flee whiche sothe troye see vpon chase faste gan spede vnto tyme worthy dyomede pand eke kynge pallamydes hye despyte cruell mercyles twenty thousande worthy knyghtes al vpon troyans sodaynly fall mortally made lese waye resorte home agayne troye pand eke grekes felle furious tyme came thelamonius hyght ayax stronge knightly man lyke lyon amonge ran vpon troyans ouer sette casually waye mette pcecylien lusty freshe lyght tyme wonder manly knyght sonne pryam rede thelemon pryckyng stede slewe cruelly sworde anone rasynge arme shuldre bone ala fell dead fyelde deth whan deiphobus behelde wodder anone tygre lyon spere rauhe thelamon smette plate bright force made hym lyght lese sadell set amonge prese pthe whiche stroke whan pallamydes behelde sawe clerely gan aduerte irous wood furyous herte caste hym anone auenge thelamowne deiphobus full worthy renowne mortally guerdon quyte spere grounde byte sharpe kene large rounde square full cruelly ware harneys without areste pdeiphobus smote breste stroke brake ye shafte two tronchone head also lefte breste waye fynally must deye none helpe remedye wounde cruell mortall lyfe myght abyde pand whyle parys came besyde auenture whyle deiphobus wounde inly anguyshous gan hast approche nere face pale right heuy chere distresse wepte pyteously knightes commaunded hastely wounded brother syde softe feare hast shulde forthwt beare wardes great prese vnto payne relese brethe hym leyser auente open eyre vnto hym wente maugre grekes wounded bare full easy pase towarde walle faste towne great dole lamentaciowne full softely grounde hym layde tyll laste deadly man abrayde mortall loke face funerall pyteous eche ball gan tourne vp deadly eye euen thus parys gan seye oh brother myne loued haue pyte rewe vpon wo kyndnesse brotherheade wordes routhe take hede syth death muste sonder twynne pfor attropose shal longer spynne lyues threde knotte breke wherfore brother praye wreke vpon deth hense pace thou lyste suche grace kyndnesse yet deade breste speres heade rent away thou auenged vpon foe truste may wyt dead spyryte passe fynally fyrste discende depe downe helle eternally pluto dwelle myd boundes derke byn lowe fynally may knowe dead saye gyue force soone deye pto whose request parys toke good hede fyelde faste gan hym spede thought woe pyteously wepynge whyle brother laye lanquyshynge awaytynge onely death vpon poynt yelden vp breth pand knightes parys vp downe wardes sought enuyrowne ptyll laste pallamydes fonde sarpedon fyghtyng hande hande king worthi sarpedown come defence troye towne whiche hande noble knight whyle full myght pmoste busy pallamydes presse lyke lyon whetted woodnesse pallamydes herte ferde let flye hym sharpe sworde myghtely wonder thygh parted hath sonder smote herde bone pthat sarpedon fyll downe dead anone troyans whan slawe compelled force withdrawe pursuite kyng pallamydes whiche vpon merciles cruell wood lyon pafter death kyng sarpedon whiche ala whan parys dyd espye marked hym cruell eye hente bowe passyngly strong arowe tyller longe entoxycat venym head smote therwith dead hytte hym auentayle throughout stuffe thicke mayle throte gan pace fell dead selfe place ppallamydes manfull worthy knight grek toke flight made noyse wofull crye death complaynyng wonder piteouslye lorde myghty gouernour late chose emperour chiefe socour soueraine refute ala stonde destitute gouernaunce broke disarayed without guyde ryght shepe dismayed disconsolate comfortlesse yshent eche flyeth vnto tente troye sued chace horsebacke wonder huge pace merciles slewe fle euery syde pyte se without mercy grace lyke lyon gan enchace tyll compelled necessyte constrayned cruelte tourne agayne selfe diffende troye downe anone discende horsebacke euen vpon playne attones none gayne gan grekes proudely outraye cruelly disamaye fynally gayneth diffence mortall mighty violence troyans grekes diffoyle alderfyrste leyser dispoyle grekes tentes golde rychesse whiche time troylus gan dresse parys eke downe nauye thirtye thousande companye kyllyng tho playnly mette shyppes wylde fyre sette wall troye cyte men myght well hydous flawme se pand gone destruction ne ayax ycalled thelamon manhode knyghtly excellence come anone made resystence grekes many worthy knyght tho new began mortall fyght atwene troyans grekes stoute red bloud raylyng aboute vpon playne hydously blede length brede dead maymed full pale syght vpon soyle full many noble knyght atwyxe cruell hate fyght togyther debate wylde bore euen fare none lyste spare fyelde worthy thelamowne knyghthod high renowne manly bare hym grekes deffende might manhode amende thrugh ye world though men sought day person hath wroughte meruailes armes thrugh great might sothnesse grekes anone ryght without hym fynally shent shyppes attones loste brent pursuite parys day pand worthy troilus yt made affraye amonges hygh prowesse fyfty shyypes guydo doth expresse loste brent thelamowne reskus came knightes downe vnto sea remenaunt saue troyans daye haue hygher hande mortall fyght force great myght troylus hath many slaine grekes soth fayne withdrawe fielde lete abydyng fonde full vnswete wherfore gan lese place pamonge kinges sonne trace heber hyght wounded death ne myght vnneth drawe breth spere breste styckynge pto achylles came complaynyng vnto tent euen laye whiche fyelde daye pfor sake onely pollycene loue sharpe kene aye herte ylyke grene newe heber mortall hewe complayneth sore arrettyng cowardyse manhode trewandyse day myght shame withdrawe selfe hindring name fyelde hym full great reprefe grekes seynge mischiefe confusyon vpon brinke destruction abrode fielde se lye deade lyste one take hede knyghthode grekes releue pand whyle heber gan hym thus repreue spere whiche body sodaynly drawen ala eye vp caste rancoure yre full pyteously heber dyd expyre pin presence achylles therwith came sodayne re tente certayne knyght pof achylles axeth amonge grekes clerely stode answered full irours mode certes quod full vnhappely troye haue cruelly grekes daye fyght full shamefully put vnto flyghte many slayne ala welawaye vnneth none escape myght awaye vnhurte maymed withouten wounde fell v troyans yfounde eke suche multitude suppose shortely conclude daye opynyowne lefte man within troye towne able stande battayle spere sworde enmye assayle wene soth byn come v fyght huge route ne myght force take hande fyelde agaynst stande pbut nowe lorde draweth vnto night faynte fyght pleasyng worthynesse manhode hygh noblesse take encrese fame euermore getten name withall owne glorye perpetually memorye ryse vp arme anone sodaynely vpon gone feble weake make resystence agaynst manly famous excellence victours e er conquerours duryng worlde remembraunce euer brought vnto outraunce sothfastnesse haue dread pbut achylles toke hym hede heber laye afore dead full colde strake coloure lyke leade one lyste gyue hym audience vnto hym haue aduertence may worde herte myne sayde maken hym enclyne vtterly euen lyke ferde though maner worde ne herde eares passed sowne plo maner condiciowne custome playne vsaunce louers hangyng traunce phonour worshyp manhode prowesse strength might fame hardynesse encrease name vertue victorye knyghthode noblesse armes glorye myghtye loueley asyde suche myght god cupyde whiche hertes hye hoke sease loth playnly displease outher chere countenaunce wyll dede disobeysaunce theyr souerayne lady dere loke eyen clere full well daunte pride venus soone prouyde arrowes kene perce nerfe vayne enlace fyry chayne onely importable charge restrayned go large whiche cause day doubtles noble hardy achylles wolde withouten wene come fyelde drede polycene leste offended herte thynge escaped asterte achylles throughe mysgouernaunce whyles hengeth thus balaunce grekes faught twone tyll bryght phebus goinge downe troyans necessytye lacke lyght entre citye whyle homewarde repeyred laye deiphobus lyfe dispeyred compleynyng aye deadly wounde whan parys troylus haue hym found myschyefe gan wepe crye wolde routhe dye wofull noyse pyteous sowne salte teares gan renne downe chekes vpon outher syde whyles vpon hym abyde wounded man gan drawe ende whose spyryte redy wende brest wery goste full hastely another coste deadly eyen tourned vp downe whan knewe relacyowne pthat parys hath pallamydes yslawe anone bad shulde drawe large tronchone stelen head anone fell downe dead corp gan faste spede towarde towne nede dole wryte lamentaciowne made noble sarpedowne cytye namely kynge quene euer wepynge brother systers dere vayne reherse pbut pryam hath great dylygence two towmbes royall excellence deyphobus kynge sarpedowne many ymage grauen enuyron many knotte koruen yonder buryed lyttle sonder lyke custome rytes olde whyles feste halowe holde called feste funerall grekes haue make specyall ryche toumbe worthy kyng ppallamydes buryinge solempnely made ordinaunce amonges vsaunce great dole pyteous heuynesse haue kynge great worthynesse royally brought sepulture pand myght longe endure without head gouernour chosen haue emperour one assente affection worthy kyng wyse agamenon pand made lettynge troye next day ensuynge wardes fielde gone fully purposed fyght foen grekes manly face mette worthy troylus ouer sette greke none shortly telle thilke daye afore myght dwelle cruelly gan chace came rode place fledde sworde lyfe doubte yonge knightes ridinge aboute suche vsaunt lede euer one grekes bloud shede whiche lyke streame disteined al playne whyle huge rayne day huge myste euery man hath felowe myste specially vpon grekes syde storme woundes wide manhode troian knight pworthy troilus freshe yonge light coact cruelte maugre might dred death fle tentes succour fynde troyans aye pursuynge behynde iull mortally wish sterne pase storme cease case home repayre eitie stronge tyll morowe larke songe troylus efte manly battayle grekes newe caste hym assayle pand guydo wryt yonge
