champyowne thylke daye rode vp downe amonge foen hygh renowne ne king duke erle barown sworde wende lyfe made mortall ende whyle phebus gaue lyght tyll laste drewe nyght troye repayreth manfully pand seuen dayes suynge lyfe ledde knyghtes felle vpon grekes guydo telle aye newe new gan confounde cruell sworde kene grounde ne myght mortall tene afore syght abyde sustene vengeaunce toke rode weye forsoke trase renges redde soth fielde lay dead whiche slaughte confusyowne grekes new sent towne pfor trewse pryamus kyng anone graunted axynge two monthes fully assent lordes parlement wherof made full relacion pthe enbassadours agamenon lodgyng forth wente pbut vnto achylles sente meane whyle messangers wyse shall anone deuyse agamenon guydo lyste endyte lordes sent achylles vysyte certayne cause lyke ye shall whiche storye rehersed vlixes worthy diomede pduke nestor wente playnely reade fyne onely counsellyng herte myght brynge endure hym haue fantasye wyllynge thorugh chyualrye stande hath toforne haue many troye men ylorne lacke onely hygh presence pand achylles dygne reuerence receyued right knightly chere whan set yfeare lyke theyr degree anone aduenture pwhyle vlixes full eloquence gan tale prudently deuyse pto achylles saying wise psyr achylles moste renowned glorye throughout worlde memorye knyghthode shoures wel displease shall tell noble famous excellence eares let none offence shall say goodlyhead pacyently ye wyll take hede wordes sayd herte thought ensure fayne noughte saye yf ye remembre wel fyrst cause purpose euery dell grekes yf ye haue mencyon fully sette one entencyon well v pardye whan come fyrst citye kynges prynces except none whiche soth recken euerychone selfe speake speciall one fyrst moste pryncypall assented full troye cite manhode destroyed shulde perpetually brought vnto ruyne nowe newe note doth enclyne worthynesse sodeynly varye purpose contrarye pconsyder fyrst sage wronges done great damage grekes lande towne conspyryng aye destructiowne ye aduerte wysely thought slayne haue ende brought full many worthy syth gone full yore treasour man may restore dispoyled v brought great distresse goodes raught golde rychesse shyppes brent cruelte ala ye lyste se whiche may delayed manhode fynally outtrayed sith ye haue slaine hope suffisauce phector affyaunce fully truste diffence also pand deyphobus also go lykely apeyred fro day day fynally dispeyred frowardly fortune loureth honour fame flouteth worshyp high renowne atteyned hath exaltaciowne hyghest prycke fortune whele great wronge ye loke wele wylfulnes vnkynde ye frendly fynde frowarde whyle benynge influence graciously assygne spoukes meue vnto pleasaunce hap tourne wt plente chaunce whose helpe nedeth calle pwherfore ala wyll ye suffer palle noble fame wylfulnesse whyle hyest worthynesse knyghtly prudence shulde asterte whiche thynge euery gentyll herte shulde haue routhe compassyon wherfore praye iscrecyon ye shape purpose amende ye wolde herte condiscende v stonde knyghtly werre manhode spoke ferre renowne worlde ende reported men wende perpetually freshenesse hewe day day encrease newe tryumphe hygh victorye put storye eke memorye enprynted foryetfulnesse power haue malys oppresse fame knyghthode derke difface shyneth yet clere many place without eclypsyng sothly lesse whiche conserne ye reckelesse wylfulnesse cloude lyght renowne ye whylom shone bryght myghty hande manhode wtdrawe consyder fyrst grekes yslawe tofore tent wt mortal woundes wyde fyelde vpon euery syde haue disdayne onely lacke routhe ala whyle lyttle slouthe ley honde mischyefe whylom stroge mighty wall chiefe diffence champiowne souerayne helpe protectiowne ye haue ofte shedde bloud agayne foen whan stode full myghtely enmyes assayle without lyttell may auayle soth ne none v echone ye knyghthode lyste v gone agayne troyans ye wont trust fynall hope also ye shall helpe socour pand hereupon praye ye saye aduyce full wyll pand anone hardy fyerse achylle whan vlixes concluded tale sith face anger dead pale sayde euen thus openly playne sir vlixes ryght ye sayne haue declared conclusyon purpose entensyon fynally brenne destroye royall citie called troye holde soth lyketh lye entent grounded folye put v indiscrecion reckleshede hasty mocyon lyfe death suche ieopardye specyally chiualrye grekes lande smale thynge many prynce many worthy kyng haue ieoparted body good yloste lyfe yspent bloud might haue ful well home peace pand nowe kyng pallamydes yslawe also sayth newe wise manly trewe lyfe pryce alone cause whiche echone gathered loke ryght grekes many noble knyght haue slayne worthyest worlde seke manlyest euery lande regyowne grekes partye ye towne chyualry knighthod ye soueraine floure wynne arme worshippe honour assembled come fro ferre whiche soth duresse werre full many one fyelde dead veryly without drede shall well mo werre laste fro euery day numbre lasseth faste worthy knyghtes dede without routh dare saye conclude trouth rage furyous wood full lykely gentyl bloude worlde shall destroyed rural folke great pyty shall haue lordshyp hooly gouernaunce churles eke sorowe mischaunce euery londe shall lordes alone whan gentyll men slayne echone pi hector noble knight worldes sonne light manhode floure slayne pyteously werte soth myghty parauenture whiche may attayne noblesse shall fayne way shall death eschewe myght pursewe fro day daye whyle lye therfore shortely requere touchynge werre outher praye veyne herken saye wyll purpose werre stryfe ieoparte lyfe leuer haue palled name slayne haue ydle fame worthinesse death yblowe wynde lasteth throwe though renowne prise blowe wide foryetfulnesse leyth ofte asyde length yeres oblyuion enuye false conclusyon lande knyghthode worthynesse wysedome eke gentylnesse fredam bounte vertue suche grace foryetfulnesse darke defface therwithall male enuye ysered hath palme chyualrye false reporte wherfore saye wyll wysedome suche folye let quyet forth lyfe nowe lede pand ouer three rede seke peace troyans ye may hasty wyse without delaye counsayle platly myschyefe death vpon fall well done ye toke hede pboth vlixes thou dyomede pand nestor eke sythen ye wyse worke playnely lyke deuyse summe fyne myne entent reporteth hym hath sent anone shorte conclusyon prepeyred agamenon answere ye haue herde seine nedeth wryte newe againe pand herevpon kynge agamenon let make anone conuocasyon lordes presence fro poynt poynt sothly sentence hath rehersed achylles desyrous haue peace troye platly prayer wyll degree agayne troians spere shelde helpe grekes armed felde wherfore kynge ful wise hereupon axed deuyse whan thought best matter syth stode pand fyrste speaketh menelay angry chere sayde platly nay haue peace entent ne wolde therto assent sythen cyte conclusion stode prycke distruction hector deiphob dead yt whylom trust euery nede diffence ago farewell truste hope also without hole pryde maye death abyde pand truste well without lesse though achylles ne helpe v towarde empryse therof drede maner wyse without hym haue victorye manhode owne glorye full sure therof certayne vlixes gan replye agayne nestor also sodayne mocyon contrayre opynyon affyrmynge playnely wonder though menelay sothly case vnto peace wolde assent openly wyste ment ground roote al werre cause also come ferre lande quene heleyne pand sake onely tweyne grekes whiche man may denye lyues put suche ieopardye hym grounde soughte well wyste rought nought menelay wo endure wyfe myght agayne recure pand sayth hector dead hath heyre speake manlyhead knyghthode wyll founde called hector seconde pworthy troylus whiche yt brother worlde suche worthynesse recken troye myghty wall pand diffence hector gone ye knowe well selfe euerychone ye lyste take hede whose sharpe sworde sore doth v blede euery day furyous hete amyd fyelde whan hym mete stede worthy deiphobus whiche tyme wonderly famous phi brother parys nowe founde worthynesse knyghthode perygall haue none auauntage vnto houre rather great damage recken syth gonne soth lyttle wonne lykely alwaye lese contune syth may chese holsome lyue quyet haue peace werre lete one assent syth ye wyse yt worde calchas gan ryse troyan treytour wt pale chere ire sayde ye shall pa worthy prynces thynke ye done chaunge lyke doth moone olde purpose fyrst entent agayne wyll commaundement godder euery thynge gouerne purueyaunce discerne ala als ne wyll ye leste credence fayth geue theyr heste whiche wyse may fallyble soth impossyble vtterly troye citye ordynaunce necessytye myght destroyed hense alyte slouth wyte victorye worshyp honour fynall palme eke labour reported water lande reserued hooly hande purpose yf ye forth contune hynder foly fortune soth dare well conclude peryllous goddes yllude neclygence slouth wylfully wherfore read manfully herte thought full vnyte platly deuoydyng ambyguyte set vpon knyghtly resume force agayne fully consume cruell foen let shet without wanhope drede dispeyre euery doubte castyng parrell slouth cowardyse let manhode vtterly dispyse dread death causeth hertes feynt cowardyse atteynt fynally goddes haue hyght prescyence eternall might victorye ye shall attayne lyke desyre sayne pand whan calchas conclusyowne false treytour vnto troye towne grekes wordes fayre touchynge werre put dyspayre herte one caste fulfyll hooly counsayle though achylle frowarde aye helpe nede gaue force toke hede euerychone redy make ye shall fielde haste take trewes passed ye monthes twayne ye felde grek gan theim ordayne troye agayne theim yssue oute pand worthy troylus huge route grekes gan alderfirste assayle swerde made rayle red bloud harneys bright death fled fro syght daye thrugh cruelte caste platly auenged vpon death hector vtterly pand dare wryteth specyally knightes troyan champyowne day hath slayne rydyng vp downe pa myne auctour guydo lyst endyte saue hym ferther wryte boke geueth suche name manhode knyghtly fame grekes dryuen vnto flyght daye tyll drewe nyght pand morowe dawnynge grekes haue phebus vprysynge yarmed great dylygence agayne troyans standen diffence amonges whome daye rede pso well hym bare worthy dyomede many troyan cruelte phath loste lyfe tyll troylus gan se dyomede fyelde rydynge anone without lettynge spere throwen reste troylus rode smote hym brest myghtely nede downe horse smote dyomede albe wounde tho domage furyously troylus rage hygh enuye gan abrayde whan ye loue faire creseide deceyte false trecherye grekes faste gan hye amonge horse mischiefe whiche lay drawe hast yt may shelde brosed affrayde bare hym home dysmayde stroke home vnto tent pand menelay whyle hath hente myghty spere tauenge dyomede towardes troylus fast gan spede fully auysed hym vnhorse anone troylus fyrste made stede gone swyfte course towardes menelay anone earth laye myghtely ye hyt hym spere shelde plate might body ne mortall wounde knightes anone hym founde prese rent bare hym home owne tent grekes aye standyng distresse knighthode ye hye prowesse troilus whiche hath belaine euery part rode plaine ptyll vnto tyme agamenowne fyelde valed downe many worthy banere shone full shene agayne sonne clere wt knight hym rydyng enuyrowne sore enchased troye towne woundeth sleeth put theim ye flyght hym selfe acquytynge lyke manly knyght without abode amonge troyans fyersly rode pthis worthy kyng great agamenowne troylus spere hath smytten downe maugre grekes gameth socour whan sawe lorde gouernour suche myschyefe grounde lyende hente hym vp made hym assende manhode stronge stede wyt gan taken hede consydered wisely thought disioynt troilus brought grekes great pryde tofore swerde myght abyde prudently hygh discrecyon pthis noble knyght kyng agomenon hadde aye aduertence gouernaunce prouydence whan sawe grekes gan fayle wexe feble standen battayle lacke stuffe shulde recomfort full prudently made resorte eueryche owne tent pand hath pryam sent trewse troye cyte syxe monthes myghte counsayle pryamus kynge without abode graunted axynge albe guydo lyste endyte euyll apayde longe respyte mortall foen maner wyse yet graunt ye haue harde deuyse stode strength fully read pin whiche tyme womanhead creseyde lyste longer tarye though father therto contrarye vysyte haue syght pof dyomede become knyght pwhich troilus late caught woud tent hath hym founde benygnely vpon beddes syde set downe selfe tyde platly caste owne thought ptouchynge troylus yt nought lyue hope recure thought wolde nothing vnsure purueyaunce without store gaue anone without hooly herte vnto dyomede lo pytye womanhead mercy eke benynge routhe newly olde trouthe nature lette slyppe ouer slyde rather lysten abyde man myschiefe sake chaunge redy make lumbardstrete crowne doket poyse good prent set letter chaunge doth man abyde wynde redy tyde passage aye lyste pace man loste lyste seke grace daunger none counterfeyte disdeyne sea calme rockes plain mercyles neuer man ne deyde sought grace record creseide whiche fynally hath gyuen herte dyomede relese smerte prayed hym right glad lyght calleth owne man knyght hym behyghte rather deye euery thynge howe wolde obeye honest hym pleasaunce leuer chaunge varyaunce founde lacke pytye syttynge femynyte nature vengeable fayth othe rather mercyable mannes lyfe standynge distresse phereof wyll dresse tell forth translacyon ceriously agamenon durynge trewse time peace hym selfe wente vnto achylles besechynge regarde haue knyghthode grekes saue presence withdrawe suffer mortally slawe enmyes pompous elate pbut achylles alway indurate ilyche newe herte thought purpose platly chaungeth nought fully enclyned haue peace pbut moche achylles entyernesse hyghe affection louyng vnto agamenon vnto hym graunted leste great parcell touchynge requeste saye achylles graunteth hym myrmydones full knyghtly men onely absence grekes maken resystence fyelde agayne towne whiche graunte kynge agamenowne duke nestor thanked hym herte alwaye conteynynge smerte loue fayre pollycene ne knewe gayne wounde sgrene dispeyred languysheth euer one whan trewse passed gone vpon day morowe full benynge achylles knyghtes dyd assygne fylde take agamenon story maketh mencion gaue bandes freshe read men may knowe manlyhead withholde specyall lyke man deadly mortall within tent achylles abode fyelde rode dole shulden twinne absence werre begynne maugre wyll agayne towne pbut forth went agamenowe vpon troyans sterne full pryde mette syde manly knyghtes troyan bloud whiche furyous wood cruelly grekes oppresse backe feare gan dresse inly fell kene ptyll myghty duke athene entred grekes diffende vpon hym vnwarely wende came myghty troylus lyke wood lyown stede anone bare downe put hym prese tyll hath mette myrmydones slewe daye full many one fer troylus ygone grekes put vtterly flyght knyghthod til drewe night fro swerde raunsom might borow guydo wryte next morowe full mortall slaught outher syde amyd fielde togyther ryde manly knightes wonder sene pand faught kyng phylymene helpe onely pollydamas taken hath worthy kyng thoas gan hym leade towarde troye ye towne myrmydones helpe came downe wonder proudly gan sewe myght thoas rescue hym delyuer stronge pbut troylus hurtled amonge furyously full lyke champyowne cast threwe downe slewe made blede tyll cruelly slewe myghty stede whiche sat yet neuerthelesse fought foote agaynst myrmydones cast troylus haue take pbut parys tho gan awake brothern hym rode place troylus stode vpon fete selfe alone mirmydones sleine haue many one knighthod malyhead vnto hym brought stede amyd foen made hym ascende full knightly gan selfe dyffende pbe set grekes felfe stounde neuer yet better knyght founde felte well tho foen brother called margaryton fought puttyng hym selfe prese slayne ala amonge myrmydones death cruell yre troylus anger sette fyer playnely purposeth tauenge may sworde began make way pand parys aye fast hym rydyng brethern vpon hym awaytyng whiche yfeare mercylesse pand fynde myrmydones force necessyte compelled playnly flee troylus furyous vengeable eke dispyteous gaue many mortall wounde yet soth day founde noble knyghtes quyt wonder wele crafte knewe euerydele longyng armes reade made sydes blede mayle plate shene ne myght playnly sustene sword troilus chasing ouerall albe kepte close wall hole together went sonder troilus aye chaseth yonder seuered mauger myght tyll fielde many worthy knyght came menelay kyng agamenon vlyxes eke cruell thelamon dyomede whiche woundes grene recured sayth myne auctour clene troyans sodaynly fall wardes knyghtes tho began fyght renewe euery halfe blouddy hewe plate bryght newe ysteyned troy manly haue peyned agayne foen myghty stryfe many greke berafte lyfe myghty bataile troylus came gan assayle euery parte many blouddy wounde knighthod gan confoude aye fledde ferde mortall stroke sharpe sworde deadly foe destruction contynueth tyll kyng thelamon manhode whan behelde grekes made recure agayne fyelde gan troyans assayle wonder sore tho began slaughter eche syde till troylus newe agayne grekes hath fyersly ouerlayne myrmydones euerychone afore sworde made gone tentes fyelde forsake hande day hath take hundred knightes came weye prowesse sent troye euer one gan enchace pmyrmydones loste place pand achylles lying tent repeyred forwounded rent herneys broke plate maile nombre fynde fayle hundred knyghtes slayne dead ala founde taas amyd fyeld thrugh girt wt many woude pof troylus sword hector secounde wherof achylles syght heauy nexte nyght bedde walowynge fro deuoyde slepe constreynt wo herte wounde kene men fayre polycene wyttynge well dyd payne venged shulde attayne wise vnto desyre thus brent double fyre loue yre made syghe sore cause loue aferde agayne towne person offenciowne pleste pryamus hecuba quene offended namely polycene thus stode double weer herte satte wonder nere many wonder dyuers fantasye haue louers poynt dye ryght euen fareth wofull man wo rede ne entryked wende deye recure knewe better weye whyle laye throwes wyte lyke guydo playnly lyste endyte story maketh mencyowne dayes seuen troye towne encrese augment sorowe grekes metten euery morowe thrugh ye force alder might outher parte slayne many knight pand whyle laye achylles grekes death ylyke reckeles loue onely toke maner hede hole mortally doth blede plaineth wound large hym thought parcell charge moche hath thyng thincke ofte waketh whan shulde wynke thoughtfull aye ymagynatyfe wery owne lyfe ptyll day kyng agamenon seynge death destruction grekes halfe withouten remedye troye sent enbassadrye trewse certayne dayes space myght therof haue grace lenger tyme platly endure leyser sepulture worthy knyghtes dead aforne fyelde outher party lorne whiche taas full busyly soughte plainly wrought durynge syege great vyolence shall descryuen pacyence phowe achylles slewe worthy troylus vnknyghtly trayled body fyelde tyed horse cap xxxi cruell force mortall yre martyr myght alway set fyre newe enuye gonne olde hatrede brennyng hertes hole glede atwyxe grekes troye cytye whiche lykely staunched tyll deth consume mortall darte full many worthy vpon outher parte execute ala fynall fate eyther parte enuious deadly hate whiche ne myght destyne remewe set nedely must insewe attropos wyll suffer none maystresse guyder rother deathes shyp tyll goth vnto wrake fortune gan tourne face abake highe disdayne fro troye cytye story shortly ye shall se whan trewse ytake wered gan redy make proude grekes fyelde gone vpon morowe whan phebus bright shone armed full shene eueryche deuyse pand menelay hath first met paris day storye read eche smytte stede whiche tyme dan pollydamas pto vlixes rode sterne pase eche cruell enmyte styffe swordes gan together flee nouther manhode wyte spere squared byte pthe myghty duke called meneste rode lyne ryght myght se anthenor troyan full pryde sadell caste hym downe asyde furye hatefull tene tho haste come kyng phylomene helpe towne gan assayle kyng agamenowne knyghthode hardinesse hym brought great distresse vtter myschyefe confusyon pne kyng thelamon full proudely came hym reskewe sore gan pursewe spere vpon phelomene horse layde hym grene maugre force story telleth thus hym mortally yrous yonge archylogus mortall course ran vnto brumius one sonnes pryamus kynge yonge delyuer beste lykyng hym smytte great myght fell dead freshe lusty knyght death wha troy espye made shoute pyteously gan crye wofull routhe death complayne tyll noyse gan vtterly attayne troylus eares platly rode lenger abode place felly gan approche sworde sette broche without routhe grekes hatefull bloud mercyles hym withstode slewe daye cruell auenture greke none yt might endure tofore sworde gan oppresse knyghthode hygh prowesse put vtterly flyght ne byn manhode myght pof myrmydones al longe day one assent vpon troylus lay wherof full melancolyus courage manhode moste famous ne lyste longer lette attones vpon sette furyously gan amonge ryde smote euen syde body ye herte wt sworde thrugh doublet shert shelde plate thrugh haberion perccd hath lyke wood lyon slewe day many one maugre fledde eueryche grekes eueryche tent pand troy went swyftly horse tyll haue take slaught grekes ther make fynally bette reskuse death passyngly confuse grekes myschyefe desolate troylus narowe brought chekmate coulde tho better remedye hydously wayle crye death forwounded grisely chere pthat achylles whan gan fyrst dredefull noyse wofull sowne caused reflectiowne eyre agayne coulde knowe rochys harde kauernes lowe lyke one worde spoke two men wont callen ecco confuse lamentaciowne grekes syde whiche deadly sowne pyteously achylles ronne lay agayne hote sonne mortall woundes yeldyng vp breth roumble swowhe resownyng deth noyse grekes maden ment achylles dyd enquere cause clamour tolde lacke socour grekes eche tentorye pof troylus slayne victorye goth fynally troye towne euermore conclusyowne many greke slayne laye tent gapynge vpwarde wt bloud yspent constreynt wounde smert pand whyle achilles gan case aduerte full sodaynely came hym man whiche tale euen thus began ala quod may ye thus sustene se men hereupon grene afore face slayne lye deade lyste one take hede stande styll pensyfe tent vpon poynt selfe shent hasty houre yf ye abyde fyfty thousande knyghtes besyde redy armed plate mayle caste playnly assayle doubte vnarmed ye stande ye knyghthode manly take hande resyste selfe place lyke man meten face pfor whiche anone cruell mode achylles lyke woode hath armed hym fomyng bore farewell loue sette store hasty hete yre kene pthat forgat fayre pollycene beaute yt whylom made smert rage vp anone starte toke stede lyon wroth agayne troyans fyelde goth lyke wolfe hunger gnawe ryght gan agayne foen drawe rode without excepciowne woundeth sleeth killeth bereth downe lyttle throwe troy gan sworde knowe whiche infecte newe bloud none yet yt withstode mortally gan aboute hym layne dead bodyes enlonge playne ptyll casually troylus gan espye achylles caste eye gan horse might payne pbut achylles hym ware also smette stede made hym go towarde troylus selfe tyde full course together ryde full lyne ryght speres sharpe whette suche myght haue together mette hyghe dysdayne sayne grounde felle tway pbut achylles caught hath suche wounde body depe profounde longe lay myn auctour saith certain helth restored agayne pand troilus eke thrugh plate maile al wryte guydo wounde small whiche vnto hym dyd greunaunce thus daye contynuaunce dayes syxe suynge proude grekes mette cruelly amyd fyelde troye towne great damage confusyowne outher partye playnely nay many worthy slayne day day rancour hertye hoote enuye albe guydo doth specyfye none theyr name playnely boke ye shall fynde yf ye lyste loke al whyle sodeine thinge pensyfe tryste pryam kyng achylles tourned hath clene luste awaye yonge pollycene chaunge sodeyne newe thought behestes trewe pbut deceyte doublenesse fraude falsly newe fangelnesse sleyghty treason vncouert gyle rage loue lasteth whyle vtterly founde beheste lyke wynde man may areste faceth worde discordaunt fro dede whiche wyse man take shall hede lette passe reckelesse albeit achylles whylom caught within loues snare hym lyste nowe one spare hygh rancour lady offende lyke troye wende hecuba nouther yet pollycene angre gan abreyde truste entyerly hath leyde achylles falsly mene wherfore full tryste pollycene enclyned eyen clere counsayle mother dere pto haue wedded achylles fyne onely shulde haue peace atwene grekes troy towne false inconclusyowne pin fyne trouthe ysene whan achylles woundes grene fully cured certayne day gan compasse euer may ymagine enuyous herte venged woundes smerte vpon troylus thot stacke aye mynde auauntage myght hym fynde hym bare passyngly hatrede herte brennynge glede whiche day nyght may degree fully queynt tyll auenged hoote rancour gan hym gnawe auysed platly shall beslawe handes whan falle day hym gan calle myrmydones knightes euerychone vpon morowe whan grekes gone tofore towne stele armed bryght agayne troyans purpose fyght come proudely fielde opposyte many ryche shelde newly depeynt colour freshe fyne vpon whiche full bryght gan shyne fyry titan golde tressed sphere vpryste beames clere whan felle enuyous achylles knightes called myrmydones pvpon troylus gan hym complayne besechynge theyr payne agayne troylus fielde daye catche hym myschyefe may busyly dylygence haue full aduertence one assent ryde thynge sette asyde nought elles take hede saufe fynally agayne hym procede myght catche hym trappe within selfe troylus clappe enclose sette hym rounde abouie wyse go oute whan beset amonge siea euer fall myght manly coserue tyll hym selfe come make hym sterue sworde none wyght plo manhode preyse ryght vengeaunce deth rancour pryde compassed treason knighthode layde asyde worthynesse false enuye yslawe falshede lofte trouthe backe ydrawe ala armes shulde befall trecherye bytter galle shulde world knight foude trouth order bounde palas ala achylles conspyred hath myrmydones death one yt worthyest wight euer eke beste knyght ala wo herte fele deade sake storye whan rede whan fortune hath thynge ordeyned though euer wayled compleyned gayne remedye though men galen aye crye touchynge mattere wryte forth lyke ye shall myrmydones haue lord behyght power full myght fulfyll commaundement fielde grekes went pbut troylus fyrst opposyte without abode manly mete ybrent feruent hete hardynesse hyghe courage worthynesse vasselage ne lyste longer abyde folke began ryde amonge grekes folke hyghe renowne wt sword woudeth bereth downe sleeth kylleth vpon euery haiue mortally may salue sore sounde death rode yeldyng vp breth furyously gan enchase made lese lyttell space lande echone afore flee troylus sworde suche cruelte maugre fielde hath wonne tyme whan bryght sonne hye southe mydday marke shone euen houre drewe noone myrmydones gathred one compasse wyse rounde aboute hym gone furyously one entenciowne made cercle enuyrowne hym sawe helpe desolate herte dysconsolate vpon syde manlyhead lyke lyon toke theym hede famous knyghtly excellece tygre standeth diffence manfully gan encomber gan lesse dyscrease nomber maymeth woudeth ye death made yelden vp breath layde earthe lowe made ouerthrowe wyth hys swerde theyr bloud wete great myschyefe vnder horse fete vpon stede sturdy wall worthy knyght man mercial pleyeth play amonge myrmydones hym selfe god wot alone helples pbut tho ala might force auayle thre thousande knightes assayle euery parte lengthe brede cowardly fyrst slewe stede speres sharpe square ygroud whych ala stante ye grounde wythout reskuse refute socoure daye chyualrye floure well awaye haue beset head smote basenet brake harueys hym assaile seuer stele myghty stronge mayle dysarmed necke also heade ala whyle wyght toke none hede knyghtes longynge towne yet alway troyan champyowne knyghtly wyse naked phym selfe defendeth tyll achylles ala came rydynge furyous wood wha sawe howe troylus stode longe fyghtynge awhaped mate folkes alone disconsolate sole hym myschyefe pyteously achylles wonder cruelly behynde vnwarely toke hede swerde smyteth heade cast forthe cruell cursed herte thought sure hym asterte shewe malice wolfe vnmercyable full vnknyghtly vengeable vpon body dead laye colde ala euer knyght tolde wryte rehersed foule deede boke ala men shall rede knyght storye horryble vnto eares passyngly odyble achilles crueltye ala dead corp toke taas vengeably bonde fynde tayle horse behynde hatefully euery wyght behelde drewe selfe endlonge felde renges wardes oh ala euer fall knyght herte cruell hatred spytefull fell drawe man deade oh thou homer shame red ye amase yt holdest thy selfe wyse achylles set suche great pryse thy bokes chyualrye aboue echone dost hym magnyfye sleyghty full fraude geuest thou hye prayse laude pcertys homer thy excellence rethoryke sugred eloquence thy lusty songes thy dytees swete thy hony mouth doth wyth sugre flete yet one thynge thou greatly art blame causeles gyue hym suche name tytle suche tryumphe glorye passyngely put memorye thy bookes saye wryte thrugh knighthod slain hath hector two first yt lyke vnto none pand sith troilus yt owne brother thou arte meued affection whych thou hast grekes nacion preyse thou caust endyte thou shouldest aye fauour wryte trouthe playnly indyfferent saye sothe clerely entente pfor slewe hector felde afore disarmed shelde busy eke spoylynge kynge yf beware comynge hym quyt chyualrye false deceyt trecherye ne lyghtly gone palso troylus naked alone amyd thre thousand closed yshet pwhen achilles hath head smet backe full cruell herte nothing treason dyd aduerte pwas dede manly knyght slee man forweryed fyght faynt trauayle longe daye amonge many standynge baye kynges sonne hye borne naked head armure torne euen death selfe poynt great myschyefe playnly ioynt lyfe standynge wrake pwhen achilles came falsly bake assaylynge hym halfe deade lyke cowarde smote heade tofore hurte wounded sore pwherfor homer ne praise therfore let prease thy royall booke difface haste renowne outrace name neuen veryly vp thirde heauen semeth infecte eyre sowne therof foule vnfayre vsed aduertence eye prouydence vnto knyghthod worthynesse manhode gentyllesse renowne owne name reporte knyghtly fame wyse haue taken hede hadde neuer done foule dede vengeably haue ydrawe kynges sonne slawe namely hym good knight whyche tyme loke aryght passed achylles dare well expresse manhode gentylnesse nowe dead ala pthe death pollydamas parys eke fyrst gan espye fared sothe woulden dye specyally wyth face dead fade pparys ala suche inly sorowe made constreynt deadly wo sawe well troylus ago shall lyfe neuer se suche sorowe also troyan dan enee hym hath made many mo one togyther go dead corp recure maye pbut grekes fell daye theyr haste vtterly vayne wyse corp get agayne tyll menon noble worthy kynge whych loued troylus ouer thynge caught routhe affection haste fearser lyon death cast wreake fyrst ire thus gan speake achylles hye treasowne oh thou tratoure oh thou scorpyowne oh thou serpent full trecherye whych dishonour chyualrye false engyne hast daye yslawe onely best hadde felowe whylom worlde alyue ala ala maye aryght deseryue thy venym hyd thy malice vntrouthe wythout pyte knyghtly routhe drawe knyght gentyll good kynges sonne worthy bloud ye feld thy horse tale behynde euer shalbe mynde cruell dede vngentylnesse pand wyth yt word menon gan dresse towarde achylles wythout areste wyth spere smet brest enuyously great hatrede vnneth kepte stede menon pulled swerde cast hym manly mete berde rode fully deuoyde dreade suche wound gaue head maugre many mannes syght earthe made alyght pryde mortall traunce wound felt greuaunce death laye huge whyle swowne space halfe myle tyll myrmydones assembled one great laboure hente vp anone full deadly pale gan blede set stede last hert caught agayne smet horse hate hye disdayne towarde menon fast gan hye cominge gan espye full lyke knyght lyst abyde hit horse sharply syde mette achilles proudly playne wyth theyr swordes togither layne gan hurtle horse backe tho yfere wyth herte enuyous despytous chere pbut kynge menon auauntage achylles wood rage poynt abrought confusyowne tyll yt wardes newe comen downe parte yonder whych sodaynly seuered asonder story telleth playnly began slaughter many manly man nother party felde ne would leue pryde tyll drewe eue phebus gan aswage hete gan bathe wawes wete bryght beames occyan fro felde home goth euery man theyr lodginge seuen dayes faught yfere made delayes pfull mortall cruell aduenture whyle achylles full busy cure woundes grene sore sounde newe treason founde venged vpon kynge menon wytte sette thervpon cruell enuyous achilles ycharged hath myrmydones worthy menon amonge theim enbrace hym founde opportune place theyr might theyr busy thought theyr handes escape nought tyll hym selfe auenged hym pand befell menon se nexte morowe lyke manly knyght agayne grekes armed fyght troye syde wonte auenture daye yt fell achilles menon mette eche theim gan sette horse backe wyth full great emiye longe theyr melancolye mine auctour wryt togyther fyght eche made force alyght pand whan menon stode vpon ye grounde myrmydones wente aboute rounde charged fyerse achylle ala wythout goddes wylle dysseuered knyghtes myschyefe vpon fall destitute alone helples suche poynt slewe achylles story lyke founde menon fyrst gaue wounde tofore death fell stryfe dyspeyred lyfe achylles false treason take hede homer demeth thy reason false fraude sleyghty gyle treason caste afore wyth many wyle achylles iudge ryght euer slewe worthy knyght yt preodycyon recorde take kynge menon tytle laude ala entriked wyth fraude fallace pthat thou homer mayst coloure though thou paynte gold wt asoure thy wrytynge venym enclose thorne hyd vnder rose whose malyce aye dareth roote though floure aboue fayre soote men fraude vnder may se treason ye get bvt wyll tell grekes day meneste kynge menelay dyomede thelamonyus troyans passyng despytous cruelly wyth theyr wardes theyr myschyefe vpon fall made theim flee home vnto towne whylom troylus chyefe champyowne deade ala hath nowe forsake haue dead body take daye great difficulte dolefully cyte haue tho brought cry oft ala death wo trowe man alyue whych could aryght halfe dele descriue theyr pyteous wo lamentacyowne certeyse boy hath suche renowne drery wordes wepe crye pin complaynynge phylosophye throughe boke accusynge aye fortune selde nought one contune full transmutaciowne oh stace thebe make bost sowne drerynesse wryte nother death festes funerall makynge sorowe aduersyte plet thy wepynge oh thou nyobe pye syster also ayeliager custome haue flee fer fro yere yere brother complayne thou weptest thine eyen twaine oedippus kyng thebe cyte thou wofull myrrha calyxtone well rage bemene dydo eke whylome cartage quene lette dole contrycyon pand phyllys eke thy dymophon pand eke cecho newe dost begyn crye wayle also thou corynne whylom great affray death onely thy popyngay boke telleth v ouyde let wo layde asyde make comparisowne vnto wo troye towne death onely worthy knyght loue euery maner wyght hygh lowe olde yonge age falle newe suche rage ne coulde wo none ende whose salte teares wyll eyen shende pyteous lamentaciowne euery strete throughout towne ala coulde sorowes telle pi trowe certeys pluto depe helle torment paynes kene nouther proserpyna quene nother wery wood tycius iryon hungry tantalus ne coulde well bytter peyne furyously wepen complayne troyans troylus thy sake nowe suche sorowe make por wepe kyng pryamus wepeth face full pyteous sorowe maketh hecuba quene pwho wepeth fayre pollycene wepeth nowe parys heleyne wepe teares reyne troyans deadly swole chere neded wepers hyer ynough owne store ala nowe euermore helpe sole comforte destytute shall nowe refute pnowe hector also deyphobus troylus eke vertuous dead ala shall succour helpe sustene werre cyte conclusyon death fully destruction theyr towres walles stronge matter shulde playne longe vayleth alway morne wherfore wyll agayne retorne matter tell forth kyng grekes hath without taryinge trewse peace ysent certayne tyme great auysement whyche graunted agamenowne ayene repeyred towne phowe parys slewe achylles archylogus duke nestor sonne temple apollo cap xxxii kynge pryamus dyd busye cure make ryche sepulture troylus corp full noble royall sayth guydo stone metall enclosed great affection pand nighe besyde kyng menon solempnely buryed laide graue day day haue lyke custome feste funerall ryghtes ceremonyall bothe dewe obseruaunce seruyse done aye contynuaunce temple lyke guyse whiche longe deuyse tedyus eke dwell purpose ceriously tell howe hecuba endyte caste fully achylles requyte tirannye sothly yf may vnto calleth day alexsaunder full secrete wyse vnto hym shall deuyse wepynge eyen full heuy chere sayde euen thus ye shall pparys quod ala saue goddes wyll thou knowest well howe fyerse achylle sonnes hath slayne well nye euerychone none lefte thy selfe alone hath made ala gayne full cowardly chyldren baraine hector troylus eke therto whiche euery trouble wo fully comforte pleasaunce solace wherfore caste playnely compase engyne death ordayne lyke treason dyd payne trayterously sworde smyte ryght thynke treason quite syttynge ryght equyte syth thou wotest platly hath sette herte loue clene vpon doughter yonge polycene fyne onely haue vnto wyue whiche caste hym sende blyue come treate mattere pin temple appollo temple moste chiefe cyte whiche tyme wyll thou thy selfe armed full pryuelye certayne knyghtes thy companye armed also agayne daye wyse ne scape maye handes dead haue saide therfore take good hede vnto thynge herte praye poynt poynt byddyng obeye assenteth hole herte behotynge shulde asterte hym toke twenty mo manly men ryght well durste temple full good aduyse pthey yhid biddynge parys whyle hecuba couert entente messager achylles hath sent ye haue herde conclusyowne come haste vnto troye towne effecte whiche myssage onely treate maryage haste commeth sonde coulde nothyng vnderstonde treason hyd playnly aduerte hote marked herte loues bronde fyry glede lyfe death toke hede sette syde wytte reason caste afore good discrecion lokynge full prudent soth loue blent troye whan shulde gone lyke fareth louers euerychone whan haue caught herte fantasye peryll though shulden dye haue myght power beware tyll vnwares trapped snare maladye aye furyous pand thus achylles anthylogus nestor sonne haue waye nome towarde towne togither come temple ye haue harde telle parys tho lyste longer dwelle vnwarely knyghtes achylles myschyefe fall eueryche sworde full bryght bokes saye done night whan death longe afore desyred pby hecuba parys conspyred pbut achylles mortall case amonge naked hent sworde selfe steuen lyke knyght slewe seuen force mauger myght pbut whan parys therof syght thre dartes raught kene square sodeynly ware full secretely hyd vnder shade markynge hym noyse made caste hym euen euer head shafte body ran therwithall knyghtes fewe sharpe swordes gan vpon hym hewe lefte tyll lay grounde pfull pale dead many mortall wounde ryghtfully reason syt thus fraude falshed quyt pof achylles hygh treason deth deth skylfully guerdon egall mede without fable pto mercyles vengeable thilke daye guydo wryteth thus achylles anthylogus pof parys temple slawe afterwarde bodye outdrawe achylle fro holy boundes cruelly throwen vnto houndes deuoured brode streste canell rennynge fylthy water wete without pytye maner routhe lo ende falshed vntrouth lo fyne suche trecherye false deceyte compassed enuye lo knotte conclusyon god aye quytteth slaughter treason lo guerdon fynall mede delyten falshede euery thyng platly sayne lyke guerdon doth attayne ye may se achilles whiche nyght temple le lyfe aye customable fraude treason vengeable pbut befell request heleyne bodyes ylke tweyne conserued hungry rage beste foule gredy ramage yet lay amyddes cytye full openly men myght se great gladnesse towne pinto tyme agamenowne kyng pryam sent massageres haue license fette home beares graunt haue corse take grekes suche sorowe make pytye routh eueryche spake thus vnto feare farewell truste nowe achylles dede farewell hope hooly spede farewell ioye chiefe diffence hadde manhode great excellence farewell ala souerayne assuraunce farewell knighthode suffysaunce ala vnlykely shall euer wynne getten cite v ala frowarde fortune myghten contune alway wo payne endure caused make ryche sepulture achylles stone precyous pand anthylogus shulde longer dwell ceryously rytes telle buryinge wo make wepynge clothes blake loure hode go mylke bloud dolefull herte fyre shete casten gummes swete amydde great flaumes funerall playes called pallestrall wrastlynge wake vayne vndertake tellen wherfore lette fully purpose lyke ye shall se resorte conclusyon tellen great agamenon lordes haste hath sent assembled tent full prudently kyng manly man great aduyse thus tale began syres quod fortune varyaunce chere froward double countenance sodeyne tourne false vysage hertes hath put suche arage murdre god man odyble pof achylles death horryble compassynge hecuba quene semeth shall sene manhode hertes knightly force aduersytye endure vertue suffraunce tyll death ye taken may vengeaunce manly quyte outragious offence whan time cometh make full recompence syth ye manly prudent wolde fyrst se playne entent matter wyse hereupon aduyse one assent voyce comune whether ye wyll werre forth contune syege ygonne vpon towne tyll brought destructiowne grece resorte agayne cause achylles slayne whilom strong champiowne distence chiefe protectiowne fynally dead hereupon let se reade saye openly longer tarye pand anone gonne varye grutche castynge fro standynge doute beste pand sayde tother syde lyfe death wolde ende abyde wytte rude partye gonnen conclude wolde efte home agayne retourne sayd wyll soiourne styll syege happe happe may thus treate longe day euery man lyke opynyon tyll laste conclusyon accorded fully one fro syege neuer gone vnto tyme haue towne knyghthode full possessyowne free wyll spylle elles saue albe achylles buryed graue truste euery worthy knyght fynally goddes haue behyght haste shall towne possede hope fully deuoyde drede vndispeyred opynyon pand anone ayax thelamon worthy knyght famous hande amonge tho grekes londe sayde euen thus playnly sentence psyres quod presence counsayle platly rede standeth achylles dead sonne haste sende hyther come se ende syege helpe v nede pwhiche nowe abyt kynge lycomede bysayle named pirrus hym call neptolonyus ryght lusty freshe lykelynesse able attayne great worthynesse reporte fame kouthe drawe hym armes youth pand sothfastly yf bokes lye haue redde herde prophecye fynally troye cyte without hym shall neuer wonne thus bokes saye olde memorye howe grekes shall haue victorye tyll come sonne achylles wherfore haste reckeles sende hym done anone commende counsaile euerichone reade fully assent aduise full prudently sente haste embassyat wyse kynge full famous estate meane prudent noble menelay forth goeth selfe day iourney gan hym faste spede ptyll came vnto lycomede olde kynge ye haue harde telle tyme wyll lette dwelle pand grekes meane whyle derecte againe style phowe parys thelamon ayax slewe eche fylde cap xxxiii tyme yere shene sonne crabbe course yronne hyghest ascencyon whiche called somer stacyon whan vertue euery roote drawen vp bawme soote croppe freshe floure lusty hewe coloure tyll phebus chare discencion crabbe towarde lyon holdeth course fyrmament meane whan retrogradyent dryeth vp moysture wete herbe floure feruent hete veer afore hym made grene white tourneth beames shene sede grayne decoction naturally dygestyon fyrst rawe fruites floures watry eke plente humoures dryeth vp rypeth full feruence men may pull eche kynde season fro yeare yeare reuolucyon braunches freshely sprede whan cheryes powbly rede pfirst iune seweth maye whan hote mery somers daye dwery lyke gyaunt longe tyme grekes stoute stronge rancour brent enuyous hete haue shapen foen mete bryght armed fyelde go troye towne also wardes ordeyned euerychone fyelde haue take meten foen gan assemble vpon outher syde pbut thelamon foly pryde daye hym reade death dread disarmed battayle arest mayle plate bare vpon brest foly surquedons outrage bare heade bare vysage bare also without basenet naked eke vyser palet rode daye nothynge tho aferde hauynge weapon naked sworde wylfully lefte home shelde spere toke fyelde full lyke knight syttynge stede pand hym foloweth dyomede lyke mar hym selfe hym meyne faste came duke meneste kyng vlixes agamenon pryamus wt troy towne toke eke fyelde wt full heuy chere feareful great dispeyre inly full dreade yssue syth hector nowe dede pworthy troylus also deyphobus hym selfe demed playnely thus febled greatly myght death grekes fyght goth hap hap maye parys eke full knyghtly array pkyng phylomene pollydamas pworthy esdre eneas one assent saye daye knightly lyue deye diffence vtterly ieoparte goddes lyste felde daye departe proudely fyrste grek gan perce parys tho perce fell syde sonne shene archer arrowes square kene grekes gan sondre disseuere felde myght persenere onely shot stronge archer perce londe arbalasters whiche made fle ryght nede pinto tyme proude dyomede whan grekes sawe sodeyne flyghte releue lyke manly knyght come vpon felly tene pand fyrste sette phylomene worthy kynge came troye syde whyche agayne gan hym ryde dyomede hath lyttell wonne swordes styffe togyther ronne beholde noble syght eche quyte hym lyke knyght togyther ran horse backe man coulde nother se lacke euer one troyans felle vpon grekes ne myght dwelle kepe londe made blede mauger force dyomede slaughter hydous stronge ye fielde woful noyse ronge mortall crye wounded folke laye slayne soyle endlonge waye ptyll meneste syttynge stede worthy duke gan take hede myschyefe grekes beset hent anone spere sharpe ywhet smyttynge horse felly syde renges knightly gan ryde stynt furyous ptyll mette pollydamas troyan knyght manly man vnwarely hym ran hytte many mannes fyghte erthe made lyght sworde grounde whan laye slayne selfe daye rage cruell tene ne kynge phylomene reskewed auenture whiche frendely hym dyde cure maugre myght menestee handes went free hathed spreynt bloude whyle ayax proudely rode surquedy wylfulnesse foly rage foule hardynesse naked body heade euerydele amyd foen armed bryght stele troyans suche slaughter made laye dead sonne shade throughout felde thelamon amonge rode woodder lyon troian none might tho withstade held bloudy sworde hand wonder naked rode without wounde longe abode pand guydo maketh rehersayle wryteth eke great meruayle vnslayne might longe contune whan thynge shapen fortune myght falle euer thynge weale wo ioye aduersyte whan one shall dye whan shall escape ala alder fyrst iape brynge man vnwarely myschaunce whan beste weneth haue assuraunce ladye transmutacyon lyke fell worthy thelamon daye whiche foly pryde amonge foen gan ferre ryde ylyche freshe ryght began pand slewe perce many manly man hym selfe toke maner hede knightly herte deuoyde drede tyll parys sawe great hardynesse howe knight dyd oppresse enchasynge mortally narowe without abode anone toke arowe extoxycat sharpe venymous ire fell despyteous shot hym selfe tyde sayth guydo smyt hym ye side hurte saye felte well must deye pand whan sawe none remedye rode supprysed enuye thrughout ye prese sword aye hand tyme parys fonde pand vnto hym pale chere spake sayd anone ye shall pparys quod mortall wounde thyne arrowe sharpe square yground hath fynally lyfe put dispeyre neuer grece haue repeyre ryght shall shorte conclusyowne awaye shape troye towne thy lyfe thou entre shalte herte venym byt sore gayne none death pbut yet tofore yelde vp breth truste ryght well may socour thou ne shalte predecessour go afore depe downe hell pluto eternally dwell ryght necessarye thy time set thou maiest tarye trouth morgage thy corse hast shall make deuorse atwyxe quene heleyne twynne sonder eke false cheyne whiche linked colour wedlocke hath longe shet vnder locke fraude false engyne also pbut nowe knotte shalbe broke two ryght hande trouth darayne cause onely twayne werre many worthy knyght lyfe hath loste many wight outher syde sake shall ende make loue foule auoutrye pfor fynally parys thou shalte dye handes thy chaunce ye word sword gan enhaunce aboue heade smote hym face fell dead selfe place heade hath parted twayne ryght forthwith saine payax ala mortall wounde fell dead also gruflynge vnto grounde full pyteously troye haue parys take vp weye bore hym home theyr cyte pbut dyomede duke menestee many greke rydynge enuyrowne sewed chase euen towne cause tytan gan lowe downe arke dayes bowe west vnder rowes redde hesperus gan lyght shede saye drewe nyght grekes repeyred home aryght eueryche theim lodgynge place take theyr reste nyghtes space psaue reade agamenowne grekes made fast towne sette theyr tentes pauylyons pryde fast wall habytacles newe mansyons troye dyspeyred ouer refute could grekes let assent fast theyr gate shette nyght walles wake ouer suche wo make cyte parys dead fynally nowe reade wepe crye sorowe euer one nowe al ye sonnes priam gone fortune ala hath theim appeyred theyr lyfe nowe dyspeyred hope good welfare perpetually lyue care vnto death faste bye nowe maner remedye vpon syde refute none theym kepe close wythin wall se pyteous thynge pand suche wo maketh kynge pfor parys death deadly smerte hym thought platly wofull herte recureles would brast ryue tweyne teares gan dystylle reyne would tho sorowe deye pand quene ala shall seye phecuba owne mother deare crieth wepeth woful cheare pof pollycene wo begone systren also euerychone haue theyr heir theyr clothes torne yf theyr owne death ysworne drery wo pyteous peyne pbut fayre quene heleyne wayleth cryeth deadly cheare eyen whych whylom cleare forderked dolefull teares smerte corp sodaynly sterte clypped yt armes twayne pyteously embrace restrayne lyke would dye anone styll laye dombe stone marbyll colde lymmes craumpishing redy towarde buryinge tyll men force corp hent heyr chekes rente tho fallen rage chaunged ala vysage natyfe coloure rody hewe whylom freshe rose newe nowe lyke vnto ash colde wyth handes aye togyther folde selfe smote pale face euer amonge corp embrace swownes fell grounde twenty tymes wept full wounde wyth wo awhaped amate comforte ala disconsolate herte beynge inly desyrous rage passynge furyous dye attones owne knyght towarde death enclosed syght lyst lyue nowe pand trowe neuer man woman sawe fall suche distresse suche disioynt deadly heuynesse wo pyteously yraue cleopatre goynge graue wofull tesbe fro kaue sterte whan selfe smote vnto herte pnor faythfull trewe orestylle sawe lord agayne pmarcus prolancus vnto shyppe gone loue fell downe dead anone pnor sorowe trewe iulia pnor feruence faythfull porcia whych one fell dead sodaynly sawe bloud spent cruelly lordes dredfull gardment pand portia trewe entent lorde brutus lost lyfe bycause myght haue knyfe wyth rolys red slewe selfe ala also selfe case parthemysya quene tarse londe mausalus graue whan foude owne knyght whose bone smale full wofully wyth cheare pale poudre made dranke euery morowe pbut wo furyous sorowe echone yet may atteyne pvnto sorowe quene heleyne fynally wyll selfe fordo parys sake loued wyll lyue daye awreke playnly yf maye vpon lyfe rather dysseuere thus wo aye doth perseuere herte parys sat depe palas sayth woman wepe yes doubtles haue nature though wo endure yet fayne salte teares fynde plenty ynough thryr owne kynde sorowles morne compleyne pi saye quene heleyne wyth wo wounded herte fro death wende sterte deathes darte herte made ryue yet rose agayne fro death lyue onely grace fell rage euery wo processe must aswage ouer gone wasted myracle eche venym made tryacle euery wo hath remedye pfor though heleyne tho fayn wold dye kynde ne would assent yet therto sodaynly slea selfe wo woman man shulde wyte lyste wo endyte lest vnto tedyous heren paynes furyous cruell wo lamentacion whych would meue compassyon sothe wryte euerydele herte though made stele pfor kynge pryam quene also suche routhe pyteous wo se wepe furyously complayne felte much payne pa dyd almost hym parys pherof pryam deuyse rage mortall wo amyd temple sacred iuno ordayned hath full busy cure corp ryche sepulture haste therin made shette sothenesse lette tell rytes gyse made theyr paynim wise costes buryinge longe taryinge ceryously theron abyde wherfore nowe let ouerslyde paynim rite supersticious phowe pantisilia quene amazonis comming ayde troians slayne pyrrhus achylles sonne ca xxxiiii telle wyll kyng priamus comauded hath mischyefe nede troye towne onely drede shytte theyr gate strongly maye therupon nyght daye kepe watche shortly troye dysconsolate theyr olde ioye refute wepe sorowe make ne durst vndertake agayne grekes felde gone ptyll daye kynge agamenon messager good auisement pryamus troye hath sent requyrynge manhode lyke knyghte yssue wyth grekes fyght wonte wyth chyualrye pbut kynge pryam axinge gan denye shortly sayd sent ne would assignement one passe gate towne owne free electiowne whan euer lyst without compellynge pand yet sothe cause taryinge pwas hardy quene femynye towarde troye fast gan hye lande lyttell regyon whych bokes make mencion scyte fyrmamente plage oryent pand called reygne amazonis custome vse onely woman therin shall abyde wonte armed ryde haue armes great experyence theyr laboure theyr dylygence fynally haue exercyse fro daye daye martes hygh seruyce pand ouermore theyr custome vsaunce daye made remembraunce man shall nygh nere yf thre monthes yeare pthis saye iune apryll maye woman haue custome aye vnto yle lytell besyde men selfe abyde fro yere yere togyther euerychone vnto men theyr lande gone abyde regyon tyll tyme cometh concepcion wythout taryinge longer whyle anone home vnto theyr ile repeyred countre vnto tyme delyuered fast chylde borne lacke kepynge lorne fostred tyll thre yeres agone amonge woman ryght anone yle besyde adiacent vnto men chylde haste sent kynde masculyne yf fall femynyne woman abyde styll shall tyll actes mercyall full well expert eke knowe spere haddle drawe bowe lyke statute regyon whych bookes make mencyon sette betwene ewrope asya pand lande pantasilia whylom lady chyefe gouernesse full renowmed strength hardinesse thrugh ye worlde length brede yet sothe speake womanhead myght huge pryse vertuous wyse wonder dyscrete honest name notwythstandynge excellence fame renowne armes glorye conquest high victorye surmountynge drede woman rede sothely yet bookes bere wytnesse womanhead gentylnesse kepte nothynge asterte pthe whych loued wyth hole herte worthy hector wyth myght onely good knyght ioye worldly plesaunce harty ease soueraygne suffysaunce sothe wake wyncke euer one vpon thynke fayth wythout slouthe vnto hym bonde trouthe confederate olde affectiowne herde troye towne beseiged grekes fell thys hardy quene lyst longer dwell hasteth fast euer maye towarde troye infull good araye worthy woman lande full well experte preued hande well horsed eke armed rychely fynde companye thousande maydens rydyng side worthy quene durst well abyde wyth brought stele armed bryght loue hector owne trewe knyght waye fast gan spede helpe hym yf se cause nede nothynge could delyte towarde faythfully quyte lust hertes ioye pbut come troye hath hard tell relacyowne dead worthy renowne louynge trewe anone gan chaunge cheare hewe pyteously gan wepe crye fared sothe would dye wo hertely heuynesse thought would thrugh wortthynesse auenge death platly maye grekes vpon daye pshe prayeth pryam wt great affectiowne open gate towne go grekes fyght maye knowe expert aright woman great worthynesse quene famous hardynesse kynge hopynge beste without abode graunted requeste next morowe whe pheb shone ful shene pand tofore goth philomene noble kinge wt pafflagonye knightes manye folowed worthy eneas troyan eke dan pollidamas quene pantasilla gate called dardanica towarde grekes proudly yssued oute woman rydynge aboute whych anone grekes espye felde gan fast hye fyrste worthy meneste pantasylla dyd se wyth sporres made stede gone wyth spere rode anone pof quene astoned neuer dele kaught spere squared wele round ye shafte head well grounde coupe smet hi downe groud maugre hym reued stede haste came dyomede cruelly quene gan ryde fast syde rode eke plate bryght shene met wyth theyr speres kene hytte fell diomede myght manlyhead made sadell lese myght tho chese despyte men echone hath shelde berafte anone delyuereth proudly rode mayde vpon abode lyke tygre gredynesse lyke sothe lionesse daye fared rydynge vp downe amonge grekes till thelamowne gan beholde slaughter made high despyte rancour ouerlade myght yre sustene gan reyne horse fall vpon quene pbut comynge dyd espye fell melancolye mortally maugre knightes grounde made fall grekes put great disraye euer rode ylke daye ne might afore sustene helpe kyng philomene myn auctour recordeth boke amyd felde thelamon toke sent forth hie renowne prysoner towarde troye towne ptyll vnto reskuse came dyomede cruelly gan lede fell vnwarely huge route knyghtes rydynge aboute theyr hades maugre al might delyuereth lyke manly knyght whych tyme hardy quene anone woman aboute euerichone grekes hath afore playne wryt guydo mortally belayne made necessytee felde wyth sworde fle verely semed incredible leue maner impossyble se woman grekes enchase might abide afore face felde wise stande dryue selfe stronde downe clyffe salte see slewe huge great plentee fynally dystroyed euermore vtterly acloyed pne dyomede stande tho diffence knighthod made theim resistence daye partye grekes stode sturdy wall alone helpe chefe succour pbut worshyp honour pantasilla made memorye repeyred conquest victorye wyth woman troye towne vpon houre phebus goyng downe pand syde hardy quene parmed stele rode kynge phylomene pryam hath wyth great reuerence knightly receyued diligence theim refreshe euery maner thinge might vnto theyr lykinge theyr hertes could best deuyse pand ful goodly wyse thanked hath noble hardy quene goodnesse lyst sene helpe great nede offred guydo reade hath treasour rychesse hopynge fully worthinesse vpon grekes auenged kepe hym safe cyte maugre grekes whych theim saye naye pfor reade daye daye slinte proudly theim assayle agayne whose swerde myght auayl mortally made theyr sydes blede ptyll menelay fro kinge lycomede repeyred neptolonyus bokes called eke pirrhus whylom sonne cruell achillles se full huge prese grekes goynge enuyron pand successyon pborne heyre achilles hath receyued myrmydones great honour great solempnyte glad theyr yonge lorde se echone made affiaunce eke sworne bonde assuraunce lyfe deathe trewe liege chaunge newe obeye lust maner thynge pand agamenon kinge made knight thelamonius wyth swerde gyrte anone pirrhus sayinge selfe place yt baudrik hym enbrace ptake hede quod mine owne cosin deare resemble manhode chere knighthod eke worthinesse thy father sothfastnesse tyme noble knight ouermore thy full might auenge death thou thy payne pand grekes worthy duke twayne full humbly began downe knele set sporre vpon eyther hele maner golde bourned bryght whyle pirrhus made knighte ye haue herde full high presence great honour due reuerence lyke custome grekes layes rytes vsed tho dayes anone hath kyng agamenon full glad chere great affection delyuered hym fully sentence armes hole without difference achilles life bare worthy father shoulder square nexte heyre lyne discente treasour also tente armure deliuered anone vnto pirrhus grekes euerychone eyght dayes suynge hoste full solempnely halowe honour yong knyght til morow whe pheb shone ful bright lyght shineth fro fer diffaced hath streames sterre lucifer dayes messagere grekes gan plate bryght clere enarmed daye soure swete fulle purpose wyth theyr fone mete manfully theyr tentes wide agaynst troyans began ride warde warde proudly felde pirrhus bare daye vpon shelde father armes lyke sayth guydo vpon also cote armure became hym wele forth rode armed bright stele casually formest mette fyrst wyth pollydamas knyght troye full manly man pand furyously pirrhus ran horsebacke myghty swerde gan hurtle berde myghtely hatefull stryfe ppollydamas lost lyfe ne ben reskued without taryinge phylomene noble worthy kinge onely knighthod worthynesse pto pirrhus hastely gan dresse swerde smit syghte horse made alighte stroke might sustene sothfastly worthy phylomene pirrhus ytake anone saue knightes assembled one pafflagonye came reskue pirrhus aye fyersly gan pursewe vpon king myrmydones beset myschefe amonge great prese many knight noble kynge yslayne reskuynge stode death streyght case ptyl fortune came pollydamas reskuse full myght delyuer quyte lyke knight sothenesse suche resystence pof pirrhus knightes standing diffence aye mischyef stode king philomene ptyll pantasilla femenie quene woman great companye gan thinge auenture espye echone delyte theyr armure daye clad white veryly lylye floure snowe yt flaketh fro iubyters towre whytenesse fresher sene felde hardy quene firste amonge grekes chees proudly fall myrmydones amonges rydinge vp downe vnhorseth hie renowne slewe vpon euery syde makinge theyr renges seuer wyde tyll thelamon furyous heate spere vnwarely mete rage smote playne anone ful lyfely rose agayne pand wt swerd marketh thelamown fro horse made light downe plat grounde handes twayne woman theyr busy payne make theyr quene stede recure pand stode auenture life worthy philomene pirrhus knightes kene maugre men haue take geyneth diffence make grekes haue strongly beset pand forth lad might bet toward theyr tentes throughout al felde thinge quene behelde woman aboute rode pursewed without abode fynally haue sewed force reskued maugre manhode myrmidon pand pantasilla mercyles vpon grekes necessyte force crueltee afore swerde durst abyde pbut pirrhus sawe great pryde knightes loud gan crye sayde shame villanye woman lese theyr lande slayne felly hande wherfore echone hertes doth resume assent let v nowe consume pryde none awaye escape remedye shape ylke daye theyr force confounde shamefull reporte v shall rebounde perpetually slepe wake pand pirrhus gan swerde take furyously wyth knyghtly chere hardy quene happed heare pall pirrhus knightes spake lyst one tourne bake thret take hede platly dreade right proudly gan drawe nere sayde anone ye shall heare poh thou pirrhe sonne achilles slewe hector knyghthod pereles trenys trecherye malice onely false enuye vnware nothinge aduerte whych neuer maye herte grene sticketh remembraunce vpon death vengeaunce syt well semeth vnto death venged vpon fyrste thy father bloud loue gentyll good deth shuld al ye world coplayne onely men theyr busy payne quyte death woman eke also theyr myght helpe eke therto right requyreth without excepcion full execution nowe stande plyte thou hast v wonnen despite power shortly sentence thou shalt haste haue experyence knowe force sothly euerydele right shorte tyme truste right wele felde shedynge thy bloud wherfore pirrhus gan wood tygre bore wood lyon fret coloure complexion ire fell despytous toke spere pale furyous ran al myght payne agaynwarde list feyne encountred hym deuoyde feare pirrhus fyrste brake spere albe myght remeue sadell lyttel greue agayne sore gan hytte stede maye sytte descendeth endlonge playne vp rose full great disdayne toke swerde hande anone made stede lyne ryght gone vpon quene passynge worthinesse inwardly hate woodnesse herte yfret smet many stroke euer sat styll oke force yre pale efte agayne made auale earthe maugre payne thus fyght lasteth theym twayne large whyle till myrmydones haue take theyr lorde force ye prese made horse recure agayne pand tyme selfe playne baner descended downe worthy kinge great agamenowne kinges duke endlonge grene theyr wardes wonder sene prudently felde battayled hath troians mortally assayled pbut tho haste kynge phylomene ye haue herde reskued quene hath thanked worthinesse knightes gan dresse pand pantasilla assembled one vpon grekes gan gone men may se wt speres sharpe grounde eueryche beare vnto grounde men maye se proudly without lacke manly knightes renne horse backe pand woman mortally oppresse fell grekes theyr hardynesse onely force myghty quene dead laye couerynge al grene pwherwith came dan pollydamas fro death reskued eke eneas pkinge esdras eke troye cyte pand tho wardes gan togyther fle eyther partye fell furious neptolonius pirrhus hight ye grekes champiowne irous wood troye towne made swerde theyr fleshe byte pand pantasilla proudly quyte ne spareth wyth mortall woundes wide grekes slee vpon euery syde theyr confusyon pand pirrhus fall glawcon halfe brother pollydamas anthenor eke father pirrhus cruell yre melancolye newe set fyre smote glawcon toke hede amonge prease fell downe dead pand pantasillya woman pthe tyde pirrhus fall syghte rode eke agayne lyke manly knyght hurtle horse backe yfere auenture swerdes styffe clere eueryche made alyghte hatefully fote fyghte longe myght wynne tyll made force twynne wardes wente atwene meane pirrhus hardy quene pand tyme dan pollydamas wood yre herte amyd grekes brother deathe mette loue sleth without mercy hateful tene alone worthy quene suche slaughter grekes make felde vtterty forsake gan fle theyr tentes downe tyll dyomede ayax thelamowne pyrrhus eke made tourne agayne sothe ouerlayne ne myght daye releue thus faughte tyll drewe eue domage grekes syde tyll phebus gan bryght chayre hyde lowe west shroude lyght vnder courtayne blacke nyght eyther parte thought best departe drawe theyr reste toke theyr ease nyght may moneth suynge day daye without interrupcion fought yfere albe mencion made therof wryte specyall person generall euer dyd euyll well troye boke fynde neuer dele saue quene lyke wryt guydo woman hundred hath forgo slayne thylke moneth daye death playnly maye shall well quyt fortune fauorable frendly contune face chaunge contrarye euery daye varye ala whyle selde one soiourne gan fro quene loke awaye tourne enhaste vngoodlyhead attropose breake lyues threde storye playnly shall lere beningly ye lyst heare fatall houre harde remewe cruel deth may eschewe lyfe fynally escape specially parchas haue shape approche gan may none bene ala whyle hardy quene pwhych daye furyous wrothe felde troye goth gan grekes proudly sette alderfyrst pirrhus met mortall hate indignaciowne haste renges downe rode vnto swyftly stede whose spore sharpe made side blede mette speres reste bare euen markynge breste theyr shaftes sothly tale gan shyuer peces smale without bowynge backe chine neyther made enclyne saue head forged harde stele pantasillia grounde wele pirrhus herte perced hath depe plate soth maile might kepe sharpnesse speres head bloud party redde stroke grekes gan espye astoned loude gan crye attones noyse sowne vpon quene felde came downe compasse wyse goynge enuyrowne thrugh prowesse high renowne defendeth meruayle ala sore gan assayle hewe haue basenet amyd grekes thycke beset wyth ax swerdes square shelde sothe made bare shoulder naked eke ala mayle hewen rere bra pand pirrhus like founde anguishe onely grene wounde doubte playnly eskape towarde quene faste gan rape auenged whatsoeuer fall amyd felde amonge grekes pand sawe came faste force onely mete yet cast wyth swerde fyrste gan assayle stroke happed fayle amonge prese narowe besette pand pirrhus sworde sharpe whet sodaynly arme smet ala none armure lette raceth al shoulder bone quene fel downe dead anone malice venge herte yre fret sore chere anger pale hath hewen peces smale whych foule cruell dede pbut euer one pirrhus gan blede nigh death mortall wounde lacke bloud fell grounde traunce full longe groflynge laye tyll knyghtes haste may haue take vp laid shelde dolefully home felde haue borne wounded pand woman quene ala sorowe inwarde deadly wo sawe theyr lady ago dead desyrous haste wood furyous rage without gouernayle grekes gan newe assayle auege quene wer herty kide slewe sothly fynde two thousad grek wood oh ala great dysioynt stode onely lacke haue gouernour gon yt theyr chiefe succoure whych also speake hardynesse woman al lady maystresse hande rede oh ye troians ye stande great dread amid ye felde gouernaunce daye come vnhappy chaunce nowe haue ye leder none guyde farewell truste euery syde grekes vpon stronge ye felde maye kepe longe caste felly quyte daye dare lyst endyte wryt homeward drawe ten thousand troians grek slawe theyr wardes came attones downe mortally wythout excepciowne kylle slee al withstode vpon woman wood auenged playnly reade euery halfe theyr bloud shede without mercy remyssyowne chasynge troyans home towne felde ma none abode pyteously tho wyth stode ne none recure caste kepe theyr towne shit gate faste theyr hope clene agone fyght wyth theyr fone theyr trust knyghthod away theyr worthy men slayne welawaye refute none theyr cyte kepe close maye none theim thought might kepe longe walles mighty stronge plenty vytayle though ye worlde attones assayle may sure kepe theim euermore men shall wyn yet neuerthelesse earely eke late grekes made tofore euery gate full myghty watche awayte full stronge wyth preuy spyes goynge amonge theyr foen none escape away none engyne ferforth maye pand whyle wythin troye towne make descriptiowne quene great sorowe euery wyght eue morowe ala slayne mede aldermost ne myght haue dead corp burye graue reuerence wyth honour dewe whych gan grekes sewe great prayer wyth great busynesse vayne ydelnesse theyr request yt grekes wrothe fynally wyth many sondry othe onely malyce hote enuye dead corp theim denye shortly sayde mortall enmyte houndes shall deuoured gayne racour copesse pbut pyrrhus gentylnesse ne would assent foule dede wood wroth cruell dyomede sayde openly syttynge fayle buryinge slaine hadde many worthy man thus stryfe amonge grekes gan great rumoure alteraciowne tyll laste vnder troye towne haue dead corp ytake cruelly profounde lake haue cast let lye vnto troye agayne wyll hye tell forth lyue pyne oh cruell mar yt hast made fyne thyne yre al ye worthy blode troye ala hast thou wood agaynst slee theyr knightes hast thou let thy bitter venim fall theim ala thou sterre infortunate wyth worlde make debate oh hatefull sterre hote combust drye fyryirous grounde enuye hasty euer ful discension coleryk thy complexion murdre death aye thy delyte takinge vengeaunce thin appetite first meuer anger hate roote contek causinge debate stryfe murmur thy desyre fearfull loke wylde fyre gastfull euer thy wood syght leuen flawminge thy lyght lyke twyncklynge spakes redde great fyres abrode sprede consumynge aye melancolye hertes embraced wyth enuye thy wrathe aye fretynge kene causeth men longe lene comsumpt sklendre browne citren hewed vnmercyable right euell thewed wonder sleyghty engenyous compassynge suspecyous tryste solen full heuynesse assentynge cursednesse awaytinge death roberye murdre also trecherye without remors conscyence venymous thine influence helper arte vnto false treason house scorpyon crowned arte caprycorne bull thy kingdome lorne therin thy deiection thy power loste dominacion hast also thy subiection exyle werre chaynes pryson proscripsyon captyuyte thy malyce troye cyte would god could chyde aryghte hast theim kydde thy fell myghte thy rancour hooly outtraunce first theim vengeaunce speres sharpe swerdes kene whette nowe pryson enclose shet vengeably dare grekes fell aye lying holde maner wyse thy temple sacrafyse nother bulles wt bore wylde beastes euer vnmylde tygres beares wood lyon whych thou arte souerayne patron hold brymstone smoke thyne aulters whiche art felly wroke theym ala worst thou hast shad chefe thy gall amonge selfe bryng treason fayned trouthe symulacyon make hertes amonge selfe deuide lo serpent dyscorde gan glyde full slyly tyll haue caughte place voyde awaye happe grace venym dyscensyon spred regyon common borough towne cyte amonges men high lowe degre hertes loue one farewell fortune theyr grace clene agone dyscorde holdeth resydence well worse swerde pestylence worse ferre nere foe famylyere maye harme yf lust enemye vpon men trust descriue shortly clause roote trewe cause myschyefe confusyon euery lande discenscion peryllous yf pryuye recorde take troye cyte founde fortune frendly aye nede tyll longe hid hate gan abrode sprede prudence sothly hath prouyded renge selfe deuyded shall recureles tourne wylde waste dweller desolate haste mar enuye lorde amonge selfe sowen hath discorde agayne whych maye sucoure worse werre sothly semeth treason cured vnder fayned peace pand roote olde anchises pwith sonne called eneas dan anthenor pollydamas haue contriued amonge theym vtterly vnder veil conceyued secretly fall grekes troye haue fyrst maye theyr owne lyues saue engyne sleyghtes treate maye caste maner waye would rather traytours troye pryuely spyed couertly grekes ben allyed stande hole wyth towne trouthe wylfully neclygence slouthe suraunce othe olde made towne refuse playnly conclusyowne allyaunce let slake slyde theyr lygaunce set also asyde theyr aduyse thought beste theim caste lyue reste meryer eke ernest game saue theyr life wandre forth shame wylfully dye mischyefe trayish town held reprefe might escape selfe alyue lyst nothynge towne stryue sought sothe soure swete meane waye lyue queet therupon haue theyr waye nome vnto kinge yt come presence full couert wyse vnder coloure began deuyse tell theyr tayle fynally ptheyr counsayle pryam vtterly maner reckles pursewe grekes peace get maye yelde againe king menelaye without stryfe freshe quene heleyne ouermore disdayne harmes done parys gon full yore citheron iustly restore bvt oh ala false iniquytye counsayle rose vnder secrete venim sugre vnder gall well wyste grekes ne would accorde conclusyowne haue peace troie towne whyles mischyefe brought treate therof sothe nought pfor pryamus hecuba quene sonnes pollycene yet left wyth towne myght haue reygned longe successyowne grekes full repented vnto peace hooly assented pbut counsayle gyuen late sythen grekes well elder date profered fyrst tenedowne aduyse kynge agamenowne fynall peace shortly seyne would restore agayne heleyne amendes requyred reason damage wrought cytheron messangers fyrste whan sente pryamus wolde assente requeste iustly brought peace meanes sought pryde denyed wylfulnesse ala guyded lacke onely wyt prudence nowe haue wt cost great dispence slaughter men many great damage sharpe shoutes cruel rage abyde fully mortall werre full sure wyll differre tyme forth treate peace lyste nothynge reckelesse vnaduysed ought trowe ye wyll lyghtly go home grece without recompence wolde seme neglygence speake therof wyll specyally troye cyte myschyefe stande vpon fynall fate remedye shape late grekes thought ryght truste troye stode luste holdynge selfe veryly victours foen fully conquerous without doubte ambyguyte counsayle ylke enee pof anthenor anchyses ye haue herde treate peace ne rose sothe doublenesse onely treason hyghe falsenesse pryamus conceyueth theyr chere lyke boke ye shall pfor daye whan pryamus sonne called amphymacus counsayle helde towne three haue made suggestyowne vnto kynge touchynge treate anone discrete aduyse prudently woulde assente gan vndergrope playnely mente onely wytte discrecion put execucion makynge therof maner delaye proudely standyng baye anthenor without reuerence spake kynge open audyence shortly saide sterne chere lyst counsayle heare therafter platly thou mayst chese thou wylt thou wynne lese fyne thou gettest worke thy counsayle kynge wonder soberly answered agayne full beningenely syr anthenor ye ought greue myne entente repreue wyse counsayle prudent rede conclude common spede people saluacyon wyte ryght well iustly reason vnder suger cured gall preiudyce lyeges causynge myschyefe fyne wyll vtterly declyne ryght requyreth alder ease semeth displease thy conceyte none offence euery man holden prudence worst leue better take wysedome sewe folye forsake remedye seke sore worde troian anthenor sodayne yre gan chaunge bloud abreydynge fete stode full felly sayde vnto kynge pnow sykerly wonder thynge wysedome auysenesse blynded wylfulnesse ye maye syde se great myschyefe aduersytee vpon euery syde maye dissimule hide disioynt playnly stande foen also hande haue beset wall rounde aboute feare dare yssue oute bolde vndo gate fyght v deadly hate feble stronge sothly yet haue amonge fyfty kynges worthy renowne confederat destructiowne therupon platly wyll abyde whych vowed haue theyr great pryde neuer parte hense fro towne tyll walles tourned vp downe worthy sonnes also dead wont helpe nede manly knyghtes slayne euerychone v saue remedye none vayne treaty dyffence wherfore read reason prudence slayne cyte lese two harmes least chese saye entente syttynge expedyent treate peace longer feyne herewythall restore agayne heleyne loue many worthy man hath lost lyfe sythen werre began nowe parys vnder stone ygraue best rede sothe ye maye haue sende home agayne menelaye profre fer forth ye maye restore within littell whyle harmes done parys yle whych men wont cithera call reade afore wyth word vp rose amphimacus counsayle full contraryous shortly sayde shall pa anthenor hath rade degre euer thus without respyte spake hygh despyte thou anthenor haue espyed wele may truste neuer dele wyth v stande great nede trouth fayth nowe deade falshed hath slayne stabilnesse stede thy sykernesse fynde sothly varyaunce become fayth thy lygeaunce hestes made stande wyth thy kinge thine othes double meaninge hyd thy olde assuraunce become thy fayned false constaunce stede whych mutabylyte hath take place like ye maye se dewe chaunge thou art remewable vpo ground thou mayst stande stable thy trouth gone olde affectiowne yu shuldest haue stand ye towne fayth v lyue deye truste hope exyled aweye thy persone shortly wryte busy arte kynge excyte disencrease estate royall vnto grekes thrall seke peace dread thou shouldest rather thy manlyhead haue profered citye diffende thy lyfe outraunce dispende wherfore sothe assure rather shoulde endure twenty thousande shall spere shelde vpon daye slayne felde thy worde holde prophecye procedeth trecherye doubilnesse false treason vndermyninge prodycyon though thou outwarde shewe fayre venym hyd thy tayle doth repayre lyke serpent styngynge vnder floures thereby fele counsayloures pand whyle wordes despytous pfull bytingly hath amphymacus pall openly anthenor repreued counsayle agreued seynge treason would mene tyll eneas gan go betwene floryshed speche full flatterye gan tale modefye lyke mente trouth entente pbut therin double attendemente spake one yet mente twayne pamphymacus onely refrayne attempre melancolye onely tyll might time espie like purpose maye procede execute fully vp dede founde space vnder pretence trewe face tale gan breake oute many troyan standinge aboute shortly sayde conclusyowne touchynge diffence playnly towne howe henge onely balaunce hope trust assuraunce cyte taken haue theyr flyght fynally manhod myght knyghthod togyther ago grekes haue ado theim stoutly fyght whych hath lost many worthy knyght redy vpon v set dare gat vnshet ala supprised wyth dread semeth great nede pby good aduyse seke meane matter shall v demeane pand parte sothfastly saye knowe nowe none redy waye prudentlye peace treate pbut pyram sodayne heate without abode cheare face pale rancoure gan interrupte tale attempre myght herte fretingely treason made smerte pand myght selfe restrayne thus sayde vnto twayne anthenor also enee wonder greatly ye hardy trouthe shame varye ye rebell contrarye onely false collusyon v brynge desperacyon lyeges yf shall fayne false entente catche v trayne ala howe maye herte fynde agayne nature vnkynde whylom counsayle chefe euery thynge brought prefe pfor ye absente could nothynge fyne nowe ala ye caste declyne awaye fro barayne lefte sole remembre great dole wyght ala chaunge shall truste man ye founde double entente ye thynke assente counsayle aduyse whylom sente forth parys grece full yore ago pand anthenor thou wotest thy selfe also thou fyrste made imbassadour therupon chyefe counsaylour touchinge sonde made exeon cause
