mocyon though sothe parys shulde go grece thou wotest well ne durste presumpcion haue sente parys vnto citheron without aduyce auctorytye eneas playnly vpon grekes werre haue gonne trowe sothe neuer konne excuse selfe aduysed euerye thynge wrought deuised execute counsayle twayne parys went heleyne grounde roote speake speciall thou enee cause principall present also euery thing wrought grece hither brought sothe regyowne neuer come towne thou haddest therto contrayre albe thou wouldest thy wordes fayre thy selfe excuse audience thou knewe nought offence fully vnwittinge dede nowe sonnes euerychone deade ye se alone destitute counsayle chyefe refute pursewe grekes peace foryetell reckles remembre infinite outrage mortall werre slaughter damage cruelte destructiowne haue wrought herupo towne veryly recorde dead accorde treate like ye deuise espye many sondry wyse entente right peryllous snare couertly vnder falshed dare wyll confusyon ye acheue entencion fynally ye haue shape impossyble escape shamefully myschyefe dye without recure remedye fyne knowe doubte treate ye aboute pand ryght anone troian eneas yre rancoure ameued agayne kynge swellynge herte sodaynly dore sterte awroke full many worde agayne kynge yspoke wente waye anthenor also pand pyramus yre wo sodainly braste wepe might selfe anguishe kepe anger fret vpon sore within selfe conceyuinge euydence discrescyon couert guyle false treason cyte yshapen haue auysed dredynge aye ylke twayne engyne conspyred trayne grekes would hym betrayet wherfore kynge caste would saye shape awaye theyr malyce withstande treason toke hande onely ryght dede founde vpon selfe myght agayne rebounde full execucyon theyr contryued conspyracion resorte agayne ful dewe wyse onely theym gan fyrste deuyse treason treason conuenyent falshed guerdon pertynente shamefull deathe fynall mede wherfore shape great nede pa remedye olde pryamus pcalleth sonne amphymacus pytyously alone twayne teares drowned gan complayne anthenor eneas sayde sonne take hede case thynke thy father deare yfere sonnes lefte wyth alyue thou alone therfore blyue touching ye treason conspyred ysworne eu r fall let v toforne onely wysedome away make maye fyrst trappe theim take puruey theym euen ylyche iustly maye fall dyche whych haue made v ytreyned haste let ordeyned matter close kept mewe fyne onely eschewe slayue equite ryght place euen towarde night purpose playnly theyr sake agayne houre counsayle make vnder coloure make call thou vnwarely shalt vpon fall knightes sworne vnto matter secre right anone amphimacus nede men stande dreade great awayte vpon layde happeth thinge sayde one spoke lordes mouthe falleth ofte full kouthe reported ysprad full wyde many coste theim stande asyde ware sodayne auenture hap prudence euery man charge tunge ouer large trouthes sayne wysedome sometyme fayne dissymule aduersytye specyally men trouble se theyr speche maye auayle better theyr tunge fayle folyly theyr domage agayne mischyefe mysauenture euery trouble trybulacyon susteynynge releuacion soueraygne helpe eke cyte whych neuer maye destroyed engyne men maye purchase goddes haue graunted grace vertue annexed eke therto troye sothe maye neuer fordo tyll relyke stole awaye yet sothe man maye place slere remewe preieste dewe onely offyce touche honde mightely conserued bonde attempteth conclusyon remewe palladyowne lyke clerkes wryte sayne pallas make towne certayne relike sente fro heauen downe conclude shortly reasowne cause purpose let pthan quod vlixus sith maye bet labour ydell vayne without although dylacyowne maner anone shall tell ye lyst whyle dwell without noyse perturbaunce pthe prieste whych gouernaunce relike shalbe spoke vnto good aduyse ytreated shall full assente golde treasour shal blent accorde shall purpose brynge relyke kept close place ye lyste assigne styll porte goodly benygne workes tyll haue brought fully thinge nothyng doubte dare selfe take well hande meaninge hym counsaylinge make delay call lordes agayne nexte daye lyeges assemble yfere fynally engroce mattere syttynge expedyent kinge open perliament crowned sat regalye anthenor gan specyfye audyence men saye naye contrarye anthenor sayde well euyll payde ful assent conclusyowne haste throughout towne collatours gathered vp golde lyke summe haue tolde poore ryche spared none whych tyme anthenor gone vnto priest called tonaunt might wise daunt make herte fully enclyne full craftely layde hooke lyne lusty bayte false couetyse excytynge full secret wyse would assente condescende vnto entente put possession relyke called palladion without abode maye delyuered gaue golde huge quantytye blend much behyght done pryuely nyghte shortly concludinge condescende would state amende passyngly euer heyres shoulde haue golde store plenty ynough none indygence shoulde haue power hym offence vnto vowe make quod anthenor platly vndertake golde good thou shalt haue suffysaunce treasour passynge habundaunce thou shalt sykernesse thy kyn excelle rychesse thou delyuer lyke myne axynge palladyon whych thy kepynge behote thou mayste trust bonde shalbe secree lest hyndrynge thy name thou dreadest shame esclaundred foule deede shape shall thou nede drede agaste maner wyse waye sothe shall deuyse man shall suspecyous thy person engenyous deme amysse matter goth well ware lothe diffamed foule thynge knowe therof assentynge maner towne shoulde haue suspecyowne let let leuer deye shall therfore caste wey honour saue thou shall go quyte saye vtterly neyther shall beholde ne perceyuere thefte stande hole clere euer fall without shame vlyxes shall beare blame dede thefe also men shall saye ago engyne sleyghty wyle traynes false guyle hath stole awaye palladyowne temple leasynge towne fynally durynge lyue men shall hym falshede descryue gylte arreten offence thou onely innocence throughout worlde iniquytye shall excused platly go free nedeth tarye mattere come attones lo thy golde thou ne shalt longer delayed sith thou seest difficultye parte perle reprefe shame dread slaundre mischyefe delaye take thinge hande first priest gan withstande full myghtely sayde nothinge nother prayer manasinge golde good ne maner mede ne would assente foule deede thus answered pryme face ofte sith happeth men purchase gifte good speake wordes playne trouth pouerte might neuer attayne mede falshed maye conquere tytle ryght men trouthe lere gyftes great hertes enclyne golde maye stele marbyll mine priestes herte hath depe graue anthenor shall purpose haue possede palladion false engyne contune without assaulte infortune leade lyfe prosperitye maydens remembreth vpon take ensample ye shall kepe ye wolde fewe teares wepe ye thynke vpon fayre pollyne age yeres grene whan slayne cruell auenture goddes haue cure dredfull goste holely betake eternally thus ende make pand yt word head gan enclyne full humbly shulde fyne eyen helde lede downe pand pirrhus wodder lyon dismembred hath sherpe sworde yonge made dredefull aferde ouer cruelte shewe peces smale hath hewe endelonge father sepulture ala myght cruell herte endure mercyles foule dede astoned sothly reade death hym good lyke tiraunt caste abrode bloude tygre routhe haue rounde enuyrowne father graue sprent hate cruelte oh thou pyrrhus thou mayste well ybe achylles sonne lyneall discent lyke hym herte entente thou soth deuoyde pytye worse yet one degree thy father lyuinge ne radde neuer yet foule thynge though wolde hatred abrayde rancour euer slewe amayde fynde well parte whylom loue cupydes darte made sore lyue smerte wounded herte castynge onely eye wenynge therby wystly dye myght sodeyne stroke escape afterwarde fate hath shape phe murdred loue pollicene thou haste slayne cruell tene furyously without routh shame whiche thynge foule hatefull fame al world hereafter shalbe spred story rehersed red shalbe sayd pirrhus routhlesse slewe yre mayde gyltelesse woryed shall thy name odyble dede passyngly horryble loue onely fayre pollycene death hecuba quene hath sene ala besyde stode wo gan wood sorowe wyt went clothes heire rent rage wot doth gan anone handes tothe furye scrache eke byte stone caste fystes smyte mette tyll grekes made bynde sente forth also fynde yle troye partment slayne onely iudgement grekes stoned death whan yelde vp breth wofull quene cruell auenture grekes dyd make sepulture ceryously metall stone toke corp buryed anone great honour solempnitee longe men might se ryche toumbe costfull royall set made memoryall hecuba whylom great fame gaue place name called longe mynde plocus festus guydo fynde thus quene onely sorowe wood whan doughter shad bloud grekes stone dyd ende make ye haue herde plainly sake policene whylom calchas vnto apollo falsly offred selfe gan dwellyng make fraudently folkes yllude full suttyll hym selfe illude ymages make holde forged syluer golde errour false illusyon hath ybrought confusyon mischance worthy kinde man syth tyme erthe derkenesse wo elues wont go vndyrmeles phebus shene nother fawny tender greues grene water nymphes naydes satyrye nother driades goddes wood wildernesse goddes nother lesse morpheus god slepe holde hym wood taketh kepe obseruaunce may fayle haue myschaunce ende playnely mede suche feyned falsenesse drede rose deuyll fyrst engyne sleyghty treynes serpentyne onely mankynde whan made loute false ydoles whiche doubte deuylles dauyd beareth wytnesse saulter wryt expresse confyrmeth endites howe goddes paganisme rytes one excepteth none made golde syluer stone forged brasse metall tree eyen haue yet may se fendes dauyd sayth haueth fayth hope credence delyte drede wyll hym quyte suche guerdon soule sleeth perpetually fyne death seruyce men hense pace lyfe vnhap euell grace mischyefe wo confusyowne men may se example towne wende well assured haue haue stande longe prosperitye agayne foen helpe apollo venus eke fauour iuno pallas might dyane mynerue wonte honour serue cerimonyes sacrafyce ye tofore haue herde deuyse haue brought ruyne cruell death bed fyne may ye se venym byte ende suche olde rytes euydence noble towne may auayle palladyowne may helpe frauded fantasye olde false ydolatrye ala ala bought sore farewell troye farewell euermore farewell ala cruell thy fall wryte shall thy sake forsoth whan take hede inwarde wo herte fele blede remembre thought ruine thou arte brought noughte whylom noble ryche worlde trowe none liche perygall speake fayrenesse speake knyghthode worthynesse clerkes say thy byldynge knewe worlde ought rewe thy piteous waste walles wilde whylom royall men gan bylde thy towres hye kynge pryamus fyrst began ryche gloryous sette see noble ilyon oh wryte lamentacion conuenient oh troye thy sake thy great myschiefe complayne crye pcertes trowe olde ieremye wepte captiuitye thylke noble royall chyefe cyte ierusalem destruction hole transmygracion pof iewes thou ezechyell tyme mischiefe fell vnto kynge ycalled sedeclye babylon thy prophesye stone cruelly yslawe departed sawe ye bothe two colde complaine danyell felte great peyne kynges transmutasyon beast tyll oryson danyell restored mynde agayne eate grasse pyet veryly though ye thre wepynge gan aliue present eke destructiowne noble worthy royall towne haue bewayled mischiefe wo slaughter syege outher partye full cruell wyse teares might suffyce haue bewepte sorowes euerychone treason wrought aswell foen phereof may auayle lyke gynneth sayle agayne wynde maste ryue ryght vayne stryue agayne face bytter galle vengeaunce vpon troye falle presume furyes sharpe whette ceryously boke sette great thyng dare vndertake euen pyteous ende make syege symplesse though stile blotted rudenesse metre rusty vnfyled pthe fourthe boke haue compyled humble hande drede yt doth quake vnto grace hooly betake pof mercy nothynge dispryre makynge repeyre grekes longer dwelle aduentures sea telle resorte home countre receyued onely supporte ye despyse fyfthe boke shortely shall deuyse pthus endeth fourth boke fyfthe boke phere begynneth fyfth booke howe grekes retourned grece distruction howe perysshed almoste sea escaped dyed myscheuously cap xxxvi eolus whiche dothe wyndes rore appeased yt blewe whiche stormes gouernoure lorde also fully accorde myghty iuno lady ayre make skye wether fayre cloude none heauen dyd appere neptunus blaundyshynge chere assent story sayeth soth make sea fro tempest calme smoth without boyling trouble wawe mighty grek shipward gan draw repeyre home countre wonnen citye put fomen fully werse fortune aye frowarde peruerse hath mirth meynt aduersyte wende full assured haue stande stedfaste quyete blynde lady falsly made flete sugred galle discordaunce amonge selfe brynge varyaunce hertes rancour pryde contagyously seueryne deuyde sat hyghest glorye palme conquest victorye fully reioysynge hye renowne crowne laurer possessyowne also lust wonne bryghtest shone lustye freshe sonne east west worthynesse cloudye skye vnwarely derkenesse eclypsed hath partye light eke diffaced holsome beames bryght welfare prosperitie enuyous false contagyosytie serpent pompouse ellate amonge selfe make debate indusynge rancour discorde entre within shyppes borde agayne vlyxes worthy thelamon presence kynge agamenon purposed hath playnely mattere tofore grekes anone ye shall sire quod greue semeth iustly reason may meue touchyng ye winning getting towne golde richesse possessyowne fully delyuered taken hande treasour founde londe whiche thincketh inward sight ne hath ben departed halfe ryght amonge v iuste deuysyon ne egall dystribucion consydered fyrst tytle equyte euery wyght estate dignitie remembred eke howe sharpe shoure worthyest meryte labour desertes mortall stryfe grauntynge eueryche prerogatyfe lyke fortune hath deserued ordre hath obserued amonges v without excepcyon delyueraunce palladyon whiche vlyxes saye without drede tofore vniustly doth possede hym vsurpynge false opynyon merytorye retrybucyon apparence tytle grounde vnder pretense colour falsely founde relyke reioyse shulde ryght sleyght wonne rather myght vsurpeth maner vaunt gyuen vnto hym graunt echone chyefe guerdon wyll make replycation relyke hym mete whiche shall reioyse quyete maye disturbe hym lette cleyme duely dette guerdon conuenyent ye lyste indifferent reason onely doth seme atwene v two egally deme iustly fyrst euery circumstaunce outher meryte weyed balaunce firste consydered forth fro day daye longe whyle syege laye ye shulde plentye vitayle syde fro myschyefe fayle pand shall without auaunt breke armes knyghthode speke fyelde longe continuaunce manly force perseueraunce vpon foen felle kene day daye armed clene nedeth make mencyon right hand slewe phylomene ye well knowe whiche kepynge yonge sonne pryamus kynge freshe lusty great fayrenesse hym infynyte rychesse treasoure golde passyngly plentye euery dele brought ye remembre lyste take hede ye quyet indygence nede occasyon great good manhode shed ye blode mercyles full cruell wyse sake kynge fryse treasour cofers sought yfeare syege ybrought knyghthode syth go full yore haue eke augmented made grekes lande possessyons conquest onely two regyons prudence laboure sythen ye syege fyrst begonne prouynces troye adiacent encrease dyligent pand achylles worthy warryour ye experte full well laboure wrought auauntage sythen ye prudent sage foryetell fully remembrynge nedeth rehersen euery thynge pand dispreue manly knyght tytle cleyme hath ryght dome comyttynge opynyons rehersayle condycyons nother hath manhode prowesse force knyghthode nother hardynesse poynt haue rewarde darynge preued cowarde experyence hath shewed dede cometh nede worde wynde sleyghty copassyng falshode euer ymagynynge neuer yet daye preued thynge hym acheued whiche might entitled laude ende medlyd fraude vnder colour cure pretende fayre lyke paynted walle dyuerse hewed nother hye lowe may man plaine mening know pand suche sleyght copassed treason troye gat palladyon whiche great shame sclaunder v conquest thus befalle treason haue cytye wonne knyghthode men reporte koune crop rote yf reherse shall vlyxes grounde cause gynnynge fyrste vnhappy fame reboundeth alder shame syth trouthe platly knowen wiste tale ended demyth ye lyste vlyxes aduertence conceyued hath great inpacyence thelamon great enuye feruent rancour melancolye pforbare fyrst full great aduyse full prudent ryght wise thought wolde make therof iape worde haste shulde escape nother none vnbrydled countenaunce outwarde conceyued regardaunce pand abraydynge stable face syres quod may haue grace vnder supporte hyghe presence tale maye haue audyence nother doubte drede equytye shall possede palladyon durynge lyues daye maugre myght say naye yf ye lyst reason se syege layde fyrst cyte haue selfe double wise acquyt well knyghthod sothly wyt counsell busy cure ofre cause theyr discomfiture aye dylygent auauntage wrought compassed vnto theyr domage daye sothe ne floured theyr felycytye theyr force contuned welfare trouth shall spare dempt loked reason cause theyr confusyon euer agaynst replye phow ofte went imbassadrye importable charge dyspense treate aye concludynge sentence forthrynge entenciowne disencrease hindringe towne sawe meane none myne aduyse wittes euerichone force cyte win yt relyke within therupon sotylly wrought vnto palladyon brought thelamon malyce striueth olde hatred vnto gilt ascriueth hooly thinge yt haue wrought pbut ye prudent thought aduerteth wysely ende maketh hande quarell fully taketh palladion iustly prouyde fauour let layde asyde sith thinge ye platly vnderstande let v demynge stande one assent matter wende lo tale ende pthen thelamon ire full feruent rancoure made inpacient enuye inwardely ameued vlyxes hath dispyteously repreued onely malys hyghe disdaine vlixes rebukyng agayne full bytterly without abode anone twayne made full mortall foen presence agamenon pbut furyously ayax thelamon melancolye pale nothynge red thrette vlyxes shall dead handes shulde eschewe grekes tho rancour remewe quarell put arbytration menclaye agamenon caused full mortall stryfe sentence anone dyffynytyfe put vlixes possessyon perpetually thilke palladyon hym confyrmynge abyde stable cause fauourable vlyxes lyke guydo wryte goodly hath hym quyte vnto heleyne gettynge towne beynge cause sauaciowne dispeyred lyfe drede grekes willynge haue dead prudent mediacyon maugre myght thelamon hath quene fro death preserued albe well deserued grekes sayde opynyon thus defrauded palladyon ye haue harde worthy knyght manhode great myght gan herte brede passynge enuye full great hatrede thought wolde auenged day vpon vlixes menelay eke also vppon agamenon brake lyke wood lyon knightes yt stronge sayd playnly great wronge dead woulde auenged specyally ilke three therwithall furious wrothe tournyng backe anone goeth herte fret full mortall tene many greke quarell sustene herte sore gan dysdayne agayne vlixes tother twayne full ware euer falle knightes made aboute call gret stuffe wake slepe awayte manly kepe full good watche enuyron close pbut full erely sonne arose worthy ayax bed vpryght ymurdred selfe nyght albe blede morowe founde peces hewe many mortall wounde thyng cruell horryble god man lothsome odyble full many greke wofull morowe wepe se knyght murdred slepe crye noyse ran throughout hooste anone fro man constreynt foule deede eueryche felte herte blede full desyrous make ordynaunce murdre vengeaunce hauynge therof great suspection menelay agamenon pbut vlixes specyall comon voyce hym arrettynge foule fame myght asterte pbut pyrrhus toke thyng hert makyng vowe furyous wood venged playnely bloud thelamon vpon vlixes heade hym manasynge shalbe deade sore hym frettynge sorowe pbut vlixes erly morowe dread pirrhus taken hath sea shyppes faste gan flee pbut wente platly reade palladyon toke dyomede hauynge herte therof full great remorse pand pirrhus taken hath corse thelamon loue specyall dyd make flawme funerall large great cole hote red amyddes feruent fyry glede full many greke stondynge beholde lette brenne ash colde storye tolde closed vrne golde full reuerently hath shette thervpon hath prynte ysette armes curyously ygraue myschyefe asshes saue sent home great affection conserued regyon kyng whyle lyue euery thynge perfourmed blyue rytes tho dayes vsed p euer one pyrrhus hath ymused vpon murdre trayterously ywrought caste shulde full dere abought pyteous death thelamon hauynge aye hate agamenon eke suspecte olde menelay wayte eche laye makyng selfe knight stronge trye hath ryght wronge pyrrhus ne wolde let lyghtly gone thus made mortall fone ylke three platly death false enuy hertes sleeth amonge selfe vntrue stryfe vpon stryfe gan euery day renewe debate multiplye tyll anthenor gan thynge espye wysedome stynten disdayne reconsyled vnto peace agayne caused accorde made solempne feast royall besechynge full lowely al thre graunt hym therat gentylnesse grekes myghte echone outwarde conceyue al alone feast goodly made calle writ guydo worthy grekes hye ne lowe none excepcion yf shulde make descrypcion howe lordes estate sette sundrye course gyftes great anthenor gaue euery syde longe abyde plente great suffysaunce pand fynde fell dalyaunce syttyng meate speken enee brought hate enmite disdaye shortely sentence put hym many great offence specyally hasty tene whylom concealed polycene sleyght made withdrawe whiche cause achylles yslawe shortly concludyng one opynyon fynall exyle troye towne notwithstandyng graunt lyberte gyuen hym abyde cyte also longe hym lyste deuyse grekes haue adnulled fraunchyse fro lowest vp vnto meste present hye feste pbut doubtelesse well espye brought conspyracye troye boke fynde saue hym selfe wytte anthenor ylyche false bothe one degre ye haue herde betrayshynge cytye lyke spronge one roote whe knew ther none boote eneas dome modefye prayed courtesye least graunten grace foure monthes myght haue space make stuffe apparayle hym selfe puruey vytayle eke graunt hym wolde assent thylke shyppes parys went cytheron vnto temple olde nombre two twenty tolde full graunt petycyowne retourned home troye towne tryste heuy se beholde waste cytye walles olde sorowe felte herte blede within hym selfe taketh hede remembred aduertence false treason great offence hym compassed towne aforne sodeynely hath lorne grace grekes stode disconsolate whylom great estate herte fully dispeyred vnwarely euyll apayred vnto grekes beyonde backe beynge vngylty without lacke whome coulde well deme saue sygnes shulde seme anthenor moste wyte caste playnely wolde hym quyte towne made sende blyue thilke fewe lefte alyue commynge anone commaundemente euerychone present sire quod ye se howe fortune towardes gynneth discontune aye vnstable eyen blynde ye experte selfe fynde whilom frowarde tourned werse clerkes called aduerse lyst cruelte shewe standeth ye fewe must parte ye styll abyde ye prouyde standynge alone deuoyde succoure amonge selfe make gouernoure se beaute shalbe acloyed euery parte fynally destroyed sely shepe ne reade disparkled man doth leade wherfore best dredefull thynge one assent chosen kynge moste able estate occupye assaulte manly guye anthenor knyghthode renowne accorde opynyowne wherfore haste vnto entent without abode lette hym sent comynge plainely towne vpon heade lette sette crowne grauntynge scepter regalye wysedome maye guye assaulte parturbaunce knyghthode prudent gouernaunce assent makyng delaye neuer one lyketh saye nay ryght gladde maner thynge ye haue herde make hym kynge pbut full lyttle sothly sonde eneas meanyng vnderstande ne mente treason falsehede howe entrynge shalbe dead full trayterously awayte lying slea hym falsely commynge anthenor nothyng ware dysarmed came weapen bare eneas huge route swordes drawe set hym rounde aboute tyll troye yonge olde ran atwene manly hym holde knee fell mekely downe besechynge hym haue compassyowne worthynesse also manlyhead lyke knyght taken hede howe lefte people bare besechynge hym dredfull sworde spare rancoure yre leue lest slaughter wolde greue commo besought rewe sayth myne auctour mischiefe ye londe founde sonde almost death without remedye hym mynerua hath great enuye woodly temple wente cassandra autur hente cruell force hatefull vyolence plo peryll offence hye dyspyte holy place doubte shall fayle grace euer vseth deede laste god wyll quyte mede rewarde lyke dysserueth thyng many greke striueth bycause onely suche occasyon exemplefye presumpcyon folyly full knightly stode theyr yre furyously wood venged loude gan crye maye man theyr malice modefye merciles finde specyall kinge menelay agamenon onely meued indignacion would haue proceded vnto iudgemtnt hasty rancour without auysement treason auenged notwithstandinge al hie degre sothnesse worthy kinge conceyued hath malice workinge first astoned inwarde syght sodaynly stert vplike knight wise worthy pallamides hardy lyon amid prese nothinge agaste knightly gan expresse playnly sayde would refuse acquite selfe mortall case acceptynge worthy byrth bloud hye kinred al deuoyding knighthod mahed gaue life death forse tofore theim ieoparde corse within felde theim list ordeyne like knight quarel dareyne list durst vndertake exception liked none make hye lowe bolde proue reason haue tolde besechynge make delaye prolonge daye manly requiringe maye haste yt falsly thinge compaste aunswere stoned echone hoost one hardy shal fayne chaump close quarell dareyne nother vlixes yet dyomede muse matter theyr alder ease crafte gan appease touchinge rumoure hye treason hath voyded suspection theyr hertes concludinge certayne accusynge made vayne conspyred onely hatrede albe selfe roote accomplyshed theyr entet repeyred eueryche tent tale story telleth v feyned kinge naulus touchinge death pallamides theim desclaunder giltles vlixes wyth dyomede innocent platly reade grekes nigh vnsothe falsly feyned make naulus wroth vlyxes dyomede also agamenon grekes mo lette theym homewarde theyr waye hyndre also saye repayre theyr regyons naulus occasyons oetes sonne manly man accorded maye one assente auenge mercyles cruell murdre pallamides ordayne theyr home passage worke fully theyr domage grekes must necessitye homewarde sale foreby countre wherfore kinge shapen hath wyle hylles hye lytell yle winter season euery maner nyght make fyres sette vp lyght cause theim sea erre grekes sawe fyre ferre vnware harme cast theim lande could peryll vnderstande shope theyr ful myght ariue fast lyght wherwith ij hundred shippes brake amonge rockes fully go wrake drowned many worthy thus vengeaunce alderfyrst began kinge naulus hath grekes take deadly hate sonnes sake great mischiefe confusyon grekes nauye agamenon great perill death escaped almost amonge beiaped erles duke worthy kinges crowned trayne sea drowned menelay also dyomede escaped mischefe reade daunger gone oetes wood ire anone herte shope wile thought would agamenon begile compassynge ful mortall stryfe let sende letter anone wife mighty great agamenon whych chere included false treason euen lyke yf shall lye thus effecte dyd specyfye pfyrst lorde agamenon kinge syege wrought wonder thynge preiudyce slaundre name albe maner blame lyke wrote platly trespace knyghtly honour folly difface pthis saye guydo telleth thus loued doughter kynge pryamus beaute wyfe take herte fynally forsake worthy quene whilom great fame clemestra sothly name wonder semely ryght fayre dyscent borne stocke royall cellynge eke excellence albe neuer dyd offence yet lorde newfangilnesse toke letter expresse fully purpose anone repayre though clemestra good fayre sodaynly exyle lande many thousande myle warning prudente substaunce sentemente oetes wrote vnto quene albe kynge innocente clene fore liuinge louyng true maner thinge please passyng ententyfe worde dede durynge lyfe fer oughte reson desyred letter falsly conspyred haue put parcase innocence gyue hasty credence pthankynge firste oetes trouthe goodly hym lyst haue routhe vpon wronge hygh compassyon yet storye maketh mencion afterwarde shall descriue falest one alyue vnto lorde longe absence haste made stronge diffence agayne thinge gan purueye suche fraude ne deye worke sothe wyte whych ala must anone endyte story platly doth lere whych doleful mortall heare oh vnsure truste worldly glorye wt sodayn chaunge put memorye oh ioye vnstable vayne ambycyon vnware tourne reuersed vp downe oh ydell fame blowe vp skye ouer whelmed twincklinge eye oh pompe oh boste tryumphe victorye lyke shadowe waste transytorye oh fortune false vnassured man maye fully lured hygh lowe maner estate bonde fayth conferate agayne whose myght may diffed tourne shall discende syt hyest thyne vnstable whele thy brotyll fauour forged stele meynt allyed mutabylytye welfulnesse false felicitye sodayn sweygh frowarde yu canst auale freshe chere anger pale hygh disdayne thou sparest degree prince duke highest see mighty kinges worthy emperours richest reygne theyr royal floures sceptre crowne yu canst pul downe pi take wytnesse agamenowne noble myghty lyue sondry auctours hie renowne desriue sothfastly excellence might make diffence knightes baner sewe conspyred murdre voyde eschewe rescuse none could make ala fele pen quake doth mine inke blotte boke oh mighty god wt thine inwarde loke seest euery thing thrugh thy eternal might wilt thou equit ryght punishe chastice horrible thinge specyally murdre kinge ala payne ixion hell mane sathan dwell egall equipolent venge murdre sufficient excedeth comparison al felonye falshed treason wherfore oh lord seest knowest thy power eternall suffre suche liue vpon grounde worse tygre cerberus hounde chayned lyeth bounde hel gate whych malyce playnly though hate berketh fyrst offence murdre gladly wrought sylence men aduerte take kepe palas prince sley slepe pyllowe slepeth softe cryeth wreche hye god alofte axeth vengeaunce take fast though abyde wyll laste ala kynge spoken ferre worthy outwarde werre cruell fate passynge odyous dysposed hath owne house mortall ende execute agaynst whych refute ryght shyp lande sette quene clemestra ye strond mette humble cheare loke full beninge shewed full many faythful sygne wysely trouthe countenaunce albe herte varyaunce perceyued playnly face kynge goodly embrace sothe trouth mente paleys hye waye wente aduertynge treason shape whych ala might escape falshede could nothinke fele ne maye longer consele agayne lorde clemestra wrought bond wedlocke ne thought trewe loke sothly spousayle agayne malyce lytell myght auayle vnto lorde trouthe conserue newfangilnesse caused sterue olde fayth assuraunce loue abode fykell chaunce longe absence herte apalled loued one egistus called afore grace stode nother byrth bloud lytell nought reputacyowne renowmed manhode renowne knyghthod hygh prowesse laboure busynesse good awayte vpon nyght therfore best furthred syght dread lyue alone sorowles well could grone saye life ladde except doughter exyona guydo sayth hight vnto clemestra behyght assuringe vpon payne head shulde raygne lorde dead enhaste conclusyon worthy lorde kynge agamenon next nyght murdred yslayne false egistus quene full fayne longer bode storye lere haste wedded yfere false sleyghty compassynge messene made crowned kynge put full possessyon palas synne hath dominacion wronge abate ryght worlde falshed hath ryghte full ofte syth hath ryghtwisenesse estate sette worthynesse lo synne auoutrye brought murdre conspyracye synne vpon synne lynked twayne embraced fendes chayne perpetually hell endure ala shall selfe full assure fro cruell murdre body withdrawe kinges theyr bedde slawe whiche bringeth alyenacyon extorte tytle false successyon maye coloure pretense seme full streyghtly god shall deme iustly venge due recompence intrusyon brought violence felly quyte suche horryble thinges sodayne slaughter specially kinges greatly dread euery regyon pand fynde agamenon clemestra false double quene sonne passynge faire sene right gracious euery mannes syght horestus boke sayth hyghte wonder semely yonge age great feare mortall rage lest slayne dread anul tytle succede preserue shent kinge taltibus power hath sente ful secretly countree vnto kinge called ydume helde sceptre royall sete full mightely lande crete carkasis named quene doughter called eke climene borne heyre regyon made eke mencyon horestes reken thynge quene also kinge cherished well storye lere climena theyr owne doughter deare eke kepte cherte fro poynt poynt lyke degre attendaunce conuenyent dewe estate euer vpon sewe experte sage gouerne tyll came age reioyce god gaue might heritage whych right clere discent happy chaunce thus leue vnder gouernaunce yonge sonne agamenon must make dygressyon fro matter tell diomede auentures guydo rede wofull fate paynes smerte whych ala might asterte remembred playnly writynge oetes sonne riche kinge called naulus ye haue herde toforne heuynesse herte hath borne vnto grekes repeyringe home fro troye lust inwarde ioye hyndre high lowe cause vnknowe passynge enuyous thought ylyke desyrous might sothly le death venge pallamides lyke tofore storye deuyse prudent wyse oetes malice wrought trayterously new meane sought might maner waye diomedes vnwarely destroye thinge cast fayle ceryously make rehersayle grece kingedome wide large coniunct one calidonye arge full habundaunt rychesse rente kinge called pollente worthy man noble fame sonne assandrus name doughter passinge fayre syght sothly egra finde hyght father like wryte guydo mo child two hath wisedome prouided mighty reygne deuyded atwene theim two decease eche parte lyue peace exclude fro indigence nede wyfe vnto diomede albe tofore storye sayde whilom loued one crysayde saye doubilnesse well wote guydo beareth wytnesse boke sothly sayth none assandrus owne wiues brother full lusty freshe ful manlyhead troye went dyomede sea fordriuen vp downe riued vp regyon called boece disconsolate tempest driue wery full mate refreshe none thinge lande thelephus kinge whose riuayle whan herde sayne herte high disdayne bolde great offence entre grounde hauinge licence yet sothe domage high lowe maner age toke nought might disauayle vnto lande vytayle payde iustly fine fleshe fyshe bread wine yet indignaciowne kinge thelaphus descended downe great array harme might gan bicker fight assandrus full high prowesse like lion fomen gan oppresse wonder knyghtly felde vpen wa slewe daye many worthy man hygh courage manly pryde kinge whiche stode asyde sawe men slayne euery parte hygh dysdayne hent anone darte caste hym ala mortall fate perced hathe mayles plate assandrus fel downe dead soyle bloud redde deadly wounde began blede wood tygre tho came dyomede hym auenge bare hym lyke knyght sleeth kylleth put vnto flight sorowe gan make knyghtly routh brother sake ne wyst best finde myd wo beast foule dead corp saue like estate let make graue buryed hym rite olde pbut oetes syster tolde slayne fraude dyomede fyne myght full possede reygne arge hole without stryfe wyth purpartye annexed hys wyfe death myght season take tolde eke forsake fayre egra womanhead lorde callled dyomede tolde hell chayned ouermore forged hath fained enuye assandrus lost lyfe lorde hath take wyfe dyshonour shame passyngly great sclaunder name preiudyce ydone estate tolde make debate lyke wrote conclusyon clemestra agamenon whych herte made sore greue put fully byleue treason ye haue herde tolde yre pale colde vnkyndnesse herte sleeth heuynesse brother death neuer yet guydo doth assure woman loued better creature loued hym maner age fyrst nought set herytage comparyson brother lyfe lo oetes made newe stryfe ye haue herde storye rede gyltles worthy dyomede hath longe syege layne kingdom would haue come agayn migyhty hande worthy quene lyeges assented bene exyled regyon may made medyacyon thus selfe mate dyspeyred dysconsolate agayne repeyred salerne londe great rychesse tenter worthynesse wyth crowne sceptre reygned longe wyth hys lyeges hys knyghtes stronge brother ayax thelamon murdred tofore made mencyon dyomede pore destytute maye salerne fynde refute whan tenter first gan espye sewed hym full great enuye hauynge hym aye suspection touchynge death kynge thelamon pbut dyomede certayne nyghte full secretely hath taken flyght fro salerne fast gan hym hye hope fynde better remedye helpe socour place fortune wolde graunte hym grace hym selfe ashamed confuse man forsake abiecte refuse ryght fared wandrynge fro ne wyst best bvt fynde troyan eneas still troye onely routh compassyowne support left towne beynge alway theyr life doubte theyr fomen rounde beset aboute lyued lacke hede contynually myschyefe dread knowing refute cofort case tyll counsell eneas supporte theym great nede sent haste dyomede knowynge full well desolacyon proscrypt fro regyon besechynge hym manhode routhe enhaste wythout slouthe stuffe get souldyers also manly euery man without abode troye lede succoure great nede pand dyomede came taryed nought theyr request besought releue sharpe shoure wyth hym brought many souldeour eneas waye mette frendly wyse towne hym fette made passyngly great chere gan commune yfere theyr auentures lande sea entermedled great aduersyte man maye deuoyde eschewe take parte dewe sorte hap doth brydell lede storye shortly procede cely troyans almost shent theyr fomen yles adiacent theim besette aboute enuyrowne manhod hye renowne dyomede souldeours knyghtes noble werreours reskued holpen vtterly foure dayes fought knyghtly wyse defendynge cytee prowesse also enee slewe toke withstode diffence troyanyshe bloud suche fonde cytye false hange vp hye halse punyshed theyr great wronge pand dyomede thus gan wexe stronge longe processe made mencyon chiefe protectour troye towne enuye none large space durst abyde grace lygeaunce made loute thus name sprede gan aboute fame great opynyon dylated vnto regyon swifte reporte calydonye arge quene greatly gan charge astoned taketh hede power gan might dreade lest would lande vpon wynne knighthod werre newe begynne secretly gan muse thinge lorde myghty kynge late exyled yput flyght hath grace founde fortune syght remonuted high estate wherof selfe checke mate wayes caste prudent hole aduyse parliament without grutchynge rebellyon reuoke regyon pand therupon lowly sente letter messager forth went cause annullyng exiled fully reconsyled hole assent lyeges ful lowly euerychone call theyr offence theyr trespace without rygour grace anone like manly knyght mercy sothly ryght hath theyr sonde well conceyued theyr meninge fully apparceyued stynte strife thought best goodly wise graunt theyr requeste reigne within certayne daye repeyred full riche arraye whose comynge full glad liege bene reconsiled quene rancour olde offence onely wisedome put suspense one herte blisful life lede troye booke hym reade let liue felycytee agayne resortynge tell ene hath tyme spent fro troye wt many troyan went shippes stuffed meyne sayled forth many straunge sea many daunger many strayte passage tofore aryued cartage ledinge father anchises waye finde le wife crewsa fatall auenture wo dyd endure list ceryously sene falshede quene meane dido womanhead floure gaue rychesse treasoure iewelles golde al yt mighte please euery thing might ease pbut vnkinde reade eneydos ye shall fynde howe falsly stale awaye nyghte tyme bedde laye conquest also ytayle hadde many stronge battayle auentures workes fyne fall ye maye se soueraygne style fro poynt poynt compyled virgile wryte made sythen go full yore troye boke speaketh pbut procedeth shall endyte horestes caste quyte father death playnly spare ye lyst heare guydo doth declare requyred equit right iudge myght egally holdeth balaunce death conspyred vengeaunce voyce bloud doth aye contune crye wreche clamour importune sothe iniustly shede murdre wrought wil haue egall mede guerdon hath deserued maye fle iudgement reserued sit highest trone beholdeth selfe alone full rightfully noble mighty kinge though suffer forget nothinge consydreth inspectyon murdre agamenon mighty lorde yt soueraygne good made mynystre bloud yonge horestes full high prowesse execute dome ryghtwisenesse gaue grace power might anone toke ordre knyght ydumeus like tolde foure twentye wynter olde freshe lustye wonderly prudent inwardly desyrous intente fortune would sayne heritage recure agayne pwhich egistas falsly hym denyeth crowne vniustly occupyeth false tytle wife pbut horests ieoparde lyfe auenture lasteth breth fyrst venged father death vpon tho treason wrought alderfyrst full lowly besought pkinge ydinne goodlyhead great nede pand kinge benignely anone assigned hath gone thousand knightes manly right stroge redresse great horrible wronge egistus wrought violence wisdome dyligence horestes gan purueye within seye gat storye lye thousande companye worthy knightes one accorde go wt theyr soueraygne lorde euery thinge biddinge obeye ye haue herde egistus werrey pand thus horestes full riche arraye gan hooste made delaye lodginge alderfyrst gan chese citye called troyese receyued great reuernece kinge named forence manly knyght bookes specifye bare herte passinge great enuye egistus double occasion fyrste death agamenon eke doughter deare inwardly entere good fayre yonge age whilom giuen mariage egistus doubilnesse false treson newfangilnesse kinges doughter hath vtterly forsake haste libell make forge writ repulsyon albe hadde trewe occasyon egistus forsoke saue falssy wiue toke quene clemestra agayne al right law assent murdred haue slawe agamenon afore tolde whylom myghty bolde hatefull false conspyrasye well murther auoutrye venge bothe dewe recompence worthy knyght ye mighty kyng forence offred horestes make hym stronge go hym helpe venge wronge hym ladde armed bryght stele foure hundred knightes horsed wonder wele takynge fyelde manly chere horestes kynge yfeare ryden forthe many manly man pbut horestes werre gan bryght phebus bole shone temple full lowly gone goddes best wyse humble herte dyd sacryfyce fully hope better fare bode lyfe deth spare without mercy remyssyon death venge agamenon pon clemestra moste wyte make fyrste sworde byte mother handes twayne ouermore busy payne without pytye mercye shewe smale peces tyll hewe dismembred sonder ioynt fro ioynt eke yet poynt iustly punyshe rycoure ryght pegistus eke false vntrewe knyght slowe neclygent execute commaundement goddes lyste falle pand horestes knyghtes pand forenses mighty kynge also one herte syege go cyte called methene within whiche false quene clemestra god gyue herde grace horestes syeged hath place knyghtes set rounde aboute pfalse egistus yryden gather men wreke falle vpon syege breke pif myght maner syde great stuffe thus gan ryde takynge vp men fro euery coste tyll hym made full myghtye hooste pbut horeste whiche syege laye gouernaunce espyeth daye daye sent men full sage stoppe wayes lette passage made knyghtes full huge route pursue hym euery coste aboute syege manfully begonne assaute hath towne ywonne entred nyght full late sette wardes stronge euery gate doungeon stronge princypall buildyng myghty royall horestes fyrste mother fonde pthe quene clemestra lady lande whiche drede sore gan quake mercyles anone made take put chaynes tyll next morowe pand egistus god gyue hym euyll sorowe stuffe myght accroche towarde towne faste gan aproche pin purpose full horestes greue within sodeynely releue sothe myght auayle cytye myght abayle horestes knightes vnwarely haue mette attones proudely hym sette fyrste slewe men put flyght pand taken hym maugre myght chaynes lyke hym fynde mercyles full fast bynde shet hym vp fetryd prysowne false founde towne assented wyllinge helpynge murdre worthy kynge grekes worker conspyratours agayne lorde ryfynge traytours take bounde rycour nyghte shet vp toure tyll morowe lyke lot drawe eueryche vnder fonge lawe lyke decerte excepcion none nyght passed gone phebus rose estwarde sphere toures shone full bryght clere pwhen clemestra rote falsehede brought forth quakyng drede pbefore horestes iudgement yfet sworde sharpe kene ywhet like goddes charged toforne peces smale hath shorne made bere townes boudes voured beastes houndes pytye none breste reserued quit fully hath deserued fro poynt poynt forgat right nought chayned egistus furth brought iustly dempt rigour lawe herdell naked drawe towne might se hye hanged tre rot drye agaynst sonne lo murdre hath guerdon wonne lo falshed mayster awake pand traytours towne ytake galowes enhanged euerychone tyll seuered asonder bone fro bone hye hill agayne sterres shene thus ye towne fro treason purged clene trouth augmented ymored reygne horrestes full restored storye sewinge shall expowne daye toke crowne myst euery cloudy skye false treason conspyracye tried vpon euery syde falshed hadde place abyde storye sayth ordre rehersynge time menelay kinge sea ful wawes wete fro troyewarde yriued crete frely escaped many dread peyne quene goodly freshe heleyne cause famous fayre great pres meruaylous repaire fro euery parte beaute beholde troye walles ful olde destroyed noble royall towne many man ful worthy renowne hath lost life may man say naye heleyne wife menelay thinge done may none kinge knewe fully brother agamenon murdre euerydele full trist liked nothinge wele inwardly felte ful great smerte pand neuewe also herte meane horrestes mercyles like tyraunt graceles mother slewe pytye mortall yre crueltye fully caste would bline sceptre crowne platly depriue full afferminge mortall case lawe vnworthy father reygne heyre possede iustly consydred horrible dede one furyous wroth without abode vnto ship goth melancolike great tene crete saylinge athene toke lande shippes borde duke nestor gouernour lord receyueth like gentyll knyghte power diligence myght menelay rancour great heat gan duke secretly trete fynde meane inward syght pfor depriue horrestes right therupon haue iudgement athene holde parliament lordes regyon giue theron diffinicion whych shewed openly ynough horrestes owne mother slough maner great offence selfe tho beynge presence thinge fully espye partye gan agayne replye felte frely large alledginge charge goddes shortly declare mortall sworde ne spare vpon clemestra roote false treason slewe lorde kinge agamenon murdre malice wrought wherfore horrestes humbly besought lordes manly herte equit consydre aduerte malice rancour rage depriue heritage sith sonne agamenon borne heyre regyon ye haue herde called methene albe mother clemestra quene compassed destruction pbut duke nestor ymeued reason sustaynynge horestes ryght rose vp anone lyke manly knyght offrynge hym selfe proudely sake hye quarell vndertake body death darreyne lyst tytle withseyne pbut none companye durste worde agayne hym replye hoole stode opynion knyghtly mediacyon bare hym feynynge nothynge horestes ycrowned kyng meneste beynge assent whan dissolued parlement horestes lyeges trewe receyued crowne newe treate lordes many one kyng menelay made attone gan ire rancour lete pand ydume worthy kynge crete prudently gouerneth mattere hermyone yonge doughter dere pof menelay quene heleyne yonge freshe beaute souerayne ywedded without taryinge horestes yonge lusty kynge bycause allyaunce deuoyded rancour distraunce atwene kynges menelay olde horestes ryght nowe tolde thus leue beste eche reygne lyue peace reste stryfe ceased case pbut erygona doughter egistus ye haue herde telle sorowe drede lyste longer dwelle toke rope lyst nothynge spare therwithall gan selfe gnare storye sayth hye vpon tree fyne ye gette wyll forth ceryously entreate storye telle great oh vlixes ordre wrytynge thyne auentures come rynge full wonderfull londe sea entermedlyd great aduersytye guydo fyrste descryuynge thy repayre saith thou founde wether foule fayre nowe agreable thonder sowne styll smoth wt cloudes frowne sayth also thou dyddest ordeyne thy passage myghty shyppes twayne apparayled marchandyse thou myghtest secrete wyse euery myschyefe sea escape pbut thou haddest felle iape auctour thy resorte doth wryte sayth vlyxes wordes whyte yrobbed rychesse good contraryous wynde agayne hym stode dryue confusyon myghty stronge regyon thelamon reygned lyue hent take blyue pby myghtye hande seased brest mercyles put vnder arest hym suspecte workynge touchynge murther kynge wrought sleyghty wyle tale sette suche style playnly hath iaped fro hande frely escaped excepte queynt fare treasour ymade full bare passage hym vnkouth fell agayne wolfe mouthe veryly specyfyed kynge naulus men haue hym efte espyed take bounde chayned mercyles murther kynge pallamydes pbut storye reherseth certayne prudence scaped agayne expert wyse olde although maner fully tolde escape busy peyne daunger kynges twayne tyll fortune came fro mischefe fre presence kyng ydume symple arraye torne apparayle wherof kynge greatly gan meruayle se pouert lowe manere made hym good chere though tyme ye infortunate hym receyueth lyke estate twayne alone complayninge vlixes made mone vnto kinge ful sage ceryously sorte passage face sad sobre cheare fro poynt poynt anone ye shall heare pmy lorde quod shortly expresse truste haue gentylnesse shall auentures reherse ryght fall firste troye lande forsoke water wyth shippes toke anone winde peceably blowe yle vnknowe pcalled mirma great habundaunce thynge pleasaunce maye siluer golde bought redy founde wanted ryght nought abode full longe ioye treasour gat troye shyppes stuffed men safe sounde commodyte ylke grounde lyked countre enuyron disporte recreacyon taryinge thought ful loge man dyd vnto v wronge tyll daye eyer styll winde also fully wyll sayled quyete peace vnto porte called claustafages wherwyth meyne longe many daye founde thinge accordynge paye wether lusty agreable fayre maye truste winde ayre vpon fayth smothe skye agayne shyppe faste gan hye taryed nought toke anone sea smothe calme enduringe dayes three wether founde lacke sodaynly heauen tourneth blacke hidous tempest wawes grene hope haue dyspeyred clene troubled spyrite made pensife without refute escape lyfe tossed driuen many sundrye yle tyll laste caste vp cecyle recuringe lande great annoye payne tyme reygned kynges twayne remembre doubtles tone theim called sorygines whiche vnto full contrarious pand tother named coclopas brother byrthe conclusion ylike cruell condycyon though sorte shape none pboth twayne fell attones oppressinge full great dystresse spoyled shippes treasour richesse pyte liked spare till lefte destitute bare good ala mortall chaunce greuaunce whe golde may restrayne sent downe mighty sone twayne palipham ful large longe pand polipheme ye mighty gianut stronge auenge wereful fame haue hundred slayne disarayed stande diffence malice sodayne violence toke mischiefe almost lorne pand alphenor mine owne brother sworne hatefully haue v founde chaynes caste stockes bounde ylocked prison make platly mencyon mighty man great polypheme syster shortly deme one fayrest euer yet borne might beaute set aforne nature gaue suche prerogatife cleane mayde sothly wyfe flouringe fayrenesse bounte alphenor se albe fetred prison loue loste wit eke reason wex al mad narowe binde saue vpon alway minde closed aye perillous wounde sixe monethes thus laye bounde pboth saye platte trouthe til polipheme vpon v routhe grace mediacion quit v fre pryson shewed v mercy pite sorowe great humanite pbut alphenor ylike one entente bronde cupide brent felte parte many mortall fit till wrought sotyll wit night leef lothe stale mayde waye gothe helpe men hym time pbut morowe houre prime ppoliphemus gan v sewe whose mighty hande might eschewe suche assaulte v gan make force haue mayde take pfrom alphenor mauger rage polipheme vnto domage knightes sore vpon laye might vnneth scape awaye saue selfe compassed enuyron death pursewed champyon sawe gayne fle death shortly sayne giaunt fiersly set sworde eye smet vnto ship companye fled haste man might espye pwhere became alphenor fere wawes gan clere gracious winde gan v awake countre haue anone forsake holsome v abyde man like write ouide ppoliphemus giaunt dread eye amid forhead vlixes smote stroke like browes branched oke heyre longe berde loke child aferde lost syght amonge hilles runneth daye night rage finde refuge caste rockes great stone huge euery parte enuyron countre vlixes auenged thus sayth ouide conclusion boke transformacion metamorphoseos ye maye se euer leyser ceriously storye reade writinge forth procede vlixes face dead pale ydume tolde forth tale rehersinge thus supprised awaked fro polipheme escaped vnhappe infelicyte yle middes sea driue gan night elidiu litell kingedome hight circe great enchauntresse thilke time lady goddesse could crafte wonderly fourme sodaynly man transforme haue liknesse lese reason horse bere tygre lyon wolfe list deuise dreadful crafte shapen wise mighty straunge pocions letuaries confection also fayre vpon se tho power man might fle worke sorceresse founced vpon fayrenesse fynally thus stode yeare abode paynly power none myght deparie neyther daye night lusty life ladde whych time childe right inly fayre goodly syght thelagonius sothnesse hight afterwarde wel reherse processe wexe manly man subtyll secret prouidence crafte experyence maugre enchauntementes olde stale awaye might holde fynally fate conclude connynge crafte delude men scaped fro hande went large fre lande thinge litell auayle waye gan sayle sleyght litell whyle yblowe vp yle pwhere calipha syster circe crowned quene held sceptre peace whose craftes mighty strong maugre held ful longe sothe speake womanhede bounte fredome goodlyhead surely soueraygne excellence mine abode none offence soeuer therat crye clappe laste scaped fro trappe came yle ryght lyne specyally high power diuine ordayned yore myracle spirituall oracle man haue temple sodayne answere list enquere question demaundes soules shall eke befall men dead grauen vnder stone gan axe temple anone mine auentures sewe man might fate eschewe like mine entent aunswere full conuenient saue befalleth soule gone diffinicion vnto none thinge assoyle accordeth right reserued vnto goddes myght excedeth reason wyt man fro thense forth sayle gan driuen wynde parte succoured lyke haue deuoured pof karibdes profounde well syrines meremaydens dwell fro brest scale siluer shene theyr shape fish freshe clene ouermore kinde doth compasse appeare feminine face like virgin nature without spot vndefouled pure custome wawes flete songe heauenly swete aungelike full armonye veryly sugred melodye rauishe would man alyue inly ioye almost herte ryue make man sodayne high pleasaunce forget selfe lese remembraunce deuoyde clene owne thought tyl vnwarely mischiefe brought theyr songe take kepe shall brought mortall slepe anone yt maye withdrawe wil drenche shippe lowe vnder wawe thus swetenesse theyr heauenly sowne bringeth man confusyon euer theyr bondes passe pbut lyfe scaped grace mine eares waxe gommes clere stopped ne might heare touche werble theyr instrumentes wherby reason man blinded fynally subtyltee men escaped free saylinge forth mate werinesse till came vp full great distresse pat phenice toke anone lande caste anker shippes bande sothly fell v full vnfayre pfor people cruell contrayre onely malice fell anone slewe men almost euerychone treasour good litell berafte ladde fewe theim lefte alone toke theim put prison bliue thus hath fortune lad daunce litell ioye plentye mischaunce whose daunger learned experte fall mischiefe pouerte great dole sorowe full brest sea land south east come vnto presence haue declared playnly sentence min auentures worthinesse truste onely faythfulnesse haue specyall haue rehersed tolde hyghnesse best wyse without doth suffyse though herte constrayned sore thilke time vlixes spake helde peace ful heuy lokinge pand ydumeus like gentyll kinge comforted euer might busy herte light besought heuinesse lete longe hym lyst crete abide made suerte fare also wel wante maye ease sorowe gan apease rage drewe vnto ende leue toke sayde would wende lande home countre pbut fyrst kinge fredome bounte gaue vnto hym great rychesse arraye soeuer paye golde treasour many thinges partynge two kynges shippes list sayle redy stuffed meyne vitayle thus vlixes gan redy make hath leue fully take hasted toke anone sea gan sayle towarde countre fyrste wente kinge alphenon whych passingly affeccion se vlixes home comynge desyrous ouer thynge haue newly acqueyntaunce vnto inly great plesaunce heare talke eloquence wisedome high prudence smerte receyued playnly glad herte euer yet maner man sithen tyme worlde began pand encrease felycyte herde first penolopee trewe wife without spot blame yet grene noble fame lorde longe absece thought dede neuer offence sothly chere dede throughout grece example womanhede yet bokes lyst expresse throughout ye world myrrour fayrenesse amonge grekes borne hyest blode called auctours fayre good yet saye bokes doubtles neuer none great prese kepte chaunginge newe vnto lorde euer ylyke trewe herte aye one parted twayne called quene soueraygne wifely trouthe bokes olde ofte finde herte would colde tourne pale fro lorde ferre closet heare werre dread feare eke quake fantasyes lordes sake absence eue morowe death vnto importable sorowe aye sothe ioye game fell herde hector name place anone fell swowne gan selfe teares drowne womanhead aferde heare slaughter mortall swerde lest lorde knyghtly surquedrye fortune fall ieopardye sorte mette worthy knight seld neuer felte herte lyght many dreame nightes gaste siege laste euery playe venym syght owne knight worlde ioye none high lowe playnly one whose sake myrth refuseth herte museth woman thinge good melancolye meued bloud let aduerte wysedome ysee remembre penolope deserte lest blamed oh guido thou shouldest ashamed saye wiues thinge wele good fayth ferre fele though one two amonge offence good prouidence therof nothinge wite though guydo bokes endite pthe varyaunce heleyne criseyde por medea sorowe deyde let agayne ryght equyte wifely trouth penolope maydenhode yonge polycene goodnesse hecuba quene cassandra eke stedfastnesse take vnkindnesse pantasyll withoute variaunce put togyther balaunce ye shal finde ye lyst accounte maugre grutcheth trouth shal surmout dare affirme beare prise man replye wise feble opynion pand vlixes alphenon made relacyon hatefull conspiratyon certayne lordes enuyron countre rauishe would quene penolope maugre tho agayne albe euer ylyke playne trouthe stedfaste wall yet haue caste platly shall take force maye eschewed haste reskued caste time aiourne daye nighte soiourne inly herte loue disamayde wisedome hath theim belayde none manly sage could get auauntage aduyse workynge vlixes conceyueth thinge fully knewe open euydence also specyall credence psente vnto fro penolope matter hole declarynge secretee phi owne sonne thelamonius wexe herte wood furyous would make dylacyon pbut haste besoughte alphenon mighty kinge high bounte releue aduersyte would mighty hade gentillesse conueye lande graunteth saye one naye two ful great araye toke sea winde good well fortuned nothinge theim withstode ariued lettynge vlixes ye haue herde kinge secretly night conueyed haue ligaunce disobeyed mercyles might awake theyr beddes haue theim take makynge prolongyng tyll morowe haste wight durst borow smet theyr heades iudgement fynall set theim vpon castell wall eueriche endlonge rowe vpon toure cocke gan crowe thus nyght kept theim selfe close till phebus meryly arose orient larke songe tho kinges wt theyr meyne stroge freshly besene entre cetee glad penolope made ioye goodly quene full desyrous owne lorde sene pbut ordre sette great myrthe made met make rehersayle complayntes olde gan theyr hertes vnfolde eche lyst nothinge concele gladnesse inly fele shulde put memorye reioysynge hertye glorye lyeges made comynge coste eke metynge giftes great presentes ryche worlde trowe none ylyche longe taryinge boke newe assuraunce toke lordes lyeges grace fall cheare made eke alphenowne gentylnesse high renowne doughter inly debonayre alphenon nausica fayre vlixes medyacyon ywedded vnto thelamon borne discent may man saye nay reioyce crowne daye thus came purueyaunce two reygnes myghty allyaunce brought knotte men would deme playnly sotte presume opynyon delate descripcyon sythen guydo touchinge chyefe matter stile brefe pshortly rehersynge kinge alphenon repeyred home regyon vlixes chiefe cyte abode styll penolope leue ioye solace till attropos liketh purchase fyche fynally date threde vntwine liues fate phow translatour wryteth stocke pirrhus lyneall dyscent father hight pelleus graundmother called thetydes ca xxxviii must full busy directe trace stile discriuinge shortly entente stocke pirrhus lyneall discente myn auctour folowe compendious pwhose olde father hyght pelleus graundmother called thetydes whych two came worthy achilles troye treason lost lyfe dardanica called wife ppirrhus mother doughter reade vnto kynge called lychomede phauinge father atastus hight whych sothnesse euer myght pbare heauy herte kinge pelleus achilles also pirrhus kyn playnly side malyce rancour pryde enuye hatefull rage pwhen pelleus fall age berafte sceptre crowne see lowe alight downe exyle auayle maye stryfe made go thetydes wyfe high disdayne gayne maye grace herte gan daye night copace death pyrrhus kepe ye therupon maliciously began shape waye awayte lyinge sley home comynge pyrrhus treynes free many daunger escaped sea many wawe many tempest wood great losse men good malasus alderfyrst gan londe stronge cyte lytell stronde refreshed wonder wele knewe grounde euery dele fyrste thexyle lyke men tolde pof thetides pelleus olde atastus bare hatrede vnto death wherof gan drede thought would yt right wise engyne eschewe malyce therupon busy payne pnow atastus sonnes twayne pmenalippus polistenes doughter ycalled thetydes whyle wofull pelleus castell olde ruynous thetydes full sorowe care dread death daye night gan dare dispeyred vnweldy age recure fynde mortall rage except hope yore pyrrhus shoulde helpe restore repeyre fall whose comynge often gan call tyme curse longe abode pyrrhus vnderstode malasus relacyowne ful faste gan haste towne toke sea fast gan hye towarde lande called thesalye entent make ordynaunce atastus vengeaunce alder fyrste pyrrhus ful prudent espyes twayne tofore hath sent thesalye forth togyther gone pand crilippus named tone adrastus named fere expert theim nedeth lere whose exployte auauntage pthis pyrrhus hath dyrecte message thesalye cytezyne called assandrus maner chamberlayne pelleus whilom ful secree flourynge felycytee pyrrhus conclusyon knewe sothe relacyon sea lande hym ne lyst tarye albe founde winde contrarye pbut escaped many dreadful stoundes thesalye approcheth boundes eolus lust obeyed fortune wonderlye conueyed dryuen grace ariue place pelleus doleful caue dread death laye selfe saue sole saue wife withouten feres al enclosed bush briares pirrhus went vp fyrst londe sole hym selfe walkynge stronde pensife trist waye toke pwhere pelleus caue quoke hauynge tho guyde saue sworde hangynge syde vnwarely dreadful herte ppelleus caue sterte dismayde life doubte behelde knight walke astoned abode stode ful styll ymagyninge sawe achille pby pirrhus stondynge place sygnes shewed face nature without varyaunce made like cheare countenauce fourme shape limmes euerychone difference effect none pand pelleus without longer space gan anone pirrhus enbrace enbrayde deadly thoughte ioye set sorowe nought gan declare exyle euyl fare pyteous lyfe pouerte mischauce fortune false varyaunce atastus feruent hoote enuye cruelte tyrannye ceriously tolde pirrhus full sobre stode still wall face pale herte wrothe specheles shyp agayne goth enformed doubtles menalippus polistenes atastus togither thre huge araye great meyne daye ful surquedous pride hunte forest lytell besyde pyrrhus therof toke good hede without abode chaunge gan wede ful porely rent dismayde like man disarayde gyrte sworde made delaye forest toke right waye sole selfe without companye secretly man might espye drough many diuers boundes herde horne vncouplinge houndes like man list make mone fro syght folke drewe aye alone casually disseuered fro prese pfirste met polistenes pmenalippus ridinge syde two pirrhus gan abyde boystously enquere fro whense came also febly cladde pore estate walkinge desolate lowly chere countenaunce styll humble daliaunce aunswered agayne sayde fordriuen myschiefe sea affirmed pale nothinge redde felowship drowned dead fiue hundred wawes rage olde yonge mydell age escaped tempest rife tolde vnneth life ouermore tolde platly eke touchinge birthe greke went destitute ioye late come fro siege troye besought towerde liuinge helpe refreshinge cattell lost good like sawe naked stode prayinge also hope auayle releue clothinge vytayle refute prouide pand bad abide wyll wytte playnly beside ran full great harte downe ryuer pand menalippus pricked courser semed dewe thinne thicke onely pursewe spareth alwaye rode brother pirrhus stil abode ppolistenes toke hede haste alight fro stede grene reste besyde wery ryde without meyne beynge selfe sole listing pirrhus ye complaynt dole sodaynly might aduerte cruell pirrhus ran herte lefte dead lyinge playne menalippus repeyred agayne seynge brother baskynge bloud pirrhus efte furyous wood face coloure pale wan menalippus yre ran slewe eke toke hede thus laye grounde blede brother two withe pirrhus sworde yslawe anone asyde gan drawe metinge knight sorte case sayth storye called cinaras pirrhus gan haste enquere whose man maketh sayde withouten tarying seruaunt myghty kinge called atastus lorde countre pand pirrhus tho deadly enmyte cruell sworde al freshe red bloud ran lyon wood forest forsoke haste ryght waye toke shippe agayne pale blacke hewe gan anone arraye newe pall purple whych clerkes telles kinges wyght elles pirrhus freshe well beseyne forest repeyred ageyne sodaynly hap walkynge shorte meteth wyth kynge polde atastus asked pirrhus man art thou thy selfe thus disconsolate walkest fro pcertes quod pirrhus full sorowe wo inly supprysed hertye complaynynge one sonnes priamus kynge lately memorye sith troyans fal whilom glory refewteles mischiefe brought thus walke sole full care thoughte farre exyle troye towne cruell pirrhus liue prison bounde vnto though full lothe hande assured ful many othe serue lust aye captyuytye lo thus standeth atastus tho full entencion many questyon enquered daliaunce ought knewe pirrhus gouernaunce could ought vnderstande kept sith came lande ywisse quod ye list haue kepeth close lo yonder caue amonge brusshayle shrouded face makinge signe place done ydellmase king thitherwarde gan gase hasty pirrhus gan sworde outdrawe purpose fully atastus haue slawe wonderly storye lere pquene thetides anone appere albe reygned teares face gan sworde pirrhus embrace prayinge deadly hande restrayne hast thou killed yong brother twayn ala father hore graye merciles fro wilt take awaye put vp sworde bloud ne shede haue pytye vpon thy kinrede aduerte clerely fyne thou art come line hatefull loke aryght vnkinde bloud euery mannes sight pyrrhus tho tygre wrothe afferme gan many sacred othe grutche agaynst playne shall hym sle handes twayne pfor hath false extorsion pput pelleus regyon whyche lorde ye trewe wyfe fynally shall lese hys lyfe anone myne handes deye matter seye pelleus darynge caue ye grace lyste lyfe saue helpe platly nought pelleus anone forthe brought croked olde vnweldy eke se tofore pyrrhus fell downe hys kne besechinge hym wyth pyteous face hys request take hym hys grace pand wolde manly herte goodly beholde deadly wo smerte pof atastus mortall payne tho hadde sonnes twaine whiche lay dead tofore hym grene slaine swerd yt sharpe kene ne may recure wyse sorow ought ynough suffyse though ye hym vengeaunce well peysed iustly balaunce sith hooly submytted myghte taketh mercy anone ryght let sworde age consume request dare presume pirrhus shortly sayne put vp sword agayne seynge mercy myght auayle without wordes rehersayle fyrste tofore theim euerychone kynges made accorden one wysedome concludynge vp dede eche theim shuld right possede pin thesalye parted twayne neyther matter complayne eueryche reygne dewe see togyther thre presence man patastus fyrste thus tale began psyres quod vnknowe age brought lowe nature kindly mocion wexed feble wyt reason beynge vnweldy lymmes many yeares vpon fall vnneth thinge discerne feble sothe kingedome gouerne lyfe death takynge nowe hede sith sonnes slayne dead sole lefte withouten heyre worldly luste fully dispeyre tyme passed felycytye fortune tourne mutabylytye hathe taughte playnlye dare well expresse worldly ioye sykernesse truste abyde wyll selfe prouyde haste prudent purueaunce clere discharge gouernaunce agayne sorte list maligne pbut sceptre crowne frely resigne thesalye lordship lande fre hole thy hande shall man reclayme saye naye interrupte make delaye touchinge thinge conclusyon put full possession hereupon euer abyde makynge full fayth hand layde quene thetides syttynge present pelleus entent vnto pirrhus purpartye resygned eke ryght thesalye fully affermynge yore ago full desyre ioye also euer one neuewe succede ryghtfull heyre kingdome possede vtterly without repentaunce belongeth vnto lygeaunce sceptre sworde crowne dyademe kynge lyfe death deme thy hande without longer date houre holy translate knot conuencion fully brought concluson perfourmed vp hole vnyte euermore atwene kinges thre atastus knightes disseuered enuyrowne forest descended downe byddynge platly theyr lorde echone sworne accorde attones lusty companye thesalye fast gan theim hye pirrhus folke lyinge sea sayled forthe streyght cytye atastus doth sytte parliament openly gaue commaundement liege hygh lowe estate wythout strife debate specially gentyll bloud yborne daye pirrhus sworne like theyr degree royall hall perseuer trewe liege durynge theyr lyfe ernest game pelleus commauded hath partye without fraude thus ioye solempne laude pirrhus euery maner age gladly accepted heritage daye fortunate good glad aspectes heuen stode well accordynge maner thinge worthy pirrhus ycrowned kinge thesalye riche regyon vayne make mencion theyr reuell theyr great arraye feast made daye eke story finde sothe wyll passe ouer mine auctour dothe saue booke specefyed kingdome fer magnefyed thesalye puyssaunce might pyrrhus whylom good knight hym leaue royall see ptournynge agayne kynge ydumee ygraue vnder stone pand hym hys sonne meeryone story saith crowned king crete awhyle reygninge equyte dyed also wolde none pand hast leorica hys brother rightfull heyre successyon crowned kinge regyon pin tyme atastus drede thassent pyrrhus rede full busy make specyal ryche toumbe passyngly royall buryed full huge prese pmenalyppus polystenes two forest slawe thorugh pirrhus swerde full cruell law pof none processe make euen fully tale take bothe also eke yfere pof atastus theyr owne father dere whome sothly hys locke hore troye booke rede pbut must pirrhus wende wryte sorye wofull ende whan sat highest see made full blinde vayne prosperyte gouerning tho lande thesalye pthere hym betydde fall fantasye sette hys loue hermyon quene phorestes wyfe reygnynge methene whome brent hote fyre fulfyllyng hys foule desyre purpose hole thus brought aboute rauyshyng lorde oute tho led hir home helde wyfe seminge hym blysfull lyfe full relese paynes smerte pof whyche horestes bare full heuy herte caste hym playnely auenged whan therto hath opportunyte time though susteined wrong phe feble pyrrhus strong pwhiche helde also storye tolde pandromecha hym housholde phectors wyfe whylom lytell chylde whyche hir ladde sege complete destructiowne whan brought troye towne laomedonte fende name encreasyng full worthy fame pand pyrrhus sonne also pachylleydos calleth hym guydo woman theyr great estate atwene selfe amonge debate pand hermyone yre full hote complayning thus father wrote fere hygh degree andronomecha cherished better tha kynge pyrrhus besechynge menelay hym enhaste al euer maye come hym selfe anone slea woman childe also naught abode fastgan hym hye heate towardes thesalye avenged swerde stele herein fauleth neuer adele maugre hym cruelte reskewed amyd cite p thynge hath herde woman kynge draw hys swerde wyll thys matter dwelle maner shamed wryte telle done pyrrh courage delos gone pilgrimage hauinge litell route pto apollo knele loute soule praye achylle hys vowes also fulfylle hym thanke hyghe affeccyon good exployte hadde troye towne wreche phorestes slewe owne hande fynde sothe made diffence sodayne mortall vyolence enuye could asterte sworde myght aduerte enuyron beset thilke tyme myght bet nother socour declyne thus pyrrhus brought fine plate crowned kinge thesalye lo guerdon auoutrye lo mede rewarde ful rife misuse mannes wife dread folowe shall vengeaunce sodayne death vnware myschaunce euery man greatly ought charge delos
