achylleydos suche eke pryson close without raunsome shall delyuered pand reioyse full lyberte custome vsed borough towne lyeges great regyon thus folke yt came thralle fro troye restored sodaynely ioye pby lamedowne ymade free eke reygneth royall sea full myghtly haue made mynde troye boke hym fynde pyrrhus kynrede fro henseforth processe reade pbut incydentes beare substaunce whiche vayne put remebrance except myne auctour note entent impeth littell incydent ywrought done full yore agone touchynge death kyng menon whyche enuye cruell achylles slayne soth amonge myrmydones onely proudely gan pursewe vpon achylles troylus reskue pwhom kynge pryam made buryed besyde troylus troye cyte temple ybylte marbell olde fyne tale tolde chapitle shall reherse anone noble quene kynge menon tyme longe many day deade grauen vnder claye toumbe heuenly gan appere albe set bryght sterres clere whose symylytude reken lyke thynge immortall man myght vtterly sustene beholde loke shene downe descendynge fro fyrmament full many man beynge present clade mantell ful celestyall porte passyngly royall swetenesse freshe rose made haste tombe vnclose lorde taketh bone chest made golde stone couched fast euer maye dispeyred went anone waye tofore certayne place neuer sayne afferminge lyklynesse aungell goddesse soule fate kynge deme suche heauenly thynge therin holde none opinyon transcendeth shortly reason lyst suche matter diffyne resorte ryght lyne vlixes dwell ende surplus tell myght escape parodye hym shape parchas haue last terme sette attropos mesured mette liues threde rocke sponne diffende thy selfe vlixes thou konne shewe thy manhode aferde welfare thy sonnes sworde shall nowe like wonte sharpe penne rude blonte descriue fine thy soioure vpon boundes set laboure almost wery weake faynt ynough beastes ox plough longe daye agayne hyll wende almost landes ende troye booke fyche wyll stake saue must spende fewe lynes blake laste chapiter shortly translate worke ympen date daye death sette areste full execute loued best lowe knee must loute god maketh men route causeth folkes haue glad swenenes morowe lusty euenes morphe u slepy wande holdeth alwaye hande hath marked agayne nyght make men mery lyght whyle haue gladnesse sodeynly falle heauynesse lyke gyueth euydence sondry sygnes apparence vnto lord must mekely preye tyme style conueye vlyxes dreame discryue laste lyue declarynge hym token full notable sygnes demonstrable slepte agayne pale mone fatall day shulde folowe soone fell thus abedde laye mydnyght tofore morowe graye phym thought sawe appeare creature syght celestyall fygure none erthly thynge veryly deuyne porte chere wonder femynyne pand hym sempte fantasye lyke thynge sent fayrye beaute goodly face recomforted playnely place surmountynge souerayne clerenesse eyen twayne sodeynly men myght aduerte perce woulde euen herte deffence none myght deuysed pand vlyxes loke supprysed gan beholde alwaye slepe syghe sore persynge aye full busy peyne enbrace armes twayne pbut aye gan pursue agaynewarde gan hym eschewe aye preysed se aye hym gan flee contrayre hym fortune whan sawe importune asked hym shortly wolde platte trouth tolde pcertes quod lyues emperysse ye woman goddesse deme iudge halfe ryght derked blynded syght pbut dare well affyrme place lyfe deth stande hoolely grace mercy requyrynge ryght rewe owne knight pyte compassyon goodly se saluacyon desyre maye fulfyll night haue wyll recure remedye lacke routhe nedely must dye haue atwixe hope dread selfe declared womanhead kept close tho full sadly gan smyle put remembraunce sayde vnto sobre countenaunce sothly quod thine affection would fully tourne confusion v perellous inly mortall contagyous vtterly gayne may reade one v must anone dead fyne hateful chaunce folowe pleasaunce vlixes gan nighen nere beholdinge aye heauenly cheare stode vp right grdunde sawe holde spere longe rounde head therof borned stele forged newe grounde wonder wele pand therupon auisiowne sawe baner blasynge vp downe felde therof coloure ynde full fyshes beaten fynde pand bokes like tolde middes large crowne golde pand tourne gan face lykly anone parte place spake sayd wordes playne full token partynge v twayne euermore efte sowre ne swete daye neuer agayne mete disaperinge anone leue toke sodaynly awoke gan musen fantasye maner thing dreme might sygnefy mente euill good secretnesse tho vnderstode surmounted sothly reason therfore sente throughout region suche subtill exposytoures fate sorte crafty dyuinours clerkes subeict crowne assemble one sweuen expowne pand knewe informacyon maner hole auision byn concluded according one time aprocheth shall come anone one next kinrede spere shulde make herte blede plet se fate gan remewe sith harde destynye teschewe saye tho folke theyr opinion worke trust constellacion vlixes musynge tale chaungeth coloure gan wexeen pale wonder dreadfull full fantasyes gan selfe seke remedyes awaye voyde thinge phe stareth brode maye se inwarde loke cloude yblent pbut weninge prudent pmade call hym sonne thelamon take shet vp pryson supposynge fully witte mischiefe therby go quite aduerteth ne toke none hede sharpenesse speares head fish baner beate sea wherin swimme flete quene called circe signes brought wer peace crowne token dignyte one holde shall royall see waltryng amid wawes fell woo amonge fyshes large floud pand shall make ful diuision tofore remembred auision agayne ignoraunce execute fatall puruyaunce vp dreame spere stele whych vlixes consydreth neuer dele pnor wyght hath suspection pbut sonne called thelamon closed shet vp towre pand vlixes coste great laboure fro daye daye doth busynesse selfe make forteresse bilte rocke lime square stone depe ditched none man maye enter syde casteth hys lyfe abyde certayne men chosen specyall pnight daye watche vpon wall maner wyght shulde haue none entree falle aye secree knowen olde counsayle sworne ye story rehersed hath forne olde foole dotarde vlixes sonne begot cyrces freshe lusty yonge coragious called thelagonyus pborne see amonge floddes rage also reken age fyue twenty yeres aboute pbut hys father aye doute man mighte beynge therof securytie tyll daye desyrous knowe hys mother fell knee lowe beseching goodly spare hys father trouthe declare shuld dwelle besought woulde hym tell pbut sothly longe many dayes hyghe prudence put hym delayes tyll sawe might haue reste importune requeste whe knew ther none bote fro poynt poynt tolde crop rote pof vlixes kynge anone made taryinge toke leue may none playnely sayde wolde hys father se pwherof quene gan herte colde saw might wtholde hym besought wyth chere debonayre wolde soone agayne repayre forthe sayleth onwarde way without abode selfe day many porte many fer countre tyll brought would pto achaya lande great renowne gan serche regyon place paleys pryncypall kinge helde see royall longe countre rode tyll taught kynge abode vlixes shytte vp mewe place haste gan pursewe great party releued hys sorow monday erely morow pvnto brydge ryghteway toke foude porter deynous hys loke lowely fyrste gan praye voutsafe hym goodly conueye courte make taryinge message hadde kynge pbut proudely denyed gate shortly sayd came late entre maner wyse eke vngoodly gan despyse frowarde speche malycyous haste thys thelagonyus heart ferde proude porter hente berde fyste rofe chawe bone fell deade muet stone eke tho withstode made proudely lepe flode whan mo came maken resistence hente swerde manly vyolence furyously hys yrous tene story sayeth slewe fyftene hym selfe almoste wounded death gan wery sothly fayle breath vlixes noyse sowne bridge descendyd downe fynding men entre gate dead slayne full mortall hate full yrous hente anone adarte auenture standinge tho aparte cruelly caste thelagon yet stroke conclusyon domaged glode asyde haste longer would abyde hent vp darte without arest smote king lowe vnder brest ribbes shortly saye wounde must nedes deye hauinge tho opinion kinge suspection owne father slawe fast gan ende drawe wound deadly kene might selfe sustene pale wan grounde gan glide men vpon euery syde busy helpe hym releue sore gan ake greue well felte must dead pbut abrayding lift vp head hauynge yet perfect minde reason remembre gan auysyon tolde dreade one next kinrede descended downe owne lyne sweuen shall parfourme fyne accomplishe wyth darte stele could naught conceyuen wele shulde badde anone vnto meyne without harme vyolence sette anone vnto presence yonge man whych gate stode hath daye shed muche bloud pand afore vlixes brought hath enquyred sought fyrste kyn next countre pcertes quod borne sea amonge fyshes myd wawes grene sayde also mother quene called circe name kouthe east west eke right fer south tolde also father kynge hym begat home comynge fro troye towne towarde countre mother circe tolde serteinly vlixes hyghte desyrous haue syghte entred myghty regyon haue pursewed vnto dungeon onely hope father haue seyne se well laboure vayne syth sothe lost trauayle maye syde auayle folly longer dwell lo tell kynred aske pwith vlixes gan syghe sore lacke bloud full pale sayde anone herde tale pnow wot well wofull destynye fulfylled maye none wot well late grutche stryue agayne piteous fate pfor sonne clerkes whilom tolde hath made ende dayes olde theron exspectant paynes full greuous pand worde thelagonius wist agayne nature lawe ala father slawe ye land longe borne crowne without abode fell anone swowne phi clothes rente yelowe heyre torne palas quod euer borne cursed woful destynye fortune haue effecte symple folke full compassyon goodly correction amende thynge hyndre neuer adele custome aye ready saye wele groude well sayinge lyfe hyndred makyng maister chaucer yt founde ful many spot condicion thinge begonne knightly abyde tyme manly set asyde rest ease coste theron spente til thou haue wonne fine thin entente pmost circumspect passinge auisee al thy workes conueyed wt high prudece sad demure like iosuee agayne whose swerde gayneth resystece hast also heauenly influence salamon wisely discerne onely grace thy people gouerne pmercy eke ment thy magnificence oppressed haue
